 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
 devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet
 vyāsaṃ vasiṣṭhanaptāraṃ śakteḥ pautram akalmaṣam
 parāśarātmajaṃ vande śukatātaṃ taponidhim
 vyāsāya viṣṇurūpāya vyāsarūpāya viṣṇave
 namo vai brahmanidhaye vāsiṣṭhāya namo namaḥ
 janamejaya uvāca
a kathaṃ yuyudhire vīrāḥ kurupāṇḍavasomakāḥ
c pārthivāś ca mahābhāgā nānādeśasamāgatāḥ
d pratyayudhyanta samare bhīṣmeṇāmitrakarṣiṇā
d kathaṃ vā kauravāḥ sarve bhīmasene camūpatau
d niveśaṃ cakrire yoddhuṃ tan me śaṃsa mahāmate
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a yathā yuyudhire vīrāḥ kurupāṇḍavasomakāḥ
c kurukṣetre tapaḥkṣetre śṛṇu tat pṛthivīpate
a avatīrya kurukṣetraṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sahasomakāḥ
c kauravān abhyavartanta jigīṣanto mahābalāḥ
a vedādhyayanasaṃpannāḥ sarve yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c āśaṃsanto jayaṃ yuddhe vadhaṃ vābhimukhā raṇe
d pūrvabhāge tu kṣetrasya sthitāḥ pratyaṅmukhā yudhi
a abhiyāya ca durdharṣāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya vāhinīm
c prāṅmukhāḥ paścime bhāge nyaviśanta sasainikāḥ
a samantapañcakād bāhyaṃ śibirāṇi sahasraśaḥ
c kārayām āsa vidhivat kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a śūnyeva pṛthivī sarvā bālavṛddhāvaśeṣitā
c niraśvapuruṣā cāsīd rathakuñjaravarjitā
a yāvat tapati sūryo hi jambūdvīpasya maṇḍalam
c tāvad eva samāvṛttaṃ balaṃ pārthivasattama
a ekasthāḥ sarvavarṇās te maṇḍalaṃ bahuyojanam
c paryākrāmanta deśāṃś ca nadīḥ śailān vanāni ca
a teṣāṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā sarveṣāṃ puruṣarṣabha
c ādideśa savāhānāṃ bhakṣyabhojyam anuttamam
a saṃjñāś ca vividhās tās tās teṣāṃ cakre yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c evaṃvādī veditavyaḥ pāṇḍaveyo 'yam ity uta
a abhijñānāni sarveṣāṃ saṃjñāś cābharaṇāni ca
c yojayām āsa kauravyo yuddhakāla upasthite
a dṛṣṭvā dhvajāgraṃ pārthānāṃ dhārtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥ
c saha sarvair mahīpālaiḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavān
a pāṇḍureṇātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani
c madhye nāgasahasrasya bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritam
a dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ hṛṣṭāḥ sarve pāṇḍavasainikāḥ
a         prahṛṣṭavadanaṃ tataḥ
a āyodhanaṃ praviviśuḥ        
c dadhmuḥ sarve mahāśaṅkhān bherīr jaghnuḥ sahasraśaḥ
a tataḥ prahṛṣṭāṃ svāṃ senām abhivīkṣyātha pāṇḍavāḥ
c babhūvur hṛṣṭamanaso vāsudevaś ca vīryavān
a tato yodhān harṣayantau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
c dadhmatuḥ puruṣavyāghrau divyau śaṅkhau rathe sthitau
a pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaṃ devadattasya cobhayoḥ
c śrutvā savāhanā yodhāḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥ
a yathā siṃhasya nadataḥ svanaṃ śrutvetare mṛgāḥ
c traseyus tadvad evāsīd dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ tadā
a udatiṣṭhad rajo bhaumaṃ na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
c antardhīyata cādityaḥ sainyena rajasāvṛtaḥ
a vavarṣa cātra parjanyo māṃsaśoṇitavṛṣṭimān
c vyukṣan sarvāṇy anīkāni tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a vāyus tataḥ prādurabhūn nīcaiḥ śarkarakarṣaṇaḥ
c vinighnaṃs tāny anīkāni vidhamaṃś caiva tad rajaḥ
a ubhe sene tadā rājan yuddhāya mudite bhṛśam
c kurukṣetre sthite yatte sāgarakṣubhitopame
a tayos tu senayor āsīd adbhutaḥ sa samāgamaḥ
c yugānte samanuprāpte dvayoḥ sāgarayor iva
a śūnyāsīt pṛthivī sarvā bālavṛddhāvaśeṣitā
c tena senāsamūhena samānītena kauravaiḥ
d tatas te samayaṃ yuddhe syāt prītiś ca parasparam
d samantān nagakalpena garjamānena rvataḥ
a tatas te samayaṃ cakruḥ kurupāṇḍavasomakāḥ
c dharmāṃś ca sthāpayām āsur yuddhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
a nivṛtte caiva no yuddhe prītiś ca syāt parasparam
c yathāpuraṃ yathāyogaṃ na ca syāc chalanaṃ punaḥ
a vācā yuddhe pravṛtte no vācaiva pratiyodhanam
c niṣkrāntaḥ pṛtanāmadhyān na hantavyaḥ kathaṃ cana
a rathī ca rathinā yodhyo gajena gajadhūrgataḥ
c aśvenāśvī padātiś ca padātenaiva bhārata
a yathāyogaṃ yathāvīryaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathāvayaḥ
c samābhāṣya prahartavyaṃ na viśvaste na vihvale
a pareṇa saha saṃyuktaḥ pramatto vimukhas tathā
c kṣīṇaśastro vivarmā ca na hantavyaḥ kathaṃ cana
a na sūteṣu na dhuryeṣu na ca śastropanāyiṣu
c na bherīśaṅkhavādeṣu prahartavyaṃ kathaṃ cana
a evaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtvā kurupāṇḍavasomakāḥ
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ prekṣamāṇāḥ parasparam
a niviśya ca mahātmānas tatas te puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c hṛṣṭarūpāḥ sumanaso babhūvuḥ sahasainikāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ pūrvāpare saṃdhye samīkṣya bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c sarvavedavidāṃ śreṣṭho vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥ
a bhaviṣyati raṇe ghore bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥ
c pratyakṣadarśī bhagavān bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyavit
a vaicitravīryaṃ rājānaṃ sa rahasyaṃ bravīd idam
c śocantam ārtaṃ dhyāyantaṃ putrāṇām anayaṃ tadā
 vyāsa uvāca
a rājan parītakālās te putrāś cānye ca bhūmipāḥ
c te haniṣyanti saṃgrāme samāsādyetaretaram
a teṣu kālaparīteṣu vinaśyatsu ca bhārata
c kālaparyāyam ājñāya mā sma śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
a yadi tv icchasi saṃgrāme draṣṭum enaṃ viśāṃ pate
c cakṣur dadāni te hanta yuddham etan niśāmaya
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a na rocaye jñātivadhaṃ draṣṭuṃ brahmarṣisattama
c yuddham etat tv aśeṣeṇa śṛṇuyāṃ tava tejasā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasminn anicchati draṣṭuṃ saṃgrāmaṃ śrotum icchati
c varāṇām īśvaro dātā saṃjayāya varaṃ dadau
 vyāsa uvāca
a eṣa te saṃjayo rājan yuddham etad vadiṣyati
c etasya sarvaṃ saṃgrāme naparokṣaṃ bhaviṣyati
a cakṣuṣā saṃjayo rājan divyenaiṣa samanvitaḥ
c kathayiṣyati te yuddhaṃ sarvajñaś ca bhaviṣyati
a prakāśaṃ vā rahasyaṃ vā rātrau vā yadi vā divā
c manasā cintitam api sarvaṃ vetsyati saṃjayaḥ
a nainaṃ śastrāṇi bhetsyanti nainaṃ bādhiṣyate śramaḥ
c gāvalgaṇir ayaṃ jīvan yuddhād asmād vimokṣyate
a ahaṃ ca kīrtim eteṣāṃ kurūṇāṃ bharatarṣabha
c pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ prathayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ
a diṣṭam etat purā caiva nātra śocitum arhasi
c na caiva śakyaṃ saṃyantuṃ yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā sa bhagavān kurūṇāṃ prapitāmahaḥ
c punar eva mahābāhuṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram uvāca ha
a iha yuddhe mahārāja bhaviṣyati mahān kṣayaḥ
c yathemāni nimittāni bhayāyādyopalakṣaye
a śyenā gṛdhrāś ca kākāś ca kaṅkāś ca sahitā balaiḥ
c saṃpatanti vanānteṣu samavāyāṃś ca kurvate
a atyugraṃ ca prapaśyanti yuddham ānandino dvijāḥ
c kravyādā bhakṣayiṣyanti māṃsāni gajavājinām
a khaṭākhaṭeti vāśanto bhairavaṃ bhayavedinaḥ
c kahvāḥ prayānti madhyena dakṣiṇām abhito diśam
a ubhe pūrvāpare saṃdhye nityaṃ paśyāmi bhārata
a         rajoyukte ca bhārata
a durnimittāni sarvāṇi        
c udayāstamane sūryaṃ kabandhaiḥ parivāritam
a śvetalohitaparyantāḥ kṛṣṇagrīvāḥ savidyutaḥ
c trivarṇāḥ parighāḥ saṃdhau bhānum āvārayanty uta
a jvalitārkendunakṣatraṃ nirviśeṣadinakṣapam
c ahorātraṃ mayā dṛṣṭaṃ tatkṣayāya bhaviṣyati
a alakṣyaḥ prabhayā hīnaḥ paurṇamāsīṃ ca kārttikīm
c candro 'bhūd agnivarṇaś ca samavarṇe nabhastale
a svapsyanti nihatā vīrā bhūmim āvṛtya pārthivāḥ
c rājāno rājaputrāś ca śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
a antarikṣe varāhasya vṛṣadaṃśasya cobhayoḥ
c praṇādaṃ yudhyato rātrau raudraṃ nityaṃ pralakṣaye
a devatāpratimāś cāpi kampanti ca hasanti ca
c vamanti rudhiraṃ cāsyaiḥ svidyanti prapatanti ca
a anāhatā dundubhayaḥ praṇadanti viśāṃ pate
c ayuktāś ca pravartante kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahārathāḥ
a kokilāḥ śatapatrāś ca cāṣā bhāsāḥ śukās tathā
c sārasāś ca mayūrāś ca vāco muñcanti dāruṇāḥ
a gṛhītaśastrābharaṇā varmiṇo vājipṛṣṭhagāḥ
c aruṇodayeṣu dṛśyante śataśaḥ śalabhavrajāḥ
a ubhe saṃdhye prakāśete diśāṃ dāhasamanvite
c āsīd rudhiravarṣaṃ ca asthivarṣaṃ ca bhārata
a yā caiṣā viśrutā rājaṃs trailokye sādhusaṃmatā
c arundhatī tayāpy eṣa vasiṣṭhaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtaḥ
a rohiṇīṃ pīḍayann eṣa sthito rājañ śanaiścaraḥ
c vyāvṛttaṃ lakṣma somasya bhaviṣyati mahad bhayam
a anabhre ca mahāghoraṃ stanitaṃ śrūyate 'niśam
c vāhanānāṃ ca rudatāṃ prapatanty aśrubindavaḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a kharā goṣu prajāyante ramante mātṛbhiḥ sutāḥ
c anārtavaṃ puṣpaphalaṃ darśayanti vane drumāḥ
a garbhiṇyo rājaputryaś ca janayanti vibhīṣaṇān
c kravyādān pakṣiṇaś caiva gomāyūn aparān mṛgān
a triviṣāṇāś caturnetrāḥ pañcapādā dvimehanāḥ
c dviśīrṣāś ca dvipucchāś ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ paśavo 'śivāḥ
a jāyante vivṛtāsyāś ca vyāharanto 'śivā giraḥ
c tripadāḥ śikhinas tārkṣyāś caturdaṃṣṭrā viṣāṇinaḥ
a tathaivānyāś ca dṛśyante striyaś ca brahmavādinām
c vainateyān mayūrāṃś ca janayantyaḥ pure tava
a govatsaṃ vaḍavā sūte śvā sṛgālaṃ mahīpate
c krakarāñ śārikāś caiva śukāṃś cāśubhavādinaḥ
a striyaḥ kāś cit prajāyante catasraḥ pañca kanyakāḥ
c tā jātamātrā nṛtyanti gāyanti ca hasanti ca
a pṛthagjanasya kuḍakāḥ stanapāḥ stenaveśmani
c nṛtyanti parigāyanti vedayanto mahad bhayam
a pratimāś cālikhanty anye saśastrāḥ kālacoditāḥ
c anyonyam abhidhāvanti śiśavo daṇḍapāṇayaḥ
e uparundhanti kṛtvā ca nagarāṇi yuyutsavaḥ
a padmotpalāni vṛkṣeṣu jāyante kumudāni ca
c viṣvagvātāś ca vānty ugrā rajo na vyupaśāmyati
a abhīkṣṇaṃ kampate bhūmir arkaṃ rāhus tathāgrasat
c śveto grahas tathā citrāṃ samatikramya tiṣṭhati
a abhāvaṃ hi viśeṣeṇa kurūṇāṃ pratipaśyati
c dhūmaketur mahāghoraḥ puṣyam ākramya tiṣṭhati
a senayor aśivaṃ ghoraṃ kariṣyati mahāgrahaḥ
c maghāsv aṅgārako vakraḥ śravaṇe ca bṛhaspatiḥ
a bhāgyaṃ nakṣatram ākramya sūryaputreṇa pīḍyate
c śukraḥ proṣṭhapade pūrve samāruhya viśāṃ pate
e uttare tu parikramya sahitaḥ pratyudīkṣate
a śyāmo grahaḥ prajvalitaḥ sadhūmaḥ sahapāvakaḥ
c aindraṃ tejasvi nakṣatraṃ jyeṣṭhām ākramya tiṣṭhati
a dhruvaḥ prajvalito ghoram apasavyaṃ pravartate
b rohiṇīṃ pīḍayaty evam ubhau ca śaśibhāskarau
c citrāsvātyantare caiva dhiṣṭhitaḥ paruṣo grahaḥ
a vakrānuvakraṃ kṛtvā ca śravaṇe pāvakaprabhaḥ
c brahmarāśiṃ samāvṛtya lohitāṅgo vyavasthitaḥ
a sarvasasyapraticchannā pṛthivī phalamālinī
c pañcaśīrṣā yavāś caiva śataśīrṣāś ca śālayaḥ
a pradhānāḥ sarvalokasya yāsv āyattam idaṃ jagat
c tā gāvaḥ prasnutā vatsaiḥ śoṇitaṃ prakṣaranty uta
a niścerur apidhānebhyaḥ khaḍgāḥ prajvalitā bhṛśam
c vyaktaṃ paśyanti śastrāṇi saṃgrāmaṃ samupasthitam
a agnivarṇā yathā bhāsaḥ śastrāṇām udakasya ca
c kavacānāṃ dhvajānāṃ ca bhaviṣyati mahān kṣayaḥ
d pṛthivī śoṇitāvartā dhvajoḍupasamākulā
d kurūṇāṃ vaiśase rājan pāṇḍavaiḥ saha bhārata
a dikṣu prajvalitāsyāś ca vyāharanti mṛgadvijāḥ
c atyāhitaṃ darśayanto vedayanti mahad bhayam
a ekapakṣākṣicaraṇaḥ śakuniḥ khacaro niśi
c raudraṃ vadati saṃrabdhaḥ śoṇitaṃ chardayan muhuḥ
a grahau tāmrāruṇaśikhau prajvalantāv iva sthitau
c saptarṣīṇām udārāṇāṃ samavacchādya vai prabhām
a saṃvatsarasthāyinau ca grahau prajvalitāv ubhau
c viśākhayoḥ samīpasthau bṛhaspatiśanaiścarau
a kṛttikāsu grahas tīvro nakṣatre prathame jvalan
c vapūṃṣy apaharan bhāsā dhūmaketur iva sthitaḥ
d viṣamaṃ vedayanty eta ākrandajananaṃ mahat
a triṣu pūrveṣu sarveṣu nakṣatreṣu viśāṃ pate
c budhaḥ saṃpatate 'bhīkṣṇaṃ janayan sumahad bhayam
a caturdaśīṃ pañcadaśīṃ bhūtapūrvāṃ ca ṣoḍaśīm
c imāṃ tu nābhijānāmi amāvāsyāṃ trayodaśīm
a candrasūryāv ubhau grastāv ekamāse trayodaśīm
c aparvaṇi grahāv etau prajāḥ saṃkṣapayiṣyataḥ
a rajovṛtā diśaḥ sarvāḥ pāṃsuvarṣaiḥ samantataḥ
c utpātameghā raudrāś ca rātrau varṣanti śoṇitam
a māṃsavarṣaṃ punas tīvram āsīt kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm
c ardharātre mahāghoram atṛpyaṃs tatra rākṣasāḥ
a pratisroto 'vahan nadyaḥ saritaḥ śoṇitodakāḥ
c phenāyamānāḥ kūpāś ca nardanti vṛṣabhā iva
e patanty ulkāḥ sanirghātāḥ śuṣkāśanivimiśritāḥ
a adya caiva niśāṃ vyuṣṭām udaye bhānur āhataḥ
c jvalantībhir maholkābhiś caturbhiḥ sarvatodiśam
a ādityam upatiṣṭhadbhis tatra coktaṃ maharṣibhiḥ
c bhūmipālasahasrāṇāṃ bhūmiḥ pāsyati śoṇitam
a kailāsamandarābhyāṃ tu tathā himavato gireḥ
c sahasraśo mahāśabdaṃ śikharāṇi patanti ca
a mahābhūtā bhūmikampe caturaḥ sāgarān pṛthak
c velām udvartayanti sma kṣobhayantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
a vṛkṣān unmathya vānty ugrā vātāḥ śarkarakarṣiṇaḥ
b ābhagnāḥ sumahāvātair aśanībhiḥ samāhatāḥ
c patanti caityavṛkṣāś ca grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca
a pītalohitanīlaś ca jvalaty agnir huto dvijaiḥ
c vāmārciḥ śāvagandhī ca dhūmaprāyaḥ kharasvanaḥ
e sparśā gandhā rasāś caiva viparītā mahīpate
a dhūmāyante dhvajā rājñāṃ kampamānā muhur muhuḥ
c muñcanty aṅgāravarṣāṇi bheryo 'tha paṭahās tathā
a prāsādaśikharāgreṣu puradvāreṣu caiva hi
c gṛdhrāḥ paripatanty ugrā vāmaṃ maṇḍalam āśritāḥ
a pakvāpakveti subhṛśaṃ vāvāśyante vayāṃsi ca
c nilīyante dhvajāgreṣu kṣayāya pṛthivīkṣitām
a dhyāyantaḥ prakirantaś ca vālān vepathusaṃyutāḥ
c rudanti dīnās turagā mātaṅgāś ca sahasraśaḥ
d gṛhakṣakṣetrakhalādyeṣu valmīkā madhukāni ca
d hastyaśvarathaśālās tu 
su kapotāś cāśritās tathā
d ete cānye ca bahava utpātā ghoradarśanāḥ

d evaṃvidhaṃ durnimittaṃ kṣayāya pṛthivīkṣitām
d bhaumaṃ divyaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ trividhaṃ jāyate 'niśam

a pitur vaco niśamyaitad dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bravīd idam
c diṣṭam etat purā manye bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a kṣatriyāḥ kṣatradharmeṇa vadhyante yadi saṃyuge

a iha kīrtiṃ pare loke dīrghakālaṃ mahat sukham

 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam ukto munis tattvaṃ kavīndro rājasattama
c putreṇa dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa dhyānam anvagamat param
a punar evābravīd vākyaṃ kālavādī mahātapāḥ
c asaṃśayaṃ pārthivendra kālaḥ saṃkṣipate jagat
a sṛjate ca punar lokān neha vidyati śāśvatam
c jñātīnāṃ ca kurūṇāṃ ca saṃbandhisuhṛdāṃ tathā
a dharmyaṃ deśaya panthānaṃ samartho hy asi vāraṇe
c kṣudraṃ jñātivadhaṃ prāhur mā kuruṣva mamāpriyam
a kālo 'yaṃ putrarūpeṇa tava jāto viśāṃ pate
c na vadhaḥ pūjyate vede hitaṃ naitat kathaṃ cana
a hanyāt sa eva yo hanyāt kuladharmaṃ svakāṃ tanum
c kālenotpathagantāsi śakye sati yathāpathi
a kulasyāsya vināśāya tathaiva ca mahīkṣitām
c anartho rājyarūpeṇa tyajyatām asukhāvahaḥ
a luptaprajñaḥ pareṇāsi dharmaṃ darśaya vai sutān
c kiṃ te rājyena durdharṣa yena prāpto 'si kilbiṣam
a yaśo dharmaṃ ca kīrtiṃ ca pālayan svargam āpsyasi
c labhantāṃ pāṇḍavā rājyaṃ śamaṃ gacchantu kauravāḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca vārayiṣyāmi saṃyuge
a evaṃ bruvati viprendre dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c ākṣipya vākyaṃ vākyajño vākpathenāpy ayāt punaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yathā bhavān veda tathāsmi vettā
bhāvābhāvau viditau me yathāvat
c svārthe hi saṃmuhyati tāta loko
māṃ cāpi lokātmakam eva viddhi
a prasādaye tvām atulaprabhāvaṃ
tvaṃ no gatir darśayitā ca dhīraḥ
c na cāpi te vaśagā me maharṣe
na kalmaṣaṃ kartum ihārhase mām
a tvaṃ hi dharmaḥ pavitraṃ ca yaśaḥ kīrtir dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca mānyaś cāsi pitāmahaḥ
d kuruṣva kāryaṃ yat satyaṃ tvatto mānyo na vidyate
 vyāsa uvāca
a vaicitravīrya nṛpate yat te manasi vartate
c abhidhatsva yathākāmaṃ chettāsmi tava saṃśayam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yāni liṅgāni saṃgrāme bhavanti vijayiṣyatām
c tāni sarvāṇi bhagavañ śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a prasannabhāḥ pāvaka ūrdhvaraśmiḥ
pradakṣiṇāvartaśikho vidhūmaḥ
c puṇyā gandhāś cāhutīnāṃ pravānti
jayasyaitad bhāvino rūpam āhuḥ
a gambhīraghoṣāś ca mahāsvanāś ca
śaṅkhā mṛdaṅgāś ca nadanti yatra
c viśuddharaśmis tapanaḥ śaśī ca
jayasyaitad bhāvino rūpam āhuḥ
a iṣṭā vācaḥ pṛṣṭhato vāyasānāṃ
saṃprasthitānāṃ ca gamiṣyatāṃ ca
c ye pṛṣṭhatas te tvarayanti rājan
ye tv agratas te pratiṣedhayanti
a kalyāṇavācaḥ śakunā rājahaṃsāḥ
śukāḥ krauñcāḥ śatapatrāś ca yatra
c pradakṣiṇāś caiva bhavanti saṃkhye
dhruvaṃ jayaṃ tatra vadanti viprāḥ
a alaṃkāraiḥ kavacaiḥ ketubhiś ca
mukhaprasādair hemavarṇaiś ca nṝṇām
c bhrājiṣmatī duṣpratiprekṣaṇīyā
yeṣāṃ camūs te vijayanti śatrūn
a hṛṣṭā vācas tathā sattvaṃ yodhānāṃ yatra bhārata
c na mlāyante srajaś caiva te taranti raṇe ripūn
a iṣṭo vātaḥ praviṣṭasya dakṣiṇā pravivikṣataḥ
c paścāt saṃsādhayaty arthaṃ purastāt pratiṣedhate
a śabdarūparasasparśagandhāś cāviṣkṛtāḥ śubhāḥ
c sadā yodhāś ca hṛṣṭāś ca yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ dhruvaṃ jayaḥ
a anv eva vāyavo vānti tathābhrāṇi vayāṃsi ca
c anuplavante meghāś ca tathaivendradhanūṃṣi ca
a etāni jayamānānāṃ lakṣaṇāni viśāṃ pate
c bhavanti viparītāni mumūrṣūṇāṃ janādhipa
a alpāyāṃ vā mahatyāṃ vā senāyām iti niścitam
c harṣo yodhagaṇasyaikaṃ jayalakṣaṇam ucyate
a eko dīrṇo dārayati senāṃ sumahatīm api
c taṃ dīrṇam anudīryante yodhāḥ śūratamā api
a durnivāratamā caiva prabhagnā mahatī camūḥ
c apām iva mahāvegas trastā mṛgagaṇā iva
a naiva śakyā samādhātuṃ saṃnipāte mahācamūḥ
c dīrṇā ity eva dīryante yodhāḥ śūratamā api
e bhītān bhagnāṃś ca saṃprekṣya bhayaṃ bhūyo vivardhate
a prabhagnā sahasā rājan diśo vibhrāmitā paraiḥ
c naiva sthāpayituṃ śakyā śūrair api mahācamūḥ
a saṃbhṛtya mahatīṃ senāṃ caturaṅgāṃ mahīpatiḥ
b śaknoti na samādhātuṃ dīrṇām indrasamo yudhi
c upāyapūrvaṃ medhāvī yateta satatotthitaḥ
a upāyavijayaṃ śreṣṭham āhur bhedena madhyamam
c jaghanya eṣa vijayo yo yuddhena viśāṃ pate
e mahādoṣaḥ saṃnipātas tato vyaṅgaḥ sa ucyate
f paraspareṇa saṃdṛṣṭā surair api mahācamūḥ
f naiva sthāpayituṃ śakyā prabhagnā bhayavihvalā
a parasparajñāḥ saṃhṛṣṭā vyavadhūtāḥ suniścitāḥ
c pañcāśad api ye śūrā mathnanti mahatīṃ camūm
e atha vā pañca ṣaṭ sapta vijayanty anivartinaḥ
a na vainateyo garuḍaḥ praśaṃsati mahājanam
c dṛṣṭvā suparṇopacitiṃ mahatīm api bhārata
a na bāhulyena senāyā jayo bhavati bhārata
c adhruvo hi jayo nāma daivaṃ cātra parāyaṇam
e jayanto hy api saṃgrāme kṣayavanto bhavanty uta
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā yayau vyāso dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dhīmate
c dhṛtarāṣṭro 'pi tac chrutvā dhyānam evānvapadyata
a sa muhūrtam iva dhyātvā viniḥśvasya muhur muhuḥ
c saṃjayaṃ saṃśitātmānam apṛcchad bharatarṣabha
a saṃjayeme mahīpālāḥ śūrā yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c anyonyam abhinighnanti śastrair uccāvacair api
a pārthivāḥ pṛthivīhetoḥ samabhityaktajīvitāḥ
c na ca śāmyanti nighnanto vardhayanto yamakṣayam
a bhaumam aiśvaryam icchanto na mṛṣyante parasparam
c manye bahuguṇā bhūmis tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a bahūni ca sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
c koṭyaś ca lokavīrāṇāṃ sametāḥ kurujāṅgale
a deśānāṃ ca parīmāṇaṃ nagarāṇāṃ ca saṃjaya
c śrotum icchāmi tattvena yata ete samāgatāḥ
a divyabuddhipradīpena yuktas tvaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā
c prasādāt tasya viprarṣer vyāsasyāmitatejasaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yathāprajñaṃ mahāprājña bhaumān vakṣyāmi te guṇān
c śāstracakṣur avekṣasva namas te bharatarṣabha
a dvividhānīha bhūtāni trasāni sthāvarāṇi ca
c trasānāṃ trividhā yonir aṇḍasvedajarāyujāḥ
a trasānāṃ khalu sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhā rājañ jarāyujāḥ
c jarāyujānāṃ pravarā mānavāḥ paśavaś ca ye
a nānārūpāṇi bibhrāṇās teṣāṃ bhedāś caturdaśa
c araṇyavāsinaḥ sapta saptaiṣāṃ grāmavāsinaḥ
a siṃhavyāghravarāhāś ca mahiṣā vāraṇās tathā
c ṛkṣāś ca vānarāś caiva saptāraṇyāḥ smṛtā nṛpa
a gaur ajo manujo meṣo vājyaśvataragardabhāḥ
c ete grāmyāḥ samākhyātāḥ paśavaḥ sapta sādhubhiḥ
a ete vai paśavo rājan grāmyāraṇyāś caturdaśa
c vedoktāḥ pṛthivīpāla yeṣu yajñāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
a grāmyāṇāṃ puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ siṃhaś cāraṇyavāsinām
c sarveṣām eva bhūtānām anyonyenābhijīvanam
a udbhijjāḥ sthāvarāḥ proktās teṣāṃ pañcaiva jātayaḥ
c vṛkṣagulmalatāvallyas tvaksārās tṛṇajātayaḥ
a eṣāṃ viṃśatir ekonā mahābhūteṣu pañcasu
c caturviṃśatir uddiṣṭā gāyatrī lokasaṃmatā
a ya etāṃ veda gāyatrīṃ puṇyāṃ sarvaguṇānvitām
c tattvena bharataśreṣṭha sa lokān na praṇaśyati
a bhūmau hi jāyate sarvaṃ bhūmau sarvaṃ praṇaśyati
c bhūmiḥ pratiṣṭhā bhūtānāṃ bhūmir eva parāyaṇam
a yasya bhūmis tasya sarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam
c tatrābhigṛddhā rājāno vinighnantītaretaram
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a nadīnāṃ parvatānāṃ ca nāmadheyāni saṃjaya
c tathā janapadānāṃ ca ye cānye bhūmim āśritāḥ
a pramāṇaṃ ca pramāṇajña pṛthivyā api sarvaśaḥ
c nikhilena samācakṣva kānanāni ca saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a pañcemāni mahārāja mahābhūtāni saṃgrahāt
c jagat sthitāni sarvāṇi samāny āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
a bhūmir āpas tathā vāyur agnir ākāśam eva ca
c guṇottarāṇi sarvāṇi teṣāṃ bhūmiḥ pradhānataḥ
a śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥ
c bhūmer ete guṇāḥ proktā ṛṣibhis tattvavedibhiḥ
d śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca rasaś cāpi prakīrtitāḥ
a catvāro 'psu guṇā rājan gandhas tatra na vidyate
c śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca tejaso 'tha guṇās trayaḥ
e śabdaḥ sparśaś ca vāyos tu ākāśe śabda eva ca
a ete pañca guṇā rājan mahābhūteṣu pañcasu
c vartante sarvalokeṣu yeṣu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
a anyonyaṃ nābhivartante sāmyaṃ bhavati vai yadā
c yadā tu viṣamībhāvam āviśanti parasparam
e tadā dehair dehavanto vyatirohanti nānyathā
f bhāvaṃ na ca bhajantas te nāśaṃ gacchanti nānyathā
a ānupūrvyād vinaśyanti jāyante cānupūrvaśaḥ
c sarvāṇy aparimeyāni tad eṣāṃ rūpam aiśvaram
a tatra tatra hi dṛśyante dhātavaḥ pāñcabhautikāḥ
c teṣāṃ manuṣyās tarkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate
a acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvā na tāṃs tarkeṇa sādhayet
c prakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yat tu tad acintyasya lakṣaṇam
a sudarśanaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvīpaṃ te kurunandana
c parimaṇḍalo mahārāja dvīpo 'sau cakrasaṃsthitaḥ
a nadījalapraticchannaḥ parvataiś cābhrasaṃnibhaiḥ
c puraiś ca vividhākārai ramyair janapadais tathā
a vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaphalopetaiḥ saṃpannadhanadhānyavān
c lāvaṇena samudreṇa samantāt parivāritaḥ
a yathā ca puruṣaḥ paśyed ādarśe mukham ātmanaḥ
c evaṃ sudarśanadvīpo dṛśyate candramaṇḍale
a dvir aṃśe pippalas tatra dvir aṃśe ca śaśo mahān
c sarvauṣadhisamāvāpaiḥ sarvataḥ paribṛṃhitaḥ
e āpas tato 'nyā vijñeyā eṣa saṃkṣepa ucyate
f tato 'nya ucyate cāyam enaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ukto dvīpasya saṃkṣepo vistaraṃ brūhi saṃjaya
a         vidhivad buddhimaṃs tvayā
a tattvajñaś cāsi sarvasya        
c yāvad bhūmyavakāśo 'yaṃ dṛśyate śaśalakṣaṇe
e tasya pramāṇaṃ prabrūhi tato vakṣyasi pippalam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktaḥ sa rājñā tu saṃjayo vākyam abravīt
c prāgāyatā mahārāja ṣaḍ ete ratnaparvatāḥ
d sthitā samudram ākramya avarūḍhā bhavaṃs tataḥ
e avagāḍhā hy ubhayataḥ samudrau pūrvapaścimau
a himavān hemakūṭaś ca niṣadhaś ca nagottamaḥ
c nīlaś ca vaiḍūryamayaḥ śvetaś ca rajataprabhaḥ
e sarvadhātuvinaddhaś ca śṛṅgavān nāma parvataḥ
a ete vai parvatā rājan siddhacāraṇasevitāḥ
c teṣām antaraviṣkambho yojanāni sahasraśaḥ
a tatra puṇyā janapadās tāni varṣāṇi bhārata
c vasanti teṣu sattvāni nānājātīni sarvaśaḥ
d gandharvādyā vasanti sma hy apsarogaṇasevitāḥ
a idaṃ tu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tato haimavataṃ param
b tataḥ kiṃpuruṣāvāsaṃ varṣaṃ himavataḥ param
c hemakūṭāt paraṃ caiva harivarṣaṃ pracakṣate
a dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa ca
c prāgāyato mahārāja mālyavān nāma parvataḥ
a tataḥ paraṃ mālyavataḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥ
b tenaiva kramayogena parvato gandhamādanaḥ
c parimaṇḍalas tayor madhye meruḥ kanakaparvataḥ
a ādityataruṇābhāso vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
c yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśādhaḥ kila smṛtaḥ
a uccaiś ca caturāśītir yojanānāṃ mahīpate
c ūrdhvam antaś ca tiryak ca lokān āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
a tasya pārśve tv ime dvīpāś catvāraḥ saṃsthitāḥ prabho
c bhadrāśvaḥ ketumālaś ca jambūdvīpaś ca bhārata
d ketumālaś caturthaś ca meroḥ paścimataḥ sthitaḥ
e uttarāś caiva kuravaḥ kṛtapuṇyapratiśrayāḥ
a vihagaḥ sumukho yatra suparṇasyātmajaḥ kila
c sa vai vicintayām āsa sauvarṇān prekṣya vāyasān
a merur uttamamadhyānām adhamānāṃ ca pakṣiṇām
c aviśeṣakaro yasmāt tasmād enaṃ tyajāmy aham
a tam ādityo 'nuparyeti satataṃ jyotiṣāṃ patiḥ
c candramāś ca sanakṣatro vāyuś caiva pradakṣiṇam
a sa parvato mahārāja divyapuṣpaphalānvitaḥ
c bhavanair āvṛtaḥ sarvair jāmbūnadamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ
a tatra devagaṇā rājan gandharvāsurarākṣasāḥ
c apsarogaṇasaṃyuktāḥ śaile krīḍanti nityaśaḥ
a tatra brahmā ca rudraś ca śakraś cāpi sureśvaraḥ
c sametya vividhair yajñair yajante 'nekadakṣiṇaiḥ
a tumburur nāradaś caiva viśvāvasur hahā huhūḥ
c abhigamyāmaraśreṣṭhāḥ stavai stunvanti cābhibho
a saptarṣayo mahātmānaḥ kaśyapaś ca prajāpatiḥ
c tatra gacchanti bhadraṃ te sadā parvaṇi parvaṇi
a tasyaiva mūrdhany uśanāḥ kāvyo daityair mahīpate
c tasya hīmāni ratnāni tasyeme ratnaparvatāḥ
a tasmāt kubero bhagavāṃś caturthaṃ bhāgam aśnute
c tataḥ kalāṃśaṃ vittasya manuṣyebhyaḥ prayacchati
a pārśve tasyottare divyaṃ sarvartukusumaṃ śivam
c karṇikāravanaṃ ramyaṃ śilājālasamudgatam
a tatra sākṣāt paśupatir divyair bhūtaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
c umāsahāyo bhagavān ramate bhūtabhāvanaḥ
a karṇikāramayīṃ mālāṃ bibhrat pādāvalambinīm
c tribhir netraiḥ kṛtoddyotas tribhiḥ sūryair ivoditaiḥ
a tam ugratapasaḥ siddhāḥ suvratāḥ satyavādinaḥ
c paśyanti na hi durvṛttaiḥ śakyo draṣṭuṃ maheśvaraḥ
a tasya śailasya śikharāt kṣīradhārā nareśvara
c triṃśad bāhuparigrāhyā bhīmanirghātanisvanā
a puṇyā puṇyatamair juṣṭā gaṅgā bhāgīrathī śubhā
c pataty ajasravegena hrade cāndramase śubhe
e tayā hy utpāditaḥ puṇyaḥ sa hradaḥ sāgaropamaḥ
a tāṃ dhārayām āsa purā durdharāṃ parvatair api
c śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ śirasā vai maheśvaraḥ
a meros tu paścime pārśve ketumālo mahīpate
c jambūṣaṇḍaś ca tatraiva sumahān nandanopamaḥ
a āyur daśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tatra bhārata
c suvarṇavarṇāś ca narāḥ striyaś cāpsarasopamāḥ
a anāmayā vītaśokā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ
c jāyante mānavās tatra niṣṭaptakanakaprabhāḥ
d pūrveṇa yasya vikhyātaḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥ
a gandhamādanaśṛṅgeṣu kuberaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ
c saṃvṛto 'psarasāṃ saṃghair modate guhyakādhipaḥ
a gandhamādanapādeṣu pareṣv aparagaṇḍikāḥ
c ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ paramāyuṣaḥ
a tatra kṛṣṇā narā rājaṃs tejoyuktā mahābalāḥ
c striyaś cotpalapatrābhāḥ sarvāḥ supriyadarśanāḥ
a nīlāt parataraṃ śvetaṃ śvetād dhairaṇyakaṃ param
b hiraṇmayaṃ ca śvetādreḥ paraṃ varṣaṃ narādhipa
b kuruvarṣaṃ tato rājañ śṛṅgavat parvatāt param
c varṣam airāvataṃ nāma tataḥ śṛṅgavataḥ param
a dhanuḥsaṃsthe mahārāja dve varṣe dakṣiṇottare
c ilāvṛtaṃ madhyamaṃ tu pañca varṣāṇi caiva ha
a uttarottaram etebhyo varṣam udricyate guṇaiḥ
c āyuṣpramāṇam ārogyaṃ dharmataḥ kāmato 'rthataḥ
a samanvitāni bhūtāni teṣu varṣeṣu bhārata
c evam eṣā mahārāja parvataiḥ pṛthivī citā
a hemakūṭas tu sumahān kailāso nāma parvataḥ
c yatra vaiśravaṇo rājā guhyakaiḥ saha modate
d tatra devo mahādevo nityam āste sahomayā
d citre śilātale ramye devarṣigaṇapūjitaḥ
a asty uttareṇa kailāsaṃ mainākaṃ parvataṃ prati
c hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ sumahān divyo maṇimayo giriḥ
a tasya pārśve mahad divyaṃ śubhaṃ kāñcanavālukam
c ramyaṃ bindusaro nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ
e dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathīṃ gaṅgām uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ
a yūpā maṇimayās tatra cityāś cāpi hiraṇmayāḥ
c tatreṣṭvā tu gataḥ siddhiṃ sahasrākṣo mahāyaśāḥ
a sṛṣṭvā bhūtapatir yatra sarvalokān sanātanaḥ
c upāsyate tigmatejā vṛto bhūtaiḥ samāgataiḥ
e naranārāyaṇau brahmā manuḥ sthāṇuś ca pañcamaḥ
a tatra tripathagā devī prathamaṃ tu pratiṣṭhitā
c brahmalokād apakrāntā saptadhā pratipadyate
a vasvokasārā nalinī pāvanā ca sarasvatī
c jambūnadī ca sītā ca gaṅgā sindhuś ca saptamī
a acintyā divyasaṃkalpā prabhor eṣaiva saṃvidhiḥ
c upāsate yatra satraṃ sahasrayugaparyaye
a dṛśyādṛśyā ca bhavati tatra tatra sarasvatī
c etā divyāḥ sapta gaṅgās triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ
a rakṣāṃsi vai himavati hemakūṭe tu guhyakāḥ
c sarpā nāgāś ca niṣadhe gokarṇe ca tapodhanāḥ
a devāsurāṇāṃ ca gṛhaṃ śvetaḥ parvata ucyate
c gandharvā niṣadhe śaile nīle brahmarṣayo nṛpa
e śṛṅgavāṃs tu mahārāja pitṝṇāṃ pratisaṃcaraḥ
a ity etāni mahārāja sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ
c bhūtāny upaniviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca
a teṣām ṛddhir bahuvidhā dṛśyate daivamānuṣī
c aśakyā parisaṃkhyātuṃ śraddheyā tu bubhūṣatā
a yāṃ tu pṛcchasi mā rājan divyām etāṃ śaśākṛtim
b jambūdvīpasya sarvasya ākṛtiṃ candramaṇḍale
b sa vai sudarśanadvīpo dṛśyate śaśavadvidhau
c pārśve śaśasya dve varṣe ubhaye dakṣiṇottare
d anyāni pañca varṣāṇi galāntaṃ kalpitāni ca
e karṇau tu nāgadvīpaṃ ca kaśyapadvīpam eva ca
a tāmravarṇaḥ śiro rājañ śrīmān malayaparvataḥ
c etad dvitīyaṃ dvīpasya dṛśyate śaśasaṃsthitam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a meror athottaraṃ pārśvaṃ pūrvaṃ cācakṣva saṃjaya
c nikhilena mahābuddhe mālyavantaṃ ca parvatam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya meroḥ pārśve tathottare
c uttarāḥ kuravo rājan puṇyāḥ siddhaniṣevitāḥ
a tatra vṛkṣā madhuphalā nityapuṣpaphalopagāḥ
c puṣpāṇi ca sugandhīni rasavanti phalāni ca
a sarvakāmaphalās tatra ke cid vṛkṣā janādhipa
c apare kṣīriṇo nāma vṛkṣās tatra narādhipa
a ye kṣaranti sadā kṣīraṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ hy amṛtopamam
c vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣv ābharaṇāni ca
a sarvā maṇimayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣmakāñcanavālukā
b maṇiratnanibhaṃ ramyaṃ vajravaiḍūryasaṃnibham
b bhūbhāgo dṛśyate tatra padmarāgasamaprabham
c sarvatra sukhasaṃsparśā niṣpaṅkā ca janādhipa
d puṣkariṇyaḥ śubhās tatra sukhasparśā manoharāḥ
a devalokacyutāḥ sarve jāyante tatra mānavāḥ
c tulyarūpaguṇopetāḥ sameṣu viṣameṣu ca
a mithunāni ca jāyante striyaś cāpsarasopamāḥ
c teṣāṃ te kṣīriṇāṃ kṣīraṃ pibanty amṛtasaṃnibham
a mithunaṃ jāyamānaṃ vai samaṃ tac ca pravardhate
c tulyarūpaguṇopetaṃ samaveṣaṃ tathaiva ca
e ekaikam anuraktaṃ ca cakravākasamaṃ vibho
f mṛtyuś ca samakālaṃ ca tayor mithunayugmayoḥ
a nirāmayā vītaśokā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ
c daśa varṣasahasrāṇi daśa varṣaśatāni ca
e jīvanti te mahārāja na cānyonyaṃ jahaty uta
a bhāruṇḍā nāma śakunās tīkṣṇatuṇḍā mahābalāḥ
c te nirharanti hi mṛtān darīṣu prakṣipanti ca
a uttarāḥ kuravo rājan vyākhyātās te samāsataḥ
c meroḥ pārśvam ahaṃ pūrvaṃ vakṣyāmy atha yathātatham
d bhadrāśvaṃ nāma varṣaṃ tu puro vai gandhamādanāt
a tasya pūrvābhiṣekas tu bhadrāśvasya viśāṃ pate
c bhadrasālavanaṃ yatra kālāmraś ca mahādrumaḥ
a kālāmraś ca mahārāja nityapuṣpaphalaḥ śubhaḥ
c dvīpaś ca yojanotsedhaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ
a tatra te puruṣāḥ śvetās tejoyuktā mahābalāḥ
c striyaḥ kumudavarṇāś ca sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
a candraprabhāś candravarṇāḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanāḥ
c candraśītalagātryaś ca nṛttagītaviśāradāḥ
a daśa varṣasahasrāṇi tatrāyur bharatarṣabha
c kālāmrarasapītās te nityaṃ saṃsthitayauvanāḥ
a dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tu
c sudarśano nāma mahāñ jambūvṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ
a sarvakāmaphalaḥ puṇyaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ
c tasya nāmnā samākhyāto jambūdvīpaḥ sanātanaḥ
a yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ ca śataṃ ca bharatarṣabha
c utsedho vṛkṣarājasya divaspṛṅ manujeśvara
a aratnīnāṃ sahasraṃ ca śatāni daśa pañca ca
c pariṇāhas tu vṛkṣasya phalānāṃ rasabhedinām
a patamānāni tāny urvyāṃ kurvanti vipulaṃ svanam
c muñcanti ca rasaṃ rājaṃs tasmin rajatasaṃnibham
a tasyā jambvāḥ phalaraso nadī bhūtvā janādhipa
c meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayāty uttarān kurūn
a pibanti tad rasaṃ hṛṣṭā janā nityaṃ janādhipa
c tasmin phalarase pīte na jarā bādhate ca tān
a tatra jāmbūnadaṃ nāma kanakaṃ devabhūṣaṇam
b indragopakasaṃkāśaṃ jāyate bhāsvaraṃ tu tat
c taruṇādityavarṇāś ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥ
a tathā mālyavataḥ śṛṅge dīpyate tatra havyavāṭ
c nāmnā saṃvartako nāma kālāgnir bharatarṣabha
a tathā mālyavataḥ śṛṅge pūrve pūrvāntagaṇḍikā
c yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi pañcāśan mālyavān sthitaḥ
a mahārajatasaṃkāśā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ
c brahmalokāc cyutāḥ sarve sarve ca brahmavādinaḥ
a tapas tu tapyamānās te bhavanti hy ūrdhvaretasaḥ
c rakṣaṇārthaṃ tu bhūtānāṃ praviśanti divākaram
a ṣaṣṭis tāni sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭir eva śatāni ca
c aruṇasyāgrato yānti parivārya divākaram
a ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭim eva śatāni ca
c ādityatāpataptās te viśanti śaśimaṇḍalam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a varṣāṇāṃ caiva nāmāni parvatānāṃ ca saṃjaya
c ācakṣva me yathātattvaṃ ye ca parvatavāsinaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dakṣiṇena tu śvetasya nīlasyaivottareṇa tu
c varṣaṃ ramaṇakaṃ nāma jāyante tatra mānavāḥ
a śuklābhijanasaṃpannāḥ sarve supriyadarśanāḥ
c ratipradhānāś ca tathā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ
a daśa varṣasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca
c jīvanti te mahārāja nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ
a dakṣiṇe śṛṅgiṇaś caiva śvetasyāthottareṇa ca
c varṣaṃ hairaṇvataṃ nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī
d yatra cāyaṃ mahārāja pakṣirāṭ patagottamaḥ
a yakṣānugā mahārāja dhaninaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
c mahābalās tatra sadā rājan muditamānasāḥ
d yakṣaḥ so 'pi mahārāja yakṣarājānugauta gottamaḥ
a ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te janādhipa
c āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca
a śṛṅgāṇi vai śṛṅgavatas trīṇy eva manujādhipa
c ekaṃ maṇimayaṃ tatra tathaikaṃ raukmam adbhutam
a sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ bhavanair upaśobhitam
c tatra svayaṃprabhā devī nityaṃ vasati śāṇḍilī
a uttareṇa tu śṛṅgasya samudrānte janādhipa
c varṣam airāvataṃ nāma tasmāc chṛṅgavataḥ param
a na tatra sūryas tapati na te jīryanti mānavāḥ
c candramāś ca sanakṣatro jyotir bhūta ivāvṛtaḥ
a padmaprabhāḥ padmavarṇāḥ padmapatranibhekṣaṇāḥ
c padmapatrasugandhāś ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥ
a aniṣpandāḥ sugandhāś ca nirāhārā jitendriyāḥ
c devalokacyutāḥ sarve tathā virajaso nṛpa
a trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te janādhipa
c āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti narā bharatasattama
a kṣīrodasya samudrasya tathaivottarataḥ prabhuḥ
c harir vasati vaikuṇṭhaḥ śakaṭe kanakātmake
a aṣṭacakraṃ hi tad yānaṃ bhūtayuktaṃ manojavam
c agnivarṇaṃ mahāvegaṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtam
a sa prabhuḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vibhuś ca bharatarṣabha
c saṃkṣepo vistaraś caiva kartā kārayitā ca saḥ
a pṛthivy āpas tathākāśaṃ vāyus tejaś ca pārthiva
c sa yajñaḥ sarvabhūtānām āsyaṃ tasya hutāśanaḥ
d sthitaḥ sthānasahasreṣu vyāpya vai sa carācaram
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktaḥ saṃjayena dhṛtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥ
c dhyānam anvagamad rājā putrān prati janādhipa
a sa vicintya mahārāja punar evābravīd vacaḥ
c asaṃśayaṃ sūtaputra kālaḥ saṃkṣipate jagat
e sṛjate ca punaḥ sarvaṃ neha vidyati śāśvatam
a naro nārāyaṇaś caiva sarvajñaḥ sarvabhūtabhṛt
c devā vaikuṇṭha ity āhur vedā viṣṇur iti prabhum
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yad idaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ yatredaṃ mūrchitaṃ balam
c yatrātimātraṃ lubdho 'yaṃ putro duryodhano mama
a yatra gṛddhāḥ pāṇḍusutā yatra me sajjate manaḥ
c etan me tattvam ācakṣva kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a na tatra pāṇḍavā gṛddhāḥ śṛṇu rājan vaco mama
c gṛddho duryodhanas tatra śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
a apare kṣatriyāś cāpi nānājanapadeśvarāḥ
c ye gṛddhā bhārate varṣe na mṛṣyanti parasparam
a atra te varṇayiṣyāmi varṣaṃ bhārata bhāratam
c priyam indrasya devasya manor vaivasvatasya ca
a pṛthoś ca rājan vainyasya tathekṣvākor mahātmanaḥ
c yayāter ambarīṣasya māndhātur nahuṣasya ca
a tathaiva mucukundasya śiber auśīnarasya ca
c ṛṣabhasya tathailasya nṛgasya nṛpates tathā
d kuśikasya ca durdharṣa gādheś caiva mahātmanaḥ
d somakasya ca durdharṣa dilīpasya tathaiva ca
a anyeṣāṃ ca mahārāja kṣatriyāṇāṃ balīyasām
c sarveṣām eva rājendra priyaṃ bhārata bhāratam
a tat te varṣaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāśrutam ariṃdama
c śṛṇu me gadato rājan yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
a mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimān ṛkṣavān api
c vindhyaś ca pāriyātraś ca saptaite kulaparvatāḥ
a teṣāṃ sahasraśo rājan parvatās tu samīpataḥ
c abhijñātāḥ sāravanto vipulāś citrasānavaḥ
a anye tato 'parijñātā hrasvā hrasvopajīvinaḥ
c āryā mlecchāś ca kauravya tair miśrāḥ puruṣā vibho
a nadīḥ pibanti bahulā gaṅgāṃ sindhuṃ sarasvatīm
c godāvarīṃ narmadāṃ ca bāhudāṃ ca mahānadīm
a śatadruṃ candrabhāgāṃ ca yamunāṃ ca mahānadīm
c dṛṣadvatīṃ vipāśāṃ ca vipāpāṃ sthūlavālukām
a nadīṃ vetravatīṃ caiva kṛṣṇaveṇāṃ ca nimnagām
c irāvatīṃ vitastāṃ ca payoṣṇīṃ devikām api
a vedasmṛtiṃ vetasinīṃ tridivām iṣkumālinīm
c karīṣiṇīṃ citravahāṃ citrasenāṃ ca nimnagām
a gomatīṃ dhūtapāpāṃ ca vandanāṃ ca mahānadīm
c kauśikīṃ tridivāṃ kṛtyāṃ vicitrāṃ lohatāriṇīm
a rathasthāṃ śatakumbhāṃ ca sarayūṃ ca nareśvara
c carmaṇvatīṃ vetravatīṃ hastisomāṃ diśaṃ tathā
a śatāvarīṃ payoṣṇīṃ ca parāṃ bhaimarathīṃ tathā
c kāverīṃ culukāṃ cāpi vāpīṃ śatabalām api
a nicīrāṃ mahitāṃ cāpi suprayogāṃ narādhipa
c pavitrāṃ kuṇḍalāṃ sindhuṃ vājinīṃ puramālinīm
a pūrvābhirāmāṃ vīrāṃ ca bhīmām oghavatīṃ tathā
c palāśinīṃ pāpaharāṃ mahendrāṃ pippalāvatīm
a pāriṣeṇām asiknīṃ ca saralāṃ bhāramardinīm
c puruhīṃ pravarāṃ menāṃ moghāṃ ghṛtavatīṃ tathā
a dhūmatyām atikṛṣṇāṃ ca sūcīṃ chāvīṃ ca kaurava
c sadānīrām adhṛṣyāṃ ca kuśadhārāṃ mahānadīm
a śaśikāntāṃ śivāṃ caiva tathā vīravatīm api
c vāstuṃ suvāstuṃ gaurīṃ ca kampanāṃ sahiraṇvatīm
a hiraṇvatīṃ citravatīṃ citrasenāṃ ca nimnagām
c rathacitrāṃ jyotirathāṃ viśvāmitrāṃ kapiñjalām
a upendrāṃ bahulāṃ caiva kucarām ambuvāhinīm
c vainandīṃ piñjalāṃ veṇṇāṃ tuṅgaveṇāṃ mahānadīm
a vidiśāṃ kṛṣṇaveṇṇāṃ ca tāmrāṃ ca kapilām api
c śaluṃ suvāmāṃ vedāśvāṃ harisrāvāṃ mahāpagām
a śīghrāṃ ca picchilāṃ caiva bhāradvājīṃ ca nimnagām
c kauśikīṃ nimnagāṃ śoṇāṃ bāhudām atha candanām
a durgām antaḥśilāṃ caiva brahmamedhyāṃ bṛhadvatīm
c carakṣāṃ mahirohīṃ ca tathā jambunadīm api
a sunasāṃ tamasāṃ dāsīṃ trasām anyāṃ varāṇasīm
c loloddhṛtakarāṃ caiva pūrṇāśāṃ ca mahānadīm
a mānavīṃ vṛṣabhāṃ caiva mahānadyo janādhipa
c sadānirāmayāṃ vṛtyāṃ mandagāṃ mandavāhinīm
d brahmamedhyāṃ bṛhadvatīm
d etāś cānyāś ca bahudhā
a brahmāṇīṃ ca mahāgaurīṃ durgām api ca bhārata
c citropalāṃ citrabarhāṃ mañjuṃ makaravāhinīm
a mandākinīṃ vaitaraṇīṃ kokāṃ caiva mahānadīm
c śuktimatīm araṇyāṃ ca puṣpaveṇyutpalāvatīm
a lohityāṃ karatoyāṃ ca tathaiva vṛṣabhaṅginīm
c kumārīm ṛṣikulyāṃ ca brahmakulyāṃ ca bhārata
a sarasvatīḥ supuṇyāś ca sarvā gaṅgāś ca māriṣa
b brahmāṇīṃ ca mahāgaurīṃ suvaśyām api bhārata
b mānavīṃ vṛṣabhāṃ caiva mahānadyo janādhipa
c viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarvāś caiva mahābalāḥ
a tathā nadyas tv aprakāśāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c ity etāḥ sarito rājan samākhyātā yathāsmṛti
a ata ūrdhvaṃ janapadān nibodha gadato mama
c tatreme kurupāñcālāḥ śālvamādreyajāṅgalāḥ
d videhā māgadhāḥ siṃhā mahadāyatayas tathā
a śūrasenāḥ kaliṅgāś ca bodhā maukās tathaiva ca
c matsyāḥ sukuṭyaḥ saubalyāḥ kuntalāḥ kāśikośalāḥ
a cedivatsāḥ karūṣāś ca bhojāḥ sindhupulindakāḥ
c uttamaujā daśārṇāś ca mekalāś cotkalaiḥ saha
a pāñcālāḥ kauśijāś caiva ekapṛṣṭhā yugaṃdharāḥ
c saudhā madrā bhujiṅgāś ca kāśayo 'parakāśayaḥ
a jaṭharāḥ kukkuśāś caiva sudāśārṇāś ca bhārata
c kuntayo 'vantayaś caiva tathaivāparakuntayaḥ
a govindā mandakāḥ ṣaṇḍā vidarbhānūpavāsikāḥ
c aśmakāḥ pāṃsurāṣṭrāś ca goparāṣṭrāḥ panītakāḥ
a ādirāṣṭrāḥ sukuṭṭāś ca balirāṣṭraṃ ca kevalam
c vānarāsyāḥ pravāhāś ca vakrā vakrabhayāḥ śakāḥ
a videhakā māgadhāś ca suhmāś ca vijayās tathā
c aṅgā vaṅgāḥ kaliṅgāś ca yakṛllomāna eva ca
a mallāḥ sudeṣṇāḥ prāhūtās tathā māhiṣakārṣikāḥ
c vāhīkā vāṭadhānāś ca ābhīrāḥ kālatoyakāḥ
a aparandhrāś ca śūdrāś ca pahlavāś carmakhaṇḍikāḥ
c aṭavīśabarāś caiva marubhaumāś ca māriṣa
a upāvṛścānupāvṛścasurāṣṭrāḥ kekayās tathā
c kuṭṭāparāntā dvaidheyāḥ kākṣāḥ sāmudraniṣkuṭāḥ
d kaṭyāś ca pātavaibodhā yākāḥ sāmudraniṣkadāḥ
a andhrāś ca bahavo rājann antargiryās tathaiva ca
c bahirgiryāṅgamaladā māgadhā mānavarjakāḥ
d antargiryās tathā caiva bahirgiryās tathaiva ca
a mahyuttarāḥ prāvṛṣeyā bhārgavāś ca janādhipa
c puṇḍrā bhārgāḥ kirātāś ca sudoṣṇāḥ pramudās tathā
a śakā niṣādā niṣadhās tathaivānartanairṛtāḥ
c dugūlāḥ pratimatsyāś ca kuśalāḥ kunaṭās tathā
a tīragrāhās taratoyā rājikā rasyakāgaṇāḥ
c tilakāḥ pārasīkāś ca madhumantaḥ prakutsakāḥ
a kāśmīrāḥ sindhusauvīrā gāndhārā darśakās tathā
c abhīsārā kulūtāś ca śaivalā bāhlikās tathā
a darvīkāḥ sakacā darvā vātajāmarathoragāḥ
c bahuvādyāś ca kauravya sudāmānaḥ sumallikāḥ
a vadhrāḥ karīṣakāś cāpi kulindopatyakās tathā
c vanāyavo daśāpārśvā romāṇaḥ kuśabindavaḥ
a kacchā gopālakacchāś ca lāṅgalāḥ paravallakāḥ
c kirātā barbarāḥ siddhā videhās tāmraliṅgakāḥ
a oṣṭrāḥ puṇḍrāḥ sasairandhrāḥ pārvatīyāś ca māriṣa
c athāpare janapadā dakṣiṇā bharatarṣabha
a draviḍāḥ keralāḥ prācyā bhūṣikā vanavāsinaḥ
c unnatyakā māhiṣakā vikalpā mūṣakās tathā
a karṇikāḥ kuntikāś caiva saudbhidā nalakālakāḥ
c kaukuṭṭakās tathā colāḥ koṅkaṇā mālavāṇakāḥ
a samaṅgāḥ kopanāś caiva kukurāṅgadamāriṣāḥ
c dhvajiny utsavasaṃketās trigartāḥ sarvasenayaḥ
a tryaṅgāḥ kekarakāḥ proṣṭhāḥ parasaṃcarakās tathā
c tathaiva vindhyapulakāḥ pulindāḥ kalkalaiḥ saha
a mālakā mallakāś caiva tathaivāparavartakāḥ
c kulindāḥ kulakāś caiva karaṇṭhāḥ kurakās tathā
a mūṣakā stanabālāś ca satiyaḥ pattipañjakāḥ
c ādidāyāḥ sirālāś ca stūbakā stanapās tathā
a hṛṣīvidarbhāḥ kāntīkās taṅgaṇāḥ parataṅgaṇāḥ
c uttarāś cāpare mlecchā janā bharatasattama
a yavanāś ca sakāmbojā dāruṇā mlecchajātayaḥ
c sakṣaddruhaḥ kuntalāś ca hūṇāḥ pāratakaiḥ saha
a tathaiva maradhāś cīnās tathaiva daśamālikāḥ
c kṣatriyopaniveśāś ca vaiśyaśūdrakulāni ca
a śūdrābhīrātha daradāḥ kāśmīrāḥ paśubhiḥ saha
c khaśikāś ca tukhārāś ca pallavā girigahvarāḥ
a ātreyāḥ sabharadvājās tathaiva stanayoṣikāḥ
c aupakāś ca kaliṅgāś ca kirātānāṃ ca jātayaḥ
d kāraskarāś ca vaṃśāś ca āndhrāś ca dramiḍās tathā
d colāś caiva tathā pāṇḍyāś cerāś caiva susiṃhalāḥ
a tāmarā haṃsamārgāś ca tathaiva karabhañjakāḥ
b ete cānye janapadāḥ prācyodīcyās tathaiva ca
c uddeśamātreṇa mayā deśāḥ saṃkīrtitāḥ prabho
a yathāguṇabalaṃ cāpi trivargasya mahāphalam
c duhyed dhenuḥ kāmadhuk ca bhūmiḥ samyag anuṣṭhitā
a tasyāṃ gṛdhyanti rājānaḥ śūrā dharmārthakovidāḥ
c te tyajanty āhave prāṇān rasāgṛddhās tarasvinaḥ
a devamānuṣakāyānāṃ kāmaṃ bhūmiḥ parāyaṇam
c anyonyasyāvalumpanti sārameyā ivāmiṣam
a rājāno bharataśreṣṭha bhoktukāmā vasuṃdharām
c na cāpi tṛptiḥ kāmānāṃ vidyate ceha kasya cit
a tasmāt parigrahe bhūmer yatante kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c sāmnā dānena bhedena daṇḍenaiva ca pārthiva
a pitā mātā ca putraś ca khaṃ dyauś ca narapuṃgava
c bhūmir bhavati bhūtānāṃ samyag acchidradarśinī
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a bhāratasyāsya varṣasya tathā haimavatasya ca
c pramāṇam āyuṣaḥ sūta phalaṃ cāpi śubhāśubham
a anāgatam atikrāntaṃ vartamānaṃ ca saṃjaya
c ācakṣva me vistareṇa harivarṣaṃ tathaiva ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni bharatarṣabha
c kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca puṣyaṃ ca kuruvardhana
a pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatas tretāyugaṃ vibho
c saṃkṣepād dvāparasyātha tataḥ puṣyaṃ pravartate
a catvāri ca sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ kurusattama
c āyuḥsaṃkhyā kṛtayuge saṃkhyātā rājasattama
a tathā trīṇi sahasrāṇi tretāyāṃ manujādhipa
c dvisahasraṃ dvāpare tu śate tiṣṭhati saṃprati
a na pramāṇasthitir hy asti puṣye 'smin bharatarṣabha
c garbhasthāś ca mriyante 'tra tathā jātā mriyanti ca
a mahābalā mahāsattvāḥ prajāguṇasamanvitāḥ
b prajāyante ca jātāś ca śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c ajāyanta kṛte rājan munayaḥ sutapodhanāḥ
a mahotsāhā mahātmāno dhārmikāḥ satyavādinaḥ
c jātāḥ kṛtayuge rājan dhaninaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
a āyuṣmanto mahāvīrā dhanurdharavarā yudhi
b varārhā yudhi jāyante kṣatriyāḥ śūrasattamāḥ
c jāyante kṣatriyāḥ śūrās tretāyāṃ cakravartinaḥ
a sarvavarṇā mahārāja jāyante dvāpare sati
c mahotsāhā mahāvīryāḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
a tejasālpena saṃyuktāḥ krodhanāḥ puruṣā nṛpa
c lubdhāś cānṛtakāś caiva puṣye jāyanti bhārata
a īrṣyā mānas tathā krodho māyāsūyā tathaiva ca
c puṣye bhavanti martyānāṃ rāgo lobhaś ca bhārata
a saṃkṣepo vartate rājan dvāpare 'smin narādhipa
c guṇottaraṃ haimavataṃ harivarṣaṃ tataḥ param
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a jambūkhaṇḍas tvayā prokto yathāvad iha saṃjaya
c viṣkambham asya prabrūhi parimāṇaṃ ca tattvataḥ
a samudrasya pramāṇaṃ ca samyag acchidradarśana
c śākadvīpaṃ ca me brūhi kuśadvīpaṃ ca saṃjaya
a śālmalaṃ caiva tattvena krauñcadvīpaṃ tathaiva ca
c brūhi gāvalgaṇe sarvaṃ rāhoḥ somārkayos tathā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a rājan subahavo dvīpā yair idaṃ saṃtataṃ jagat
c sapta tv ahaṃ pravakṣyāmi candrādityau grahāṃs tathā
a aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c ṣaṭśatāni ca pūrṇāni viṣkambho jambuparvataḥ
a lāvaṇasya samudrasya viṣkambho dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
c nānājanapadākīrṇo maṇividrumacitritaḥ
a naikadhātuvicitraiś ca parvatair upaśobhitaḥ
c siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇaḥ sāgaraḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ
a śākadvīpaṃ ca vakṣyāmi yathāvad iha pārthiva
c śṛṇu me tvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ bruvataḥ kurunandana
a jambūdvīpapramāṇena dviguṇaḥ sa narādhipa
c viṣkambheṇa mahārāja sāgaro 'pi vibhāgaśaḥ
d śalmaliś ca kuśaḥ krauñco dviguṇo hy uttarottaram
d yathāsaṃkhyaṃ parivṛttaḥ surāsarpiḥpayodhibhiḥ
e kṣīrodo bharataśreṣṭha yena saṃparivāritaḥ
a tatra puṇyā janapadā na tatra mriyate janaḥ
c kuta eva hi durbhikṣaṃ kṣamātejoyutā hi te
a śākadvīpasya saṃkṣepo yathāvad bharatarṣabha
c ukta eṣa mahārāja kim anyac chrotum icchasi
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a śākadvīpasya saṃkṣepo yathāvad iha saṃjaya
c uktas tvayā mahābhāga vistaraṃ brūhi tattvataḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tathaiva parvatā rājan saptātra maṇibhūṣitāḥ
c ratnākarās tathā nadyas teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu
e atīvaguṇavat sarvaṃ tatra puṇyaṃ janādhipa
a devarṣigandharvayutaḥ paramo merur ucyate
c prāgāyato mahārāja malayo nāma parvataḥ
e yato meghāḥ pravartante prabhavanti ca sarvaśaḥ
a tataḥ pareṇa kauravya jaladhāro mahāgiriḥ
c yatra nityam upādatte vāsavaḥ paramaṃ jalam
e yato varṣaṃ prabhavati varṣākāle janeśvara
a uccair girī raivatako yatra nityaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
c revatī divi nakṣatraṃ pitāmahakṛto vidhiḥ
a uttareṇa tu rājendra śyāmo nāma mahāgiriḥ
b navameghaprabhaḥ prāṃśuḥ śrīmān ujjvalavigrahaḥ
c yataḥ śyāmatvam āpannāḥ prajā janapadeśvara
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sumahān saṃśayo me 'dya proktaṃ saṃjaya yat tvayā
c prajāḥ kathaṃ sūtaputra saṃprāptāḥ śyāmatām iha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a sarveṣv eva mahāprājña dvīpeṣu kurunandana
c gauraḥ kṛṣṇaś ca varṇau dvau tayor varṇāntaraṃ nṛpa
a śyāmo yasmāt pravṛtto vai tat te vakṣyāmi bhārata
c āste 'tra bhagavān kṛṣṇas tat kāntyā śyāmatāṃ gataḥ
a tataḥ paraṃ kauravendra durgaśailo mahodayaḥ
c kesarī kesarayuto yato vātaḥ pravāyati
a teṣāṃ yojanaviṣkambho dviguṇaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ
c varṣāṇi teṣu kauravya saṃproktāni manīṣibhiḥ
a mahāmerur mahākāśo jaladaḥ kumudottaraḥ
c jaladhārāt paro rājan sukumāra iti smṛtaḥ
a raivatasya tu kaumāraḥ śyāmasya tu maṇīcakaḥ
c kesarasyātha modākī pareṇa tu mahāpumān
a parivārya tu kauravya dairghyaṃ hrasvatvam eva ca
c jambūdvīpena vikhyātas tasya madhye mahādrumaḥ
a śāko nāma mahārāja tasya dvīpasya madhyagaḥ
c tatra puṇyā janapadāḥ pūjyate tatra śaṃkaraḥ
a tatra gacchanti siddhāś ca cāraṇā daivatāni ca
c dhārmikāś ca prajā rājaṃś catvāro 'tīva bhārata
a varṇāḥ svakarmaniratā na ca steno 'tra dṛśyate
c dīrghāyuṣo mahārāja jarāmṛtyuvivarjitāḥ
a prajās tatra vivardhante varṣāsv iva samudragāḥ
c nadyaḥ puṇyajalās tatra gaṅgā ca bahudhāgatiḥ
a sukumārī kumārī ca sītā kāverakā tathā
c mahānadī ca kauravya tathā maṇijalā nadī
e ikṣuvardhanikā caiva tathā bharatasattama
a tataḥ pravṛttāḥ puṇyodā nadyaḥ kurukulodvaha
c sahasrāṇāṃ śatāny eva yato varṣati vāsavaḥ
a na tāsāṃ nāmadheyāni parimāṇaṃ tathaiva ca
c śakyate parisaṃkhyātuṃ puṇyās tā hi saridvarāḥ
a tatra puṇyā janapadāś catvāro lokasaṃmatāḥ
c magāś ca maśakāś caiva mānasā mandagās tathā
a magā brāhmaṇabhūyiṣṭhāḥ svakarmaniratā nṛpa
c maśakeṣu tu rājanyā dhārmikāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ
a mānaseṣu mahārāja vaiśyāḥ karmopajīvinaḥ
c sarvakāmasamāyuktāḥ śūrā dharmārthaniścitāḥ
e śūdrās tu mandage nityaṃ puruṣā dharmaśīlinaḥ
a na tatra rājā rājendra na daṇḍo na ca daṇḍikāḥ
c svadharmeṇaiva dharmaṃ ca te rakṣanti parasparam
a etāvad eva śakyaṃ tu tasmin dvīpe prabhāṣitum
c etāvad eva śrotavyaṃ śākadvīpe mahaujasi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a uttareṣu tu kauravya dvīpeṣu śrūyate kathā
c yathāśrutaṃ mahārāja bruvatas tan nibodha me
d dugdhodakasamudro 'nyaḥ punar ikṣurasodakaḥ
a ghṛtatoyaḥ samudro 'tra dadhimaṇḍodako 'paraḥ
c surodaḥ sāgaraś caiva tathānyo gharmasāgaraḥ
d ikṣūdaś ca surodaś ca sarpiḥkṣīrodadhis tadā
d dadhimaṇḍodadhiś cānyaḥ śuddhodadhir atho mahān
a paraspareṇa dviguṇāḥ sarve dvīpā narādhipa
c sarvataś ca mahārāja parvataiḥ parivāritāḥ
a gauras tu madhyame dvīpe girir mānaḥśilo mahān
c parvataḥ paścimaḥ kṛṣṇo nārāyaṇanibho nṛpa
a tatra ratnāni divyāni svayaṃ rakṣati keśavaḥ
c prajāpatim upāsīnaḥ prajānāṃ vidadhe sukham
a kuśadvīpe kuśastambo madhye janapadasya ha
b saṃpūjyate hi plakṣaś ca svadī
dvīpakhyātikṛd yathā
c saṃpūjyate śalmaliś ca dvīpe śālmalike nṛpa
a krauñcadvīpe mahākrauñco girī ratnacayākaraḥ
c saṃpūjyate mahārāja cāturvarṇyena nityadā
a gomandaḥ parvato rājan sumahān sarvadhātumān
c yatra nityaṃ nivasati śrīmān kamalalocanaḥ
e mokṣibhiḥ saṃstuto nityaṃ prabhur nārāyaṇo hariḥ
a kuśadvīpe tu rājendra parvato vidrumaiś citaḥ
c sudhāmā nāma durdharṣo dvitīyo hemaparvataḥ
a dyutimān nāma kauravya tṛtīyaḥ kumudo giriḥ
c caturthaḥ puṣpavān nāma pañcamas tu kuśeśayaḥ
a ṣaṣṭho harigirir nāma ṣaḍ ete parvatottamāḥ
c teṣām antaraviṣkambho dviguṇaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ
a audbhidaṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ dvitīyaṃ veṇumaṇḍalam
c tṛtīyaṃ vai rathākāraṃ caturthaṃ pālanaṃ smṛtam
a dhṛtimat pañcamaṃ varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ varṣaṃ prabhākaram
c saptamaṃ kāpilaṃ varṣaṃ saptaite varṣapuñjakāḥ
a eteṣu devagandharvāḥ prajāś ca jagatīśvara
c viharanti ramante ca na teṣu mriyate janaḥ
a na teṣu dasyavaḥ santi mlecchajātyo 'pi vā nṛpa
c gauraprāyo janaḥ sarvaḥ sukumāraś ca pārthiva
a avaśiṣṭeṣu varṣeṣu vakṣyāmi manujeśvara
c yathāśrutaṃ mahārāja tad avyagramanāḥ śṛṇu
a krauñcadvīpe mahārāja krauñco nāma mahāgiriḥ
c krauñcāt paro vāmanako vāmanād andhakārakaḥ
a andhakārāt paro rājan mainākaḥ parvatottamaḥ
c mainākāt parato rājan govindo girir uttamaḥ
a govindāt tu paro rājan nibiḍo nāma parvataḥ
c paras tu dviguṇas teṣāṃ viṣkambho vaṃśavardhana
a deśāṃs tatra pravakṣyāmi tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
c krauñcasya kuśalo deśo vāmanasya manonugaḥ
a manonugāt paraś coṣṇo deśaḥ kurukulodvaha
c uṣṇāt paraḥ prāvarakaḥ prāvarād andhakārakaḥ
a andhakārakadeśāt tu munideśaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ
c munideśāt paraś caiva procyate dundubhisvanaḥ
a siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇo gauraprāyo janādhipa
c ete deśā mahārāja devagandharvasevitāḥ
a puṣkare puṣkaro nāma parvato maṇiratnamān
c tatra nityaṃ nivasati svayaṃ devaḥ prajāpatiḥ
a taṃ paryupāsate nityaṃ devāḥ sarve maharṣibhiḥ
c vāgbhir manonukūlābhiḥ pūjayanto janādhipa
a jambūdvīpāt pravartante ratnāni vividhāny uta
c dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu prajānāṃ kurunandana
a viprāṇāṃ brahmacaryeṇa satyena ca damena ca
c ārogyāyuḥpramāṇābhyāṃ dviguṇaṃ dviguṇaṃ tataḥ
a eko janapado rājan dvīpeṣv eteṣu bhārata
c uktā janapadā yeṣu dharmaś caikaḥ pradṛśyate
a īśvaro daṇḍam udyamya svayam eva prajāpatiḥ
c dvīpān etān mahārāja rakṣaṃs tiṣṭhati nityadā
a sa rājā sa śivo rājan sa pitā sa pitāmahaḥ
c gopāyati naraśreṣṭha prajāḥ sajaḍapaṇḍitāḥ
a bhojanaṃ cātra kauravya prajāḥ svayam upasthitam
c siddham eva mahārāja bhuñjate tatra nityadā
a tataḥ paraṃ samā nāma dṛśyate lokasaṃsthitiḥ
c caturaśrā mahārāja trayas triṃśat tu maṇḍalam
a tatra tiṣṭhanti kauravya catvāro lokasaṃmatāḥ
c diggajā bharataśreṣṭha vāmanairāvatādayaḥ
e supratīkas tathā rājan prabhinnakaraṭāmukhaḥ
a tasyāhaṃ parimāṇaṃ tu na saṃkhyātum ihotsahe
c asaṃkhyātaḥ sa nityaṃ hi tiryag ūrdhvam adhas tathā
a tatra vai vāyavo vānti digbhyaḥ sarvābhya eva ca
c asaṃbādhā mahārāja tān nigṛhṇanti te gajāḥ
a puṣkaraiḥ padmasaṃkāśair varṣmavadbhir mahāprabhaiḥ
c te śanaiḥ punar evāśu vāyūn muñcanti nityaśaḥ
a śvasadbhir mucyamānās tu diggajair iha mārutāḥ
c āgacchanti mahārāja tatas tiṣṭhanti vai prajāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a paro vai vistaro 'tyarthaṃ tvayā saṃjaya kīrtitaḥ
c darśitaṃ dvīpasaṃsthānam uttaraṃ brūhi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a uktā dvīpā mahārāja grahān me śṛṇu tattvataḥ
c svarbhānuḥ kauravaśreṣṭha yāvad eṣa prabhāvataḥ
a parimaṇḍalo mahārāja svarbhānuḥ śrūyate grahaḥ
c yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi viṣkambho dvādaśāsya vai

c viṣkambheṇa kuruśreṣṭha trayastriṃśat tu maṇḍalam

a sūryas tv aṣṭau sahasrāṇi dve cānye kurunandana

a aṣṭapañcāśataṃ rājan vipulatvena cānagha
c śrūyate paramodāraḥ pataṃgo 'sau vibhāvasuḥ
e etat pramāṇam arkasya nirdiṣṭam iha bhārata
a sa rāhuś chādayaty etau yathākālaṃ mahattayā
c candrādityau mahārāja saṃkṣepo 'yam udāhṛtaḥ
a ity etat te mahārāja pṛcchataḥ śāstracakṣuṣā
c sarvam uktaṃ yathātattvaṃ tasmāc chamam avāpnuhi
a yathādṛṣṭaṃ mayā proktaṃ saniryāṇam idaṃ jagat
c tasmād āśvasa kauravya putraṃ duryodhanaṃ prati
a śrutvedaṃ bharataśreṣṭha bhūmiparva manonugam
c śrīmān bhavati rājanyaḥ siddhārthaḥ sādhusaṃmataḥ
e āyur balaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca tasya tejaś ca vardhate
a yaḥ śṛṇoti mahīpāla parvaṇīdaṃ yatavrataḥ
c prīyante pitaras tasya tathaiva ca pitāmahāḥ
a idaṃ tu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ yatra vartāmahe vayam
c pūrvaṃ pravartate puṇyaṃ tat sarvaṃ śrutavān asi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 vacanād dhṛtarāṣṭrasya kurukṣetraṃ jagāma ha
 vyāsasya varadānena tvaramāṇas tu saṃjayaḥ
 dṛṣṭvā tu samare rājan kṣaṇenaiva samāgataḥ
a atha gāvalgaṇir dhīmān samarād etya saṃjayaḥ
c pratyakṣadarśī sarvasya bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyavit
a dhyāyate dhṛtarāṣṭrāya sahasopetya duḥkhitaḥ
c ācaṣṭa nihataṃ bhīṣmaṃ bharatānām amadhyamam
a saṃjayo 'haṃ mahārāja namas te bharatarṣabha
c hato bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥ
a kakudaṃ sarvayodhānāṃ dhāma sarvadhanuṣmatām
c śaratalpagataḥ so 'dya śete kurupitāmahaḥ
a yasya vīryaṃ samāśritya dyūtaṃ putras tavākarot
c sa śete nihato rājan saṃkhye bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā
a yaḥ sarvān pṛthivīpālān samavetān mahāmṛdhe
c jigāyaikarathenaiva kāśipuryāṃ mahārathaḥ
a jāmadagnyaṃ raṇe rāmam āyodhya vasusaṃbhavaḥ
c na hato jāmadagnyena sa hato 'dya śikhaṇḍinā
a mahendrasadṛśaḥ śaurye sthairye ca himavān iva
c samudra iva gāmbhīrye sahiṣṇutve dharāsamaḥ
a śaradaṃṣṭro dhanurvaktraḥ khaḍgajihvo durāsadaḥ
c narasiṃhaḥ pitā te 'dya pāñcālyena nipātitaḥ
a pāṇḍavānāṃ mahat sainyaṃ yaṃ dṛṣṭvodyantam āhave
c pravepata bhayodvignaṃ siṃhaṃ dṛṣṭveva gogaṇaḥ
a parirakṣya sa senāṃ te daśarātram anīkahā
c jagāmāstam ivādityaḥ kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
a yaḥ sa śakra ivākṣobhyo varṣan bāṇān sahasraśaḥ
c jaghāna yudhi yodhānām arbudaṃ daśabhir dinaiḥ
a sa śete niṣṭanan bhūmau vātarugṇa iva drumaḥ
c tava durmantrite rājan yathā nārhaḥ sa bhārata
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ kurūṇām ṛṣabho hato bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā
c kathaṃ rathāt sa nyapatat pitā me vāsavopamaḥ
a katham āsaṃś ca me putrā hīnā bhīṣmeṇa saṃjaya
c balinā devakalpena gurvarthe brahmacāriṇā
a tasmin hate mahāsattve maheṣvāse mahābale
c mahārathe naravyāghre kim u āsīn manas tadā
a ārtiḥ parā māviśati yataḥ śaṃsasi me hatam
c kurūṇām ṛṣabhaṃ vīram akampyaṃ puruṣarṣabham
a ke taṃ yāntam anupreyuḥ ke cāsyāsan purogamāḥ
c ke 'tiṣṭhan ke nyavartanta ke 'bhyavartanta saṃjaya
a ke śūrā rathaśārdūlam acyutaṃ kṣatriyarṣabham
c rathānīkaṃ gāhamānaṃ sahasā pṛṣṭhato 'nvayuḥ
a yas tamo 'rka ivāpohan parasainyam amitrahā
c sahasraraśmipratimaḥ pareṣāṃ bhayam ādadhat
e akarod duṣkaraṃ karma raṇe kauravaśāsanāt
a grasamānam anīkāni ya enaṃ paryavārayan
c kṛtinaṃ taṃ durādharṣaṃ samyag yāsyantam antike
e kathaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yuddhe pāṇḍavāḥ pratyavārayan
a nikṛntantam anīkāni śaradaṃṣṭraṃ tarasvinam
c cāpavyāttānanaṃ ghoram asijihvaṃ durāsadam
a atyanyān puruṣavyāghrān hrīmantam aparājitam
c pātayām āsa kaunteyaḥ kathaṃ tam ajitaṃ yudhi
a ugradhanvānam ugreṣuṃ vartamānaṃ rathottame
c pareṣām uttamāṅgāni pracinvantaṃ śiteṣubhiḥ
a pāṇḍavānāṃ mahat sainyaṃ yaṃ dṛṣṭvodyantam āhave
c kālāgnim iva durdharṣaṃ samaveṣṭata nityaśaḥ
a parikṛṣya sa senāṃ me daśarātram anīkahā
c jagāmāstam ivādityaḥ kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
a yaḥ sa śakra ivākṣayyaṃ varṣaṃ śaramayaṃ sṛjan
c jaghāna yudhi yodhānām arbudaṃ daśabhir dinaiḥ
a sa śete niṣṭanan bhūmau vātarugṇa iva drumaḥ
c mama durmantritenāsau yathā nārhaḥ sa bhārataḥ
a kathaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām anīkinī
c prahartum aśakat tatra bhīṣmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
a kathaṃ bhīṣmeṇa saṃgrāmam akurvan pāṇḍunandanāḥ
c kathaṃ ca nājayad bhīṣmo droṇe jīvati saṃjaya
a kṛpe saṃnihite tatra bharadvājātmaje tathā
c bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kathaṃ sa nidhanaṃ gataḥ
a kathaṃ cātirathas tena pāñcālyena śikhaṇḍinā
c bhīṣmo vinihato yuddhe devair api durutsahaḥ
a yaḥ spardhate raṇe nityaṃ jāmadagnyaṃ mahābalam
c ajitaṃ jāmadagnyena śakratulyaparākramam
a taṃ hataṃ samare bhīṣmaṃ mahārathabalocitam
c saṃjayācakṣva me vīraṃ yena śarma na vidmahe
a māmakāḥ ke maheṣvāsā nājahuḥ saṃjayācyutam
c duryodhanasamādiṣṭāḥ ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan
a yac chikhaṇḍimukhāḥ sarve pāṇḍavā bhīṣmam abhyayuḥ
c kaccin na kuravo bhītās tatyajuḥ saṃjayācyutam
a maurvīghoṣastanayitnuḥ pṛṣatkapṛṣato mahān
c dhanurhvādamahāśabdo mahāmegha ivonnataḥ
a yad abhyavarṣat kaunteyān sapāñcālān sasṛñjayān
c nighnan pararathān vīro dānavān iva vajrabhṛt
a iṣvastrasāgaraṃ ghoraṃ bāṇagrāhaṃ durāsadam
c kārmukormiṇam akṣayyam advīpaṃ samare 'plavam
e gadāsimakarāvartaṃ hayagrāhaṃ gajākulam
f padātimatsyakalilaṃ śaṅkhadundubhinisvanam
a hayān gajān padātāṃś ca rathāṃś ca tarasā bahūn
c nimajjayantaṃ samare paravīrāpahāriṇam
a vidahyamānaṃ kopena tejasā ca paraṃtapam
c veleva makarāvāsaṃ ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan
a bhīṣmo yad akarot karma samare saṃjayārihā
c duryodhanahitārthāya ke tadāsya puro 'bhavan
a ke 'rakṣan dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ bhīṣmasyāmitatejasaḥ
c pṛṣṭhataḥ ke parān vīrā upāsedhan yatavratāḥ
a ke purastād avartanta rakṣanto bhīṣmam antike
c ke 'rakṣann uttaraṃ cakraṃ vīrā vīrasya yudhyataḥ
a vāme cakre vartamānāḥ ke 'ghnan saṃjaya sṛñjayān
c sametāgram anīkeṣu ke 'bhyarakṣan durāsadam
a pārśvataḥ ke 'bhyavartanta gacchanto durgamāṃ gatim
c samūhe ke parān vīrān pratyayudhyanta saṃjaya
a rakṣyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ vīrair gopyamānāś ca tena te
c durjayānām anīkāni nājayaṃs tarasā yudhi
a sarvalokeśvarasyeva parameṣṭhiprajāpateḥ
c kathaṃ prahartum api te śekuḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavāḥ
a yasmin dvīpe samāśritya yudhyanti kuravaḥ paraiḥ
c taṃ nimagnaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmaṃ śaṃsasi saṃjaya
a yasya vīrye samāśvasya mama putro bṛhadbalaḥ
c na pāṇḍavān agaṇayat kathaṃ sa nihataḥ paraiḥ
a yaḥ purā vibudhaiḥ sendraiḥ sāhāyye yuddhadurmadaḥ
c kāṅkṣito dānavān ghnadbhiḥ pitā mama mahāvrataḥ
a yasmiñ jāte mahāvīrye śaṃtanur lokaśaṃkare
c śokaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca dainyaṃ ca prājahāt putralakṣmaṇi
a prajñā parāyaṇaṃ tajjñaṃ saddharmanirataṃ śucim
c vedavedāṅgatattvajñaṃ kathaṃ śaṃsasi me hatam
a sarvāstravinayopetaṃ dāntaṃ śāntaṃ manasvinam
c hataṃ śāṃtanavaṃ śrutvā manye śeṣaṃ balaṃ hatam
a dharmād adharmo balavān saṃprāpta iti me matiḥ
c yatra vṛddhaṃ guruṃ hatvā rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a jāmadagnyaḥ purā rāmaḥ sarvāstravid anuttamaḥ
c ambārtham udyataḥ saṃkhye bhīṣmeṇa yudhi nirjitaḥ
a tam indrasamakarmāṇaṃ kakudaṃ sarvadhanvinām
c hataṃ śaṃsasi bhīṣmaṃ me kiṃ nu duḥkham ataḥ param
a asakṛt kṣatriyavrātāḥ saṃkhye yena vinirjitāḥ
c jāmadagnyas tathā rāmaḥ paravīranighātinā
d na hato yo mahābuddhiḥ sa hato 'dya śikhaṇḍinā
a tasmān nūnaṃ mahāvīryād bhārgavād yuddhadurmadāt
c tejovīryabalair bhūyāñ śikhaṇḍī drupadātmajaḥ
a yaḥ śūraṃ kṛtinaṃ yuddhe sarvaśāstraviśāradam
c paramāstravidaṃ vīraṃ jaghāna bharatarṣabham
a ke vīrās tam amitraghnam anvayuḥ śatrusaṃsadi
c śaṃsa me tad yathā vṛttaṃ yuddhaṃ bhīṣmasya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a yoṣeva hatavīrā me senā putrasya saṃjaya
c agopam iva codbhrāntaṃ gokulaṃ tad balaṃ mama
a pauruṣaṃ sarvalokasya paraṃ yasya mahāhave
c parāsikte ca vas tasmin katham āsīn manas tadā
a jīvite 'py adya sāmarthyaṃ kim ivāsmāsu saṃjaya
c ghātayitvā mahāvīryaṃ pitaraṃ lokadhārmikam
a agādhe salile magnāṃ nāvaṃ dṛṣṭveva pāragāḥ
c bhīṣme hate bhṛśaṃ duḥkhān manye śocanti putrakāḥ
a adrisāramayaṃ nūnaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama
c yac chrutvā puruṣavyāghraṃ hataṃ bhīṣmaṃ na dīryate
a yasminn astraṃ ca medhā ca nītiś ca bharatarṣabhe
c aprameyāṇi durdharṣe kathaṃ sa nihato yudhi
a na cāstreṇa na śauryeṇa tapasā medhayā na ca
c na dhṛtyā na punas tyāgān mṛtyoḥ kaś cid vimucyate
a kālo nūnaṃ mahāvīryaḥ sarvalokaduratyayaḥ
c yatra śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ hataṃ śaṃsasi saṃjaya
a putraśokābhisaṃtapto mahad duḥkham acintayan
c āśaṃse 'haṃ purā trāṇaṃ bhīṣmāc chaṃtanunandanāt
a yadādityam ivāpaśyat patitaṃ bhuvi saṃjaya
c duryodhanaḥ śāṃtanavaṃ kiṃ tadā pratyapadyata
a nāhaṃ sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ vā buddhyā saṃjaya cintayan
c śeṣaṃ kiṃ cit prapaśyāmi pratyanīke mahīkṣitām
a dāruṇaḥ kṣatradharmo 'yam ṛṣibhiḥ saṃpradarśitaḥ
c yatra śāṃtanavaṃ hatvā rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a vayaṃ vā rājyam icchāmo ghātayitvā pitāmaham
c kṣatradharme sthitāḥ pārthā nāparādhyanti putrakāḥ
a etad āryeṇa kartavyaṃ kṛcchrāsv āpatsu saṃjaya
c parākramaḥ paraṃ śaktyā tac ca tasmin pratiṣṭhitam
a anīkāni vinighnantaṃ hrīmantam aparājitam
c kathaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ tāta pāṇḍuputrā nyapātayan
a kathaṃ yuktāny anīkāni kathaṃ yuddhaṃ mahātmabhiḥ
c kathaṃ vā nihato bhīṣmaḥ pitā saṃjaya me paraiḥ
a duryodhanaś ca karṇaś ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
c duḥśāsanaś ca kitavo hate bhīṣme kim abruvan
a yac charīrair upastīrṇāṃ naravāraṇavājinām
c śaraśaktigadākhaḍgatomarākṣāṃ bhayāvahām
a prāviśan kitavā mandāḥ sabhāṃ yudhi durāsadām
c prāṇadyūte pratibhaye ke 'dīvyanta nararṣabhāḥ
a ke 'jayan ke jitās tatra hṛtalakṣā nipātitāḥ
c anye bhīṣmāc chāṃtanavāt tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a na hi me śāntir astīha yudhi devavrataṃ hatam
c pitaraṃ bhīmakarmāṇaṃ śrutvā me duḥkham āviśat
a ārtiṃ me hṛdaye rūḍhāṃ mahatīṃ putrakāritām
c tvaṃ siñcan sarpiṣevāgnim uddīpayasi saṃjaya
a mahāntaṃ bhāram udyamya viśrutaṃ sārvalaukikam
b taṃ vimagnaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmaṃ śaṃsasi saṃjaya
c dṛṣṭvā vinihataṃ bhīṣmaṃ manye śocanti putrakāḥ
a śroṣyāmi tāni duḥkhāni duryodhanakṛtāny aham
c tasmān me sarvam ācakṣva yad vṛttaṃ tatra saṃjaya
a saṃgrāme pṛthivīśānāṃ mandasyābuddhisaṃbhavam
c apanītaṃ sunītaṃ vā tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a yat kṛtaṃ tatra bhīṣmeṇa saṃgrāme jayam icchatā
c tejoyuktaṃ kṛtāstreṇa śaṃsa tac cāpy aśeṣataḥ
a yathā tad abhavad yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥ
c krameṇa yena yasmiṃś ca kāle yac ca yathā ca tat
d yac ca yasmiṃś ca kāle ca vṛttaṃ yac ca yathā ca tat
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tvadyukto 'yam anupraśno mahārāja yathārhasi
c na tu duryodhane doṣam imam āsaktum arhasi
a ya ātmano duścaritād aśubhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ
c enasā tena nānyaṃ sa upāśaṅkitum arhati
a mahārāja manuṣyeṣu nindyaṃ yaḥ sarvam ācaret
c sa vadhyaḥ sarvalokasya ninditāni samācaran
a nikāro nikṛtiprajñaiḥ pāṇḍavais tvatpratīkṣayā
c anubhūtaḥ sahāmātyaiḥ kṣāntaṃ ca suciraṃ vane
a hayānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca śūrāṇāṃ cāmitaujasām
c pratyakṣaṃ yan mayā dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yogabalena ca
a śṛṇu tat pṛthivīpāla mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
c diṣṭam etat purā nūnam evaṃbhāvi narādhipa
a namaskṛtvā pitus te 'haṃ pārāśaryāya dhīmate
c yasya prasādād divyaṃ me prāptaṃ jñānam anuttamam
a dṛṣṭiś cātīndriyā rājan dūrāc chravaṇam eva ca
c paracittasya vijñānam atītānāgatasya ca
a vyutthitotpattivijñānam ākāśe ca gatiḥ sadā
c śastrair asaṅgo yuddheṣu varadānān mahātmanaḥ
a śṛṇu me vistareṇedaṃ vicitraṃ paramādbhutam
c bhāratānāṃ mahad yuddhaṃ yathābhūl lomaharṣaṇam
a teṣv anīkeṣu yat teṣu vyūḍheṣu ca vidhānataḥ
c duryodhano mahārāja duḥśāsanam athābravīt
a duḥśāsana rathās tūrṇaṃ yujyantāṃ bhīṣmarakṣiṇaḥ
c anīkāni ca sarvāṇi śīghraṃ tvam anucodaya
a ayaṃ mā samanuprāpto varṣapūgābhicintitaḥ
c pāṇḍavānāṃ sasainyānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca samāgamaḥ
a nātaḥ kāryatamaṃ manye raṇe bhīṣmasya rakṣaṇāt
c hanyād gupto hy asau pārthān somakāṃś ca sasṛñjayān
a abravīc ca viśuddhātmā nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinam
c śrūyate strī hy asau pūrvaṃ tasmād varjyo raṇe mama
a tasmād bhīṣmo rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇeti me matiḥ
c śikhaṇḍino vadhe yattāḥ sarve tiṣṭhantu māmakāḥ
a tathā prācyāḥ pratīcyāś ca dākṣiṇātyottarāpathāḥ
c sarvaśastrāstrakuśalās te rakṣantu pitāmaham
a arakṣyamāṇaṃ hi vṛko hanyāt siṃhaṃ mahābalam
c mā siṃhaṃ jambukeneva ghātayāmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā
a vāmaṃ cakraṃ yudhāmanyur uttamaujāś ca dakṣiṇam
c goptārau phalgunasyaitau phalguno 'pi śikhaṇḍinaḥ
a saṃrakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena bhīṣmeṇa ca vivarjitaḥ
c yathā na hanyād gāṅgeyaṃ duḥśāsana tathā kuru
a tato rajanyāṃ vyuṣṭāyāṃ śabdaḥ samabhavan mahān
c krośatāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ yujyatāṃ yujyatām iti
a śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ siṃhanādaiś ca bhārata
c hayaheṣitaśabdaiś ca rathanemisvanais tathā
a gajānāṃ bṛṃhatāṃ caiva yodhānāṃ cābhigarjatām
c kṣveḍitāsphoṭitotkruṣṭais tumulaṃ sarvato 'bhavat
a udatiṣṭhan mahārāja sarvaṃ yuktam aśeṣataḥ
c sūryodaye mahat sainyaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥ
e tava rājendra putrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ tathaiva ca
f duṣpradhṛṣyāṇi cāstrāṇi saśastrakavacāni ca
f tataḥ prakāśe sainyāni samadṛśyanta bhārata
f tvadīyānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca śastravanti mahānti ca
a tatra nāgā rathāś caiva jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtāḥ
c vibhrājamānā dṛśyante meghā iva savidyutaḥ
d saṃnāhāḥ samadṛśyanta sveṣv anīkeṣv avasthitāḥ
a rathānīkāny adṛśyanta nagarāṇīva bhūriśaḥ
c atīva śuśubhe tatra pitā te pūrṇacandravat
a dhanurbhir ṛṣṭibhiḥ khaḍgair gadābhiḥ śaktitomaraiḥ
c yodhāḥ praharaṇaiḥ śubhraiḥ sveṣv anīkeṣv avasthitāḥ
a gajā rathāḥ padātāś ca turagāś ca viśāṃ pate
c vyatiṣṭhan vāgurākārāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a dhvajā bahuvidhākārā vyadṛśyanta samucchritāḥ
c sveṣāṃ caiva pareṣāṃ ca dyutimantaḥ sahasraśaḥ
a kāñcanā maṇicitrāṅgā jvalanta iva pāvakāḥ
c arciṣmanto vyarocanta dhvajā rājñāṃ sahasraśaḥ
a mahendraketavaḥ śubhrā mahendrasadaneṣv iva
c saṃnaddhās teṣu te vīrā dadṛśur yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a udyatair āyudhaiś citrās talabaddhāḥ kalāpinaḥ
c ṛṣabhākṣā manuṣyendrāś camūmukhagatā babhuḥ
a śakuniḥ saubalaḥ śalyaḥ saindhavo 'tha jayadrathaḥ
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
d bhagadatto mahāvīryaḥ kausalyaś ca bṛhadrathaḥ
a śrutāyudhaś ca kāliṅgo jayatsenaś ca pārthivaḥ
c bṛhadbalaś ca kauśalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
a daśaite puruṣavyāghrāḥ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
c akṣauhiṇīnāṃ patayo yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavo duryodhanavaśānugāḥ
c rājāno rājaputrāś ca nītimanto mahābalāḥ
a saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta sveṣv anīkeṣv avasthitāḥ
c baddhakṛṣṇājināḥ sarve dhvajino muñjamālinaḥ
a sṛṣṭā duryodhanasyārthe brahmalokāya dīkṣitāḥ
c samṛddhā daśa vāhinyaḥ parigṛhya vyavasthitāḥ
a ekādaśī dhārtarāṣṭrī kauravāṇāṃ mahācamūḥ
c agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ yatra śāṃtanavo 'graṇīḥ
a śvetoṣṇīṣaṃ śvetahayaṃ śvetavarmāṇam acyutam
c apaśyāma mahārāja bhīṣmaṃ candram ivoditam
a hematāladhvajaṃ bhīṣmaṃ rājate syandane sthitam
c śvetābhra iva tīkṣṇāṃśuṃ dadṛśuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
a dṛṣṭvā camūmukhe bhīṣmaṃ samakampanta pāṇḍavāḥ
c sṛñjayāś ca maheṣvāsā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
a jṛmbhamāṇaṃ mahāsiṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣudramṛgā yathā
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhāḥ sarve samudvivijire muhuḥ
a ekādaśaitāḥ śrījuṣṭā vāhinyas tava bhārata
c pāṇḍavānāṃ tathā sapta mahāpuruṣapālitāḥ
a unmattamakarāvartau mahāgrāhasamākulau
c yugānte samupetau dvau dṛśyete sāgarāv iva
a naiva nas tādṛśo rājan dṛṣṭapūrvo na ca śrutaḥ
c anīkānāṃ sametānāṃ samavāyas tathāvidhaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ
 ubhayoḥ senayos tatra dṛṣṭvā ca kurupāṇḍavān
 animittāny atho brūhi kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yathā sa bhagavān vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano 'bravīt
c tathaiva sahitāḥ sarve samājagmur mahīkṣitaḥ
a maghāviṣayagaḥ somas tad dinaṃ pratyapadyata
c dīpyamānāś ca saṃpetur divi sapta mahāgrahāḥ
a dvidhābhūta ivāditya udaye pratyadṛśyata
c jvalantyā śikhayā bhūyo bhānumān udito divi
a vavāśire ca dīptāyāṃ diśi gomāyuvāyasāḥ
c lipsamānāḥ śarīrāṇi māṃsaśoṇitabhojanāḥ
a ahany ahani pārthānāṃ vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
c bharadvājātmajaś caiva prātar utthāya saṃyatau
a jayo 'stu pāṇḍuputrāṇām ity ūcatur ariṃdamau
c yuyudhāte tavārthāya yathā sa samayaḥ kṛtaḥ
a sarvadharmaviśeṣajñaḥ pitā devavratas tava
c samānīya mahīpālān idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a idaṃ vaḥ kṣatriyā dvāraṃ svargāyāpāvṛtaṃ mahat
c gacchadhvaṃ tena śakrasya brahmaṇaś ca salokatām
a eṣa vaḥ śāśvataḥ panthāḥ pūrvaiḥ pūrvatarair gataḥ
c saṃbhāvayata cātmānam avyagramanaso yudhi
a nābhāgo hi yayātiś ca māndhātā nahuṣo nṛgaḥ
b arjunaḥ sagaro vainyo ye cānye kṣatriyottamāḥ
c saṃsiddhāḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ gatāḥ karmabhir īdṛśaiḥ
a adharmaḥ kṣatriyasyaiṣa yad vyādhimaraṇaṃ gṛhe
c yad ājau nidhanaṃ yāti so 'sya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
a evam uktā mahīpālā bhīṣmeṇa bharatarṣabha
c niryayuḥ svāny anīkāni śobhayanto rathottamaiḥ
a sa tu vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ sāmātyaḥ saha bandhubhiḥ
c nyāsitaḥ samare śastraṃ bhīṣmeṇa bharatarṣabha
a apetakarṇāḥ putrās te rājānaś caiva tāvakāḥ
c niryayuḥ siṃhanādena nādayanto diśo daśa
a śvetaiś chatraiḥ patākābhir dhvajavāraṇavājibhiḥ
c tāny anīkāny aśobhanta rathair atha padātibhiḥ
a bherīpaṇavaśabdaiś ca paṭahānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c rathanemininādaiś ca babhūvākulitā mahī
a kāñcanāṅgadakeyūraiḥ kārmukaiś ca mahārathāḥ
c bhrājamānā vyadṛśyanta jaṅgamāḥ parvatā iva
a tālena mahatā bhīṣmaḥ pañcatāreṇa ketunā
c vimalādityasaṃkāśas tasthau kurucamūpatiḥ
a ye tvadīyā maheṣvāsā rājāno bharatarṣabha
b putrāś ca tava rājendra sārohā sarathā gajaiḥ
c avartanta yathādeśaṃ rājañ śāṃtanavasya te
a sa tu govāsanaḥ śaibyaḥ sahitaḥ sarvarājabhiḥ
c yayau mātaṅgarājena rājārheṇa patākinā
e padmavarṇas tv anīkānāṃ sarveṣām agrataḥ sthitaḥ
a aśvatthāmā yayau yattaḥ siṃhalāṅgūlaketanaḥ
c śrutāyuś citrasenaś ca purumitro viviṃśatiḥ
a śalyo bhūriśravāś caiva vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
c ete sapta maheṣvāsā droṇaputrapurogamāḥ
e syandanair varavarṇābhair bhīṣmasyāsan puraḥsarāḥ
a teṣām api mahotsedhāḥ śobhayanto rathottamān
c bhrājamānā vyadṛśyanta jāmbūnadamayā dhvajāḥ
a jāmbūnadamayī vediḥ kamaṇḍaluvibhūṣitā
c ketur ācāryamukhyasya droṇasya dhanuṣā saha
a anekaśatasāhasram anīkam anukarṣataḥ
c mahān duryodhanasyāsīn nāgo maṇimayo dhvajaḥ
a tasya pauravakāliṅgau kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
c kṣemadhanvā sumitraś ca tasthuḥ pramukhato rathāḥ
a syandanena mahārheṇa ketunā vṛṣabheṇa ca
c prakarṣann iva senāgraṃ māgadhaś ca nṛpo yayau
a tad aṅgapatinā guptaṃ kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā
c śāradābhracayaprakhyaṃ prācyānām abhavad balam
a anīkapramukhe tiṣṭhan varāheṇa mahāyaśāḥ
c śuśubhe ketumukhyena rājatena jayadrathaḥ
a śataṃ rathasahasrāṇāṃ tasyāsan vaśavartinaḥ
c aṣṭau nāgasahasrāṇi sādinām ayutāni ṣaṭ
a tat sindhupatinā rājan pālitaṃ dhvajinīmukham
c anantarathanāgāśvam aśobhata mahad balam
a ṣaṣṭyā rathasahasrais tu nāgānām ayutena ca
c patiḥ sarvakaliṅgānāṃ yayau ketumatā saha
a tasya parvatasaṃkāśā vyarocanta mahāgajāḥ
c yantratomaratūṇīraiḥ patākābhiś ca śobhitāḥ
a śuśubhe ketumukhyena pādapena kaliṅgapaḥ
c śvetacchatreṇa niṣkeṇa cāmaravyajanena ca
a ketumān api mātaṅgaṃ vicitraparamāṅkuśam
c āsthitaḥ samare rājan meghastha iva bhānumān
a tejasā dīpyamānas tu vāraṇottamam āsthitaḥ
c bhagadatto yayau rājā yathā vajradharas tathā
a gajaskandhagatāv āstāṃ bhagadattena saṃmitau
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau ketumantam anuvratau
a sa rathānīkavān vyūho hastyaṅgottamaśīrṣavān
c vājipakṣaḥ patann ugraḥ prāharat sarvatomukhaḥ
a droṇena vihito rājan rājñā śāṃtanavena ca
c tathaivācāryaputreṇa bāhlīkena kṛpeṇa ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato muhūrtāt tumulaḥ śabdo hṛdayakampanaḥ
c aśrūyata mahārāja yodhānāṃ prayuyutsatām
a śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣair vāraṇānāṃ ca bṛṃhitaiḥ
c rathānāṃ nemighoṣaiś ca dīryatīva vasuṃdharā
a hayānāṃ heṣamāṇānāṃ yodhānāṃ tatra garjatām
c kṣaṇena khaṃ diśaś caiva śabdenāpūritaṃ tadā
a putrāṇāṃ tava durdharṣa pāṇḍavānāṃ tathaiva ca
c samakampanta sainyāni parasparasamāgame
a tatra nāgā rathāś caiva jāmbūnadavibhūṣitāḥ
c bhrājamānā vyadṛśyanta meghā iva savidyutaḥ
a dhvajā bahuvidhākārās tāvakānāṃ narādhipa
c kāñcanāṅgadino rejur jvalitā iva pāvakāḥ
a sveṣāṃ caiva pareṣāṃ ca samadṛśyanta bhārata
c mahendraketavaḥ śubhrā mahendrasadaneṣv iva
a kāñcanaiḥ kavacair vīrā jvalanārkasamaprabhaiḥ
c saṃnaddhāḥ pratyadṛśyanta grahāḥ prajvalitā iva
d kuruyodhavarā rājan vicitrāyudhakārmukāḥ
a udyatair āyudhaiś citrais talabaddhāḥ patākinaḥ
c ṛṣabhākṣā maheṣvāsāś camūmukhagatā babhuḥ
a pṛṣṭhagopās tu bhīṣmasya putrās tava narādhipa
c duḥśāsano durviṣaho durmukho duḥsahas tathā
a viviṃśatiś citraseno vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
c satyavrataḥ purumitro jayo bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ
a rathā viṃśatisāhasrās tathaiṣām anuyāyinaḥ
c abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayo 'tha vasātayaḥ
a śālvā matsyās tathāmbaṣṭhās trigartāḥ kekayās tathā
c sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcyodīcyamālavāḥ
a dvādaśaite janapadāḥ sarve śūrās tanutyajaḥ
c mahatā rathavaṃśena te 'bhyarakṣan pitāmaham
a anīkaṃ daśasāhasraṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
c māgadho yena nṛpatis tad rathānīkam anvayāt
a rathānāṃ cakrarakṣāś ca pādarakṣāś ca dantinām
c abhūvan vāhinīmadhye śatānām ayutāni ṣaṭ
a pādātāś cāgrato 'gacchan dhanuścarmāsipāṇayaḥ
c anekaśatasāhasrā nakharaprāsayodhinaḥ
a akṣauhiṇyo daśaikā ca tava putrasya bhārata
c adṛśyanta mahārāja gaṅgeva yamunāntare
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a akṣauhiṇyo daśaikāṃ ca vyūḍhāṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c katham alpena sainyena pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavaḥ
a yo veda mānuṣaṃ vyūhaṃ daivaṃ gāndharvam āsuram
c kathaṃ bhīṣmaṃ sa kaunteyaḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dhārtarāṣṭrāṇy anīkāni dṛṣṭvā vyūḍhāni pāṇḍavaḥ
c abhyabhāṣata dharmātmā dharmarājo dhanaṃjayam
a maharṣer vacanāt tāta vedayanti bṛhaspateḥ
c saṃhatān yodhayed alpān kāmaṃ vistārayed bahūn
a sūcīmukham anīkaṃ syād alpānāṃ bahubhiḥ saha
c asmākaṃ ca tathā sainyam alpīyaḥ sutarāṃ paraiḥ
a etad vacanam ājñāya maharṣer vyūha pāṇḍava
c tac chrutvā dharmarājasya pratyabhāṣata phalguṇaḥ
a eṣa vyūhāmi te rājan vyūhaṃ paramadurjayam
c acalaṃ nāma vajrākhyaṃ vihitaṃ vajrapāṇinā
a yaḥ sa vāta ivoddhūtaḥ samare duḥsahaḥ paraiḥ
c sa naḥ puro yotsyati vai bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumno 'grato yātu ripusainyāni bhīṣayan
a tejāṃsi ripusainyānāṃ mṛdnan puruṣasattamaḥ
c agre 'graṇīr yāsyati no yuddhopāyavicakṣaṇaḥ
d senāpraṇetā yogyo 'yaṃ devānām iva pāvakiḥ
a yaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthivāḥ sarve duryodhanapurogamāḥ
c nivartiṣyanti saṃbhrāntāḥ siṃhaṃ kṣudramṛgā iva
a taṃ sarve saṃśrayiṣyāmaḥ prākāram akutobhayam
c bhīmaṃ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vajrapāṇim ivāmarāḥ
a na hi so 'sti pumāṃl loke yaḥ saṃkruddhaṃ vṛkodaram
c draṣṭum atyugrakarmāṇaṃ viṣaheta nararṣabham
a bhīmaseno gadāṃ bibhrad vajrasāramayīṃ dṛḍhām
c caran vegena mahatā samudram api śoṣayet
a kekayā dhṛṣṭaketuś ca cekitānaś ca vīryavān
c eta tiṣṭhanti sāmātyāḥ prekṣakās te nareśvara
d bhīmasenaṃ tadā rājan darśayan sa mahābalam
a dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dāyādā iti bībhatsur abravīt
c bruvāṇaṃ tu tathā pārthaṃ sarvasainyāni māriṣa
e apūjayaṃs tadā vāgbhir anukūlābhir āhave
a evam uktvā mahābāhus tathā cakre dhanaṃjayaḥ
c vyūhya tāni balāny āśu prayayau phalgunas tadā
a saṃprayātān kurūn dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūḥ
c gaṅgeva pūrṇā stimitā syandamānā vyadṛśyata
a bhīmaseno 'graṇīs teṣāṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavān
a samudyojya tataḥ paścād rājāpy akṣauhiṇīvṛtaḥ
c bhrātṛbhiḥ saha putraiś ca so 'bhyarakṣata pṛṣṭhataḥ
a cakrarakṣau tu bhīmasya mādrīputrau mahādyutī
c draupadeyāḥ sasaubhadrāḥ pṛṣṭhagopās tarasvinaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pāñcālyas teṣāṃ goptā mahārathaḥ
c sahitaḥ pṛtanāśūrai rathamukhyaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥ
a śikhaṇḍī tu tataḥ paścād arjunenābhirakṣitaḥ
c yatto bhīṣmavināśāya prayayau bharatarṣabha
a pṛṣṭhagopo 'rjunasyāpi yuyudhāno mahārathaḥ
c cakrarakṣau tu pāñcālyau yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
a rājā tu madhyamānīke kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bṛhadbhiḥ kuñjarair mattaiś caladbhir acalair iva
a akṣauhiṇyā ca pāñcālyo yajñaseno mahāmanāḥ
c virāṭam anvayāt paścāt pāṇḍavārthe parākramī
a teṣām ādityacandrābhāḥ kanakottamabhūṣaṇāḥ
c nānācihnadharā rājan ratheṣv āsan mahādhvajāḥ
a samutsarpya tataḥ paścād dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
c bhrātṛbhiḥ saha putraiś ca so 'bhyarakṣad yudhiṣṭhiram
a tvadīyānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca ratheṣu vividhān dhvajān
c abhibhūyārjunasyaiko dhvajas tasthau mahākapiḥ
d dhvajāgre ruvato bhīmaṃ kapes tasya punaḥ punaḥ
d śrūyate bhīmaninado nādayāno diśo daśa
d dṛṣṭvā ca bhīṣayām āsa virāvair vānareśvaraḥ
d bhrūkṣepotkṣepavikṣepair lāṅgūlena punaḥ kapiḥ
d ākāśe darśayām āsa pratiśabde mahāsvanam
a pādātās tv agrato 'gacchann asiśaktyṛṣṭipāṇayaḥ
c anekaśatasāhasrā bhīmasenasya rakṣiṇaḥ
a vāraṇā daśasāhasrāḥ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥ
c śūrā hemamayair jālair dīpyamānā ivācalāḥ
d saghaṇṭā hemakakṣyābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtāḥ
a kṣaranta iva jīmūtā madārdrāḥ padmagandhinaḥ
c rājānam anvayuḥ paścāc calanta iva parvatāḥ
a bhīmaseno gadāṃ bhīmāṃ prakarṣan parighopamām
c pracakarṣa mahat sainyaṃ durādharṣo mahāmanāḥ
a tam arkam iva duṣprekṣyaṃ tapantaṃ raśmimālinam
c na śekuḥ sarvato yodhāḥ prativīkṣitum antike
a vajro nāmaiṣa tu vyūho durbhidaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ
c cāpavidyuddhvajo ghoro gupto gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
a yaṃ prativyūhya tiṣṭhanti pāṇḍavās tava vāhinīm
c ajeyo mānuṣe loke pāṇḍavair abhirakṣitaḥ
a saṃdhyāṃ tiṣṭhatsu sainyeṣu sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
c prāvāt sapṛṣato vāyur anabhre stanayitnumān
a viṣvagvātāś ca vānty ugrā nīcaiḥ śarkarakarṣiṇaḥ
c rajaś coddhūyamānaṃ tu tamasāc chādayaj jagat
a papāta mahatī colkā prāṅmukhī bharatarṣabha
c udyantaṃ sūryam āhatya vyaśīryata mahāsvanā
a atha sajjīyamāneṣu sainyeṣu bharatarṣabha
c niṣprabho 'bhyudiyāt sūryaḥ saghoṣo bhūś cacāla ha
e vyaśīryata sanādā ca tadā bharatasattama
a nirghātā bahavo rājan dikṣu sarvāsu cābhavan
c prādurāsīd rajas tīvraṃ na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a dhvajānāṃ dhūyamānānāṃ sahasā mātariśvanā
c kiṅkiṇījālanaddhānāṃ kāñcanasragvatāṃ ravaiḥ
a mahatāṃ sapatākānām ādityasamatejasām
c sarvaṃ jhaṇajhaṇībhūtam āsīt tālavaneṣv iva
a evaṃ te puruṣavyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavā yuddhanandinaḥ
c vyavasthitāḥ prativyūhya tava putrasya vāhinīm
a sraṃsanta iva majjāno yodhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c dṛṣṭvāgrato bhīmasenaṃ gadāpāṇim avasthitam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sūryodaye saṃjaya ke nu pūrvaṃ
yuyutsavo hṛṣyamāṇā ivāsan
c māmakā vā bhīṣmanetrāḥ samīke
pāṇḍavā vā bhīmanetrās tadānīm
a keṣāṃ jaghanyau somasūryau savāyū
keṣāṃ senāṃ śvāpadā vyābhaṣanta
c keṣāṃ yūnāṃ mukhavarṇāḥ prasannāḥ
sarvaṃ hy etad brūhi tattvaṃ yathāvat
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ubhe sene tulyam ivopayāte
ubhe vyūhe hṛṣṭarūpe narendra
c ubhe citre vanarājiprakāśe
tathaivobhe nāgarathāśvapūrṇe
a ubhe sene bṛhatī bhīmarūpe
tathaivobhe bhārata durviṣahye
c tathaivobhe svargajayāya sṛṣṭe
tathā hy ubhe satpuruṣāryagupte
a paścānmukhāḥ kuravo dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ
sthitāḥ pārthāḥ prāṅmukhā yotsyamānāḥ
c daityendraseneva ca kauravāṇāṃ
devendraseneva ca pāṇḍavānām
a śukro vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ
dhārtarāṣṭrāñ śvāpadā vyābhaṣanta
c gajendrāṇāṃ madagandhāṃś ca tīvrān
na sehire tava putrasya nāgāḥ
a duryodhano hastinaṃ padmavarṇaṃ
suvarṇakakṣyaṃ jātibalaṃ prabhinnam
c samāsthito madhyagataḥ kurūṇāṃ
saṃstūyamāno bandibhir māgadhaiś ca
a candraprabhaṃ śvetam asyātapatraṃ
sauvarṇī srag bhrājate cottamāṅge
c taṃ sarvataḥ śakuniḥ pārvatīyaiḥ
sārdhaṃ gāndhāraiḥ pāti gāndhārarājaḥ
a bhīṣmo 'grataḥ sarvasainyasya vṛddhaḥ
śvetacchatraḥ śvetadhanuḥ saśaṅkhaḥ
c śvetoṣṇīṣaḥ pāṇḍureṇa dhvajena
śvetair aśvaiḥ śvetaśailaprakāśaḥ
a tasya sainyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca sarve
bāhlīkānām ekadeśaḥ śalaś ca
c ye cāmbaṣṭhāḥ kṣatriyā ye ca sindhau
tathā sauvīrāḥ pañcanadāś ca śūrāḥ
a śoṇair hayai rukmaratho mahātmā
droṇo mahābāhur adīnasattvaḥ
c āste guruḥ prayaśāḥ sarvarājñāṃ
paścāc camūm indra ivābhirakṣan
a vārddhakṣatriḥ sarvasainyasya madhye
bhūriśravāḥ purumitro jayaś ca
c śālvā matsyāḥ kekayāś cāpi sarve
gajānīkair bhrātaro yotsyamānāḥ
a śāradvataś cottaradhūr mahātmā
maheṣvāso gautamaś citrayodhī
c śakaiḥ kirātair yavanaiḥ pahlavaiś ca
sārdhaṃ camūm uttarato 'bhipāti
a mahārathair andhakavṛṣṇibhojaiḥ
saurāṣṭrakair nairṛtair āttaśastraiḥ
c bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmābhigupto
balaṃ tvadīyaṃ dakṣiṇato 'bhipāti
a saṃśaptakānām ayutaṃ rathānāṃ
mṛtyur jayo vārjunasyeti sṛṣṭāḥ
c yenārjunas tena rājan kṛtāstrāḥ
prayātā vai te trigartāś ca śūrāḥ
a sāgraṃ śatasahasraṃ tu nāgānāṃ tava bhārata
c nāge nāge rathaśataṃ śataṃ cāśvā rathe rathe
a aśve 'śve daśa dhānuṣkā dhānuṣke daśa carmiṇaḥ
c evaṃ vyūḍhāny anīkāni bhīṣmeṇa tava bhārata
d devair api na śakyeta balaṃ kṣobhayituṃ nṛpa
a avyūhan mānuṣaṃ vyūhaṃ daivaṃ gāndharvam āsuram
c divase divase prāpte bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'graṇīḥ
a mahārathaughavipulaḥ samudra iva parvaṇi
c bhīṣmeṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ vyūhaḥ pratyaṅmukho yudhi
a anantarūpā dhvajinī tvadīyā
narendra bhīmā na tu pāṇḍavānām
c tāṃ tv eva manye bṛhatīṃ duṣpradhṛṣyāṃ
yasyā netārau keśavaś cārjunaś ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bṛhatīṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ dṛṣṭvā senāṃ samudyatām
c viṣādam agamad rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a vyūhaṃ bhīṣmeṇa cābhedyaṃ kalpitaṃ prekṣya pāṇḍavaḥ
c abhedyam iva saṃprekṣya viṣaṇṇo 'rjunam abravīt
a dhanaṃjaya kathaṃ śakyam asmābhir yoddhum āhave
c dhārtarāṣṭrair mahābāho yeṣāṃ yoddhā pitāmahaḥ
a akṣobhyo 'yam abhedyaś ca bhīṣmeṇāmitrakarśinā
c kalpitaḥ śāstradṛṣṭena vidhinā bhūritejasā
a te vayaṃ saṃśayaṃ prāptāḥ sasainyāḥ śatrukarśana
c katham asmān mahāvyūhād udyānaṃ no bhaviṣyati
a athārjuno 'bravīt pārthaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram amitrahā
c viṣaṇṇam abhisaṃprekṣya tava rājann anīkinīm
a prajñayābhyadhikāñ śūrān guṇayuktān bahūn api
c jayanty alpatarā yena tan nibodha viśāṃ pate
a tat tu te kāraṇaṃ rājan pravakṣyāmy anasūyave
c nāradas tam ṛṣir veda bhīṣmadroṇau ca pāṇḍava
a etam evārtham āśritya yuddhe devāsure 'bravīt
c pitāmahaḥ kila purā mahendrādīn divaukasaḥ
a na tathā balavīryābhyāṃ vijayante jigīṣavaḥ
c yathā satyānṛśaṃsyābhyāṃ dharmeṇaivodyamena ca
a tyaktvādharmaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca mohaṃ codyamam āsthitāḥ
c yudhyadhvam anahaṃkārā yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a evaṃ rājan vijānīhi dhruvo 'smākaṃ raṇe jayaḥ
c yathā me nāradaḥ prāha yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥ
d yatra kṛṣṇaś ca vedātmā sarvasarveśvaro hariḥ
d jayas tatra mahābāho yathā me prāha nāradaḥ
a guṇabhūto jayaḥ kṛṣṇe pṛṣṭhato 'nveti mādhavam
c anyathā vijayaś cāsya saṃnatiś cāparo guṇaḥ
a anantatejā govindaḥ śatrupūgeṣu nirvyathaḥ
c puruṣaḥ sanātanatamo yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥ
a purā hy eṣa harir bhūtvā vaikuṇṭho 'kuṇṭhasāyakaḥ
c surāsurān avasphūrjann abravīt ke jayantv iti
a anu kṛṣṇaṃ jayemeti yair uktaṃ tatra tair jitam
c tatprasādād dhi trailokyaṃ prāptaṃ śakrādibhiḥ suraiḥ
a tasya te na vyathāṃ kāṃ cid iha paśyāmi bhārata
c yasya te jayam āśāste viśvabhuk tridaśeśvaraḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā svāṃ senāṃ samacodayat
c prativyūhann anīkāni bhīṣmasya bharatarṣabha
a yathoddiṣṭāny anīkāni pratyavyūhanta pāṇḍavāḥ
c svargaṃ param abhīpsantaḥ suyuddhena kurūdvahāḥ
a madhye śikhaṇḍino 'nīkaṃ rakṣitaṃ savyasācinā
b bhīmasenamukhaṃ sainyaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnena pālitam
b bhīmasenādibhir yasya pṛtanā dikṣu pālitā
c dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca svayaṃ bhīmena paripālitam
a anīkaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ rājan yuyudhānena pālitam
c śrīmatā sātvatāgryeṇa śakreṇeva dhanuṣmatā
a mahendrayānapratimaṃ rathaṃ tu
sopaskaraṃ hāṭakaratnacitram
c yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kāñcanabhāṇḍayoktraṃ
samāsthito nāgakulasya madhye
a samucchritaṃ dāntaśalākam asya
supāṇḍuraṃ chatram atīva bhāti
c pradakṣiṇaṃ cainam upācaranti
maharṣayaḥ saṃstutibhir narendram
a purohitāḥ śatruvadhaṃ vadanto
maharṣivṛddhāḥ śrutavanta eva
c japyaiś ca mantraiś ca tathauṣadhībhiḥ
samantataḥ svasty ayanaṃ pracakruḥ
d japan hi vedādhyayanaṃ mahāntaṃ
d jayāya dhaumyo 'pi jayāya mantrān
d yudhiṣṭhiraṃ parivavruḥ sametāḥ
a tataḥ sa vastrāṇi tathaiva gāś ca
phalāni puṣpāṇi tathaiva niṣkān
c kurūttamo brāhmaṇasān mahātmā
kurvan yayau śakra ivāmarebhyaḥ
d tathaiva vipreṣu mahārhajātaṃ
d rukmamaṇimauktikahemaraupyam
a sahasrasūryaḥ śatakiṅkiṇīkaḥ
parārdhyajāmbūnadahemacitraḥ
c ratho 'rjunasyāgnir ivārcimālī
vibhrājate śvetahayaḥ sucakraḥ
a tam āsthitaḥ keśavasaṃgṛhītaṃ
kapidhvajaṃ gāṇḍivabāṇahastaḥ
c dhanurdharo yasya samaḥ pṛthivyāṃ
na vidyate no bhavitā vā kadā cit
a udvartayiṣyaṃs tava putrasenām
atīva raudraṃ sa bibharti rūpam
c anāyudho yaḥ subhujo bhujābhyāṃ
narāśvanāgān yudhi bhasma kuryāt
a sa bhīmasenaḥ sahito yamābhyāṃ
vṛkodaro vīrarathasya goptā
c taṃ prekṣya mattarṣabhasiṃhakhelaṃ
loke mahendrapratimānakalpam
a samīkṣya senāgragataṃ durāsadaṃ
pravivyathuḥ paṅkagatā ivoṣṭrāḥ
c vṛkodaraṃ vāraṇarājadarpaṃ
yodhās tvadīyā bhayavignasattvāḥ
d viṣaṇṇarūpāḥ kurusainyamukhyā
d babhūvire śuṣkakaṇṭhā virūpāḥ
a anīkamadhye tiṣṭhantaṃ rājaputraṃ durāsadam
c abravīd bharataśreṣṭhaṃ guḍākeśaṃ janārdanaḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a ya eṣa goptā pratapan balastho
yo naḥ senāṃ siṃha ivekṣate ca
