c sa eṣa bhīṣmaḥ kuruvaṃśaketur
yenāhṛtās triṃśato vājimedhāḥ
a etāny anīkāni mahānubhāvaṃ
gūhanti meghā iva gharmaraśmim
c etāni hatvā puruṣapravīra
kāṅkṣasva yuddhaṃ bharatarṣabheṇa
d saṃjaya uvāca
d dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya samupasthitam
d śrībhagavān uvāca
d arjunasya hitārthāya kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīt
d śucir bhūtvā mahābāho saṃgrāmābhimukhe sthitaḥ
d parājayāya śatrūṇāṃ durgāstotram udīraya
d saṃjaya uvāca
d evam ukto 'rjunaḥ saṃkhye vāsudevena dhīmatā
d arjuna uvāca
d avatīrya rathāt pārthaḥ stotram āha kṛtāñjaliḥ
d oṃ namas te siddhasenāni ārye mandaravāsini
d kumāri kāli kāpāli kapile kṛṣṇapiṅgale
d bhadrakāli namas tubhyaṃ mahākāli namo 'stu te
d caṇḍi caṇḍe namas tubhyaṃ tāriṇi varavarṇini
d kātyāyani mahābhāge karāli vijaye jaye
d śikhipicchadhvajadhare nānābharaṇabhūṣite
d aṭṭaśūlapraharaṇe khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇi
d gopendrasyānuje jyeṣṭhe nandagopakulodbhave
d mahiṣāsṛkpriye nityaṃ kauśiki pītavāsini
d aṭṭahāse kokamukhe namas te 'stu raṇapriye
d ume śākaṃbhari śvete kṛṣṇe kaiṭabhanāśini
d hiraṇyākṣi virūpākṣi sudhūmrākṣi namo 'stu te
d vedaśruti mahāpuṇye brahmaṇye jātavedasi
d jambūkaṭakacaityeṣu nityaṃ saṃnihitālaye
d tvaṃ brahmavidyā vidyānāṃ mahānidrā ca dehinām
d skandamātar bhagavati durge kāntāravāsini
d svāhākāraḥ svadhā caiva kalā kāṣṭhā sarasvatī
d sāvitri vedamātā ca tathā vedānta ucyate
d stutāsi tvaṃ mahādevi viśuddhenāntarātmanā
d jayo bhavatu me nityaṃ tvatprasādād raṇe raṇe
d kāntārabhayadurgeṣu bhaktānāṃ cālayeṣu ca
d nityaṃ vasasi pātāle yuddhe jayasi dānavān
d tvaṃ jambhanī mohinī ca māyā hrīḥ śrīs tathaiva ca
d saṃdhyā prabhāvatī caiva sāvitrī jananī tathā
d tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭir dhṛtir dīptiś candrādityavivardhinī
d bhūtir bhūtimatāṃ saṃkhye vīkṣyase siddhacāraṇaiḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d tataḥ pārthasya vijñāya bhaktiṃ mānavavatsalā
d antarikṣagatovāca govindasyāgrataḥ sthitā
d devy uvāca
d svalpenaiva tu kālena śatrūñ jeṣyasi pāṇḍava
d naras tvam asi durdharṣa nārāyaṇasahāyavān
d ajeyas tvaṃ raṇe 'rīṇām api vajrabhṛtaḥ svayam
d ity evam uktvā varadā kṣaṇenāntaradhīyata
d labdhvā varaṃ tu kaunteyo mene vijayam ātmanaḥ
d āruroha tataḥ pārtho rathaṃ paramasaṃgatam
d kṛṣṇārjunāv ekarathau divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ
d ya idaṃ paṭhate stotraṃ kalya utthāya mānavaḥ
d yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācebhyo na bhayaṃ vidyate sadā
d na cāpi ripavas tebhyaḥ sarpādyā ye ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ
d na bhayaṃ vidyate tasya sadā rājakulād api
d vivāde jayam āpnoti baddho mucyati bandhanāt
d durgaṃ tarati cāvaśyaṃ tathā corair vimucyate
d saṃgrāme vijayen nityaṃ lakṣmīṃ prāpnoti kevalām
d ārogyabalasaṃpanno jīved varṣaśataṃ tathā
d etad dṛṣṭaṃ prasādāt tu mayā vyāsasya dhīmataḥ
d mohād etau na jānanti naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
d tava putrā durātmānaḥ sarve manyuvaśānugāḥ
d prāptakālam idaṃ vākyaṃ kālapāśena guṇṭhitāḥ
d dvaipāyano nāradaś ca kaṇvo rāmas tathānaghaḥ
d avārayaṃs tava sutaṃ na cāsau tad gṛhītavān
d yatra dharmo dyutiḥ kāntir yatra hrīḥ śrīs tathā matiḥ
d yato dharmas tataḥ kṛṣṇo yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a keṣāṃ prahṛṣṭās tatrāgre yodhā yudhyanti saṃjaya
c udagramanasaḥ ke 'tra ke vā dīnā vicetasaḥ
a ke pūrvaṃ prāharaṃs tatra yuddhe hṛdayakampane
c māmakāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ vā tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a kasya senāsamudaye gandhamālyasamudbhavaḥ
c vācaḥ pradakṣiṇāś caiva yodhānām abhigarjatām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ubhayoḥ senayos tatra yodhā jahṛṣire mudā
c sragdhūpapānagandhānām ubhayatra samudbhavaḥ
a saṃhatānām anīkānāṃ vyūḍhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c saṃsarpatām udīrṇānāṃ vimardaḥ sumahān abhūt
a vāditraśabdas tumulaḥ śaṅkhabherīvimiśritaḥ
b śūrāṇāṃ raṇaśūrāṇāṃ garjatām itaretaram
b ubhayoḥ senayo rājan mahān vyatikaro 'bhavat
b anyonyaṃ vīkṣyamāṇānāṃ yodhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c kuñjarāṇāṃ ca nadatāṃ sainyānāṃ ca prahṛṣyatām
 kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanam
 vāsudevaṃ jagadyoniṃ naumi nārāyaṇaṃ harim
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a dharmakṣetre kurukṣetre samavetā yuyutsavaḥ
c māmakāḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva kim akurvata saṃjaya
d śrīrāmacandrāya namaḥ 
śrīkṛṣṇāya namaḥ  oṃ namaḥ 
d asya śrībhagavadgītāmālāmantrasya bhagavān vedavyāsa
d ṛṣiḥ  anuṣṭup chandaḥ 
śrīkṛṣṇaparamātmā devatā 
d aśocyān anvaśocas tvaṃ prajñāvādāṃś ca bhāṣase Gītā 
d ab iti bījam 
sarvadharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ
d śaraṇaṃ vraja Gītā ab
iti śaktiḥ  ahaṃ
d tvāṃ sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ Gītā
d cd iti kīlakam 
śrīkṛṣṇaprītyarthaṃ dharmārthakāmamokṣārthe
d jape viniyogaḥ 
nainaṃ chindanti śastrāṇi
d nainaṃ dahati pāvakaḥ Gītā ab
iti aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ
d namaḥ  na cainaṃ kledayanty āpo na śoṣayati mārutaḥ
d Gītā cd iti tarjanībhyāṃ namaḥ 
acchedyo 'yam
d adāhyo 'yam akledyo 'śoṣya eva ca Gītā ab
d iti madhyamābhyāṃ namaḥ 
nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sthāṇur acalo 'yaṃ
d sanātanaḥ Gītā cd
ity anāmikābhyāṃ namaḥ 
d paśya me pārtha rūpāṇi śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ Gītā
d ab iti kaniṣṭhikābhyāṃ namaḥ 
nānāvidhāni
d divyāni nānāvarṇākṛtīni ca Gītā cd iti
d karatalakarapṛṣṭhābhyāṃ namaḥ 
iti karanyāsaḥ 
aṅganyāsaḥ 
d nainaṃ chindanti śastrāṇi nainaṃ dahati pāvakaḥ
d Gītā ab iti hṛdayāya namaḥ  na cainaṃ
d kledayanty āpo na śoṣayati mārutaḥ Gītā cd
d iti śirase svāhā 
acchedyo 'yam adāhyo 'yam akledyo 'śoṣya
d eva ca Gītā ab
iti śikhāyai
d vauṣaṭ  nānāvidhāni divyāni nānāvarṇākṛtīni ca
d Gītā cd ity astrāya phaṭ 
ity aṅganyāsaḥ 
d atha dhyānaṃ 
d oṃ pārthāya pratibodhitāṃ bhagavatā nārāyaṇena svayaṃ
d vyāsena grathitāṃ purāṇamuninā madhye mahābhārate 
d advaitāmṛtavarṣiṇīṃ bhagavatīm aṣṭādaśādhyāyinīm
d āvarttair anusaṃdadhāmi bhagavadgītāṃ bhavonmocinīm  
d oṃ hṛdi vikasitapadmaṃ sūryasomāgnibimbaṃ
d praṇavamayavikāsaṃ yasya vai nirvikalpam 
d acalaparamaśāntaṃ jyotir ākāśasāraṃ
d sa bhavatu śubhado me vāsudevaḥ pratiṣṭhaḥ  
d sarvopaniṣado gāvo dogdhā gopālanandanaḥ 
d pārtho vatsaḥ sudhīr bhoktā dugdhaṃ gītāmṛtaṃ mahat  
d oṃ namo 'stu te vyāsa viśālabuddhe
d phullāravindāyatapadmanetra 
d yena tvayā bhāratatailapūrṇaḥ
d prajvālito jñānamayaḥ pradīpaḥ  
d prapannapārijātāya totravetraikapāṇaye 
d jñānamudrāya kṛṣṇāya gītāmṛtaduhe namaḥ  
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavānīkaṃ vyūḍhaṃ duryodhanas tadā
c ācāryam upasaṃgamya rājā vacanam abravīt
a paśyaitāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇām ācārya mahatīṃ camūm
c vyūḍhāṃ drupadaputreṇa tava śiṣyeṇa dhīmatā
a atra śūrā maheṣvāsā bhīmārjunasamā yudhi
c yuyudhāno virāṭaś ca drupadaś ca mahārathaḥ
a dhṛṣṭaketuś cekitānaḥ kāśirājaś ca vīryavān
c purujit kuntibhojaś ca śaibyaś ca narapuṃgavaḥ
a yudhāmanyuś ca vikrānta uttamaujāś ca vīryavān
c saubhadro draupadeyāś ca sarva eva mahārathāḥ
a asmākaṃ tu viśiṣṭā ye tān nibodha dvijottama
c nāyakā mama sainyasya saṃjñārthaṃ tān bravīmi te
d sainye mahati ye sarve netāraḥ śūrasaṃmatāḥ
a bhavān bhīṣmaś ca karṇaś ca kṛpaś ca samitiṃjayaḥ
c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca saumadattis tathaiva ca
a anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā madarthe tyaktajīvitāḥ
c nānāśastrapraharaṇāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
a aparyāptaṃ tad asmākaṃ balaṃ bhīṣmābhirakṣitam
c paryāptaṃ tv idam eteṣāṃ balaṃ bhīmābhirakṣitam
a ayaneṣu ca sarveṣu yathābhāgam avasthitāḥ
c bhīṣmam evābhirakṣantu bhavantaḥ sarva eva hi
a tasya saṃjanayan harṣaṃ kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥ
c siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccaiḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau pratāpavān
a tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca paṇavānakagomukhāḥ
c sahasaivābhyahanyanta sa śabdas tumulo 'bhavat
a tataḥ śvetair hayair yukte mahati syandane sthitau
c mādhavaḥ pāṇḍavaś caiva divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ
a pāñcajanyaṃ hṛṣīkeśo devadattaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c pauṇḍraṃ dadhmau mahāśaṅkhaṃ bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥ
a anantavijayaṃ rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sughoṣamaṇipuṣpakau
a kāśyaś ca parameṣvāsaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumno virāṭaś ca sātyakiś cāparājitaḥ
a drupado draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ pṛthivīpate
c saubhadraś ca mahābāhuḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak
a sa ghoṣo dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ hṛdayāni vyadārayat
c nabhaś ca pṛthivīṃ caiva tumulo vyanunādayan
a atha vyavasthitān dṛṣṭvā dhārtarāṣṭrān kapidhvajaḥ
c pravṛtte śastrasaṃpāte dhanur udyamya pāṇḍavaḥ
a hṛṣīkeśaṃ tadā vākyam idam āha mahīpate
c senayor ubhayor madhye rathaṃ sthāpaya me 'cyuta
a yāvad etān nirīkṣe 'haṃ yoddhukāmān avasthitān
c kair mayā saha yoddhavyam asmin raṇasamudyame
a yotsyamānān avekṣe 'haṃ ya ete 'tra samāgatāḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya durbuddher yuddhe priyacikīrṣavaḥ
a evam ukto hṛṣīkeśo guḍākeśena bhārata
c senayor ubhayor madhye sthāpayitvā rathottamam
a bhīṣmadroṇapramukhataḥ sarveṣāṃ ca mahīkṣitām
c uvāca pārtha paśyaitān samavetān kurūn iti
a tatrāpaśyat sthitān pārthaḥ pitṝn atha pitāmahān
c ācāryān mātulān bhrātṝn putrān pautrān sakhīṃs tathā
a śvaśurān suhṛdaś caiva senayor ubhayor api
c tān samīkṣya sa kaunteyaḥ sarvān bandhūn avasthitān
a kṛpayā parayāviṣṭo viṣīdann idam abravīt
c dṛṣṭvemān svajanān kṛṣṇa yuyutsūn samavasthitān
a sīdanti mama gātrāṇi mukhaṃ ca pariśuṣyati
c vepathuś ca śarīre me romaharṣaś ca jāyate
a gāṇḍīvaṃ sraṃsate hastāt tvak caiva paridahyate
c na ca śaknomy avasthātuṃ bhramatīva ca me manaḥ
a nimittāni ca paśyāmi viparītāni keśava
c na ca śreyo 'nupaśyāmi hatvā svajanam āhave
a na kāṅkṣe vijayaṃ kṛṣṇa na ca rājyaṃ sukhāni ca
c kiṃ no rājyena govinda kiṃ bhogair jīvitena vā
a yeṣām arthe kāṅkṣitaṃ no rājyaṃ bhogāḥ sukhāni ca
c ta ime 'vasthitā yuddhe prāṇāṃs tyaktvā dhanāni ca
a ācāryāḥ pitaraḥ putrās tathaiva ca pitāmahāḥ
c mātulāḥ śvaśurāḥ pautrāḥ syālāḥ saṃbandhinas tathā
a etān na hantum icchāmi ghnato 'pi madhusūdana
c api trailokyarājyasya hetoḥ kiṃ nu mahīkṛte
a nihatya dhārtarāṣṭrān naḥ kā prītiḥ syāj janārdana
c pāpam evāśrayed asmān hatvaitān ātatāyinaḥ
a tasmān nārhā vayaṃ hantuṃ dhārtarāṣṭrān sabāndhavān
c svajanaṃ hi kathaṃ hatvā sukhinaḥ syāma mādhava
a yady apy ete na paśyanti lobhopahatacetasaḥ
c kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ mitradrohe ca pātakam
a kathaṃ na jñeyam asmābhiḥ pāpād asmān nivartitum
c kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ prapaśyadbhir janārdana
a kulakṣaye praṇaśyanti kuladharmāḥ sanātanāḥ
c dharme naṣṭe kulaṃ kṛtsnam adharmo 'bhibhavaty uta
a adharmābhibhavāt kṛṣṇa praduṣyanti kulastriyaḥ
c strīṣu duṣṭāsu vārṣṇeya jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ
a saṃkaro narakāyaiva kulaghnānāṃ kulasya ca
c patanti pitaro hy eṣāṃ luptapiṇḍodakakriyāḥ
a doṣair etaiḥ kulaghnānāṃ varṇasaṃkarakārakaiḥ
c utsādyante jātidharmāḥ kuladharmāś ca śāśvatāḥ
a utsannakuladharmāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ janārdana
c narake niyataṃ vāso bhavatīty anuśuśruma
a aho bata mahat pāpaṃ kartuṃ vyavasitā vayam
c yad rājyasukhalobhena hantuṃ svajanam udyatāḥ
a yadi mām apratīkāram aśastraṃ śastrapāṇayaḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrā raṇe hanyus tan me kṣemataraṃ bhavet
a evam uktvārjunaḥ saṃkhye rathopastha upāviśat
c visṛjya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ śokasaṃvignamānasaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a taṃ tathā kṛpayāviṣṭam aśrupūrṇākulekṣaṇam
c viṣīdantam idaṃ vākyam uvāca madhusūdanaḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a kutas tvā kaśmalam idaṃ viṣame samupasthitam
c anāryajuṣṭam asvargyam akīrtikaram arjuna
a klaibyaṃ mā sma gamaḥ pārtha naitat tvayy upapadyate
c kṣudraṃ hṛdayadaurbalyaṃ tyaktvottiṣṭha paraṃtapa
 arjuna uvāca
a kathaṃ bhīṣmam ahaṃ saṃkhye droṇaṃ ca madhusūdana
c iṣubhiḥ pratiyotsyāmi pūjārhāv arisūdana
a gurūn ahatvā hi mahānubhāvāñ
śreyo bhoktuṃ bhaikṣam apīha loke
c hatvārthakāmāṃs tu gurūn ihaiva
bhuñjīya bhogān rudhirapradigdhān
a na caitad vidmaḥ kataran no garīyo
yad vā jayema yadi vā no jayeyuḥ
c yān eva hatvā na jijīviṣāmas
te 'vasthitāḥ pramukhe dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ
a kārpaṇyadoṣopahatasvabhāvaḥ
pṛcchāmi tvāṃ dharmasaṃmūḍhacetāḥ
c yac chreyaḥ syān niścitaṃ brūhi tan me
śiṣyas te 'haṃ śādhi māṃ tvāṃ prapannam
a na hi prapaśyāmi mamāpanudyād
yac chokam ucchoṣaṇam indriyāṇām
c avāpya bhūmāv asapatnam ṛddhaṃ
rājyaṃ surāṇām api cādhipatyam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam uktvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ guḍākeśaḥ paraṃtapa
c na yotsya iti govindam uktvā tūṣṇīṃ babhūva ha
a tam uvāca hṛṣīkeśaḥ prahasann iva bhārata
c senayor ubhayor madhye viṣīdantam idaṃ vacaḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a aśocyān anvaśocas tvaṃ prajñāvādāṃś ca bhāṣase
c gatāsūn agatāsūṃś ca nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ
d tvaṃ mānuṣyeṇopahatāntarātmā
d viṣādamohābhibhavād visaṃjñaḥ
d kṛpāgṛhītaḥ samavekṣya bandhūn
d abhiprapannān mukham antakasya
a na tv evāhaṃ jātu nāsaṃ na tvaṃ neme janādhipāḥ
c na caiva na bhaviṣyāmaḥ sarve vayam ataḥ param
a dehino 'smin yathā dehe kaumāraṃ yauvanaṃ jarā
c tathā dehāntaraprāptir dhīras tatra na muhyati
a mātrāsparśās tu kaunteya śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkhadāḥ
c āgamāpāyino 'nityās tāṃs titikṣasva bhārata
a yaṃ hi na vyathayanty ete puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c samaduḥkhasukhaṃ dhīraṃ so 'mṛtatvāya kalpate
a nāsato vidyate bhāvo nābhāvo vidyate sataḥ
c ubhayor api dṛṣṭo 'ntas tv anayos tattvadarśibhiḥ
a avināśi tu tad viddhi yena sarvam idaṃ tatam
c vināśam avyayasyāsya na kaś cit kartum arhati
a antavanta ime dehā nityasyoktāḥ śarīriṇaḥ
c anāśino 'prameyasya tasmād yudhyasva bhārata
a ya enaṃ vetti hantāraṃ yaś cainaṃ manyate hatam
c ubhau tau na vijānīto nāyaṃ hanti na hanyate
a na jāyate mriyate vā kadā cin
nāyaṃ bhūtvā bhavitā vā na bhūyaḥ
c ajo nityaḥ śāśvato 'yaṃ purāṇo
na hanyate hanyamāne śarīre
a vedāvināśinaṃ nityaṃ ya enam ajam avyayam
c kathaṃ sa puruṣaḥ pārtha kaṃ ghātayati hanti kam
a vāsāṃsi jīrṇāni yathā vihāya
navāni gṛhṇāti naro 'parāṇi
c tathā śarīrāṇi vihāya jīrṇāny
anyāni saṃyāti navāni dehī
a nainaṃ chindanti śastrāṇi nainaṃ dahati pāvakaḥ
c na cainaṃ kledayanty āpo na śoṣayati mārutaḥ
a acchedyo 'yam adāhyo 'yam akledyo 'śoṣya eva ca
c nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sthāṇur acalo 'yaṃ sanātanaḥ
a avyakto 'yam acintyo 'yam avikāryo 'yam ucyate
c tasmād evaṃ viditvainaṃ nānuśocitum arhasi
a atha cainaṃ nityajātaṃ nityaṃ vā manyase mṛtam
c tathāpi tvaṃ mahābāho nainaṃ śocitum arhasi
a jātasya hi dhruvo mṛtyur dhruvaṃ janma mṛtasya ca
c tasmād aparihārye 'rthe na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi
a avyaktādīni bhūtāni vyaktamadhyāni bhārata
c avyaktanidhanāny eva tatra kā paridevanā
a āścaryavat paśyati kaś cid enam
āścaryavad vadati tathaiva cānyaḥ
c āścaryavac cainam anyaḥ śṛṇoti
śrutvāpy enaṃ veda na caiva kaś cit
a dehī nityam avadhyo 'yaṃ dehe sarvasya bhārata
c tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi
a svadharmam api cāvekṣya na vikampitum arhasi
c dharmyād dhi yuddhāc chreyo 'nyat kṣatriyasya na vidyate
a yadṛcchayā copapannaṃ svargadvāram apāvṛtam
c sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pārtha labhante yuddham īdṛśam
a atha cet tvam imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ na kariṣyasi
c tataḥ svadharmaṃ kīrtiṃ ca hitvā pāpam avāpsyasi
a akīrtiṃ cāpi bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti te 'vyayām
c saṃbhāvitasya cākīrtir maraṇād atiricyate
a bhayād raṇād uparataṃ maṃsyante tvāṃ mahārathāḥ
c yeṣāṃ ca tvaṃ bahumato bhūtvā yāsyasi lāghavam
a avācyavādāṃś ca bahūn vadiṣyanti tavāhitāḥ
c nindantas tava sāmarthyaṃ tato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim
a hato vā prāpsyasi svargaṃ jitvā vā bhokṣyase mahīm
c tasmād uttiṣṭha kaunteya yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ
a sukhaduḥkhe same kṛtvā lābhālābhau jayājayau
c tato yuddhāya yujyasva naivaṃ pāpam avāpsyasi
a eṣā te 'bhihitā sāṃkhye buddhir yoge tv imāṃ śṛṇu
c buddhyā yukto yayā pārtha karmabandhaṃ prahāsyasi
a nehābhikramanāśo 'sti pratyavāyo na vidyate
c svalpam apy asya dharmasya trāyate mahato bhayāt
a vyavasāyātmikā buddhir ekeha kurunandana
c bahuśākhā hy anantāś ca buddhayo 'vyavasāyinām
a yām imāṃ puṣpitāṃ vācaṃ pravadanty avipaścitaḥ
c vedavādaratāḥ pārtha nānyad astīti vādinaḥ
a kāmātmānaḥ svargaparā janmakarmaphalapradām
c kriyāviśeṣabahulāṃ bhogaiśvaryagatiṃ prati
a bhogaiśvaryaprasaktānāṃ tayāpahṛtacetasām
c vyavasāyātmikā buddhiḥ samādhau na vidhīyate
a traiguṇyaviṣayā vedā nistraiguṇyo bhavārjuna
c nirdvaṃdvo nityasattvastho niryogakṣema ātmavān
a yāvān artha udapāne sarvataḥ saṃplutodake
c tāvān sarveṣu vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ
a karmaṇy evādhikāras te mā phaleṣu kadā cana
c mā karmaphalahetur bhūr mā te saṅgo 'stv akarmaṇi
a yogasthaḥ kuru karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā dhanaṃjaya
c siddhyasiddhyoḥ samo bhūtvā samatvaṃ yoga ucyate
d yasya sarve samārambhā nirāśīrbandhanās tv iha
d tyāge yasya hutaṃ sarvaṃ sa tyāgī sa ca buddhimān
a dūreṇa hy avaraṃ karma buddhiyogād dhanaṃjaya
c buddhau śaraṇam anviccha kṛpaṇāḥ phalahetavaḥ
a buddhiyukto jahātīha ubhe sukṛtaduṣkṛte
c tasmād yogāya yujyasva yogaḥ karmasu kauśalam
a karmajaṃ buddhiyuktā hi phalaṃ tyaktvā manīṣiṇaḥ
c janmabandhavinirmuktāḥ padaṃ gacchanty anāmayam
a yadā te mohakalilaṃ buddhir vyatitariṣyati
c tadā gantāsi nirvedaṃ śrotavyasya śrutasya ca
a śrutivipratipannā te yadā sthāsyati niścalā
c samādhāv acalā buddhis tadā yogam avāpsyasi
 arjuna uvāca
a sthitaprajñasya kā bhāṣā samādhisthasya keśava
c sthitadhīḥ kiṃ prabhāṣeta kim āsīta vrajeta kim
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a prajahāti yadā kāmān sarvān pārtha manogatān
c ātmany evātmanā tuṣṭaḥ sthitaprajñas tadocyate
a duḥkheṣv anudvignamanāḥ sukheṣu vigataspṛhaḥ
c vītarāgabhayakrodhaḥ sthitadhīr munir ucyate
a yaḥ sarvatrānabhisnehas tat tat prāpya śubhāśubham
c nābhinandati na dveṣṭi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā
a yadā saṃharate cāyaṃ kūrmo 'ṅgānīva sarvaśaḥ
c indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyas tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā
a viṣayā vinivartante nirāhārasya dehinaḥ
c rasavarjaṃ raso 'py asya paraṃ dṛṣṭvā nivartate
a yatato hy api kaunteya puruṣasya vipaścitaḥ
c indriyāṇi pramāthīni haranti prasabhaṃ manaḥ
a tāni sarvāṇi saṃyamya yukta āsīta matparaḥ
c vaśe hi yasyendriyāṇi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā
a dhyāyato viṣayān puṃsaḥ saṅgas teṣūpajāyate
c saṅgāt saṃjāyate kāmaḥ kāmāt krodho 'bhijāyate
a krodhād bhavati saṃmohaḥ saṃmohāt smṛtivibhramaḥ
c smṛtibhraṃśād buddhināśo buddhināśāt praṇaśyati
a rāgadveṣaviyuktais tu viṣayān indriyaiś caran
c ātmavaśyair vidheyātmā prasādam adhigacchati
a prasāde sarvaduḥkhānāṃ hānir asyopajāyate
c prasannacetaso hy āśu buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate
a nāsti buddhir ayuktasya na cāyuktasya bhāvanā
c na cābhāvayataḥ śāntir aśāntasya kutaḥ sukham
a indriyāṇāṃ hi caratāṃ yan mano 'nuvidhīyate
c tad asya harati prajñāṃ vāyur nāvam ivāmbhasi
a tasmād yasya mahābāho nigṛhītāni sarvaśaḥ
c indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyas tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā
a yā niśā sarvabhūtānāṃ tasyāṃ jāgarti saṃyamī
c yasyāṃ jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyato muneḥ
a āpūryamāṇam acalapratiṣṭhaṃ
samudram āpaḥ praviśanti yadvat
c tadvat kāmā yaṃ praviśanti sarve
sa śāntim āpnoti na kāmakāmī
a vihāya kāmān yaḥ sarvān pumāṃś carati niḥspṛhaḥ
c nirmamo nirahaṃkāraḥ sa śāntim adhigacchati
a eṣā brāhmī sthitiḥ pārtha naināṃ prāpya vimuhyati
c sthitvāsyām antakāle 'pi brahmanirvāṇam ṛcchati
 arjuna uvāca
a jyāyasī cet karmaṇas te matā buddhir janārdana
c tat kiṃ karmaṇi ghore māṃ niyojayasi keśava
a vyāmiśreṇaiva vākyena buddhiṃ mohayasīva me
c tad ekaṃ vada niścitya yena śreyo 'ham āpnuyām
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a loke 'smin dvividhā niṣṭhā purā proktā mayānagha
c jñānayogena sāṃkhyānāṃ karmayogena yoginām
a na karmaṇām anārambhān naiṣkarmyaṃ puruṣo 'śnute
c na ca saṃnyasanād eva siddhiṃ samadhigacchati
a na hi kaś cit kṣaṇam api jātu tiṣṭhaty akarmakṛt
c kāryate hy avaśaḥ karma sarvaḥ prakṛtijair guṇaiḥ
a karmendriyāṇi saṃyamya ya āste manasā smaran
c indriyārthān vimūḍhātmā mithyācāraḥ sa ucyate
a yas tv indriyāṇi manasā niyamyārabhate 'rjuna
c karmendriyaiḥ karmayogam asaktaḥ sa viśiṣyate
a niyataṃ kuru karma tvaṃ karma jyāyo hy akarmaṇaḥ
c śarīrayātrāpi ca te na prasidhyed akarmaṇaḥ
a yajñārthāt karmaṇo 'nyatra loko 'yaṃ karmabandhanaḥ
c tadarthaṃ karma kaunteya muktasaṅgaḥ samācara
a sahayajñāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā purovāca prajāpatiḥ
c anena prasaviṣyadhvam eṣa vo 'stv iṣṭakāmadhuk
a devān bhāvayatānena te devā bhāvayantu vaḥ
c parasparaṃ bhāvayantaḥ śreyaḥ param avāpsyatha
a iṣṭān bhogān hi vo devā dāsyante yajñabhāvitāḥ
c tair dattān apradāyaibhyo yo bhuṅkte stena eva saḥ
a yajñaśiṣṭāśinaḥ santo mucyante sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
c bhuñjate te tv aghaṃ pāpā ye pacanty ātmakāraṇāt
a annād bhavanti bhūtāni parjanyād annasaṃbhavaḥ
c yajñād bhavati parjanyo yajñaḥ karmasamudbhavaḥ
a karma brahmodbhavaṃ viddhi brahmākṣarasamudbhavam
c tasmāt sarvagataṃ brahma nityaṃ yajñe pratiṣṭhitam
a evaṃ pravartitaṃ cakraṃ nānuvartayatīha yaḥ
c aghāyur indriyārāmo moghaṃ pārtha sa jīvati
a yas tv ātmaratir eva syād ātmatṛptaś ca mānavaḥ
c ātmany eva ca saṃtuṣṭas tasya kāryaṃ na vidyate
a naiva tasya kṛtenārtho nākṛteneha kaś cana
c na cāsya sarvabhūteṣu kaś cid arthavyapāśrayaḥ
a tasmād asaktaḥ satataṃ kāryaṃ karma samācara
c asakto hy ācaran karma param āpnoti pūruṣaḥ
a karmaṇaiva hi saṃsiddhim āsthitā janakādayaḥ
c lokasaṃgraham evāpi saṃpaśyan kartum arhasi
a yad yad ācarati śreṣṭhas tat tad evetaro janaḥ
c sa yat pramāṇaṃ kurute lokas tad anuvartate
a na me pārthāsti kartavyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kiṃ cana
c nānavāptam avāptavyaṃ varta eva ca karmaṇi
a yadi hy ahaṃ na varteyaṃ jātu karmaṇy atandritaḥ
c mama vartmānuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśaḥ
a utsīdeyur ime lokā na kuryāṃ karma ced aham
c saṃkarasya ca kartā syām upahanyām imāḥ prajāḥ
a saktāḥ karmaṇy avidvāṃso yathā kurvanti bhārata
c kuryād vidvāṃs tathāsaktaś cikīrṣur lokasaṃgraham
a na buddhibhedaṃ janayed ajñānāṃ karmasaṅginām
c joṣayet sarvakarmāṇi vidvān yuktaḥ samācaran
a prakṛteḥ kriyamāṇāni guṇaiḥ karmāṇi sarvaśaḥ
c ahaṃkāravimūḍhātmā kartāham iti manyate
a tattvavit tu mahābāho guṇakarmavibhāgayoḥ
c guṇā guṇeṣu vartanta iti matvā na sajjate
a prakṛter guṇasaṃmūḍhāḥ sajjante guṇakarmasu
c tān akṛtsnavido mandān kṛtsnavin na vicālayet
a mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasyādhyātmacetasā
c nirāśīr nirmamo bhūtvā yudhyasva vigatajvaraḥ
a ye me matam idaṃ nityam anutiṣṭhanti mānavāḥ
c śraddhāvanto 'nasūyanto mucyante te 'pi karmabhiḥ
a ye tv etad abhyasūyanto nānutiṣṭhanti me matam
c sarvajñānavimūḍhāṃs tān viddhi naṣṭān acetasaḥ
a sadṛśaṃ ceṣṭate svasyāḥ prakṛter jñānavān api
c prakṛtiṃ yānti bhūtāni nigrahaḥ kiṃ kariṣyati
a indriyasyendriyasyārthe rāgadveṣau vyavasthitau
c tayor na vaśam āgacchet tau hy asya paripanthinau
a śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt
c svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a atha kena prayukto 'yaṃ pāpaṃ carati pūruṣaḥ
c anicchann api vārṣṇeya balād iva niyojitaḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a kāma eṣa krodha eṣa rajoguṇasamudbhavaḥ
c mahāśano mahāpāpmā viddhy enam iha vairiṇam
d arjuna uvāca
d bhavaty eṣa kathaṃ kṛṣṇa kathaṃ caiva vivardhate
d śrībhagavān uvāca
d kim ātmakaḥ kim ācāras tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
d eṣa sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ śatrur dehinām indriyaiḥ saha
d sukhatantra ivāsīno mohayan pārtha tiṣṭhati
d kāmakrodhamayo ghoraḥ stambhaharṣasamudbhavaḥ
d ahaṃkāro 'bhimānātmā dustaraḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ
d harṣam asya nivartyaiṣa śokam asya dadāti ca
d bhayaṃ cāsya karoty eṣa mohayaṃs tu muhur muhuḥ
d sa eṣa kaluṣaḥ kṣudraś chidraprekṣī dhanaṃjaya
d rajaḥpravṛtto mohātmā manuṣyāṇām upadravaḥ
a dhūmenāvriyate vahnir yathādarśo malena ca
c yatholbenāvṛto garbhas tathā tenedam āvṛtam
a āvṛtaṃ jñānam etena jñānino nityavairiṇā
c kāmarūpeṇa kaunteya duṣpūreṇānalena ca
a indriyāṇi mano buddhir asyādhiṣṭhānam ucyate
c etair vimohayaty eṣa jñānam āvṛtya dehinam
a tasmāt tvam indriyāṇy ādau niyamya bharatarṣabha
c pāpmānaṃ prajahihy enaṃ jñānavijñānanāśanam
a indriyāṇi parāṇy āhur indriyebhyaḥ paraṃ manaḥ
c manasas tu parā buddhir yo buddheḥ paratas tu saḥ
a evaṃ buddheḥ paraṃ buddhvā saṃstabhyātmānam ātmanā
c jahi śatruṃ mahābāho kāmarūpaṃ durāsadam
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a imaṃ vivasvate yogaṃ proktavān aham avyayam
c vivasvān manave prāha manur ikṣvākave 'bravīt
a evaṃ paraṃparāprāptam imaṃ rājarṣayo viduḥ
c sa kāleneha mahatā yogo naṣṭaḥ paraṃtapa
a sa evāyaṃ mayā te 'dya yogaḥ proktaḥ purātanaḥ
c bhakto 'si me sakhā ceti rahasyaṃ hy etad uttamam
 arjuna uvāca
a aparaṃ bhavato janma paraṃ janma vivasvataḥ
c katham etad vijānīyāṃ tvam ādau proktavān iti
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a bahūni me vyatītāni janmāni tava cārjuna
c tāny ahaṃ veda sarvāṇi na tvaṃ vettha paraṃtapa
a ajo 'pi sann avyayātmā bhūtānām īśvaro 'pi san
c prakṛtiṃ svām adhiṣṭhāya saṃbhavāmy ātmamāyayā
a yadā yadā hi dharmasya glānir bhavati bhārata
c abhyutthānam adharmasya tadātmānaṃ sṛjāmy aham
a paritrāṇāya sādhūnāṃ vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām
c dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya saṃbhavāmi yuge yuge
a janma karma ca me divyam evaṃ yo vetti tattvataḥ
c tyaktvā dehaṃ punarjanma naiti mām eti so 'rjuna
a vītarāgabhayakrodhā manmayā mām upāśritāḥ
c bahavo jñānatapasā pūtā madbhāvam āgatāḥ
a ye yathā māṃ prapadyante tāṃs tathaiva bhajāmy aham
c mama vartmānuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśaḥ
a kāṅkṣantaḥ karmaṇāṃ siddhiṃ yajanta iha devatāḥ
c kṣipraṃ hi mānuṣe loke siddhir bhavati karmajā
a cāturvarṇyaṃ mayā sṛṣṭaṃ guṇakarmavibhāgaśaḥ
c tasya kartāram api māṃ viddhy akartāram avyayam
a na māṃ karmāṇi limpanti na me karmaphale spṛhā
c iti māṃ yo 'bhijānāti karmabhir na sa badhyate
a evaṃ jñātvā kṛtaṃ karma pūrvair api mumukṣubhiḥ
c kuru karmaiva tasmāt tvaṃ pūrvaiḥ pūrvataraṃ kṛtam
a kiṃ karma kim akarmeti kavayo 'py atra mohitāḥ
c tat te karma pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā mokṣyase 'śubhāt
a karmaṇo hy api boddhavyaṃ boddhavyaṃ ca vikarmaṇaḥ
c akarmaṇaś ca boddhavyaṃ gahanā karmaṇo gatiḥ
a karmaṇy akarma yaḥ paśyed akarmaṇi ca karma yaḥ
c sa buddhimān manuṣyeṣu sa yuktaḥ kṛtsnakarmakṛt
a yasya sarve samārambhāḥ kāmasaṃkalpavarjitāḥ
c jñānāgnidagdhakarmāṇaṃ tam āhuḥ paṇḍitaṃ budhāḥ
a tyaktvā karmaphalāsaṅgaṃ nityatṛpto nirāśrayaḥ
c karmaṇy abhipravṛtto 'pi naiva kiṃ cit karoti saḥ
a nirāśīr yatacittātmā tyaktasarvaparigrahaḥ
c śārīraṃ kevalaṃ karma kurvan nāpnoti kilbiṣam
a yadṛcchālābhasaṃtuṣṭo dvaṃdvātīto vimatsaraḥ
c samaḥ siddhāv asiddhau ca kṛtvāpi na nibadhyate
a gatasaṅgasya muktasya jñānāvasthitacetasaḥ
c yajñāyācarataḥ karma samagraṃ pravilīyate
a brahmārpaṇaṃ brahmahavir brahmāgnau brahmaṇā hutam
c brahmaiva tena gantavyaṃ brahmakarmasamādhinā
a daivam evāpare yajñaṃ yoginaḥ paryupāsate
c brahmāgnāv apare yajñaṃ yajñenaivopajuhvati
a śrotrādīnīndriyāṇy anye saṃyamāgniṣu juhvati
c śabdādīn viṣayān anya indriyāgniṣu juhvati
a sarvāṇīndriyakarmāṇi prāṇakarmāṇi cāpare
c ātmasaṃyamayogāgnau juhvati jñānadīpite
a dravyayajñās tapoyajñā yogayajñās tathāpare
c svādhyāyajñānayajñāś ca yatayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
a apāne juhvati prāṇaṃ prāṇe 'pānaṃ tathāpare
c prāṇāpānagatī ruddhvā prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥ
a apare niyatāhārāḥ prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvati
c sarve 'py ete yajñavido yajñakṣapitakalmaṣāḥ
a yajñaśiṣṭāmṛtabhujo yānti brahma sanātanam
c nāyaṃ loko 'sty ayajñasya kuto 'nyaḥ kurusattama
a evaṃ bahuvidhā yajñā vitatā brahmaṇo mukhe
c karmajān viddhi tān sarvān evaṃ jñātvā vimokṣyase
a śreyān dravyamayād yajñāj jñānayajñaḥ paraṃtapa
c sarvaṃ karmākhilaṃ pārtha jñāne parisamāpyate
a tad viddhi praṇipātena paripraśnena sevayā
c upadekṣyanti te jñānaṃ jñāninas tattvadarśinaḥ
a yaj jñātvā na punar moham evaṃ yāsyasi pāṇḍava
c yena bhūtāny aśeṣeṇa drakṣyasy ātmany atho mayi
a api ced asi pāpebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpakṛttamaḥ
c sarvaṃ jñānaplavenaiva vṛjinaṃ saṃtariṣyasi
a yathaidhāṃsi samiddho 'gnir bhasmasāt kurute 'rjuna
c jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā
a na hi jñānena sadṛśaṃ pavitram iha vidyate
c tat svayaṃ yogasaṃsiddhaḥ kālenātmani vindati
a śraddhāvāṃl labhate jñānaṃ tatparaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ
c jñānaṃ labdhvā parāṃ śāntim acireṇādhigacchati
a ajñaś cāśraddadhānaś ca saṃśayātmā vinaśyati
c nāyaṃ loko 'sti na paro na sukhaṃ saṃśayātmanaḥ
a yogasaṃnyastakarmāṇaṃ jñānasaṃchinnasaṃśayam
c ātmavantaṃ na karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanaṃjaya
a tasmād ajñānasaṃbhūtaṃ hṛtsthaṃ jñānāsinātmanaḥ
c chittvainaṃ saṃśayaṃ yogam ātiṣṭhottiṣṭha bhārata
 arjuna uvāca
a saṃnyāsaṃ karmaṇāṃ kṛṣṇa punar yogaṃ ca śaṃsasi
c yac chreya etayor ekaṃ tan me brūhi suniścitam
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a saṃnyāsaḥ karmayogaś ca niḥśreyasakarāv ubhau
c tayos tu karmasaṃnyāsāt karmayogo viśiṣyate
a jñeyaḥ sa nityasaṃnyāsī yo na dveṣṭi na kāṅkṣati
c nirdvaṃdvo hi mahābāho sukhaṃ bandhāt pramucyate
a sāṃkhyayogau pṛthag bālāḥ pravadanti na paṇḍitāḥ
c ekam apy āsthitaḥ samyag ubhayor vindate phalam
a yat sāṃkhyaiḥ prāpyate sthānaṃ tad yogair api gamyate
c ekaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati
a saṃnyāsas tu mahābāho duḥkham āptum ayogataḥ
c yogayukto munir brahma nacireṇādhigacchati
a yogayukto viśuddhātmā vijitātmā jitendriyaḥ
c sarvabhūtātmabhūtātmā kurvann api na lipyate
a naiva kiṃ cit karomīti yukto manyeta tattvavit
c paśyañ śṛṇvan spṛśañ jighrann aśnan gacchan svapañ śvasan
a pralapan visṛjan gṛhṇann unmiṣan nimiṣann api
c indriyāṇīndriyārtheṣu vartanta iti dhārayan
a brahmaṇy ādhāya karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā karoti yaḥ
c lipyate na sa pāpena padmapatram ivāmbhasā
a kāyena manasā buddhyā kevalair indriyair api
c yoginaḥ karma kurvanti saṅgaṃ tyaktvātmaśuddhaye
a yuktaḥ karmaphalaṃ tyaktvā śāntim āpnoti naiṣṭhikīm
c ayuktaḥ kāmakāreṇa phale sakto nibadhyate
a sarvakarmāṇi manasā saṃnyasyāste sukhaṃ vaśī
c navadvāre pure dehī naiva kurvan na kārayan
a na kartṛtvaṃ na karmāṇi lokasya sṛjati prabhuḥ
c na karmaphalasaṃyogaṃ svabhāvas tu pravartate
a nādatte kasya cit pāpaṃ na caiva sukṛtaṃ vibhuḥ
c ajñānenāvṛtaṃ jñānaṃ tena muhyanti jantavaḥ
a jñānena tu tad ajñānaṃ yeṣāṃ nāśitam ātmanaḥ
c teṣām ādityavaj jñānaṃ prakāśayati tatparam
a tadbuddhayas tadātmānas tanniṣṭhās tatparāyaṇāḥ
c gacchanty apunarāvṛttiṃ jñānanirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ
d smaranto 'pi muhus tv etat spṛśanto 'pi svakarmaṇi
d saktā api na sajjanti paṅke ravikarā iva
a vidyāvinayasaṃpanne brāhmaṇe gavi hastini
c śuni caiva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinaḥ
a ihaiva tair jitaḥ sargo yeṣāṃ sāmye sthitaṃ manaḥ
c nirdoṣaṃ hi samaṃ brahma tasmād brahmaṇi te sthitāḥ
a na prahṛṣyet priyaṃ prāpya nodvijet prāpya cāpriyam
c sthirabuddhir asaṃmūḍho brahmavid brahmaṇi sthitaḥ
a bāhyasparśeṣv asaktātmā vindaty ātmani yat sukham
c sa brahmayogayuktātmā sukham akṣayam aśnute
a ye hi saṃsparśajā bhogā duḥkhayonaya eva te
c ādyantavantaḥ kaunteya na teṣu ramate budhaḥ
a śaknotīhaiva yaḥ soḍhuṃ prāk śarīravimokṣaṇāt
c kāmakrodhodbhavaṃ vegaṃ sa yuktaḥ sa sukhī naraḥ
a yo 'ntaḥsukho 'ntarārāmas tathāntarjyotir eva yaḥ
c sa yogī brahmanirvāṇaṃ brahmabhūto 'dhigacchati
a labhante brahmanirvāṇam ṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥ
c chinnadvaidhā yatātmānaḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
a kāmakrodhaviyuktānāṃ yatīnāṃ yatacetasām
c abhito brahmanirvāṇaṃ vartate viditātmanām
a sparśān kṛtvā bahir bāhyāṃś cakṣuś caivāntare bhruvoḥ
c prāṇāpānau samau kṛtvā nāsābhyantaracāriṇau
a yatendriyamanobuddhir munir mokṣaparāyaṇaḥ
c vigatecchābhayakrodho yaḥ sadā mukta eva saḥ
a bhoktāraṃ yajñatapasāṃ sarvalokamaheśvaram
c suhṛdaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jñātvā māṃ śāntim ṛcchati
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a anāśritaḥ karmaphalaṃ kāryaṃ karma karoti yaḥ
c sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca na niragnir na cākriyaḥ
a yaṃ saṃnyāsam iti prāhur yogaṃ taṃ viddhi pāṇḍava
c na hy asaṃnyastasaṃkalpo yogī bhavati kaś cana
a ārurukṣor muner yogaṃ karma kāraṇam ucyate
c yogārūḍhasya tasyaiva śamaḥ kāraṇam ucyate
a yadā hi nendriyārtheṣu na karmasv anuṣajjate
c sarvasaṃkalpasaṃnyāsī yogārūḍhas tadocyate
a uddhared ātmanātmānaṃ nātmānam avasādayet
c ātmaiva hy ātmano bandhur ātmaiva ripur ātmanaḥ
a bandhur ātmātmanas tasya yenātmaivātmanā jitaḥ
c anātmanas tu śatrutve vartetātmaiva śatruvat
a jitātmanaḥ praśāntasya paramātmā samāhitaḥ
c śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkheṣu tathā mānāvamānayoḥ
a jñānavijñānatṛptātmā kūṭastho vijitendriyaḥ
c yukta ity ucyate yogī samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ
a suhṛnmitrāryudāsīnamadhyasthadveṣyabandhuṣu
c sādhuṣv api ca pāpeṣu samabuddhir viśiṣyate
a yogī yuñjīta satatam ātmānaṃ rahasi sthitaḥ
c ekākī yatacittātmā nirāśīr aparigrahaḥ
a śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ
c nātyucchritaṃ nātinīcaṃ cailājinakuśottaram
a tatraikāgraṃ manaḥ kṛtvā yatacittendriyakriyaḥ
c upaviśyāsane yuñjyād yogam ātmaviśuddhaye
a samaṃ kāyaśirogrīvaṃ dhārayann acalaṃ sthiraḥ
c saṃprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaś cānavalokayan
a praśāntātmā vigatabhīr brahmacārivrate sthitaḥ
c manaḥ saṃyamya maccitto yukta āsīta matparaḥ
a yuñjann evaṃ sadātmānaṃ yogī niyatamānasaḥ
c śāntiṃ nirvāṇaparamāṃ matsaṃsthām adhigacchati
a nātyaśnatas tu yogo 'sti na caikāntam anaśnataḥ
c na cātisvapnaśīlasya jāgrato naiva cārjuna
a yuktāhāravihārasya yuktaceṣṭasya karmasu
c yuktasvapnāvabodhasya yogo bhavati duḥkhahā
a yadā viniyataṃ cittam ātmany evāvatiṣṭhate
c niḥspṛhaḥ sarvakāmebhyo yukta ity ucyate tadā
a yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtā
c yogino yatacittasya yuñjato yogam ātmanaḥ
a yatroparamate cittaṃ niruddhaṃ yogasevayā
c yatra caivātmanātmānaṃ paśyann ātmani tuṣyati
a sukham ātyantikaṃ yat tad buddhigrāhyam atīndriyam
c vetti yatra na caivāyaṃ sthitaś calati tattvataḥ
a yaṃ labdhvā cāparaṃ lābhaṃ manyate nādhikaṃ tataḥ
c yasmin sthito na duḥkhena guruṇāpi vicālyate
a taṃ vidyād duḥkhasaṃyogaviyogaṃ yogasaṃjñitam
c sa niścayena yoktavyo yogo 'nirviṇṇacetasā
a saṃkalpaprabhavān kāmāṃs tyaktvā sarvān aśeṣataḥ
c manasaivendriyagrāmaṃ viniyamya samantataḥ
a śanaiḥ śanair uparamed buddhyā dhṛtigṛhītayā
c ātmasaṃsthaṃ manaḥ kṛtvā na kiṃ cid api cintayet
a yato yato niścarati manaś cañcalam asthiram
c tatas tato niyamyaitad ātmany eva vaśaṃ nayet
a praśāntamanasaṃ hy enaṃ yoginaṃ sukham uttamam
c upaiti śāntarajasaṃ brahmabhūtam akalmaṣam
a yuñjann evaṃ sadātmānaṃ yogī vigatakalmaṣaḥ
c sukhena brahmasaṃsparśam atyantaṃ sukham aśnute
a sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cātmani
c īkṣate yogayuktātmā sarvatra samadarśanaḥ
a yo māṃ paśyati sarvatra sarvaṃ ca mayi paśyati
c tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati
a sarvabhūtasthitaṃ yo māṃ bhajaty ekatvam āsthitaḥ
c sarvathā vartamāno 'pi sa yogī mayi vartate
a ātmaupamyena sarvatra samaṃ paśyati yo 'rjuna
c sukhaṃ vā yadi vā duḥkhaṃ sa yogī paramo mataḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a yo 'yaṃ yogas tvayā proktaḥ sāmyena madhusūdana
c etasyāhaṃ na paśyāmi cañcalatvāt sthitiṃ sthirām
a cañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa pramāthi balavad dṛḍham
c tasyāhaṃ nigrahaṃ manye vāyor iva suduṣkaram
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a asaṃśayaṃ mahābāho mano durnigrahaṃ calam
c abhyāsena tu kaunteya vairāgyeṇa ca gṛhyate
a asaṃyatātmanā yogo duṣprāpa iti me matiḥ
c vaśyātmanā tu yatatā śakyo 'vāptum upāyataḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a ayatiḥ śraddhayopeto yogāc calitamānasaḥ
b lipsamānaḥ satāṃ mārgaṃ pramūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathi
b anekacitto vibhrānto mohasyaiva vaśaṃ gataḥ
c aprāpya yogasaṃsiddhiṃ kāṃ gatiṃ kṛṣṇa gacchati
a kaccin nobhayavibhraṣṭaś chinnābhram iva naśyati
c apratiṣṭho mahābāho vimūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathi
a etan me saṃśayaṃ kṛṣṇa chettum arhasy aśeṣataḥ
c tvad anyaḥ saṃśayasyāsya chettā na hy upapadyate
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a pārtha naiveha nāmutra vināśas tasya vidyate
c na hi kalyāṇakṛt kaś cid durgatiṃ tāta gacchati
a prāpya puṇyakṛtāṃl lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
c śucīnāṃ śrīmatāṃ gehe yogabhraṣṭo 'bhijāyate
a atha vā yoginām eva kule bhavati dhīmatām
c etad dhi durlabhataraṃ loke janma yad īdṛśam
a tatra taṃ buddhisaṃyogaṃ labhate paurvadehikam
c yatate ca tato bhūyaḥ saṃsiddhau kurunandana
a pūrvābhyāsena tenaiva hriyate hy avaśo 'pi saḥ
c jijñāsur api yogasya śabdabrahmātivartate
a prayatnād yatamānas tu yogī saṃśuddhakilbiṣaḥ
c anekajanmasaṃsiddhas tato yāti parāṃ gatim
a tapasvibhyo 'dhiko yogī jñānibhyo 'pi mato 'dhikaḥ
c karmibhyaś cādhiko yogī tasmād yogī bhavārjuna
a yoginām api sarveṣāṃ madgatenāntarātmanā
c śraddhāvān bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mataḥ
d bhagavannāmasaṃprāptimātrāt sarvam avāpyate
d phalitāḥ śālayaḥ samyag vṛṣṭimātre 'valokite
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a mayy āsaktamanāḥ pārtha yogaṃ yuñjan madāśrayaḥ
c asaṃśayaṃ samagraṃ māṃ yathā jñāsyasi tac chṛṇu
a jñānaṃ te 'haṃ savijñānam idaṃ vakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ
c yaj jñātvā neha bhūyo 'nyaj jñātavyam avaśiṣyate
a manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaś cid yatati siddhaye
c yatatām api siddhānāṃ kaś cin māṃ vetti tattvataḥ
a bhūmir āpo 'nalo vāyuḥ khaṃ mano buddhir eva ca
c ahaṃkāra itīyaṃ me bhinnā prakṛtir aṣṭadhā
a apareyam itas tv anyāṃ prakṛtiṃ viddhi me parām
c jīvabhūtāṃ mahābāho yayedaṃ dhāryate jagat
a etadyonīni bhūtāni sarvāṇīty upadhāraya
c ahaṃ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayas tathā
a mattaḥ parataraṃ nānyat kiṃ cid asti dhanaṃjaya
c mayi sarvam idaṃ protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva
a raso 'ham apsu kaunteya prabhāsmi śaśisūryayoḥ
c praṇavaḥ sarvavedeṣu śabdaḥ khe pauruṣaṃ nṛṣu
a puṇyo gandhaḥ pṛthivyāṃ ca tejaś cāsmi vibhāvasau
c jīvanaṃ sarvabhūteṣu tapaś cāsmi tapasviṣu
a bījaṃ māṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viddhi pārtha sanātanam
c buddhir buddhimatām asmi tejas tejasvinām aham
a balaṃ balavatāṃ cāhaṃ kāmarāgavivarjitam
c dharmāviruddho bhūteṣu kāmo 'smi bharatarṣabha
a ye caiva sāttvikā bhāvā rājasās tāmasāś ca ye
c matta eveti tān viddhi na tv ahaṃ teṣu te mayi
a tribhir guṇamayair bhāvair ebhiḥ sarvam idaṃ jagat
c mohitaṃ nābhijānāti mām ebhyaḥ param avyayam
a daivī hy eṣā guṇamayī mama māyā duratyayā
c mām eva ye prapadyante māyām etāṃ taranti te
a na māṃ duṣkṛtino mūḍhāḥ prapadyante narādhamāḥ
c māyayāpahṛtajñānā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ
a caturvidhā bhajante māṃ janāḥ sukṛtino 'rjuna
c ārto jijñāsur arthārthī jñānī ca bharatarṣabha
a teṣāṃ jñānī nityayukta ekabhaktir viśiṣyate
c priyo hi jñānino 'tyartham ahaṃ sa ca mama priyaḥ
a udārāḥ sarva evaite jñānī tv ātmaiva me matam
c āsthitaḥ sa hi yuktātmā mām evānuttamāṃ gatim
a bahūnāṃ janmanām ante jñānavān māṃ prapadyate
c vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti sa mahātmā sudurlabhaḥ
a kāmais tais tair hṛtajñānāḥ prapadyante 'nyadevatāḥ
c taṃ taṃ niyamam āsthāya prakṛtyā niyatāḥ svayā
a yo yo yāṃ yāṃ tanuṃ bhaktaḥ śraddhayārcitum icchati
c tasya tasyācalāṃ śraddhāṃ tām eva vidadhāmy aham
a sa tayā śraddhayā yuktas tasyā rādhanam īhate
c labhate ca tataḥ kāmān mayaiva vihitān hi tān
a antavat tu phalaṃ teṣāṃ tad bhavaty alpamedhasām
c devān devayajo yānti madbhaktā yānti mām api
c         siddhān yānti siddhavratāḥ
c bhūtān bhūtayajo yānti        
c         pitṝn yānti pitṛvratāḥ
c bhūtāni yānti bhūtejyā        
a avyaktaṃ vyaktim āpannaṃ manyante mām abuddhayaḥ
c paraṃ bhāvam ajānanto mamāvyayam anuttamam
a nāhaṃ prakāśaḥ sarvasya yogamāyāsamāvṛtaḥ
c mūḍho 'yaṃ nābhijānāti loko mām ajam avyayam
a vedāhaṃ samatītāni vartamānāni cārjuna
c bhaviṣyāṇi ca bhūtāni māṃ tu veda na kaś cana
a icchādveṣasamutthena dvaṃdvamohena bhārata
c sarvabhūtāni saṃmohaṃ sarge yānti paraṃtapa
a yeṣāṃ tv antagataṃ pāpaṃ janānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām
c te dvaṃdvamohanirmuktā bhajante māṃ dṛḍhavratāḥ
a jarāmaraṇamokṣāya mām āśritya yatanti ye
c te brahma tad viduḥ kṛtsnam adhyātmaṃ karma cākhilam
a sādhibhūtādhidaivaṃ māṃ sādhiyajñaṃ ca ye viduḥ
c prayāṇakāle 'pi ca māṃ te vidur yuktacetasaḥ
d sphuṭaṃ bhagavato bhaktir vihitā kalpamañjarī
d sādhanecchāsamucitāṃ yenāśāṃ paripūrayet
 arjuna uvāca
a kiṃ tad brahma kim adhyātmaṃ kiṃ karma puruṣottama
c adhibhūtaṃ ca kiṃ proktam adhidaivaṃ kim ucyate
a adhiyajñaḥ kathaṃ ko 'tra dehe 'smin madhusūdana
c prayāṇakāle ca kathaṃ jñeyo 'si niyatātmabhiḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a akṣaraṃ brahma paramaṃ svabhāvo 'dhyātmam ucyate
c bhūtabhāvodbhavakaro visargaḥ karmasaṃjñitaḥ
a adhibhūtaṃ kṣaro bhāvaḥ puruṣaś cādhidaivatam
c adhiyajño 'ham evātra dehe dehabhṛtāṃ vara
a antakāle ca mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaram
c yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ
a yaṃ yaṃ vāpi smaran bhāvaṃ tyajaty ante kalevaram
c taṃ tam evaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ
a tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu mām anusmara yudhya ca
c mayy arpitamanobuddhir mām evaiṣyasy asaṃśayaḥ
a abhyāsayogayuktena cetasā nānyagāminā
c paramaṃ puruṣaṃ divyaṃ yāti pārthānucintayan
a kaviṃ purāṇam anuśāsitāram
aṇor aṇīyāṃsam anusmared yaḥ
c sarvasya dhātāram acintyarūpam
ādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt
a prayāṇakāle manasācalena
bhaktyā yukto yogabalena caiva
c bhruvor madhye prāṇam āveśya samyak
sa taṃ paraṃ puruṣam upaiti divyam
a yad akṣaraṃ vedavido vadanti
viśanti yad yatayo vītarāgāḥ
c yad icchanto brahmacaryaṃ caranti
tat te padaṃ saṃgraheṇa pravakṣye
d sarve vedā yat padam āmananti
d tapāṃsi sarvāṇi ca yad vadanti
d yad icchanto brahmacaryaṃ caranti
d tat te padaṃ saṃgraheṇa bravīmi
a sarvadvārāṇi saṃyamya mano hṛdi nirudhya ca
c mūrdhny ādhāyātmanaḥ prāṇam āsthito yogadhāraṇām
a om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma vyāharan mām anusmaran
c yaḥ prayāti tyajan dehaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
a ananyacetāḥ satataṃ yo māṃ smarati nityaśaḥ
c tasyāhaṃ sulabhaḥ pārtha nityayuktasya yoginaḥ
a mām upetya punarjanma duḥkhālayam aśāśvatam
c nāpnuvanti mahātmānaḥ saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ gatāḥ
a ā brahmabhuvanāl lokāḥ punarāvartino 'rjuna
c mām upetya tu kaunteya punarjanma na vidyate
a sahasrayugaparyantam ahar yad brahmaṇo viduḥ
c rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ te 'horātravido janāḥ
a avyaktād vyaktayaḥ sarvāḥ prabhavanty aharāgame
c rātryāgame pralīyante tatraivāvyaktasaṃjñake
a bhūtagrāmaḥ sa evāyaṃ bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyate
c rātryāgame 'vaśaḥ pārtha prabhavaty aharāgame
a paras tasmāt tu bhāvo 'nyo 'vyakto 'vyaktāt sanātanaḥ
c yaḥ sa sarveṣu bhūteṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati
a avyakto 'kṣara ity uktas tam āhuḥ paramāṃ gatim
c yaṃ prāpya na nivartante tad dhāma paramaṃ mama
a puruṣaḥ sa paraḥ pārtha bhaktyā labhyas tv ananyayā
b yaṃ prāpya na punarjanma labhante yogino 'rjuna
c yasyāntaḥsthāni bhūtāni yena sarvam idaṃ tatam
a yatra kāle tv anāvṛttim āvṛttiṃ caiva yoginaḥ
c prayātā yānti taṃ kālaṃ vakṣyāmi bharatarṣabha
a agnir jyotir ahaḥ śuklaḥ ṣaṇmāsā uttarāyaṇam
c tatra prayātā gacchanti brahma brahmavido janāḥ
a dhūmo rātris tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṇmāsā dakṣiṇāyanam
c tatra cāndramasaṃ jyotir yogī prāpya nivartate
a śuklakṛṣṇe gatī hy ete jagataḥ śāśvate mate
c ekayā yāty anāvṛttim anyayāvartate punaḥ
a naite sṛtī pārtha jānan yogī muhyati kaś cana
c tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu yogayukto bhavārjuna
a vedeṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caiva
dāneṣu yat puṇyaphalaṃ pradiṣṭam
c atyeti tat sarvam idaṃ viditvā
yogī paraṃ sthānam upaiti cādyam
d sarvatattvagatatvena vijñāte parameśvare
d antar bahir na sāvasthā na yasyāṃ bhāsate vibhuḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a idaṃ tu te guhyatamaṃ pravakṣyāmy anasūyave
c jñānaṃ vijñānasahitaṃ yaj jñātvā mokṣyase 'śubhāt
a rājavidyā rājaguhyaṃ pavitram idam uttamam
c pratyakṣāvagamaṃ dharmyaṃ susukhaṃ kartum avyayam
a aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā dharmasyāsya paraṃtapa
c aprāpya māṃ nivartante mṛtyusaṃsāravartmani
a mayā tatam idaṃ sarvaṃ jagad avyaktamūrtinā
c matsthāni sarvabhūtāni na cāhaṃ teṣv avasthitaḥ
a na ca matsthāni bhūtāni paśya me yogam aiśvaram
c bhūtabhṛn na ca bhūtastho mamātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ
d sarvagaḥ sarvavaś cādyaḥ sarvakṛt sarvadarśanaḥ
d sarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī ca sarvātmā sarvatomukhaḥ
a yathākāśasthito nityaṃ vāyuḥ sarvatrago mahān
c tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni matsthānīty upadhāraya
d evaṃ hi sarvabhūteṣu carāmy anabhilakṣitaḥ
d bhūtaprakṛtim āsthāya sahaiva ca vinaiva ca
a sarvabhūtāni kaunteya prakṛtiṃ yānti māmikām
c kalpakṣaye punas tāni kalpādau visṛjāmy aham
a prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhya visṛjāmi punaḥ punaḥ
c bhūtagrāmam imaṃ kṛtsnam avaśaṃ prakṛter vaśāt
a na ca māṃ tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanaṃjaya
c udāsīnavad āsīnam asaktaṃ teṣu karmasu
a mayādhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram
c hetunānena kaunteya jagad viparivartate
a avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanum āśritam
c paraṃ bhāvam ajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram
a moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ
c rākṣasīm āsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohinīṃ śritāḥ
a mahātmānas tu māṃ pārtha daivīṃ prakṛtim āśritāḥ
c bhajanty ananyamanaso jñātvā bhūtādim avyayam
a satataṃ kīrtayanto māṃ yatantaś ca dṛḍhavratāḥ
c namasyantaś ca māṃ bhaktyā nityayuktā upāsate
a jñānayajñena cāpy anye yajanto mām upāsate
c ekatvena pṛthaktvena bahudhā viśvatomukham
a ahaṃ kratur ahaṃ yajñaḥ svadhāham aham auṣadham
c mantro 'ham aham evājyam aham agnir ahaṃ hutam
a pitāham asya jagato mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥ
c vedyaṃ pavitram oṃkāra ṛk sāma yajur eva ca
a gatir bhartā prabhuḥ sākṣī nivāsaḥ śaraṇaṃ suhṛt
c prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ sthānaṃ nidhānaṃ bījam avyayam
a tapāmy aham ahaṃ varṣaṃ nigṛhṇāmy utsṛjāmi ca
c amṛtaṃ caiva mṛtyuś ca sad asac cāham arjuna
a traividyā māṃ somapāḥ pūtapāpā
yajñair iṣṭvā svargatiṃ prārthayante
c te puṇyam āsādya surendralokam
aśnanti divyān divi devabhogān
a te taṃ bhuktvā svargalokaṃ viśālaṃ
kṣīṇe puṇye martyalokaṃ viśanti
c evaṃ trayīdharmam anuprapannā
gatāgataṃ kāmakāmā labhante
a ananyāś cintayanto māṃ ye janāḥ paryupāsate
c teṣāṃ nityābhiyuktānāṃ yogakṣemaṃ vahāmy aham
a ye 'py anyadevatā bhaktā yajante śraddhayānvitāḥ
c te 'pi mām eva kaunteya yajanty avidhipūrvakam
a ahaṃ hi sarvayajñānāṃ bhoktā ca prabhur eva ca
c na tu mām abhijānanti tattvenātaś cyavanti te
a yānti devavratā devān pitṝn yānti pitṛvratāḥ
c bhūtāni yānti bhūtejyā yānti madyājino 'pi mām
a patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati
c tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtam aśnāmi prayatātmanaḥ
a yat karoṣi yad aśnāsi yaj juhoṣi dadāsi yat
c yat tapasyasi kaunteya tat kuruṣva madarpaṇam
a śubhāśubhaphalair evaṃ mokṣyase karmabandhanaiḥ
c saṃnyāsayogayuktātmā vimukto mām upaiṣyasi
a samo 'haṃ sarvabhūteṣu na me dveṣyo 'sti na priyaḥ
c ye bhajanti tu māṃ bhaktyā mayi te teṣu cāpy aham
a api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhāk
c sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ
a kṣipraṃ bhavati dharmātmā śaśvacchāntiṃ nigacchati
c kaunteya pratijānīhi na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati
a māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye 'pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ
c striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te 'pi yānti parāṃ gatim
a kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathā
c anityam asukhaṃ lokam imaṃ prāpya bhajasva mām
a manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṃ namaskuru
c mām evaiṣyasi yuktvaivam ātmānaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a bhūya eva mahābāho śṛṇu me paramaṃ vacaḥ
c yat te 'haṃ prīyamāṇāya vakṣyāmi hitakāmyayā
a na me viduḥ suragaṇāḥ prabhavaṃ na maharṣayaḥ
c aham ādir hi devānāṃ maharṣīṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a yo mām ajam anādiṃ ca vetti lokamaheśvaram
c asaṃmūḍhaḥ sa martyeṣu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
a buddhir jñānam asaṃmohaḥ kṣamā satyaṃ damaḥ śamaḥ
c sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhavo 'bhāvo bhayaṃ cābhayam eva ca
a ahiṃsā samatā tuṣṭis tapo dānaṃ yaśo 'yaśaḥ
c bhavanti bhāvā bhūtānāṃ matta eva pṛthagvidhāḥ
a maharṣayaḥ sapta pūrve catvāro manavas tathā
c madbhāvā mānasā jātā yeṣāṃ loka imāḥ prajāḥ
a etāṃ vibhūtiṃ yogaṃ ca mama yo vetti tattvataḥ
c so 'vikampena yogena yujyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a ahaṃ sarvasya prabhavo mattaḥ sarvaṃ pravartate
c iti matvā bhajante māṃ budhā bhāvasamanvitāḥ
a maccittā madgataprāṇā bodhayantaḥ parasparam
c kathayantaś ca māṃ nityaṃ tuṣyanti ca ramanti ca
a teṣāṃ satatayuktānāṃ bhajatāṃ prītipūrvakam
c dadāmi buddhiyogaṃ taṃ yena mām upayānti te
a teṣām evānukampārtham aham ajñānajaṃ tamaḥ
c nāśayāmy ātmabhāvastho jñānadīpena bhāsvatā
 arjuna uvāca
a paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma pavitraṃ paramaṃ bhavān
c puruṣaṃ śāśvataṃ divyam ādidevam ajaṃ vibhum
a āhus tvām ṛṣayaḥ sarve devarṣir nāradas tathā
c asito devalo vyāsaḥ svayaṃ caiva bravīṣi me
a sarvam etad ṛtaṃ manye yan māṃ vadasi keśava
c na hi te bhagavan vyaktiṃ vidur devā na dānavāḥ
a svayam evātmanātmānaṃ vettha tvaṃ puruṣottama
c bhūtabhāvana bhūteśa devadeva jagatpate
a vaktum arhasy aśeṣeṇa divyā hy ātmavibhūtayaḥ
c yābhir vibhūtibhir lokān imāṃs tvaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhasi
a kathaṃ vidyām ahaṃ yogiṃs tvāṃ sadā paricintayan
c keṣu keṣu ca bhāveṣu cintyo 'si bhagavan mayā
a vistareṇātmano yogaṃ vibhūtiṃ ca janārdana
c bhūyaḥ kathaya tṛptir hi śṛṇvato nāsti me 'mṛtam
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a hanta te kathayiṣyāmi divyā hy ātmavibhūtayaḥ
c prādhānyataḥ kuruśreṣṭha nāsty anto vistarasya me
a aham ātmā guḍākeśa sarvabhūtāśayasthitaḥ
c aham ādiś ca madhyaṃ ca bhūtānām anta eva ca
a ādityānām ahaṃ viṣṇur jyotiṣāṃ ravir aṃśumān
c marīcir marutām asmi nakṣatrāṇām ahaṃ śaśī
a vedānāṃ sāmavedo 'smi devānām asmi vāsavaḥ
c indriyāṇāṃ manaś cāsmi bhūtānām asmi cetanā
a rudrāṇāṃ śaṃkaraś cāsmi vitteśo yakṣarakṣasām
c vasūnāṃ pāvakaś cāsmi meruḥ śikhariṇām aham
a purodhasāṃ ca mukhyaṃ māṃ viddhi pārtha bṛhaspatim
c senānīnām ahaṃ skandaḥ sarasām asmi sāgaraḥ
a maharṣīṇāṃ bhṛgur ahaṃ girām asmy ekam akṣaram
c yajñānāṃ japayajño 'smi sthāvarāṇāṃ himālayaḥ
a aśvatthaḥ sarvavṛkṣāṇāṃ devarṣīṇāṃ ca nāradaḥ
c gandharvāṇāṃ citrarathaḥ siddhānāṃ kapilo muniḥ
a uccaiḥśravasam aśvānāṃ viddhi mām amṛtodbhavam
c airāvataṃ gajendrāṇāṃ narāṇāṃ ca narādhipam
a āyudhānām ahaṃ vajraṃ dhenūnām asmi kāmadhuk
c prajanaś cāsmi kandarpaḥ sarpāṇām asmi vāsukiḥ
a anantaś cāsmi nāgānāṃ varuṇo yādasām aham
c pitṝṇām aryamā cāsmi yamaḥ saṃyamatām aham
a prahlādaś cāsmi daityānāṃ kālaḥ kalayatām aham
c mṛgāṇāṃ ca mṛgendro 'haṃ vainateyaś ca pakṣiṇām
a pavanaḥ pavatām asmi rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtām aham
c jhaṣāṇāṃ makaraś cāsmi srotasām asmi jāhnavī
a sargāṇām ādir antaś ca madhyaṃ caivāham arjuna
c adhyātmavidyā vidyānāṃ vādaḥ pravadatām aham
a akṣarāṇām akāro 'smi dvaṃdvaḥ sāmāsikasya ca
c aham evākṣayaḥ kālo dhātāhaṃ viśvatomukhaḥ
a mṛtyuḥ sarvaharaś cāham udbhavaś ca bhaviṣyatām
c kīrtiḥ śrīr vāk ca nārīṇāṃ smṛtir medhā dhṛtiḥ kṣamā
a bṛhatsāma tathā sāmnāṃ gāyatrī chandasām aham
c māsānāṃ mārgaśīrṣo 'ham ṛtūnāṃ kusumākaraḥ
d oṣadhīnāṃ yavaś cāsmi dhātūnām asmi kāñcanam
d saurabheyo gavām asmi snehānāṃ sarpir apy aham
d sarvāsāṃ tṛṇajātīnāṃ darbho 'haṃ pāṇḍunandana
a dyūtaṃ chalayatām asmi tejas tejasvinām aham
c jayo 'smi vyavasāyo 'smi sattvaṃ sattvavatām aham
a vṛṣṇīnāṃ vāsudevo 'smi pāṇḍavānāṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c munīnām apy ahaṃ vyāsaḥ kavīnām uśanā kaviḥ
a daṇḍo damayatām asmi nītir asmi jigīṣatām
c maunaṃ caivāsmi guhyānāṃ jñānaṃ jñānavatām aham
a yac cāpi sarvabhūtānāṃ bījaṃ tad aham arjuna
c na tad asti vinā yat syān mayā bhūtaṃ carācaram
a nānto 'sti mama divyānāṃ vibhūtīnāṃ paraṃtapa
c eṣa tūddeśataḥ prokto vibhūter vistaro mayā
a yad yad vibhūtimat sattvaṃ śrīmad ūrjitam eva vā
c tat tad evāvagaccha tvaṃ mama tejoṃśasaṃbhavam
a atha vā bahunaitena kiṃ jñātena tavārjuna
c viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ kṛtsnam ekāṃśena sthito jagat
 arjuna uvāca
a madanugrahāya paramaṃ guhyam adhyātmasaṃjñitam
c yat tvayoktaṃ vacas tena moho 'yaṃ vigato mama
a bhavāpyayau hi bhūtānāṃ śrutau vistaraśo mayā
c tvattaḥ kamalapatrākṣa māhātmyam api cāvyayam
a evam etad yathāttha tvam ātmānaṃ parameśvara
c draṣṭum icchāmi te rūpam aiśvaraṃ puruṣottama
a manyase yadi tac chakyaṃ mayā draṣṭum iti prabho
c yogeśvara tato me tvaṃ darśayātmānam avyayam
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a paśya me pārtha rūpāṇi śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c nānāvidhāni divyāni nānāvarṇākṛtīni ca
a paśyādityān vasūn rudrān aśvinau marutas tathā
c bahūny adṛṣṭapūrvāṇi paśyāścaryāṇi bhārata
a ihaikasthaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ paśyādya sacarācaram
c mama dehe guḍākeśa yac cānyad draṣṭum icchasi
a na tu māṃ śakyase draṣṭum anenaiva svacakṣuṣā
c divyaṃ dadāmi te cakṣuḥ paśya me yogam aiśvaram
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam uktvā tato rājan mahāyogeśvaro hariḥ
c darśayām āsa pārthāya paramaṃ rūpam aiśvaram
a anekavaktranayanam anekādbhutadarśanam
c anekadivyābharaṇaṃ divyānekodyatāyudham
a divyamālyāmbaradharaṃ divyagandhānulepanam
c sarvāścaryamayaṃ devam anantaṃ viśvatomukham
a divi sūryasahasrasya bhaved yugapad utthitā
c yadi bhāḥ sadṛśī sā syād bhāsas tasya mahātmanaḥ
a tatraikasthaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ pravibhaktam anekadhā
c apaśyad devadevasya śarīre pāṇḍavas tadā
a tataḥ sa vismayāviṣṭo hṛṣṭaromā dhanaṃjayaḥ
c praṇamya śirasā devaṃ kṛtāñjalir abhāṣata
 arjuna uvāca
a paśyāmi devāṃs tava deva dehe
sarvāṃs tathā bhūtaviśeṣasaṃghān
c brahmāṇam īśaṃ kamalāsanastham
ṛṣīṃś ca sarvān uragāṃś ca divyān
a anekabāhūdaravaktranetraṃ
paśyāmi tvā sarvato 'nantarūpam
c nāntaṃ na madhyaṃ na punas tavādiṃ
paśyāmi viśveśvara viśvarūpa
a kirīṭinaṃ gadinaṃ cakriṇaṃ ca
tejorāśiṃ sarvato dīptimantam
c paśyāmi tvāṃ durnirīkṣyaṃ samantād
dīptānalārkadyutim aprameyam
a tvam akṣaraṃ paramaṃ veditavyaṃ
tvam asya viśvasya paraṃ nidhānam
c tvam avyayaḥ śāśvatadharmagoptā
sanātanas tvaṃ puruṣo mato me
a anādimadhyāntam anantavīryam
anantabāhuṃ śaśisūryanetram
c paśyāmi tvāṃ dīptahutāśavaktraṃ
svatejasā viśvam idaṃ tapantam
a dyāvāpṛthivyor idam antaraṃ hi
vyāptaṃ tvayaikena diśaś ca sarvāḥ
c dṛṣṭvādbhutaṃ rūpam idaṃ tavograṃ
lokatrayaṃ pravyathitaṃ mahātman
a amī hi tvā surasaṃghā viśanti
ke cid bhītāḥ prāñjalayo gṛṇanti
c svastīty uktvā maharṣisiddhasaṃghāḥ
stuvanti tvāṃ stutibhiḥ puṣkalābhiḥ
a rudrādityā vasavo ye ca sādhyā
viśve 'śvinau marutaś coṣmapāś ca
c gandharvayakṣāsurasiddhasaṃghā
vīkṣante tvā vismitāś caiva sarve
a rūpaṃ mahat te bahuvaktranetraṃ
mahābāho bahubāhūrupādam
c bahūdaraṃ bahudaṃṣṭrākarālaṃ
dṛṣṭvā lokāḥ pravyathitās tathāham
a nabhaḥspṛśaṃ dīptam anekavarṇaṃ
vyāttānanaṃ dīptaviśālanetram
c dṛṣṭvā hi tvāṃ pravyathitāntarātmā
dhṛtiṃ na vindāmi śamaṃ ca viṣṇo
a daṃṣṭrākarālāni ca te mukhāni
dṛṣṭvaiva kālānalasaṃnibhāni
c diśo na jāne na labhe ca śarma
prasīda deveśa jagannivāsa
a amī ca tvāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥ
sarve sahaivāvanipālasaṃghaiḥ
c bhīṣmo droṇaḥ sūtaputras tathāsau
sahāsmadīyair api yodhamukhyaiḥ
a vaktrāṇi te tvaramāṇā viśanti
daṃṣṭrākarālāni bhayānakāni
b sahasrasūryātasaṃnibhāni
b tathā jagadgrāsakṛtakṣaṇāni
b nānārūpaiḥ puruṣair vadhyamānā
b viśanti te vaktram acintyarūpam
b yaudhiṣṭhirā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca yodhāḥ
b śastraiḥ kṛttā vividhaiḥ sarva eva
b tvattejasā nihatā nūnam ete
b tathā hīme tvaccharīraṃ praviṣṭāḥ
c ke cid vilagnā daśanāntareṣu
saṃdṛśyante cūrṇitair uttamāṅgaiḥ
a yathā nadīnāṃ bahavo 'mbuvegāḥ
samudram evābhimukhā dravanti
c tathā tavāmī naralokavīrā
viśanti vaktrāṇy abhivijvalanti
a yathā pradīptaṃ jvalanaṃ pataṃgā
viśanti nāśāya samṛddhavegāḥ
c tathaiva nāśāya viśanti lokās
tavāpi vaktrāṇi samṛddhavegāḥ
a lelihyase grasamānaḥ samantāl
lokān samagrān vadanair jvaladbhiḥ
c tejobhir āpūrya jagat samagraṃ
bhāsas tavogrāḥ pratapanti viṣṇo
a ākhyāhi me ko bhavān ugrarūpo
namo 'stu te devavara prasīda
c vijñātum icchāmi bhavantam ādyaṃ
na hi prajānāmi tava pravṛttim
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a kālo 'smi lokakṣayakṛt pravṛddho
lokān samāhartum iha pravṛttaḥ
c ṛte 'pi tvā na bhaviṣyanti sarve
ye 'vasthitāḥ pratyanīkeṣu yodhāḥ
a tasmāt tvam uttiṣṭha yaśo labhasva
jitvā śatrūn bhuṅkṣva rājyaṃ samṛddham
c mayaivaite nihatāḥ pūrvam eva
nimittamātraṃ bhava savyasācin
a droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca jayadrathaṃ ca
karṇaṃ tathānyān api yodhavīrān
c mayā hatāṃs tvaṃ jahi mā vyathiṣṭhā
yudhyasva jetāsi raṇe sapatnān
 saṃjaya uvāca
a etac chrutvā vacanaṃ keśavasya
kṛtāñjalir vepamānaḥ kirīṭī
c namaskṛtvā bhūya evāha kṛṣṇaṃ
sagadgadaṃ bhītabhītaḥ praṇamya
 arjuna uvāca
a sthāne hṛṣīkeśa tava prakīrtyā
jagat prahṛṣyaty anurajyate ca
c rakṣāṃsi bhītāni diśo dravanti
sarve namasyanti ca siddhasaṃghāḥ
a kasmāc ca te na nameran mahātman
garīyase brahmaṇo 'py ādikartre
c ananta deveśa jagannivāsa
tvam akṣaraṃ sad asat tatparaṃ yat
a tvam ādidevaḥ puruṣaḥ purāṇas
tvam asya viśvasya paraṃ nidhānam
c vettāsi vedyaṃ ca paraṃ ca dhāma
tvayā tataṃ viśvam anantarūpa
a vāyur yamo 'gnir varuṇaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ
prajāpatis tvaṃ prapitāmahaś ca
c namo namas te 'stu sahasrakṛtvaḥ
punaś ca bhūyo 'pi namo namas te
d anādimān apratimaprabhāvaḥ
d sarveśvaraḥ sarvamahāvibhūte
a namaḥ purastād atha pṛṣṭhatas te
namo 'stu te sarvata eva sarva
b na hi tvad anyaḥ kaś cid apīha deva
b lokatraye dṛśyate 'cintyakarmā
c anantavīryāmitavikramas tvaṃ
sarvaṃ samāpnoṣi tato 'si sarvaḥ
a sakheti matvā prasabhaṃ yad uktaṃ
he kṛṣṇa he yādava he sakheti
c ajānatā mahimānaṃ tavedaṃ
mayā pramādāt praṇayena vāpi
a yac cāvahāsārtham asatkṛto 'si
vihāraśayyāsanabhojaneṣu
c eko 'tha vāpy acyuta tatsamakṣaṃ
tat kṣāmaye tvām aham aprameyam
a pitāsi lokasya carācarasya
tvam asya pūjyaś ca gurur garīyān
c na tvatsamo 'sty abhyadhikaḥ kuto 'nyo
lokatraye 'py apratimaprabhāva
a tasmāt praṇamya praṇidhāya kāyaṃ
prasādaye tvām aham īśam īḍyam
c piteva putrasya sakheva sakhyuḥ
priyaḥ priyāyārhasi deva soḍhum
d divyāni karmāṇi tavādbhutāni
d pūrvāṇi pūrve 'py ṛṣayaḥ smaranti
d nānyo 'sti kartā jagatas tvam eko
d dhātā vidhātā ca vibhur bhavaś ca
d tavādbhutaṃ kiṃ nu bhaved asahyaṃ
d kiṃ vāśakyaṃ parataḥ kīrtayiṣye
d kartāsi sarvasya yataḥ svayaṃ vai
d vibho tataḥ sarvam idaṃ tvam eva
d aty adbhutaṃ karma na duṣkaraṃ te
d karmopamānaṃ na hi vidyate te
d na te guṇānāṃ parimāṇam asti
d na tejaso nāpi balasya narddheḥ
d imāni karmāṇi tavādbhutāni
d kṛtāni pūrve munayo vadanti
d na te guṇānāṃ parimāṇam asti
d na tejasaś cāpi balasya viṣṇo
a adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ hṛṣito 'smi dṛṣṭvā
bhayena ca pravyathitaṃ mano me
c tad eva me darśaya deva rūpaṃ
prasīda deveśa jagannivāsa
a kirīṭinaṃ gadinaṃ cakrahastam
icchāmi tvāṃ draṣṭum ahaṃ tathaiva
c tenaiva rūpeṇa caturbhujena
sahasrabāho bhava viśvamūrte
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a mayā prasannena tavārjunedaṃ
rūpaṃ paraṃ darśitam ātmayogāt
c tejomayaṃ viśvam anantam ādyaṃ
yan me tvad anyena na dṛṣṭapūrvam
a na vedayajñādhyayanair na dānair
na ca kriyābhir na tapobhir ugraiḥ
c evaṃrūpaḥ śakya ahaṃ nṛloke
draṣṭuṃ tvad anyena kurupravīra
a mā te vyathā mā ca vimūḍhabhāvo
dṛṣṭvā rūpaṃ ghoram īdṛṅ mamedam
c vyapetabhīḥ prītamanāḥ punas tvaṃ
tad eva me rūpam idaṃ prapaśya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity arjunaṃ vāsudevas tathoktvā
svakaṃ rūpaṃ darśayām āsa bhūyaḥ
c āśvāsayām āsa ca bhītam enaṃ
bhūtvā punaḥ saumyavapur mahātmā
 arjuna uvāca
a dṛṣṭvedaṃ mānuṣaṃ rūpaṃ tava saumyaṃ janārdana
c idānīm asmi saṃvṛttaḥ sacetāḥ prakṛtiṃ gataḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a sudurdarśam idaṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭavān asi yan mama
c devā apy asya rūpasya nityaṃ darśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a nāhaṃ vedair na tapasā na dānena na cejyayā
c śakya evaṃvidho draṣṭuṃ dṛṣṭavān asi māṃ yathā
a bhaktyā tv ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidho 'rjuna
c jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣṭuṃ ca paraṃtapa
a matkarmakṛn matparamo madbhaktaḥ saṅgavarjitaḥ
c nirvairaḥ sarvabhūteṣu yaḥ sa mām eti pāṇḍava
 arjuna uvāca
a evaṃ satatayuktā ye bhaktās tvāṃ paryupāsate
c ye cāpy akṣaram avyaktaṃ teṣāṃ ke yogavittamāḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a mayy āveśya mano ye māṃ nityayuktā upāsate
c śraddhayā parayopetās te me yuktatamā matāḥ
a ye tv akṣaram anirdeśyam avyaktaṃ paryupāsate
c sarvatragam acintyaṃ ca kūṭastham acalaṃ dhruvam
a saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ sarvatra samabuddhayaḥ
c te prāpnuvanti mām eva sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
a kleśo 'dhikataras teṣām avyaktāsaktacetasām
c avyaktā hi gatir duḥkhaṃ dehavadbhir avāpyate
a ye tu sarvāṇi karmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya matparāḥ
c ananyenaiva yogena māṃ dhyāyanta upāsate
a teṣām ahaṃ samuddhartā mṛtyusaṃsārasāgarāt
c bhavāmi nacirāt pārtha mayy āveśitacetasām
a mayy eva mana ādhatsva mayi buddhiṃ niveśaya
c nivasiṣyasi mayy eva ata ūrdhvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
a atha cittaṃ samādhātuṃ na śaknoṣi mayi sthiram
c abhyāsayogena tato mām icchāptuṃ dhanaṃjaya
a abhyāse 'py asamartho 'si matkarmaparamo bhava
c madartham api karmāṇi kurvan siddhim avāpsyasi
a athaitad apy aśakto 'si kartuṃ madyogam āśritaḥ
c sarvakarmaphalatyāgaṃ tataḥ kuru yatātmavān
a śreyo hi jñānam abhyāsāj jñānād dhyānaṃ viśiṣyate
c dhyānāt karmaphalatyāgas tyāgāc chāntir anantaram
a adveṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ maitraḥ karuṇa eva ca
c nirmamo nirahaṃkāraḥ samaduḥkhasukhaḥ kṣamī
a saṃtuṣṭaḥ satataṃ yogī yatātmā dṛḍhaniścayaḥ
c mayy arpitamanobuddhir yo madbhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ
a yasmān nodvijate loko lokān nodvijate ca yaḥ
c harṣāmarṣabhayodvegair mukto yaḥ sa ca me priyaḥ
a anapekṣaḥ śucir dakṣa udāsīno gatavyathaḥ
c sarvārambhaparityāgī yo madbhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ
a yo na hṛṣyati na dveṣṭi na śocati na kāṅkṣati
c śubhāśubhaparityāgī bhaktimān yaḥ sa me priyaḥ
a samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā mānāvamānayoḥ
c śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkheṣu samaḥ saṅgavivarjitaḥ
a tulyanindāstutir maunī saṃtuṣṭo yena kena cit
c aniketaḥ sthiramatir bhaktimān me priyo naraḥ
a ye tu dharmyāmṛtam idaṃ yathoktaṃ paryupāsate
c śraddadhānā matparamā bhaktās te 'tīva me priyāḥ
 arjuna uvāca
 prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva kṣetraṃ kṣetrajñam eva ca
 etad veditum icchāmi jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ ca keśava
 śrībhagavān uvāca
 prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva kṣetraṃ kṣetrajñam eva ca
 etat te kathayiṣyāmi jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ ca bhārata
a idaṃ śarīraṃ kaunteya kṣetram ity abhidhīyate
c etad yo vetti taṃ prāhuḥ kṣetrajña iti tadvidaḥ
a kṣetrajñaṃ cāpi māṃ viddhi sarvakṣetreṣu bhārata
c kṣetrakṣetrajñayor jñānaṃ yat taj jñānaṃ mataṃ mama
a tat kṣetraṃ yac ca yādṛk ca yadvikāri yataś ca yat
c sa ca yo yatprabhāvaś ca tat samāsena me śṛṇu
a ṛṣibhir bahudhā gītaṃ chandobhir vividhaiḥ pṛthak
c brahmasūtrapadaiś caiva hetumadbhir viniścitaiḥ
a mahābhūtāny ahaṃkāro buddhir avyaktam eva ca
c indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca pañca cendriyagocarāḥ
a icchā dveṣaḥ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ saṃghātaś cetanā dhṛtiḥ
c etat kṣetraṃ samāsena savikāram udāhṛtam
a amānitvam adambhitvam ahiṃsā kṣāntir ārjavam
c ācāryopāsanaṃ śaucaṃ sthairyam ātmavinigrahaḥ
a indriyārtheṣu vairāgyam anahaṃkāra eva ca
c janmamṛtyujarāvyādhiduḥkhadoṣānudarśanam
a asaktir anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ putradāragṛhādiṣu
c nityaṃ ca samacittatvam iṣṭāniṣṭopapattiṣu
a mayi cānanyayogena bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī
c viviktadeśasevitvam aratir janasaṃsadi
a adhyātmajñānanityatvaṃ tattvajñānārthadarśanam
c etaj jñānam iti proktam ajñānaṃ yad ato 'nyathā
a jñeyaṃ yat tat pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvāmṛtam aśnute
c anādimat paraṃ brahma na sat tan nāsad ucyate
a sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tat sarvatokṣiśiromukham
c sarvataḥśrutimal loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
a sarvendriyaguṇābhāsaṃ sarvendriyavivarjitam
c asaktaṃ sarvabhṛc caiva nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ ca
a bahir antaś ca bhūtānām acaraṃ caram eva ca
c sūkṣmatvāt tad avijñeyaṃ dūrasthaṃ cāntike ca tat
a avibhaktaṃ ca bhūteṣu vibhaktam iva ca sthitam
c bhūtabhartṛ ca taj jñeyaṃ grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca
a jyotiṣām api taj jyotis tamasaḥ param ucyate
c jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānagamyaṃ hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitam
a iti kṣetraṃ tathā jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ coktaṃ samāsataḥ
c madbhakta etad vijñāya madbhāvāyopapadyate
a prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva viddhy anādī ubhāv api
c vikārāṃś ca guṇāṃś caiva viddhi prakṛtisaṃbhavān
a kāryakāraṇakartṛtve hetuḥ prakṛtir ucyate
c puruṣaḥ sukhaduḥkhānāṃ bhoktṛtve hetur ucyate
a puruṣaḥ prakṛtistho hi bhuṅkte prakṛtijān guṇān
c kāraṇaṃ guṇasaṅgo 'sya sadasadyonijanmasu
a upadraṣṭānumantā ca bhartā bhoktā maheśvaraḥ
c paramātmeti cāpy ukto dehe 'smin puruṣaḥ paraḥ
a ya evaṃ vetti puruṣaṃ prakṛtiṃ ca guṇaiḥ saha
c sarvathā vartamāno 'pi na sa bhūyo 'bhijāyate
a dhyānenātmani paśyanti ke cid ātmānam ātmanā
c anye sāṃkhyena yogena karmayogena cāpare
a anye tv evam ajānantaḥ śrutvānyebhya upāsate
c te 'pi cātitaranty eva mṛtyuṃ śrutiparāyaṇāḥ
a yāvat saṃjāyate kiṃ cit sattvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam
c kṣetrakṣetrajñasaṃyogāt tad viddhi bharatarṣabha
a samaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantaṃ parameśvaram
c vinaśyatsv avinaśyantaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati
a samaṃ paśyan hi sarvatra samavasthitam īśvaram
c na hinasty ātmanātmānaṃ tato yāti parāṃ gatim
a prakṛtyaiva ca karmāṇi kriyamāṇāni sarvaśaḥ
c yaḥ paśyati tathātmānam akartāraṃ sa paśyati
a yadā bhūtapṛthagbhāvam ekastham anupaśyati
c tata eva ca vistāraṃ brahma saṃpadyate tadā
a anāditvān nirguṇatvāt paramātmāyam avyayaḥ
c śarīrastho 'pi kaunteya na karoti na lipyate
a yathā sarvagataṃ saukṣmyād ākāśaṃ nopalipyate
c sarvatrāvasthito dehe tathātmā nopalipyate
a yathā prakāśayaty ekaḥ kṛtsnaṃ lokam imaṃ raviḥ
c kṣetraṃ kṣetrī tathā kṛtsnaṃ prakāśayati bhārata
a kṣetrakṣetrajñayor evam antaraṃ jñānacakṣuṣā
c bhūtaprakṛtimokṣaṃ ca ye vidur yānti te param
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a paraṃ bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi jñānānāṃ jñānam uttamam
c yaj jñātvā munayaḥ sarve parāṃ siddhim ito gatāḥ
a idaṃ jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ
c sarge 'pi nopajāyante pralaye na vyathanti ca
a mama yonir mahad brahma tasmin garbhaṃ dadhāmy aham
c saṃbhavaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tato bhavati bhārata
a sarvayoniṣu kaunteya mūrtayaḥ saṃbhavanti yāḥ
c tāsāṃ brahma mahad yonir ahaṃ bījapradaḥ pitā
a sattvaṃ rajas tama iti guṇāḥ prakṛtisaṃbhavāḥ
c nibadhnanti mahābāho dehe dehinam avyayam
a tatra sattvaṃ nirmalatvāt prakāśakam anāmayam
c sukhasaṅgena badhnāti jñānasaṅgena cānagha
a rajo rāgātmakaṃ viddhi tṛṣṇāsaṅgasamudbhavam
c tan nibadhnāti kaunteya karmasaṅgena dehinam
a tamas tv ajñānajaṃ viddhi mohanaṃ sarvadehinām
c pramādālasyanidrābhis tan nibadhnāti bhārata
a sattvaṃ sukhe sañjayati rajaḥ karmaṇi bhārata
c jñānam āvṛtya tu tamaḥ pramāde sañjayaty uta
a rajas tamaś cābhibhūya sattvaṃ bhavati bhārata
c rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamaś caiva tamaḥ sattvaṃ rajas tathā
a sarvadvāreṣu dehe 'smin prakāśa upajāyate
c jñānaṃ yadā tadā vidyād vivṛddhaṃ sattvam ity uta
a lobhaḥ pravṛttir ārambhaḥ karmaṇām aśamaḥ spṛhā
c rajasy etāni jāyante vivṛddhe bharatarṣabha
a aprakāśo 'pravṛttiś ca pramādo moha eva ca
c tamasy etāni jāyante vivṛddhe kurunandana
a yadā sattve pravṛddhe tu pralayaṃ yāti dehabhṛt
c tadottamavidāṃ lokān amalān pratipadyate
a rajasi pralayaṃ gatvā karmasaṅgiṣu jāyate
c tathā pralīnas tamasi mūḍhayoniṣu jāyate
a karmaṇaḥ sukṛtasyāhuḥ sāttvikaṃ nirmalaṃ phalam
c rajasas tu phalaṃ duḥkham ajñānaṃ tamasaḥ phalam
a sattvāt saṃjāyate jñānaṃ rajaso lobha eva ca
c pramādamohau tamaso bhavato 'jñānam eva ca
a ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti sattvasthā madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥ
c jaghanyaguṇavṛttasthā adho gacchanti tāmasāḥ
a nānyaṃ guṇebhyaḥ kartāraṃ yadā draṣṭānupaśyati
c guṇebhyaś ca paraṃ vetti madbhāvaṃ so 'dhigacchati
a guṇān etān atītya trīn dehī dehasamudbhavān
c janmamṛtyujarāduḥkhair vimukto 'mṛtam aśnute
 arjuna uvāca
a kair liṅgais trīn guṇān etān atīto bhavati prabho
c kimācāraḥ kathaṃ caitāṃs trīn guṇān ativartate
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a prakāśaṃ ca pravṛttiṃ ca moham eva ca pāṇḍava
c na dveṣṭi saṃpravṛttāni na nivṛttāni kāṅkṣati
a udāsīnavad āsīno guṇair yo na vicālyate
c guṇā vartanta ity eva yo 'vatiṣṭhati neṅgate
a samaduḥkhasukhaḥ svasthaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ
c tulyapriyāpriyo dhīras tulyanindātmasaṃstutiḥ
a mānāvamānayos tulyas tulyo mitrāripakṣayoḥ
c sarvārambhaparityāgī guṇātītaḥ sa ucyate
a māṃ ca yo 'vyabhicāreṇa bhaktiyogena sevate
c sa guṇān samatītyaitān brahmabhūyāya kalpate
a brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāham amṛtasyāvyayasya ca
c śāśvatasya ca dharmasya sukhasyaikāntikasya ca
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a ūrdhvamūlam adhaḥśākham aśvatthaṃ prāhur avyayam
c chandāṃsi yasya parṇāni yas taṃ veda sa vedavit
a adhaś cordhvaṃ prasṛtās tasya śākhā
guṇapravṛddhā viṣayapravālāḥ
c adhaś ca mūlāny anusaṃtatāni
karmānubandhīni manuṣyaloke
a na rūpam asyeha tathopalabhyate
nānto na cādir na ca saṃpratiṣṭhā
c aśvattham enaṃ suvirūḍhamūlam
asaṅgaśastreṇa dṛḍhena chittvā
a tataḥ padaṃ tatparimārgitavyaṃ
yasmin gatā na nivartanti bhūyaḥ
c tam eva cādyaṃ puruṣaṃ prapadye
yataḥ pravṛttiḥ prasṛtā purāṇī
a nirmānamohā jitasaṅgadoṣā
adhyātmanityā vinivṛttakāmāḥ
c dvaṃdvair vimuktāḥ sukhaduḥkhasaṃjñair
gacchanty amūḍhāḥ padam avyayaṃ tat
a na tad bhāsayate sūryo na śaśāṅko na pāvakaḥ
c yad gatvā na nivartante tad dhāma paramaṃ mama
a mamaivāṃśo jīvaloke jīvabhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ
c manaḥṣaṣṭhānīndriyāṇi prakṛtisthāni karṣati
a śarīraṃ yad avāpnoti yac cāpy utkrāmatīśvaraḥ
c gṛhītvaitāni saṃyāti vāyur gandhān ivāśayāt
a śrotraṃ cakṣuḥ sparśanaṃ ca rasanaṃ ghrāṇam eva ca
c adhiṣṭhāya manaś cāyaṃ viṣayān upasevate
a utkrāmantaṃ sthitaṃ vāpi bhuñjānaṃ vā guṇānvitam
c vimūḍhā nānupaśyanti paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥ
a yatanto yoginaś cainaṃ paśyanty ātmany avasthitam
c yatanto 'py akṛtātmāno nainaṃ paśyanty acetasaḥ
a yad ādityagataṃ tejo jagad bhāsayate 'khilam
c yac candramasi yac cāgnau tat tejo viddhi māmakam
a gām āviśya ca bhūtāni dhārayāmy aham ojasā
c puṣṇāmi cauṣadhīḥ sarvāḥ somo bhūtvā rasātmakaḥ
a ahaṃ vaiśvānaro bhūtvā prāṇināṃ deham āśritaḥ
c prāṇāpānasamāyuktaḥ pacāmy annaṃ caturvidham
a sarvasya cāhaṃ hṛdi saṃniviṣṭo
mattaḥ smṛtir jñānam apohanaṃ ca
c vedaiś ca sarvair aham eva vedyo
vedāntakṛd vedavid eva cāham
a dvāv imau puruṣau loke kṣaraś cākṣara eva ca
c kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭastho 'kṣara ucyate
a uttamaḥ puruṣas tv anyaḥ paramātmety udāhṛtaḥ
c yo lokatrayam āviśya bibharty avyaya īśvaraḥ
a yasmāt kṣaram atīto 'ham akṣarād api cottamaḥ
c ato 'smi loke vede ca prathitaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
a yo mām evam asaṃmūḍho jānāti puruṣottamam
c sa sarvavid bhajati māṃ sarvabhāvena bhārata
a iti guhyatamaṃ śāstram idam uktaṃ mayānagha
c etad buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaś ca bhārata
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a abhayaṃ sattvasaṃśuddhir jñānayogavyavasthitiḥ
c dānaṃ damaś ca yajñaś ca svādhyāyas tapa ārjavam
a ahiṃsā satyam akrodhas tyāgaḥ śāntir apaiśunam
c dayā bhūteṣv aloluptvaṃ mārdavaṃ hrīr acāpalam
a tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucam adroho nātimānitā
c bhavanti saṃpadaṃ daivīm abhijātasya bhārata
a dambho darpo 'timānaś ca krodhaḥ pāruṣyam eva ca
c ajñānaṃ cābhijātasya pārtha saṃpadam āsurīm
a daivī saṃpad vimokṣāya nibandhāyāsurī matā
c mā śucaḥ saṃpadaṃ daivīm abhijāto 'si pāṇḍava
a dvau bhūtasargau loke 'smin daiva āsura eva ca
c daivo vistaraśaḥ prokta āsuraṃ pārtha me śṛṇu
a pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca janā na vidur āsurāḥ
c na śaucaṃ nāpi cācāro na satyaṃ teṣu vidyate
a asatyam apratiṣṭhaṃ te jagad āhur anīśvaram
c aparasparasaṃbhūtaṃ kim anyat kāmahaitukam
a etāṃ dṛṣṭim avaṣṭabhya naṣṭātmāno 'lpabuddhayaḥ
c prabhavanty ugrakarmāṇaḥ kṣayāya jagato 'hitāḥ
a kāmam āśritya duṣpūraṃ dambhamānamadānvitāḥ
c mohād gṛhītvāsadgrāhān pravartante 'śucivratāḥ
a cintām aparimeyāṃ ca pralayāntām upāśritāḥ
c kāmopabhogaparamā etāvad iti niścitāḥ
a āśāpāśaśatair baddhāḥ kāmakrodhaparāyaṇāḥ
c īhante kāmabhogārtham anyāyenārthasaṃcayān
a idam adya mayā labdham idaṃ prāpsye manoratham
c idam astīdam api me bhaviṣyati punar dhanam
a asau mayā hataḥ śatrur haniṣye cāparān api
c īśvaro 'ham ahaṃ bhogī siddho 'haṃ balavān sukhī
a āḍhyo 'bhijanavān asmi ko 'nyo 'sti sadṛśo mayā
c yakṣye dāsyāmi modiṣya ity ajñānavimohitāḥ
a anekacittavibhrāntā mohajālasamāvṛtāḥ
c prasaktāḥ kāmabhogeṣu patanti narake 'śucau
a ātmasaṃbhāvitāḥ stabdhā dhanamānamadānvitāḥ
c yajante nāmayajñais te dambhenāvidhipūrvakam
a ahaṃkāraṃ balaṃ darpaṃ kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca saṃśritāḥ
c mām ātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto 'bhyasūyakāḥ
a tān ahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamān
c kṣipāmy ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣv eva yoniṣu
a āsurīṃ yonim āpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani
c mām aprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yānty adhamāṃ gatim
a trividhaṃ narakasyedaṃ dvāraṃ nāśanam ātmanaḥ
c kāmaḥ krodhas tathā lobhas tasmād etat trayaṃ tyajet
a etair vimuktaḥ kaunteya tamodvārais tribhir naraḥ
c ācaraty ātmanaḥ śreyas tato yāti parāṃ gatim
a yaḥ śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ
c na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatim
a tasmāc chāstraṃ pramāṇaṃ te kāryākāryavyavasthitau
c jñātvā śāstravidhānoktaṃ karma kartum ihārhasi
 arjuna uvāca
a ye śāstravidhim utsṛjya yajante śraddhayānvitāḥ
c teṣāṃ niṣṭhā tu kā kṛṣṇa sattvam āho rajas tamaḥ
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a trividhā bhavati śraddhā dehināṃ sā svabhāvajā
c sāttvikī rājasī caiva tāmasī ceti tāṃ śṛṇu
a sattvānurūpā sarvasya śraddhā bhavati bhārata
c śraddhāmayo 'yaṃ puruṣo yo yacchraddhaḥ sa eva saḥ
a yajante sāttvikā devān yakṣarakṣāṃsi rājasāḥ
c pretān bhūtagaṇāṃś cānye yajante tāmasā janāḥ
a aśāstravihitaṃ ghoraṃ tapyante ye tapo janāḥ
c dambhāhaṃkārasaṃyuktāḥ kāmarāgabalānvitāḥ
a karśayantaḥ śarīrasthaṃ bhūtagrāmam acetasaḥ
c māṃ caivāntaḥśarīrasthaṃ tān viddhy āsuraniścayān
a āhāras tv api sarvasya trividho bhavati priyaḥ
c yajñas tapas tathā dānaṃ teṣāṃ bhedam imaṃ śṛṇu
a āyuḥsattvabalārogyasukhaprītivivardhanāḥ
c rasyāḥ snigdhāḥ sthirā hṛdyā āhārāḥ sāttvikapriyāḥ
a kaṭvamlalavaṇātyuṣṇatīkṣṇarūkṣavidāhinaḥ
c āhārā rājasasyeṣṭā duḥkhaśokāmayapradāḥ
a yātayāmaṃ gatarasaṃ pūti paryuṣitaṃ ca yat
c ucchiṣṭam api cāmedhyaṃ bhojanaṃ tāmasapriyam
a aphalākāṅkṣibhir yajño vidhidṛṣṭo ya ijyate
c yaṣṭavyam eveti manaḥ samādhāya sa sāttvikaḥ
a abhisaṃdhāya tu phalaṃ dambhārtham api caiva yat
c ijyate bharataśreṣṭha taṃ yajñaṃ viddhi rājasam
a vidhihīnam asṛṣṭānnaṃ mantrahīnam adakṣiṇam
c śraddhāvirahitaṃ yajñaṃ tāmasaṃ paricakṣate
a devadvijaguruprājñapūjanaṃ śaucam ārjavam
c brahmacaryam ahiṃsā ca śārīraṃ tapa ucyate
a anudvegakaraṃ vākyaṃ satyaṃ priyahitaṃ ca yat
c svādhyāyābhyasanaṃ caiva vāṅmayaṃ tapa ucyate
a manaḥprasādaḥ saumyatvaṃ maunam ātmavinigrahaḥ
c bhāvasaṃśuddhir ity etat tapo mānasam ucyate
a śraddhayā parayā taptaṃ tapas tat trividhaṃ naraiḥ
c aphalākāṅkṣibhir yuktaiḥ sāttvikaṃ paricakṣate
a satkāramānapūjārthaṃ tapo dambhena caiva yat
c kriyate tad iha proktaṃ rājasaṃ calam adhruvam
a mūḍhagrāheṇātmano yat pīḍayā kriyate tapaḥ
c parasyotsādanārthaṃ vā tat tāmasam udāhṛtam
a dātavyam iti yad dānaṃ dīyate 'nupakāriṇe
c deśe kāle ca pātre ca tad dānaṃ sāttvikaṃ smṛtam
a yat tu pratyupakārārthaṃ phalam uddiśya vā punaḥ
c dīyate ca parikliṣṭaṃ tad dānaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtam
a adeśakāle yad dānam apātrebhyaś ca dīyate
c asatkṛtam avajñātaṃ tat tāmasam udāhṛtam
a oṃ tat sad iti nirdeśo brahmaṇas trividhaḥ smṛtaḥ
c brāhmaṇās tena vedāś ca yajñāś ca vihitāḥ purā
a tasmād om ity udāhṛtya yajñadānatapaḥkriyāḥ
c pravartante vidhānoktāḥ satataṃ brahmavādinām
a tad ity anabhisaṃdhāya phalaṃ yajñatapaḥkriyāḥ
c dānakriyāś ca vividhāḥ kriyante mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥ
a sadbhāve sādhubhāve ca sad ity etat prayujyate
c praśaste karmaṇi tathā sacchabdaḥ pārtha yujyate
a yajñe tapasi dāne ca sthitiḥ sad iti cocyate
c karma caiva tadarthīyaṃ sad ity evābhidhīyate
a aśraddhayā hutaṃ dattaṃ tapas taptaṃ kṛtaṃ ca yat
c asad ity ucyate pārtha na ca tat pretya no iha
 arjuna uvāca
a saṃnyāsasya mahābāho tattvam icchāmi veditum
c tyāgasya ca hṛṣīkeśa pṛthak keśiniṣūdana
 śrībhagavān uvāca
a kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaṃ saṃnyāsaṃ kavayo viduḥ
c sarvakarmaphalatyāgaṃ prāhus tyāgaṃ vicakṣaṇāḥ
a tyājyaṃ doṣavad ity eke karma prāhur manīṣiṇaḥ
c yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyam iti cāpare
a niścayaṃ śṛṇu me tatra tyāge bharatasattama
c tyāgo hi puruṣavyāghra trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ
a yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyaṃ kāryam eva tat
c yajño dānaṃ tapaś caiva pāvanāni manīṣiṇām
a etāny api tu karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā phalāni ca
c kartavyānīti me pārtha niścitaṃ matam uttamam
a niyatasya tu saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇo nopapadyate
c mohāt tasya parityāgas tāmasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
a duḥkham ity eva yat karma kāyakleśabhayāt tyajet
c sa kṛtvā rājasaṃ tyāgaṃ naiva tyāgaphalaṃ labhet
a kāryam ity eva yat karma niyataṃ kriyate 'rjuna
c saṅgaṃ tyaktvā phalaṃ caiva sa tyāgaḥ sāttviko mataḥ
a na dveṣṭy akuśalaṃ karma kuśale nānuṣajjate
c tyāgī sattvasamāviṣṭo medhāvī chinnasaṃśayaḥ
a na hi dehabhṛtā śakyaṃ tyaktuṃ karmāṇy aśeṣataḥ
c yas tu karmaphalatyāgī sa tyāgīty abhidhīyate
a aniṣṭam iṣṭaṃ miśraṃ ca trividhaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam
c bhavaty atyāgināṃ pretya na tu saṃnyāsināṃ kva cit
a pañcaitāni mahābāho kāraṇāni nibodha me
c sāṃkhye kṛtānte proktāni siddhaye sarvakarmaṇām
a adhiṣṭhānaṃ tathā kartā karaṇaṃ ca pṛthagvidham
c vividhāś ca pṛthakceṣṭā daivaṃ caivātra pañcamam
a śarīravāṅmanobhir yat karma prārabhate naraḥ
c nyāyyaṃ vā viparītaṃ vā pañcaite tasya hetavaḥ
a tatraivaṃ sati kartāram ātmānaṃ kevalaṃ tu yaḥ
c paśyaty akṛtabuddhitvān na sa paśyati durmatiḥ
a yasya nāhaṃkṛto bhāvo buddhir yasya na lipyate
c hatvāpi sa imāṃl lokān na hanti na nibadhyate
a jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ parijñātā trividhā karmacodanā
c karaṇaṃ karma karteti trividhaḥ karmasaṃgrahaḥ
a jñānaṃ karma ca kartā ca tridhaiva guṇabhedataḥ
c procyate guṇasaṃkhyāne yathāvac chṛṇu tāny api
a sarvabhūteṣu yenaikaṃ bhāvam avyayam īkṣate
c avibhaktaṃ vibhakteṣu taj jñānaṃ viddhi sāttvikam
a pṛthaktvena tu yaj jñānaṃ nānābhāvān pṛthagvidhān
c vetti sarveṣu bhūteṣu taj jñānaṃ viddhi rājasam
a yat tu kṛtsnavad ekasmin kārye saktam ahaitukam
c atattvārthavad alpaṃ ca tat tāmasam udāhṛtam
a niyataṃ saṅgarahitam arāgadveṣataḥ kṛtam
c aphalaprepsunā karma yat tat sāttvikam ucyate
a yat tu kāmepsunā karma sāhaṃkāreṇa vā punaḥ
c kriyate bahulāyāsaṃ tad rājasam udāhṛtam
a anubandhaṃ kṣayaṃ hiṃsām anapekṣya ca pauruṣam
c mohād ārabhyate karma yat tat tāmasam ucyate
a muktasaṅgo 'nahaṃvādī dhṛtyutsāhasamanvitaḥ
c siddhyasiddhyor nirvikāraḥ kartā sāttvika ucyate
a rāgī karmaphalaprepsur lubdho hiṃsātmako 'śuciḥ
c harṣaśokānvitaḥ kartā rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
a ayuktaḥ prākṛtaḥ stabdhaḥ śaṭho naikṛtiko 'lasaḥ
c viṣādī dīrghasūtrī ca kartā tāmasa ucyate
a buddher bhedaṃ dhṛteś caiva guṇatas trividhaṃ śṛṇu
c procyamānam aśeṣeṇa pṛthaktvena dhanaṃjaya
a pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca kāryākārye bhayābhaye
c bandhaṃ mokṣaṃ ca yā vetti buddhiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī
a yayā dharmam adharmaṃ ca kāryaṃ cākāryam eva ca
c ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ sā pārtha rājasī
a adharmaṃ dharmam iti yā manyate tamasāvṛtā
c sarvārthān viparītāṃś ca buddhiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī
a dhṛtyā yayā dhārayate manaḥprāṇendriyakriyāḥ
c yogenāvyabhicāriṇyā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī
a yayā tu dharmakāmārthān dhṛtyā dhārayate 'rjuna
c prasaṅgena phalākāṅkṣī dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha rājasī
a yayā svapnaṃ bhayaṃ śokaṃ viṣādaṃ madam eva ca
c na vimuñcati durmedhā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī
a sukhaṃ tv idānīṃ trividhaṃ śṛṇu me bharatarṣabha
c abhyāsād ramate yatra duḥkhāntaṃ ca nigacchati
a yat tadagre viṣam iva pariṇāme 'mṛtopamam
c tat sukhaṃ sāttvikaṃ proktam ātmabuddhiprasādajam
a viṣayendriyasaṃyogād yat tadagre 'mṛtopamam
c pariṇāme viṣam iva tat sukhaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtam
a yad agre cānubandhe ca sukhaṃ mohanam ātmanaḥ
c nidrālasyapramādotthaṃ tat tāmasam udāhṛtam
a na tad asti pṛthivyāṃ vā divi deveṣu vā punaḥ
c sattvaṃ prakṛtijair muktaṃ yad ebhiḥ syāt tribhir guṇaiḥ
a brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca paraṃtapa
c karmāṇi pravibhaktāni svabhāvaprabhavair guṇaiḥ
a śamo damas tapaḥ śaucaṃ kṣāntir ārjavam eva ca
c jñānaṃ vijñānam āstikyaṃ brahmakarma svabhāvajam
a śauryaṃ tejo dhṛtir dākṣyaṃ yuddhe cāpy apalāyanam
c dānam īśvarabhāvaś ca kṣatrakarma svabhāvajam
a kṛṣigorakṣyavāṇijyaṃ vaiśyakarma svabhāvajam
c paricaryātmakaṃ karma śūdrasyāpi svabhāvajam
a sve sve karmaṇy abhirataḥ saṃsiddhiṃ labhate naraḥ
c svakarmanirataḥ siddhiṃ yathā vindati tac chṛṇu
a yataḥ pravṛttir bhūtānāṃ yena sarvam idaṃ tatam
c svakarmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhiṃ vindati mānavaḥ
a śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt
b svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmodayād api
c svabhāvaniyataṃ karma kurvan nāpnoti kilbiṣam
a sahajaṃ karma kaunteya sadoṣam api na tyajet
c sarvārambhā hi doṣeṇa dhūmenāgnir ivāvṛtāḥ
a asaktabuddhiḥ sarvatra jitātmā vigataspṛhaḥ
c naiṣkarmyasiddhiṃ paramāṃ saṃnyāsenādhigacchati
a siddhiṃ prāpto yathā brahma tathāpnoti nibodha me
c samāsenaiva kaunteya niṣṭhā jñānasya yā parā
a buddhyā viśuddhayā yukto dhṛtyātmānaṃ niyamya ca
c śabdādīn viṣayāṃs tyaktvā rāgadveṣau vyudasya ca
a viviktasevī laghvāśī yatavākkāyamānasaḥ
c dhyānayogaparo nityaṃ vairāgyaṃ samupāśritaḥ
a ahaṃkāraṃ balaṃ darpaṃ kāmaṃ krodhaṃ parigraham
c vimucya nirmamaḥ śānto brahmabhūyāya kalpate
a brahmabhūtaḥ prasannātmā na śocati na kāṅkṣati
c samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu madbhaktiṃ labhate parām
a bhaktyā mām abhijānāti yāvān yaś cāsmi tattvataḥ
c tato māṃ tattvato jñātvā viśate tadanantaram
a sarvakarmāṇy api sadā kurvāṇo madvyapāśrayaḥ
c matprasādād avāpnoti śāśvataṃ padam avyayam
a cetasā sarvakarmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya matparaḥ
c buddhiyogam upāśritya maccittaḥ satataṃ bhava
a maccittaḥ sarvadurgāṇi matprasādāt tariṣyasi
c atha cet tvam ahaṃkārān na śroṣyasi vinaṅkṣyasi
a yad ahaṃkāram āśritya na yotsya iti manyase
c mithyaiṣa vyavasāyas te prakṛtis tvāṃ niyokṣyati
a svabhāvajena kaunteya nibaddhaḥ svena karmaṇā
c kartuṃ necchasi yan mohāt kariṣyasy avaśo 'pi tat
a īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛddeśe 'rjuna tiṣṭhati
c bhrāmayan sarvabhūtāni yantrārūḍhāni māyayā
a tam eva śaraṇaṃ gaccha sarvabhāvena bhārata
c tatprasādāt parāṃ śāntiṃ sthānaṃ prāpsyasi śāśvatam
a iti te jñānam ākhyātaṃ guhyād guhyataraṃ mayā
c vimṛśyaitad aśeṣeṇa yathecchasi tathā kuru
a sarvaguhyatamaṃ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu me paramaṃ vacaḥ
c iṣṭo 'si me dṛḍham iti tato vakṣyāmi te hitam
a manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṃ namaskuru
c mām evaiṣyasi satyaṃ te pratijāne priyo 'si me
a sarvadharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja
c ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ
a idaṃ te nātapaskāya nābhaktāya kadā cana
c na cāśuśrūṣave vācyaṃ na ca māṃ yo 'bhyasūyati
a ya idaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣv abhidhāsyati
c bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā mām evaiṣyaty asaṃśayaḥ
a na ca tasmān manuṣyeṣu kaś cin me priyakṛttamaḥ
c bhavitā na ca me tasmād anyaḥ priyataro bhuvi
a adhyeṣyate ca ya imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃvādam āvayoḥ
c jñānayajñena tenāham iṣṭaḥ syām iti me matiḥ
a śraddhāvān anasūyaś ca śṛṇuyād api yo naraḥ
c so 'pi muktaḥ śubhāṃl lokān prāpnuyāt puṇyakarmaṇām
a kaccid etac chrutaṃ pārtha tvayaikāgreṇa cetasā
c kaccid ajñānasaṃmohaḥ pranaṣṭas te dhanaṃjaya
 arjuna uvāca
a naṣṭo mohaḥ smṛtir labdhā tvatprasādān mayācyuta
c sthito 'smi gatasaṃdehaḥ kariṣye vacanaṃ tava
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity ahaṃ vāsudevasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ
c saṃvādam imam aśrauṣam adbhutaṃ romaharṣaṇam
a vyāsaprasādāc chrutavān etad guhyam ahaṃ param
c yogaṃ yogeśvarāt kṛṣṇāt sākṣāt kathayataḥ svayam
a rājan saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya saṃvādam imam adbhutam
c keśavārjunayoḥ puṇyaṃ hṛṣyāmi ca muhur muhuḥ
a tac ca saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya rūpam atyadbhutaṃ hareḥ
c vismayo me mahān rājan hṛṣyāmi ca punaḥ punaḥ
a yatra yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇo yatra pārtho dhanurdharaḥ
c tatra śrīr vijayo bhūtir dhruvā nītir matir mama
d bhagavadbhaktiyuktasya tatprasādātmabodhataḥ
d sukhaṃ bandhavimuktiḥ syād iti gītārthasaṃgrahaḥ
d ṣaṭ śatāni saviṃśāni ślokānāṃ prāha keśavaḥ
d arjunaḥ saptapañcāśat saptaṣaṣṭis tu saṃjayaḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ślokam ekaṃ gītāyā mānam ucyate
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d gītā sugītā kartavyā kim anyaiḥ śāstravistaraiḥ
d yā ceyaṃ padmanābhasya mukhapadmād viniḥsṛtā
d sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadevamayo hariḥ
d sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvavedamayo manuḥ
d gaṅgā gītā ca gāyatrī govindeti hṛdi sthite
d caturgakārasaṃyukte punarjanma na vidyate
d bhāratāmṛtasarvasvagītāyā mathitasya ca
d sāram uddhṛtya kṛṣṇena arjunasya mukhe hutam
dA arjuna uvāca
dA yad etan niṣkalaṃ brahma vyomātītaṃ nirañjanam 
dA kaivalyaṃ kevalaṃ śāntaṃ śuddham atyantanirmalam  
dA apratarkyam avijñeyaṃ vināśotpattivarjitam 
dA śrībhagavān uvāca
dA jñānayogavinirmuktaṃ taj jñānaṃ brūhi keśava  
dA sarvatojyotir ākāśaṃ sarvabhūtaguṇānvitam 
dA sarvataḥparamātmānam akṣayaṃ paramaṃ padam  
dA anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ mahājyotir atidhruvam 
dA atyantaparamaṃ sthānaṃ śabdādiguṇavarjitam  
dA yat tat parataraṃ jyotir dhruvāt parataraṃ sthitam
