dA ācaturyugam adyāpi kathitaṃ na hi kasya cit  
dA ātmadehe mayā sṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ kṣetram eva ca 
dA sakalaṃ tu bhavet kṣetraṃ niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ padam  
dA arjuna tvatprasādena śṛṇvantu munisattamāḥ 
dA adya muktā mahābāho tvatprasādād dhanaṃjaya  
dA pramāṇaṃ vedatattvānāṃ sāṃkhyādīny abhiyoginām 
dA teṣāṃ na vidyate niṣṭhā sarvaiḥ pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ saha  
dA kathitaṃ ca mayā jñānaṃ devānām api durlabham 
dA viśvarūpamayaṃ divyaṃ bhairavagranthibindunā  
dA suṣumṇā dakṣiṇe mārge darśitā viśvarūpiṇā 
dA aprakāśam idaṃ praśnaṃ yan mayā kathitaṃ tava  
dA nāgnir vāyur na cākāśaṃ na kṣitir nāpi vā jalam 
dA na manobuddhyahaṃkāraṃ gūḍhārthaṃ kathitaṃ tava  
dA anityo nityatāṃ yāti yadā bhāvaṃ na paśyati 
dA śūnyaṃ nirañjanākāraṃ nirvāṇaṃ dhruvam avyayam  
dA puruṣaṃ nirguṇaṃ sākṣāt sarvataś caiva tiṣṭhati 
dA sarvaṃ tat syāt paraṃ brahma buddhiś cāsya na budhyati  
dA pratibhāvaprayatnena hariṃ trailokyabāndhavam 
dA daśamaṃ cāṅgulaṃ vyāpya cāśābāhyaṃ vyavasthitam  
dA jīvo yatra pralīyeta sā kalā ṣoḍaśī smṛtā 
dA tayā sarvam idaṃ vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  
dA tac cintyaṃ tena vai jñānaṃ tad atrādyā upāsate 
dA brahmaṇaiva hi vikhyātaṃ vedānteṣu prakāśitam  
dA vedeṣu vedam ity āhur vedadhāma paraṃ matam 
dA tat paraṃ viditaṃ yasya sa vipro vedapāragaḥ  
dA āhutiḥ sā parā jñeyā sā ca saṃdhyā pratiṣṭhitā 
dA gāyatrī sā parā jñeyā ajapā nāma viśrutā  
dA tapasy atha tathā vede munibhiḥ samupāsyate 
dA tāṃ kalāṃ yo 'bhijānāti sa kalājño 'bhidhīyate  
dA yāṃ jñātvā mucyate jantur garbhajanmajarādibhiḥ 
dA parijñānena mucyante narāḥ pātakakilbiṣaiḥ  
dA iḍā bhagavatī gaṅgā piṅgalā yamunā nadī 
dA tayor madhye tṛtīyā tu tat prayāgam anusmaret  
dA iḍā vai vaiṣṇavī nāḍī brahmanāḍī tu piṅgalā 
dA suṣumṇā caiśvarī nāḍī tridhā prāṇavahā smṛtā 
dA brahmā viṣṇur mahādevo recakaḥ pūrakumbhakaḥ  
dA sakrāntiviṣuvac caiva yo 'bhijānāti vigraham 
dA nityayuktaḥ sa yogīśo brahmavidyāṃ prapadyate  
dA iḍā vai gārhapatyas tu piṅgalāhavanīyakaḥ 
dA suṣumṇā dakṣiṇāgnis tu hy etad agnitrayaṃ smṛtam  
dA tasya madhye sthitaṃ jyotiḥ somamaṇḍalam eva ca 
dA somamaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ tanmadhye sūryamaṇḍalam  
dA sūryamaṇḍalamadhyastho jvalat tejo hutāśanaḥ 
dA hutāśanasya madhye tu nirdhūmāṅgāravarcasam  
dA tatrāsthito mahātmāsau yogibhis tu pragīyate 
dA sugītaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ mana ekāgracetasā  
dA śivo binduḥ śivo devo ghargharāmṛtavarcasā 
dA nikhilaṃ pūrayed dehaṃ viṣadāhajvarāpaham  
dA sarpavatkuṭilākārasuṣumṇāveṣṭitāṃ tanum 
dA makāraveṣṭitāṃ kṛtvā mātṛvat pariyojayet  
dA tristhānaṃ ca trimātraṃ ca tribrahma ca trirakṣaram 
dA ardhamātraṃ ca yo vetti sa bhaved vedapāragaḥ  
dA sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tat sarvatokṣiśiromukham 
dA arjuna uvāca
dA nirmalaṃ vimalākāraṃ śuddhasphaṭikasaṃnibham  
dA jīvo jīvati jīvena nāsti jīvam ajīvitam 
dA śrībhagavān uvāca
dA nirgataḥ saha saṅgena sa jīvaḥ kena jīvati  
dA mukhanāsikayor madhye prāṇaḥ saṃcarate sadā 
dA ākāśaṃ pibate nityaṃ sa jīvas tena jīvati  
dA kākīmukhaṃ kakārāntaṃ makāraṃ cetanānugam 
dA akārasya tu luptasya ko 'rthaḥ saṃpratipadyate  
dA tāvat paśyet khagākāraṃ khakāraṃ tu vicintayet 
dA khamadhye kuru cātmānam ātmamadhyaṃ ca khaṃ kuru  
dA khamadhye ca praveṣṭavyaṃ khaṃ ca brahma sanātanam 
dA ātmānaṃ khamayaṃ kṛtvā na kiṃ cid api cintayet  
dA ūrdhvaśūnyam adhaḥśūnyaṃ madhyeśūnyaṃ nirāmayam 
dA triśūnyaṃ yo 'bhijānāti sa bhavet kulanandanaḥ  
dA tasya bhāvasya bhāvātmā bhāvanā naiva yujyate 
dA anāvṛttasya śabdasya tasya śabdasya yo gatiḥ  
dA tat padaṃ viditaṃ yena sa yogī chinnasaṃśayaḥ 
dA puṇyapāpaharāś caiva ye cānye pañcadaivatāḥ  
dA jīvinaḥ saha gacchanti yāvat tattvaṃ na vindati 
dA pāpaṃ dahati jñānāgniḥ puṇyena somasūryayoḥ  
dA puṇyapāpavinirmuktir eṣa yogo 'bhidhīyate 
dA dhṛtirodhi manodhīti saṃtoṣaṃ samidhāmṛtam  
dA indriyāṇi paśuṃ kṛtvā yo yajeta sa dīkṣitaḥ 
dA paraṃ brahmādhigacchanti śabdabrahmavicintanāt  
dA sakale dṛṣṭapāro 'pi bhāvaṃ yuñjati yuñjati 
dA niṣkale darśanaṃ nāsti svabhāvo bhāvaṃ yuñjati  
dA tālumūle ca lampāyāṃ trikūṭaṃ tripathāntaram 
dA ekaṃ tattvaṃ vijānīyād vighnasyāyatanaṃ mahat  
dA chinnamūlasya vṛkṣasya yathā janma na vidyate 
dA jñānadagdhaśarīrasya punar deho na vidyate  
dA gītāḥ sugītāḥ kartavyāḥ kim anyaiḥ śāstrasaṃgrahaiḥ 
dA yāḥ purā padmanābhasya mukhapadmād viniḥsṛtāḥ  
dA gītāgāṅgodakaṃ pītvā punarjanma na vidyate 
dA sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadharmamayo hariḥ  
dA sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī 
dA sarvabhogamayaś cāyaṃ sarvamokṣamayo hy ayam  
dA gītā gaṅgā ca gāyatrī govindo hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ 
dA caturgakārasmaraṇāt punarjanma na vidyate  
dA gītāsāraṃ paṭhed yas tu hy acyutasya ca saṃnidhau 
dA tasmād guṇasahasreṇa viṣṇor nirvacanaṃ yathā  
dA etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam 
dA paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam  
dB arjuna uvāca
