dB amātraśabdarahitaṃ svaravyañjanavarjitam 
dB bindunādakalātītaṃ yas taṃ veda sa vedavit  
dB saṃprāpte jñānavijñāne jñeye ca hṛdi saṃsthite 
dB labdhaśāntapade bhāve na yogo na ca dhāraṇā  
dB vedādau yaḥ suraḥ prokto vedānte ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
dB tasya prakṛtilīnasya yaḥ paraḥ sa maheśvaraḥ  
dB nā nāvārthī bhavet tāvad yāvat pāraṃ na gacchati 
dB uttīrṇe tu pare pāre kiṃ nāvā vai prayojanam  
dB dūrastho nāpi dūrasthaḥ piṇḍasthaḥ piṇḍavarjitaḥ 
dB arjuna uvāca
dB amalo nirmalaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sarvavyāpī nirañjanaḥ  
dB akṣarāṇi samātrāṇi sarve bindusamāśritāḥ 
dB śrībhagavān uvāca
dB bindur bhidyati nādena sa nādaḥ kena bhidyate  
dB oṃkāradhvaninādena vāyuḥ saṃharaṇāntikam 
dB nirālambhas tu nirdeho yatra nādo layaṃ gataḥ  
dB arjuna uvāca
dB bāhyena vyāpitaṃ vyoma vyoma cānanunāsikam 
dB śrībhagavān uvāca
dB adhaś cordhvaṃ kathaṃ caiva kaṇṭhe caiva nirañjanaḥ  
dB anūṣmam avyañjakam asvaraṃ yat
dB tat tālukaṇṭheṣv anunāsikaṃ ca 
dB arephajātaṃ śubham ūṣmavarjitaṃ
dB na duṣkarāṇāṃ kurute kadā cit  
dB ākāśam apy anākāśaṃ puruṣatve pratiṣṭhitam 
dB śabdaṃ guṇam ivākāśaṃ niḥśabdaṃ brahma cocyate  
dB sarvagaṃ sarvabodhādi vāsanājālavarjitam 
dB indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena dehe paśyanti mānavāḥ  
dB dehe naṣṭe kuto buddhir jñānaṃ vijñānam eva ca 
dB jñānaṃ vijñānayuktaṃ ca rakṣaṇīyaṃ prayatnataḥ  
dB chinnamūlasya vṛkṣasya yathā janma na vidyate 
dB jñānadagdhaśarīrasya punar deho na vidyate  
dB gītāḥ sugītāḥ kartavyāḥ kim anyaiḥ śāstrasaṃgrahaiḥ 
dB yāḥ purā padmanābhasya mukhapadmaviniḥsṛtāḥ  
dB gītāgaṅgodakaṃ pītvā punarjanma na vidyate 
dB sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadharmamayo hariḥ  
dB sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī 
dB sarvabhogamayaś cāyaṃ sarvamokṣamayo hy ayam  
dB gakārapūrvāś catvāro rakṣanti mahato bhayāt 
dB gītā gaṅgā ca gāyatrī govindo hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ  
dB snāto vā yadi vāsnātaḥ śucir vā yadi vāśuciḥ 
dB yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantare śuciḥ  
dB sa gacchet tatkṣaṇāt prāyo brahmamūrte namo 'stu te 
dB gītāsāraṃ paṭhed yas tu viṣṇuloke mahīyate  
dB etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam 
dB paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam  
 saṃjaya uvāca
 prabodhitaḥ sa tu tadā viṣṇunā viśvamūrtinā
 avināśisvarūpaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tattvena phālgunaḥ
 kṛtrimaṃ tu jagadrūpaṃ jñātvā yuddhodyato 'bhavat
 devadattaṃ samāyujya śastrāṇi jagṛhe punaḥ
a tato dhanaṃjayaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāṇagāṇḍīvadhāriṇam
c punar eva mahānādaṃ vyasṛjanta mahārathāḥ
a pāṇḍavāḥ somakāś caiva ye caiṣām anuyāyinaḥ
c dadhmuś ca muditāḥ śaṅkhān vīrāḥ sāgarasaṃbhavān
a tato bheryaś ca peśyaś ca krakacā goviṣāṇikāḥ
c sahasaivābhyahanyanta tataḥ śabdo mahān abhūt
a atha devāḥ sagandharvāḥ pitaraś ca janeśvara
c siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca samīyus te didṛkṣayā
a ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgāḥ puraskṛtya śatakratum
c samīyus tatra sahitā draṣṭuṃ tad vaiśasaṃ mahat
d te sene stimite cāstāṃ vīkṣamāṇe parasparam
d gaṅgāyamunayor vegau yathaivaitya parasparam
d evaṃ pravṛtte te sene niḥśabde janasaṃsadi
d citre iva paṭālekhye darśanīyatare śubhe
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya susamudyate
c te sene sāgaraprakhye muhuḥ pracalite nṛpa
a vimucya kavacaṃ vīro nikṣipya ca varāyudham
c avaruhya rathāt tūrṇaṃ padbhyām eva kṛtāñjaliḥ
a pitāmaham abhiprekṣya dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c vāgyataḥ prayayau yena prāṅmukho ripuvāhinīm
a taṃ prayāntam abhiprekṣya kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito 'nvayāt
d bhītaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraṃ matvā bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
a vāsudevaś ca bhagavān pṛṣṭhato 'nujagāma ha
b sātyakiś cārjunaś caiva abhimanyuś ca vīryavān
c yathāmukhyāś ca rājānas tam anvājagmur utsukāḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a kiṃ te vyavasitaṃ rājan yad asmān apahāya vai
c padbhyām eva prayāto 'si prāṅmukho ripuvāhinīm
 bhīmasena uvāca
a kva gamiṣyasi rājendra nikṣiptakavacāyudhaḥ
c daṃśiteṣv arisainyeṣu bhrātṝn utsṛjya pārthiva
 nakula uvāca
a evaṃgate tvayi jyeṣṭhe mama bhrātari bhārata
c bhīr me dunoti hṛdayaṃ brūhi gantā bhavān kva nu
d kvaivaṃ gamiṣyasi śreṣṭha tyaktvāsmān durbalo yathā
d rājā hi tvaṃ mahābāho vāgyato manyumān iva
 sahadeva uvāca
a asmin raṇasamūhe vai vartamāne mahābhaye
c yoddhavye kva nu gantāsi śatrūn abhimukho nṛpa
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam ābhāṣyamāṇo 'pi bhrātṛbhiḥ kurunandana
c novāca vāgyataḥ kiṃ cid gacchaty eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tān uvāca mahāprājño vāsudevo mahāmanāḥ
c abhiprāyo 'sya vijñāto mayeti prahasann iva
a eṣa bhīṣmaṃ tathā droṇaṃ gautamaṃ śalyam eva ca
c anumānya gurūn sarvān yotsyate pārthivo 'ribhiḥ
a śrūyate hi purākalpe gurūn ananumānya yaḥ
c yudhyate sa bhaved vyaktam apadhyāto mahattaraiḥ
d yuddhāyāvataraty eva tasya nāsti jayo raṇe
d yas tu yuddhe samutpanne gurūn dṛṣṭvātha daṃśitān
a anumānya yathāśāstraṃ yas tu yudhyen mahattaraiḥ
c dhruvas tasya jayo yuddhe bhaved iti matir mama
a evaṃ bruvati kṛṣṇe tu dhārtarāṣṭracamūṃ prati
b netrair animiṣaiḥ sarve prekṣante sma yudhiṣṭhiram
c hāhākāro mahān āsīn niḥśabdās tv apare 'bhavan
a dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dūrād dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāḥ
c mithaḥ saṃkathayāṃ cakrur neśo 'sti kulapāṃsanaḥ
a vyaktaṃ bhīta ivābhyeti rājāsau bhīṣmam antikāt
c yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sasodaryaḥ śaraṇārthaṃ prayācakaḥ
a dhanaṃjaye kathaṃ nāthe pāṇḍave ca vṛkodare
c nakule sahadeve ca bhīto 'bhyeti ca pāṇḍavaḥ
a na nūnaṃ kṣatriyakule jātaḥ saṃprathite bhuvi
c yathāsya hṛdayaṃ bhītam alpasattvasya saṃyuge
a tatas te kṣatriyāḥ sarve praśaṃsanti sma kauravān
c hṛṣṭāḥ sumanaso bhūtvā cailāni dudhuvuḥ pṛthak
a vyanindanta tataḥ sarve yodhās tatra viśāṃ pate
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ sasodaryaṃ sahitaṃ keśavena ha
a tatas tat kauravaṃ sainyaṃ dhikkṛtvā tu yudhiṣṭhiram
c niḥśabdam abhavat tūrṇaṃ punar eva viśāṃ pate
a kiṃ nu vakṣyati rājāsau kiṃ bhīṣmaḥ prativakṣyati
b kiṃ nu vakṣyati rājāsau dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b kiṃ nu vakṣyati bhīṣmo 'sau bharatānāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥ
c kiṃ bhīmaḥ samaraślāghī kiṃ nu kṛṣṇārjunāv iti
a vivakṣitaṃ kim asyeti saṃśayaḥ sumahān abhūt
c ubhayoḥ senayo rājan yudhiṣṭhirakṛte tadā
a sa vigāhya camūṃ śatroḥ śaraśaktisamākulām
c bhīṣmam evābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a tam uvāca tataḥ pādau karābhyāṃ pīḍya pāṇḍavaḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ rājā yuddhāya samupasthitam
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a āmantraye tvāṃ durdharṣa yotsye tāta tvayā saha
c anujānīhi māṃ tāta āśiṣaś ca prayojaya
d jayeyaṃ ca ripūn sarvān anujñātas tvayānagha
d yudhyantaṃ māṃ raṇe vīra tvam anujñātum arhasi
 bhīṣma uvāca
a yady evaṃ nābhigacchethā yudhi māṃ pṛthivīpate
c śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya bhārata
a prīto 'smi putra yudhyasva jayam āpnuhi pāṇḍava
c yat te 'bhilaṣitaṃ cānyat tad avāpnuhi saṃyuge
a vriyatāṃ ca varaḥ pārtha kim asmatto 'bhikāṅkṣasi
c evaṃ gate mahārāja na tavāsti parājayaḥ
a arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya cit
c iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiḥ
a atas tvāṃ klībavad vākyaṃ bravīmi kurunandana
c hṛto 'smy arthena kauravya yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a mantrayasva mahāprājña hitaiṣī mama nityaśaḥ
c yudhyasva kauravasyārthe mamaiṣa satataṃ varaḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a rājan kim atra sāhyaṃ te karomi kurunandana
b mantrayiṣyāmy ahaṃ rājan yac ca te hitam uttamam
c kāmaṃ yotsye parasyārthe brūhi yat te vivakṣitam
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kathaṃ jayeyaṃ saṃgrāme bhavantam aparājitam
c etan me mantraya hitaṃ yadi śreyaḥ prapaśyasi
 bhīṣma uvāca
a na taṃ paśyāmi kaunteya yo māṃ yudhyantam āhave
c vijayeta pumān kaś cid api sākṣāc chatakratuḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a hanta pṛcchāmi tasmāt tvāṃ pitāmaha namo 'stu te
c jayopāyaṃ bravīhi tvam ātmanaḥ samare paraiḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a na śatruṃ tāta paśyāmi samare yo jayeta mām
b ayudhyamānaṃ saṃhatya sauhṛdena pariplutam
b nyastaśastraṃ nirudyogaṃ hanyur mā śatravo yudhi
b nikṣiptaśastre patite vimuktakavace tathā
b dravamāṇe ca bhīte ca tavāsmīti ca yo vadet
b striyāṃ strīnāmadheye ca vikale caikaputrake
b aprasūte ca hīne ca na yuddhaṃ rocayāmy aham
b idaṃ ca gaditaṃ pārtha paramaṃ vratam āhave
c na tāvan mṛtyukālo me punarāgamanaṃ kuru
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro vākyaṃ bhīṣmasya kurunandana
c śirasā pratijagrāha bhūyas tam abhivādya ca
a prāyāt punar mahābāhur ācāryasya rathaṃ prati
c paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ madhyena bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
a sa droṇam abhivādyātha kṛtvā caiva pradakṣiṇam
c uvāca vācā durdharṣam ātmaniḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥ
a āmantraye tvāṃ bhagavan yotsye vigatakalmaṣaḥ
c jayeyaṃ ca ripūn sarvān anujñātas tvayā dvija
 droṇa uvāca
a yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ
c śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya sarvaśaḥ
a tad yudhiṣṭhira tuṣṭo 'smi pūjitaś ca tvayānagha
c anujānāmi yudhyasva vijayaṃ samavāpnuhi
a karavāṇi ca te kāmaṃ brūhi yat te 'bhikāṅkṣitam
c evaṃ gate mahārāja yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
a arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya cit
c iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiḥ
a atas tvāṃ klībavad brūmo yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
c yotsyāmi kauravasyārthe tavāśāsyo jayo mayā
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a jayam āśāssva me brahman mantrayasva ca maddhitam
c yudhyasva kauravasyārthe vara eṣa vṛto mayā
 droṇa uvāca
a dhruvas te vijayo rājan yasya mantrī haris tava
c ahaṃ ca tvābhijānāmi raṇe śatrūn vijeṣyasi
a yato dharmas tataḥ kṛṣṇo yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥ
c yudhyasva gaccha kaunteya pṛccha māṃ kiṃ bravīmi te
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a pṛcchāmi tvāṃ dvijaśreṣṭha śṛṇu me yad vivakṣitam
c kathaṃ jayeyaṃ saṃgrāme bhavantam aparājitam
 droṇa uvāca
a na te 'sti vijayas tāvad yāvad yudhyāmy ahaṃ raṇe
c mamāśu nidhane rājan yatasva saha sodaraiḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a hanta tasmān mahābāho vadhopāyaṃ vadātmanaḥ
c ācārya praṇipatyaiṣa pṛcchāmi tvāṃ namo 'stu te
 droṇa uvāca
a na śatruṃ tāta paśyāmi yo māṃ hanyād raṇe sthitam
c yudhyamānaṃ susaṃrabdhaṃ śaravarṣaughavarṣiṇam
a ṛte prāyagataṃ rājan nyastaśastram acetanam
c hanyān māṃ yudhi yodhānāṃ satyam etad bravīmi te
a śastraṃ cāhaṃ raṇe jahyāṃ śrutvā sumahad apriyam
c śraddheyavākyāt puruṣād etat satyaṃ bravīmi te
 saṃjaya uvāca
a etac chrutvā mahārāja bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ
c anumānya tam ācāryaṃ prāyāc chāradvataṃ prati
a so 'bhivādya kṛpaṃ rājā kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam
c uvāca durdharṣatamaṃ vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
a anumānaye tvāṃ yotsyāmi guro vigatakalmaṣaḥ
c jayeyaṃ ca ripūn sarvān anujñātas tvayānagha
 kṛpa uvāca
a yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ
c śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya sarvaśaḥ
d kiṃ te karomi vai kāmaṃ brūhi pāṇḍavanandana
d evaṃ gate mahārāja yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
a arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya cit
c iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiḥ
a teṣām arthe mahārāja yoddhavyam iti me matiḥ
c atas tvāṃ klībavad brūmi yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a hanta pṛcchāmi te tasmād ācārya śṛṇu me vacaḥ
b vadhopāyaṃ bravīhi tvam ātmanaḥ samare paraiḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity uktvā vyathito rājā novāca gatacetanaḥ
c taṃ gautamaḥ pratyuvāca vijñāyāsya vivakṣitam
e avadhyo 'haṃ mahīpāla yudhyasva jayam āpnuhi
a prītas tv abhigamenāhaṃ jayaṃ tava narādhipa
c āśāsiṣye sadotthāya satyam etad bravīmi te
a etac chrutvā mahārāja gautamasya vacas tadā
c anumānya kṛpaṃ rājā prayayau yena madrarāṭ
a sa śalyam abhivādyātha kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇam
c uvāca rājā durdharṣam ātmaniḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥ
a anumānaye tvāṃ yotsyāmi guro vigatakalmaṣaḥ
c jayeyaṃ ca mahārāja anujñātas tvayā ripūn
 śalya uvāca
a yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ
c śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya vai raṇe
a tuṣṭo 'smi pūjitaś cāsmi yat kāṅkṣasi tad astu te
c anujānāmi caiva tvāṃ yudhyasva jayam āpnuhi
a brūhi caiva paraṃ vīra kenārthaḥ kiṃ dadāmi te
c evaṃ gate mahārāja yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
a arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya cit
c iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiḥ
d teṣām arthe mahārāja yoddhavyam iti me matiḥ
a kariṣyāmi hi te kāmaṃ bhāgineya yathepsitam
c bravīmy ataḥ klībavat tvāṃ yuddhād anyat kim icchasi
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a mantrayasva mahārāja nityaṃ maddhitam uttamam
c kāmaṃ yudhya parasyārthe varam etad vṛṇomy aham
 śalya uvāca
a brūhi kim atra sāhyaṃ te karomi nṛpasattama
c kāmaṃ yotsye parasyārthe vṛto 'smy arthena kauravaiḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a sa eva me varaḥ satya udyoge yas tvayā kṛtaḥ
c sūtaputrasya saṃgrāme kāryas tejovadhas tvayā
d tvāṃ hi yokṣyati sūtatve sūtaputrasya mātula
d duryodhano raṇe śūram iti me naiṣṭhikī matiḥ
 śalya uvāca
a saṃpatsyaty eṣa te kāmaḥ kuntīputra yathepsitaḥ
c gaccha yudhyasva visrabdhaṃ pratijāne jayaṃ tava
 saṃjaya uvāca
a anumānyātha kaunteyo mātulaṃ madrakeśvaram
c nirjagāma mahāsainyād bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a vāsudevas tu rādheyam āhave 'bhijagāma vai
c tata enam uvācedaṃ pāṇḍavārthe gadāgrajaḥ
a śrutaṃ me karṇa bhīṣmasya dveṣāt kila na yotsyasi
c asmān varaya rādheya yāvad bhīṣmo na hanyate
a hate tu bhīṣme rādheya punar eṣyasi saṃyuge
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya sāhāyyaṃ yadi paśyasi cet samam
 karṇa uvāca
a na vipriyaṃ kariṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭrasya keśava
c tyaktaprāṇaṃ hi māṃ viddhi duryodhanahitaiṣiṇam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃnyavartata bhārata
c yudhiṣṭhirapurogaiś ca pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃgataḥ
a atha sainyasya madhye tu prākrośat pāṇḍavāgrajaḥ
c yo 'smān vṛṇoti tad ahaṃ varaye sāhyakāraṇāt
a atha tān samabhiprekṣya yuyutsur idam abravīt
c prītātmā dharmarājānaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a ahaṃ yotsyāmi miṣataḥ saṃyuge dhārtarāṣṭrajān
c yuṣmadarthe mahārāja yadi māṃ vṛṇuṣe 'nagha
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a ehy ehi sarve yotsyāmas tava bhrātṝn apaṇḍitān
c yuyutso vāsudevaś ca vayaṃ ca brūma sarvaśaḥ
d na bhaviṣyanti te bālā dhārtarāṣṭrā na saṃśayaḥ
a vṛṇomi tvāṃ mahābāho yudhyasva mama kāraṇāt
c tvayi piṇḍaś ca tantuś ca dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dṛśyate
d tato jalakriyā caiva tvayā kāryā tathaiva ca
a bhajasvāsmān rājaputra bhajamānān mahādyute
c na bhaviṣyati durbuddhir dhārtarāṣṭro 'tyamarṣaṇaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato yuyutsuḥ kauravyaḥ parityajya sutāṃs tava
b sa satyam iti manvāno yudhiṣṭhiravacas tadā
c jagāma pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ senāṃ viśrāvya dundubhim
d sabalo dhārtarāṣṭrasya kutsayan karma duṣkṛtam
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ sahānujaiḥ
c jagrāha kavacaṃ bhūyo dīptimat kanakojjvalam
a pratyapadyanta te sarve rathān svān puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c tato vyūhaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ pratyavyūhanta te punaḥ
a avādayan dundubhīṃś ca śataśaś caiva puṣkarān
c siṃhanādāṃś ca vividhān vineduḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
a rathasthān puruṣavyāghrān pāṇḍavān prekṣya pārthivāḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnādayaḥ sarve punar jahṛṣire mudā
a gauravaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ mānyān mānayatāṃ ca tān
c dṛṣṭvā mahīkṣitas tatra pūjayāṃ cakrire bhṛśam
a sauhṛdaṃ ca kṛpāṃ caiva prāptakālaṃ mahātmanām
c dayāṃ ca jñātiṣu parāṃ kathayāṃ cakrire nṛpāḥ
a sādhu sādhv iti sarvatra niśceruḥ stutisaṃhitāḥ
c vācaḥ puṇyāḥ kīrtimatāṃ manohṛdayaharṣiṇīḥ
a mlecchāś cāryāś ca ye tatra dadṛśuḥ śuśruvus tadā
c vṛttaṃ tat pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ rurudus te sagadgadāḥ
a tato jaghnur mahābherīḥ śataśaś caiva puṣkarān
c śaṅkhāṃś ca gokṣīranibhān dadhmur hṛṣṭā manasvinaḥ
 bhagavān uvāca sic
 kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanam
 vāsudevaṃ jagadyoniṃ naumi nārāyaṇaṃ harim
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a evaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu māmakeṣv itareṣu ca
c ke pūrvaṃ prāharaṃs tatra kuravaḥ pāṇḍavās tathā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rājan putro duryodhanas tava
c bhīṣmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtvā prayayau saha senayā
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve bhīmasenapurogamāḥ
c bhīṣmeṇa yuddham icchantaḥ prayayur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
a kṣveḍāḥ kilakilāśabdāḥ krakacā goviṣāṇikāḥ
c bherīmṛdaṅgamurajā hayakuñjaranisvanāḥ
a ubhayoḥ senayo rājaṃs tatas te 'smān samādravan
c vayaṃ pratinadantaś ca tadāsīt tumulaṃ mahat
a mahānty anīkāni mahāsamucchraye
samāgame pāṇḍavadhārtarāṣṭrayoḥ
c cakampire śaṅkhamṛdaṅganisvanaiḥ
prakampitānīva vanāni vāyunā
a narendranāgāśvarathākulānām
abhyāyatīnām aśive muhūrte
c babhūva ghoṣas tumulaś camūnāṃ
vātoddhutānām iva sāgarāṇām
a tasmin samutthite śabde tumule lomaharṣaṇe
c bhīmaseno mahābāhuḥ prāṇadad govṛṣo yathā
a śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaṃ vāraṇānāṃ ca bṛṃhitam
c siṃhanādaṃ ca sainyānāṃ bhīmasenaravo 'bhyabhūt
a hayānāṃ heṣamāṇānām anīkeṣu sahasraśaḥ
c sarvān abhyabhavac chabdān bhīmasenasya nisvanaḥ
a taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ tasya sainyās tava vitatrasuḥ
c jīmūtasyeva nadataḥ śakrāśanisamasvanam
a vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥ
c śabdena tasya vīrasya siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ
a darśayan ghoram ātmānaṃ mahābhram iva nādayan
c vibhīṣayaṃs tava sutāṃs tava senāṃ samabhyayāt
a tam āyāntaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ sodaryāḥ paryavārayan
c chādayantaḥ śaravrātair meghā iva divākaram
a duryodhanaś ca putras te durmukho duḥsahaḥ śalaḥ
c duḥśāsanaś cātirathas tathā durmarṣaṇo nṛpa
a viviṃśatiś citraseno vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
c purumitro jayo bhojaḥ saumadattiś ca vīryavān
a mahācāpāni dhunvanto jaladā iva vidyutaḥ
c ādadānāś ca nārācān nirmuktāśīviṣopamān
a atha tān draupadīputrāḥ saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
a dhārtarāṣṭrān pratiyayur ardayantaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vajrair iva mahāvegaiḥ śikharāṇi dharābhṛtām
a tasmin prathamasaṃmarde bhīmajyātalanisvane
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nāsīt kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥ
a lāghavaṃ droṇaśiṣyāṇām apaśyaṃ bharatarṣabha
c nimittavedhināṃ rājañ śarān utsṛjatāṃ bhṛśam
a nopaśāmyati nirghoṣo dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ tathā
c viniśceruḥ śarā dīptā jyotīṃṣīva nabhastalāt
a sarve tv anye mahīpālāḥ prekṣakā iva bhārata
c dadṛśur darśanīyaṃ taṃ bhīmaṃ jñātisamāgamam
a tatas te jātasaṃrambhāḥ parasparakṛtāgasaḥ
c anyonyaspardhayā rājan vyāyacchanta mahārathāḥ
a kurupāṇḍavasene te hastyaśvarathasaṃkule
c śuśubhāte raṇe 'tīva paṭe citragate iva
a tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥ
c sahasainyāḥ samāpetuḥ putrasya tava śāsanāt
d teṣām ādhāvatāṃ tatra gajāśvakalilo mahān
d siṃhanādaravonmiśraḥ śaṅkhabherīsamākulaḥ
d sa ghoṣavāñ śaragrāho dhanurnāgo 'sikacchapaḥ
d vyāvalgitapurovāta āsīt kṣubdhābdhivat svanaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhireṇa cādiṣṭāḥ pārthivās te sahasraśaḥ
c vinadantaḥ samāpetuḥ putrasya tava vāhinīm
a ubhayoḥ senayos tīvraḥ sainyānāṃ sa samāgamaḥ
c antardhīyata cādityaḥ sainyena rajasāvṛtaḥ
a prayuddhānāṃ prabhagnānāṃ punarāvartatām api
c nātra sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ vā viśeṣaḥ samajāyata
a tasmiṃs tu tumule yuddhe vartamāne mahābhaye
c ati sarvāṇy anīkāni pitā te 'bhivyarocata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a pūrvāhṇe tasya raudrasya yuddham ahno viśāṃ pate
c prāvartata mahāghoraṃ rājñāṃ dehāvakartanam
a kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca saṃgrāme vijigīṣatām
c siṃhānām iva saṃhrādo divam urvīṃ ca nādayan
a āsīt kilakilāśabdas talaśaṅkharavaiḥ saha
c jajñire siṃhanādāś ca śūrāṇāṃ pratigarjatām
a talatrābhihatāś caiva jyāśabdā bharatarṣabha
c pattīnāṃ pādaśabdāś ca vājināṃ ca mahāsvanāḥ
a tottrāṅkuśanipātāś ca āyudhānāṃ ca nisvanāḥ
c ghaṇṭāśabdāś ca nāgānām anyonyam abhidhāvatām
a tasmin samudite śabde tumule lomaharṣaṇe
c babhūva rathanirghoṣaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥ
a te manaḥ krūram ādhāya samabhityaktajīvitāḥ
c pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta sarva evocchritadhvajāḥ
a svayaṃ śāṃtanavo rājann abhyadhāvad dhanaṃjayam
c pragṛhya kārmukaṃ ghoraṃ kāladaṇḍopamaṃ raṇe
a arjuno 'pi dhanur gṛhya gāṇḍīvaṃ lokaviśrutam
c abhyadhāvata tejasvī gāṅgeyaṃ raṇamūrdhani
a tāv ubhau kuruśārdūlau parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
c gāṅgeyas tu raṇe pārthaṃ viddhvā nākampayad balī
e tathaiva pāṇḍavo rājan bhīṣmaṃ nākampayad yudhi
a sātyakiś ca maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt
c tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
a sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ kṛtavarmā ca sātyakim
c ānarchatuḥ śarair ghorais takṣamāṇau parasparam
a tau śarācitasarvāṅgau śuśubhāte mahābalau
c vasante puṣpaśabalau puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
a abhimanyur maheṣvāso bṛhadbalam ayodhayat
c tataḥ kosalako rājā saubhadrasya viśāṃ pate
e dhvajaṃ ciccheda samare sārathiṃ ca nyapātayat
a saubhadras tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ pātite rathasārathau
c bṛhadbalaṃ mahārāja vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a athāparābhyāṃ bhallābhyāṃ pītābhyām arimardanaḥ
c dhvajam ekena ciccheda pārṣṇim ekena sārathim
e anyonyaṃ ca śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kruddhau rājaṃs tatakṣatuḥ
a māninaṃ samare dṛptaṃ kṛtavairaṃ mahāratham
c bhīmasenas tava sutaṃ duryodhanam ayodhayat
a tāv ubhau naraśārdūlau kurumukhyau mahābalau
c anyonyaṃ śaravarṣābhyāṃ vavṛṣāte raṇājire
d tau vīrāv atisaṃrabdhau kṛtinau viṣame sthitau
a tau tu vīkṣya mahātmānau kṛtinau citrayodhinau
c vismayaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ samapadyata bhārata
a duḥśāsanas tu nakulaṃ pratyudyāya mahāratham
c avidhyan niśitair bāṇair bahubhir marmabhedibhiḥ
a tasya mādrīsutaḥ ketuṃ saśaraṃ ca śarāsanam
c ciccheda niśitair bāṇaiḥ prahasann iva bhārata
e athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samārdayat
a putras tu tava durdharṣo nakulasya mahāhave
c yugeṣāṃ cicchide bāṇair dhvajaṃ caiva nyapātayat
a durmukhaḥ sahadevaṃ tu pratyudyāya mahābalam
c vivyādha śaravarṣeṇa yatamānaṃ mahāhave
a sahadevas tato vīro durmukhasya mahāhave
c śareṇa bhṛśatīkṣṇena pātayām āsa sārathim
a tāv anyonyaṃ samāsādya samare yuddhadurmadau
c trāsayetāṃ śarair ghoraiḥ kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇau
a yudhiṣṭhiraḥ svayaṃ rājā madrarājānam abhyayāt
b śalyam abhyardayām āsa mahābalaparākramam
c tasya madrādhipaś cāpaṃ dvidhā ciccheda māriṣa
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c anyat kārmukam ādāya vegavad balavattaram
a tato madreśvaraṃ rājā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c chādayām āsa saṃkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato droṇam abhyadravata bhārata
c tasya droṇaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ parāsukaraṇaṃ dṛḍham
e tridhā ciccheda samare yatamānasya kārmukam
a śaraṃ caiva mahāghoraṃ kāladaṇḍam ivāparam
c preṣayām āsa samare so 'sya kāye nyamajjata
a athānyad dhanur ādāya sāyakāṃś ca caturdaśa
c droṇaṃ drupadaputras tu prativivyādha saṃyuge
e tāv anyonyaṃ susaṃkruddhau cakratuḥ subhṛśaṃ raṇam
a saumadattiṃ raṇe śaṅkho rabhasaṃ rabhaso yudhi
c pratyudyayau mahārāja tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a tasya vai dakṣiṇaṃ vīro nirbibheda raṇe bhujam
c saumadattis tathā śaṅkhaṃ jatrudeśe samāhanat
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
c dṛptayoḥ samare tūrṇaṃ vṛtravāsavayor iva
a bāhlīkaṃ tu raṇe kruddhaṃ kruddharūpo viśāṃ pate
c abhyadravad ameyātmā dhṛṣṭaketur mahārathaḥ
a bāhlīkas tu tato rājan dhṛṣṭaketum amarṣaṇam
c śarair bahubhir ānarchat siṃhanādam athānadat
a cedirājas tu saṃkruddho bāhlīkaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyādha samare tūrṇaṃ matto mattam iva dvipam
a tau tatra samare kruddhau nardantau ca muhur muhuḥ
c samīyatuḥ susaṃkruddhāv aṅgārakabudhāv iva
a rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ krūrakarmā ghaṭotkacaḥ
c alambusaṃ pratyudiyād balaṃ śakra ivāhave
a ghaṭotkacas tu saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahābalam
c navatyā sāyakais tīkṣṇair dārayām āsa bhārata
a alambusas tu samare bhaimaseniṃ mahābalam
c bahudhā vārayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a vyabhrājetāṃ tatas tau tu saṃyuge śaravikṣatau
c yathā devāsure yuddhe balaśakrau mahābalau
a śikhaṇḍī samare rājan drauṇim abhyudyayau balī
c aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddhaḥ śikhaṇḍinam avasthitam
a nārācena sutīkṣṇena bhṛśaṃ viddhvā vyakampayat
c śikhaṇḍy api tato rājan droṇaputram atāḍayat
a sāyakena supītena tīkṣṇena niśitena ca
c tau jaghnatus tadānyonyaṃ śarair bahuvidhair mṛdhe
a bhagadattaṃ raṇe śūraṃ virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
c abhyayāt tvarito rājaṃs tato yuddham avartata
a virāṭo bhagadattena śaravarṣeṇa tāḍitaḥ
c abhyavarṣat susaṃkruddho megho vṛṣṭyā ivācalam
a bhagadattas tatas tūrṇaṃ virāṭaṃ pṛthivīpatim
c chādayām āsa samare meghaḥ sūryam ivoditam
a bṛhatkṣatraṃ tu kaikeyaṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvato yayau
c taṃ kṛpaḥ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata
a gautamaṃ kekayaḥ kruddhaḥ śaravṛṣṭyābhyapūrayat
c tāv anyonyaṃ hayān hatvā dhanuṣī vinikṛtya vai
a virathāv asiyuddhāya samīyatur amarṣaṇau
c tayos tad abhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇam
a drupadas tu tato rājā saindhavaṃ vai jayadratham
c abhyudyayau saṃprahṛṣṭo hṛṣṭarūpaṃ paraṃtapa
a tataḥ saindhavako rājā drupadaṃ viśikhais tribhiḥ
c tāḍayām āsa samare sa ca taṃ pratyavidhyata
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇam
c īkṣitṛprītijananaṃ śukrāṅgārakayor iva
a vikarṇas tu sutas tubhyaṃ sutasomaṃ mahābalam
c abhyayāj javanair aśvais tato yuddham avartata
a vikarṇaḥ sutasomaṃ tu viddhvā nākampayac charaiḥ
c sutasomo vikarṇaṃ ca tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a suśarmāṇaṃ naravyāghraṃ cekitāno mahārathaḥ
c abhyadravat susaṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍavārthe parākramī
a suśarmā tu mahārāja cekitānaṃ mahāratham
c mahatā śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a cekitāno 'pi saṃrabdhaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ mahāhave
c prācchādayat tam iṣubhir mahāmegha ivācalam
a śakuniḥ prativindhyaṃ tu parākrāntaṃ parākramī
c abhyadravata rājendra matto mattam iva dvipam
a yaudhiṣṭhiras tu saṃkruddhaḥ saubalaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vyadārayata saṃgrāme maghavān iva dānavam
a śakuniḥ prativindhyaṃ tu pratividhyantam āhave
c vyadārayan mahāprājñaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a sudakṣiṇaṃ tu rājendra kāmbojānāṃ mahāratham
c śrutakarmā parākrāntam abhyadravata saṃyuge
a sudakṣiṇas tu samare sāhadeviṃ mahāratham
c viddhvā nākampayata vai mainākam iva parvatam
a śrutakarmā tataḥ kruddhaḥ kāmbojānāṃ mahāratham
c śarair bahubhir ānarchad dārayann iva sarvaśaḥ
a irāvān atha saṃkruddhaḥ śrutāyuṣam amarṣaṇam
c pratyudyayau raṇe yatto yattarūpataraṃ tataḥ
a ārjunis tasya samare hayān hatvā mahārathaḥ
c nanāda sumahan nādaṃ tat sainyaṃ pratyapūrayat
a śrutāyus tv atha saṃkruddhaḥ phālguneḥ samare hayān
c nijaghāna gadāgreṇa tato yuddham avartata
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau kuntibhojaṃ mahāratham
c sasenaṃ sasutaṃ vīraṃ saṃsasajjatur āhave
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma āvantyānāṃ parākramam
c yad ayudhyan sthirā bhūtvā mahatyā senayā saha
a anuvindas tu gadayā kuntibhojam atāḍayat
c kuntibhojas tatas tūrṇaṃ śaravrātair avākirat
a kuntibhojasutaś cāpi vindaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
c sa ca taṃ prativivyādha tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca gāndhārān pañca māriṣa
c sasainyās te sasainyāṃś ca yodhayām āsur āhave
a vīrabāhuś ca te putro vairāṭiṃ rathasattamam
c uttaraṃ yodhayām āsa vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d ulūkaṃ tu śatānīkaḥ śarair bahubhir āvṛṇot
e uttaraś cāpi taṃ dhīraṃ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a cedirāṭ samare rājann ulūkaṃ samabhidravat
b tathaiva śaravarṣeṇa ulūkaṃ samavidhyata
c ulūkaś cāpi taṃ bāṇair niśitair lomavāhibhiḥ
a tayor yuddhaṃ samabhavad ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
c dārayetāṃ susaṃkruddhāv anyonyam aparājitau
d tathaiva cedirājo 'pi ulūkaṃ pratyavidhyata
a evaṃ dvaṃdvasahasrāṇi rathavāraṇavājinām
c padātīnāṃ ca samare tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkulam
a muhūrtam iva tad yuddham āsīn madhuradarśanam
c tata unmattavad rājan na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a gajo gajena samare rathī ca rathinaṃ yayau
c aśvo 'śvaṃ samabhipretya padātiś ca padātinam
a tato yuddhaṃ sudurdharṣaṃ vyākulaṃ samapadyata
c śūrāṇāṃ samare tatra samāsādya parasparam
a tatra devarṣayaḥ siddhāś cāraṇāś ca samāgatāḥ
c praikṣanta tad raṇaṃ ghoraṃ devāsuraraṇopamam
a tato dantisahasrāṇi rathānāṃ cāpi māriṣa
c aśvaughāḥ puruṣaughāś ca viparītaṃ samāyayuḥ
a tatra tatraiva dṛśyante rathavāraṇapattayaḥ
c sādinaś ca naravyāghra yudhyamānā muhur muhuḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a rājañ śatasahasrāṇi tatra tatra tadā tadā
c nirmaryādaṃ prayuddhāni tat te vakṣyāmi bhārata
a na putraḥ pitaraṃ jajñe na pitā putram aurasam
c na bhrātā bhrātaraṃ tatra svasrīyaṃ na ca mātulaḥ
a mātulaṃ na ca svasrīyo na sakhāyaṃ sakhā tathā
c āviṣṭā iva yudhyante pāṇḍavāḥ kurubhiḥ saha
a rathānīkaṃ naravyāghrāḥ ke cid abhyapatan rathaiḥ
c abhajyanta yugair eva yugāni bharatarṣabha
a ratheṣāś ca ratheṣābhiḥ kūbarā rathakūbaraiḥ
c saṃhatāḥ saṃhataiḥ ke cit parasparajighāṃsavaḥ
a na śekuś calituṃ ke cit saṃnipatya rathā rathaiḥ
c prabhinnās tu mahākāyāḥ saṃnipatya gajā gajaiḥ
a bahudhādārayan kruddhā viṣāṇair itaretaram
c satomarapatākaiś ca vāraṇāḥ paravāraṇaiḥ
a abhisṛtya mahārāja vegavadbhir mahāgajaiḥ
c dantair abhihatās tatra cukruśuḥ paramāturāḥ
a abhinītāś ca śikṣābhis tottrāṅkuśasamāhatāḥ
c suprabhinnāḥ prabhinnānāṃ saṃmukhābhimukhā yayuḥ
a prabhinnair api saṃsaktāḥ ke cit tatra mahāgajāḥ
c krauñcavan ninadaṃ muktvā prādravanta tatas tataḥ
a samyak praṇītā nāgāś ca prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥ
c ṛṣṭitomaranārācair nirviddhā varavāraṇāḥ
a vinedur bhinnamarmāṇo nipetuś ca gatāsavaḥ
c prādravanta diśaḥ ke cin nadanto bhairavān ravān
a gajānāṃ pādarakṣās tu vyūḍhoraskāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c ṛṣṭibhiś ca dhanurbhiś ca vimalaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
a gadābhir musalaiś caiva bhiṇḍipālaiḥ satomaraiḥ
c āyasaiḥ parighaiś caiva nistriṃśair vimalaiḥ śitaiḥ
a pragṛhītaiḥ susaṃrabdhā dhāvamānās tatas tataḥ
c vyadṛśyanta mahārāja parasparajighāṃsavaḥ
a rājamānāś ca nistriṃśāḥ saṃsiktā naraśoṇitaiḥ
c pratyadṛśyanta śūrāṇām anyonyam abhidhāvatām
a avakṣiptāvadhūtānām asīnāṃ vīrabāhubhiḥ
c saṃjajñe tumulaḥ śabdaḥ patatāṃ paramarmasu
a gadāmusalarugṇānāṃ bhinnānāṃ ca varāsibhiḥ
c dantidantāv abhinnānāṃ mṛditānāṃ ca dantibhiḥ
a tatra tatra naraughāṇāṃ krośatām itaretaram
c śuśruvur dāruṇā vācaḥ pretānām iva bhārata
a hayair api hayārohāś cāmarāpīḍadhāribhiḥ
c haṃsair iva mahāvegair anyonyam abhidudruvuḥ
a tair vimuktā mahāprāsā jāmbūnadavibhūṣaṇāḥ
c āśugā vimalās tīkṣṇāḥ saṃpetur bhujagopamāḥ
a aśvair agryajavaiḥ ke cid āplutya mahato rathān
c śirāṃsy ādadire vīrā rathinām aśvasādinaḥ
a bahūn api hayārohān bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c rathī jaghāna saṃprāpya bāṇagocaram āgatān
a nagameghapratīkāśāś cākṣipya turagān gajāḥ
c pādair evāvamṛdnanta mattāḥ kanakabhūṣaṇāḥ
a pāṭyamāneṣu kumbheṣu pārśveṣv api ca vāraṇāḥ
c prāsair vinihatāḥ ke cid vineduḥ paramāturāḥ
a sāśvārohān hayān ke cid unmathya varavāraṇāḥ
c sahasā cikṣipus tatra saṃkule bhairave sati
a sāśvārohān viṣāṇāgrair utkṣipya turagān dvipāḥ
c rathaughān avamṛdnantaḥ sadhvajān paricakramuḥ
a puṃstvād abhimadatvāc ca ke cid atra mahāgajāḥ
c sāśvārohān hayāñ jaghnuḥ karaiḥ sacaraṇais tathā
d aśvārohaiś ca samare hastisādibhir eva ca
a ke cid ākṣipya kariṇaḥ sāśvān api rathān karaiḥ
c vikarṣanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ samīyuḥ sarvaśabdagāḥ
d pratimāneṣu gātreṣu pārśveṣv abhi ca vāraṇān
d muktās tu rathibhir bāṇā rukmapuṅkhāḥ sutejanāḥ
d te nipetur akuṇṭhāgrā nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu ca
a āśugā vimalās tīkṣṇāḥ saṃpetur bhujagopamāḥ
c narāśvakāyān nirbhidya lauhāni kavacāni ca
a nipetur vimalāḥ śaktyo vīrabāhubhir arpitāḥ
c maholkāpratimā ghorās tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a dvīpicarmāvanaddhaiś ca vyāghracarmaśayair api
c vikośair vimalaiḥ khaḍgair abhijaghnuḥ parān raṇe
a abhiplutam abhikruddham ekapārśvāvadāritam
c vidarśayantaḥ saṃpetuḥ khaḍgacarmaparaśvadhaiḥ
a śaktibhir dāritāḥ ke cit saṃchinnāś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
c hastibhir mṛditāḥ ke cit kṣuṇṇāś cānye turaṃgamaiḥ
a rathaneminikṛttāś ca nikṛttā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vikrośanti narā rājaṃs tatra tatra sma bāndhavān
a putrān anye pitṝn anye bhrātṝṃś ca saha bāndhavaiḥ
c mātulān bhāgineyāṃś ca parān api ca saṃyuge
a vikīrṇāntrāḥ subahavo bhagnasakthāś ca bhārata
c bāhubhiḥ subhujācchinnaiḥ pārśveṣu ca vidāritāḥ
e krandantaḥ samadṛśyanta tṛṣitā jīvitepsavaḥ
a tṛṣṇāparigatāḥ ke cid alpasattvā viśāṃ pate
c bhūmau nipatitāḥ saṃkhye jalam eva yayācire
a rudhiraughapariklinnāḥ kliśyamānāś ca bhārata
c vyanindan bhṛśam ātmānaṃ tava putrāṃś ca saṃgatān
a apare kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ kṛtavairāḥ parasparam
c naiva śastraṃ vimuñcanti naiva krandanti māriṣa
e tarjayanti ca saṃhṛṣṭās tatra tatra parasparam
a nirdaśya daśanaiś cāpi krodhāt svadaśanac chadān
c bhrukuṭīkuṭilair vaktraiḥ prekṣante ca parasparam
d tarjayitvā susaṃhṛṣṭā yāvat prāṇasya dhāraṇam
a apare kliśyamānās tu vraṇārtāḥ śarapīḍitāḥ
c niṣkūjāḥ samapadyanta dṛḍhasattvā mahābalāḥ
a anye tu virathāḥ śūrā ratham anyasya saṃyuge
c prārthayānā nipatitāḥ saṃkṣuṇṇā varavāraṇaiḥ
e aśobhanta mahārāja puṣpitā iva kiṃśukāḥ
a saṃbabhūvur anīkeṣu bahavo bhairavasvanāḥ
c vartamāne mahābhīme tasmin vīravarakṣaye
a ahanat tu pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ raṇe
c svasrīyo mātulaṃ cāpi svasrīyaṃ cāpi mātulaḥ
a sakhāyaṃ ca sakhā rājan saṃbandhī bāndhavaṃ tathā
c evaṃ yuyudhire tatra kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
a vartamāne bhaye tasmin nirmaryāde mahāhave
c bhīṣmam āsādya pārthānāṃ vāhinī samakampata
a ketunā pañcatāreṇa tālena bharatarṣabha
c rājatena mahābāhur ucchritena mahārathe
e babhau bhīṣmas tadā rājaṃś candramā iva meruṇā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a gatapūrvāhṇabhūyiṣṭhe tasminn ahani dāruṇe
c vartamāne mahāraudre mahāvīravarakṣaye
a durmukhaḥ kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyo viviṃśatiḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ jugupur āsādya tava putreṇa coditāḥ
a etair atirathair guptaḥ pañcabhir bharatarṣabha
c pāṇḍavānām anīkāni vijagāhe mahārathaḥ
a cedikāśikarūṣeṣu pāñcāleṣu ca bhārata
c bhīṣmasya bahudhā tālaś caran ketur adṛśyata
a śirāṃsi ca tadā bhīṣmo bāhūṃś cāpi sahāyudhān
b dhanūṃṣi rathināṃ bhīṣmaḥ sotsedhāni śirāṃsi ca
b bāhūn api tathā corūn rathāṃś ca vipuladhvajān
c nicakarta mahāvegair bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d ekaikena tu mātaṅgā nārācena mahātmanā
d tāḍitāḥ sahasā jagmuḥ pṛthivīṃ parvatopamāḥ
a nṛtyato rathamārgeṣu bhīṣmasya bharatarṣabha
c ke cid ārtasvaraṃ cakrur nāgā marmaṇi tāḍitāḥ
d durādharṣas tu śatrūṇāṃ manāṃsi samakampayat
d hayāṃś ca sahayārohān pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
d sa rathena maheṣvāso vicaran bahudhā balī
d maṇḍalāni ca vīthīś ca gomūtrāṇi ca bhārata
d anyāṃś ca subahūn mārgān rathena rathakovidaḥ
d vismāpayañ śatrusaṃghān vyacaraj jāhnavīsutaḥ
a abhimanyuḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ piśaṅgais turagottamaiḥ
c saṃyuktaṃ ratham āsthāya prāyād bhīṣmarathaṃ prati
a jāmbūnadavicitreṇa karṇikāreṇa ketunā
b abhyavarṣac chalyamukhān rathān satālaketunā
c abhyavarṣata bhīṣmaṃ ca tāṃś caiva rathasattamān
a sa tālaketos tīkṣṇena ketum āhatya patriṇā
c bhīṣmeṇa yuyudhe vīras tasya cānucaraiḥ saha
a kṛtavarmāṇam ekena śalyaṃ pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
c viddhvā navabhir ānarchac chitāgraiḥ prapitāmaham
a pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena samyak praṇihitena ca
c dhvajam ekena vivyādha jāmbūnadavibhūṣitam
a durmukhasya tu bhallena sarvāvaraṇabhedinā
c jahāra sāratheḥ kāyāc chiraḥ saṃnataparvaṇā
d viviṃśatis tribhir bāṇaiḥ sarvāvaraṇabhedibhiḥ
a dhanuś ciccheda bhallena kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
c kṛpasya niśitāgreṇa tāṃś ca tīkṣṇamukhaiḥ śaraiḥ
a jaghāna paramakruddho nṛtyann iva mahārathaḥ
c tasya lāghavam udvīkṣya tutuṣur devatā api
a labdhalakṣyatayā karṣṇeḥ sarve bhīṣmamukhā rathāḥ
c sattvavantam amanyanta sākṣād iva dhanaṃjayam
a tasya lāghavamārgastham alātasadṛśaprabham
c diśaḥ paryapatac cāpaṃ gāṇḍīvam iva ghoṣavat
a tam āsādya mahāvegair bhīṣmo navabhir āśugaiḥ
c vivyādha samare tūrṇam ārjuniṃ paravīrahā
a dhvajaṃ cāsya tribhir bhallaiś ciccheda paramaujasaḥ
c sārathiṃ ca tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna yatavrataḥ
a tathaiva kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyaś ca māriṣa
b viviṃśatis tathā rājan sarve viddhvā mahārathāḥ
c viddhvā nākampayat kārṣṇiṃ mainākam iva parvatam
a sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūro dhārtarāṣṭrair mahārathaiḥ
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi kārṣṇiḥ pañcarathān prati
a tatas teṣāṃ mahāstrāṇi saṃvārya śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
c nanāda balavān kārṣṇir bhīṣmāya visṛjañ śarān
a tatrāsya sumahad rājan bāhvor balam adṛśyata
c yatamānasya samare bhīṣmam ardayataḥ śaraiḥ
a parākrāntasya tasyaiva bhīṣmo 'pi prāhiṇoc charān
c sa tāṃś ciccheda samare bhīṣmacāpacyutāñ śarān
a tato dhvajam amogheṣur bhīṣmasya navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c ciccheda samare vīras tata uccukruśur janāḥ
a sa rājato mahāskandhas tālo hemavibhūṣitaḥ
c saubhadraviśikhaiś chinnaḥ papāta bhuvi bhārata
a dhvajaṃ saubhadraviśikhaiḥ patitaṃ bharatarṣabha
c dṛṣṭvā bhīmo 'nadad dhṛṣṭaḥ saubhadram abhiharṣayan
a atha bhīṣmo mahāstrāṇi divyāni ca bahūni ca
c prāduścakre mahāraudraḥ kṣaṇe tasmin mahābalaḥ
a tataḥ śatasahasreṇa saubhadraṃ prapitāmahaḥ
c avākirad ameyātmā śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
a tato daśa maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c rakṣārtham abhyadhāvanta saubhadraṃ tvaritā rathaiḥ
a virāṭaḥ saha putreṇa dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c bhīmaś ca kekayāś caiva sātyakiś ca viśāṃ pate
a javenāpatatāṃ teṣāṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo raṇe
c pāñcālyaṃ tribhir ānarchat sātyakiṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena kṣureṇa niśitena ca
c dhvajam ekena ciccheda bhīmasenasya patriṇā
a jāmbūnadamayaḥ ketuḥ kesarī narasattama
c papāta bhīmasenasya bhīṣmeṇa mathito rathāt
a bhīmasenas tribhir viddhvā bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ raṇe
c kṛpam ekena vivyādha kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥ
a pragṛhītāgrahastena vairāṭir api dantinā
c abhyadravata rājānaṃ madrādhipatim uttaraḥ
a tasya vāraṇarājasya javenāpatato rathī
c śalyo nivārayām āsa vegam apratimaṃ raṇe
a tasya kruddhaḥ sa nāgendro bṛhataḥ sādhuvāhinaḥ
c padā yugam adhiṣṭhāya jaghāna caturo hayān
a sa hatāśve rathe tiṣṭhan madrādhipatir āyasīm
c uttarāntakarīṃ śaktiṃ cikṣepa bhujagopamām
a tayā bhinnatanutrāṇaḥ praviśya vipulaṃ tamaḥ
c sa papāta gajaskandhāt pramuktāṅkuśatomaraḥ
a samādāya ca śalyo 'sim avaplutya rathottamāt
c vāraṇendrasya vikramya cicchedātha mahākaram
a bhinnamarmā śaravrātaiś chinnahastaḥ sa vāraṇaḥ
c bhīmam ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā papāta ca mamāra ca
a etad īdṛśakaṃ kṛtvā madrarājo mahārathaḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ bhāsvaraṃ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
a uttaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā vairāṭir bhrātaraṃ śubham
c kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śalyam avasthitam
d śvetaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla haviṣā havyavāḍ iva
d sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ śakracāpopamaṃ balī
d abhyadhāvaj jighāṃsan vai śalyaṃ madrādhipaṃ balī
d mahatā rathavaṃśena samantāt parivāritaḥ
d muñcan bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ prāyāc chalyarathaṃ prati
d tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya mattavāraṇavikramam
d tāvakānāṃ rathāḥ sapta samantāt paryavārayan
d madrarājam abhīpsanto mṛtyor daṃṣṭrāntaraṃ gatam
d bṛhadbalaś ca kausalyo jayatsenaś ca māgadhaḥ
d tathā rukmaratho rājañ śalyaputraḥ pratāpavān
d vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
d bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥ
d nānāvarṇavicitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca mahātmanām
d visphāritāni dṛśyante toyadeṣv iva vidyutaḥ
d te tu bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ śvetamūrdhany apātayan
d nidāghānte 'niloddhūtā meghā iva nage jalam
d tataḥ kruddho maheṣvāsaḥ saptabhallaiḥ sutejanaiḥ
d dhanūṃṣi teṣām ācchidya mamarda pṛtanāpatiḥ
d nikṛttāny eva tāni sma samadṛśyanta bhārata
d tatas te tu nimeṣārdhāt pratyapadyan dhanūṃṣi ca
d sapta caiva pṛṣatkāṃś ca śvetasyoparyapātayan
d tataḥ punar ameyātmā bhallaiḥ saptabhir āśugaiḥ
d nicakarta mahābāhus teṣāṃ cāpāni dhanvinām
d te nikṛttamahācāpās tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥ
d rathaśaktīḥ parāmṛśya vinedur bhairavān ravān
d anvayur bharataśreṣṭha sapta śvetarathaṃ prati
d tatas tā jvalitāḥ sapta mahendrāśaninisvanāḥ
d aprāptāḥ saptabhir bhallaiś ciccheda paramāstravit
d tataḥ samādāya śaraṃ sarvakāyavidāraṇam
d prāhiṇod bharataśreṣṭha śveto rukmarathaṃ prati
d tasya dehe nipatito bāṇo vajrātigo mahān
d tato rukmaratho rājan sāyakena dṛḍhāhataḥ
d niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalaṃ cāviśan mahat
d taṃ visaṃjñaṃ vimanasaṃ tvaramāṇas tu sārathiḥ
d apovāha susaṃbhrāntaḥ sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
d tato 'nyān ṣaṭ samādāya śveto hemavibhūṣitān
d teṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ mahābāhur dhvajaśīrṣāṇy apātayat
d hayāṃś ca teṣāṃ nirbhidya sārathīṃś ca paraṃtapa
d śaraiś caitān samākīrya prāyāc chalyarathaṃ prati
d tato halahalāśabdas tava sainyeṣu bhārata
d dṛṣṭvā senāpatiṃ tūrṇaṃ yāntaṃ śalyarathaṃ prati
d tato bhīṣmaṃ puraskṛtya tava putro mahābalaḥ
d vṛtas tu sarvasainyena prāyāc chvetarathaṃ prati
d mṛtyor āsyam anuprāptaṃ madrarājam amocayat
d tato yuddhaṃ samabhavat tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
d tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca vyatiṣiktarathadvipam
d saubhadre bhīmasene ca sātyakau ca mahārathe
d kaikeye ca virāṭe ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca pārṣate
d eteṣu narasiṃheṣu cedimatsyeṣu caiva ha
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
d evaṃ śvete maheṣvāse prāpte śalyarathaṃ prati
d kuravaḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca kim akurvata saṃjaya
d saṃjaya uvāca
d bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ kiṃ vā tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
d rājañ śatasahasrāṇi tataḥ kṣatriyapuṃgavāḥ
d śvetaṃ senāpatiṃ śūraṃ puraskṛtya mahārathāḥ
d rājño balaṃ darśayantas tava putrasya bhārata
d śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya trātum aicchan mahārathāḥ
d abhyavartanta bhīṣmasya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam
d jighāṃsantaṃ yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tadāsīt tumulaṃ mahat
d tat te 'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāvaiśasam acyuta
d tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca yathā yuddham avartata
d tatrākarod rathopasthāñ śūnyāñ śāṃtanavo bahūn
d prākṛntad uttamāṅgāni śarair ārchad rathottamān
d samāvṛṇoc charair arkam arkatulyapratāpavān
d nudan samantāt samare ravir udyan yathā tamaḥ
d tenājau preṣitā rājañ śarāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
d kṣatriyāntakarāḥ saṃkhye mahāvegā mahābalāḥ
d śirāṃsi pātayām āsur vīrāṇāṃ śataśo raṇe
d gajān kaṇṭakasaṃnāhān vajreṇeva śiloccayān
d rathā ratheṣu saṃsaktā vyadṛśanta viśāṃ pate
d eke rathaṃ paryavahaṃs turagāḥ saturaṃgamam
d yuvānaṃ nihataṃ vīraṃ lambamānaṃ sakārmukam
d udīrṇāś ca hayā rājan vahantas tatra tatra ha
d baddhakhaḍganiṣaṅgāś ca vidhvastaśiraso hatāḥ
d śataśaḥ patitā bhūmau vīraśayyāsu śerate
d paraspareṇa dhāvantaḥ patitāḥ punar utthitāḥ
d utthāya ca pradhāvanto dvaṃdvayuddham avāpnuvan
d pīḍitāḥ punar anyonyaṃ luṭhanto raṇamūrdhani
d sacāpān saniṣaṅgāṃś ca jātarūpapariṣkṛtān
d visrabdhahatavīrāś ca śataśaḥ paripīḍitāḥ
d tena tenābhyadhāvanta visṛjantaś ca bhārata
d matto gajaḥ paryavartad dhayāṃś ca hatasādinaḥ
d sarathā rathinaś cāpi vimṛdnantaḥ samantataḥ
d syandanād apatat kaś cin nihato 'nyena sāyakaiḥ
d hatasārathir apy uccaiḥ papāta kāṣṭhavad rathaḥ
d yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme vyūḍhe rajasi cotthite
d dhanuḥkūjitavijñānaṃ tatrāsīt pratiyudhyataḥ
d gātrasparśena yodhānāṃ vyajñāsta paripanthinam
d yudhyamānaṃ śarai rājan siñjinī dhvajinī ravāt
d anyonyaṃ vīrasaṃśabdo nāśrūyata bhaṭaiḥ kṛtaḥ
d śabdāyamāne saṃgrāme paṭahe karṇadāriṇi
d yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme kurvataḥ pauruṣaṃ svakam
d nāśrauṣīn nāmagotroktiṃ kīrtanaṃ ca parasparam
d bhīṣmacāpacyutair bāṇair ārtānāṃ yudhyatāṃ mṛdhe
d paraspareṣāṃ vīrāṇāṃ manāṃsi samakampayan
d tasminn atyākule yuddhe dāruṇe lomaharṣaṇe
d pitā putraṃ ca samare nābhijānāti kaś cana
d cakre bhagne yuge chinne eko dhuryo hayo hataḥ
d ākṣiptaḥ syandanād vīraḥ sasārathir ajihmagaiḥ
d evaṃ ca samare sarve vīrāś ca virathīkṛtāḥ
d tena tena sma dṛśyante dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ
d gajo hataḥ śiraś chinnaṃ marma bhinnaṃ hayo hataḥ
d ahataḥ ko 'pi naivāsīd bhīṣme nighnati śātravān
d śvetaḥ kurūṇām akarot svayaṃ tasmin mahāhave
d rājaputrān rathodārān avadhīc chatasaṃghaśaḥ
d ciccheda rathināṃ bāṇaiḥ śirāṃsi bharatarṣabha
d sāṅgadā bāhavaś caiva dhanūṃṣi ca samantataḥ
d ratheṣāṃ rathacakrāṇi tūṇīrāṇi yugāni ca
d chatrāṇi ca mahārhāṇi patākāś ca viśāṃ pate
d hayaughāś ca rathaughāś ca naraughāś caiva bhārata
d vāraṇāḥ śataśaś caiva hatāḥ śvetena bhārata
d vayaṃ śvetabhayād bhītā vihāya rathasattamam
d avaśiṣṭās tathā paścād vibhuṃ paśyāma dhṛṣṇavaḥ
d śarapātam apakramya kuravaḥ kurunandana
d bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yuddhe sthitāḥ paśyāma sarvaśaḥ
d adīno dīnasamaye bhīṣmo 'smākaṃ mahāhave
d ekas tasthau naravyāghro girir merur ivācalaḥ
d ādadāna iva prāṇān savitā śiśirātyaye
d gabhastibhir ivādityas tasthau śaramarīcimān
d sa mumoca maheṣvāsaḥ śarasaṃghān anekaśaḥ
d nighnann amitrān samare vajrapāṇir ivāsurān
d te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa prajahus taṃ mahābalam
d svayūthād iva te yūthān muktaṃ bhūmiṣu dāruṇam
d tam ekam upalabhyaiko hṛṣṭaḥ puṣṭaḥ paraṃtapa
d duryodhanapriye yuktaḥ pāṇḍavān pariśocayan
d jīvitaṃ dustyajaṃ tyaktvā bhayaṃ ca sumahāhave
d pātayām āsa sainyāni pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ pate
d praharantam anīkāni pitā devavratas tava
d dṛṣṭvā senāpatiṃ bhīṣmas tvaritaḥ śvetam abhyayāt
d sa bhīṣmaṃ śarajālena mahatā samavākirat
d śvetaṃ cāpi tathā bhīṣmaḥ śaraughaiḥ samavākirat
d tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau mattāv iva mahādvipau
d vyāghrāv iva susaṃrabdhāv anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
d astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya tatas tau puruṣarṣabhau
d bhīṣmaḥ śvetaś ca yuyudhe parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
d ekāhnā nirdahed bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
d śaraiḥ paramasaṃkruddho yadi śveto na pālayet
d pitāmahaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā śvetena vimukhīkṛtam
d praharṣaṃ pāṇḍavā jagmuḥ putras te vimanābhavat
d tato duryodhanaḥ kruddhaḥ pārthivaiḥ parivāritaḥ
d sasainyaḥ pāṇḍavānīkam abhyadravata saṃyuge
d durmukhaḥ kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyo viśāṃ pate
d bhīṣmaṃ jugupur āsādya tava putreṇa coditāḥ
d dṛṣṭvā tu pārthivaiḥ sarvair duryodhanapurogamaiḥ
d pāṇḍavānām anīkāni vadhyamānāni saṃyuge
d śveto gāṅgeyam utsṛjya tava putrasya vāhinīm
d nāśayām āsa vegena vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasā
d drāvayitvā camūṃ rājan vairāṭiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
d āpatat sahasā bhūyo yatra bhīṣmo vyavasthitaḥ
d tau tatropagatau rājañ śaradīptau mahābalau
d ayudhyetāṃ mahātmānau yathobhau vṛtravāsavau
d anyonyaṃ tu mahārāja parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
d nigṛhya kārmukaṃ śveto bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥ
d parākramaṃ tatas tasya parākramya parākramī
d tarasā vārayām āsa matto mattam iva dvipam
d śvetaḥ śāṃtanavaṃ bhūyaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d vivyādha pañcaviṃśatyā tad adbhutam ivābhavat
d taṃ pratyavidhyad daśabhir bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadā
d sa viddhas tena balavān nākampata yathācalaḥ
d vairāṭiḥ samare kruddho bhṛśam āyamya kārmukam
d ājaghāna tato bhīṣmaṃ śvetaḥ kṣatriyanandanaḥ
d saṃprahasya tataḥ śvetaḥ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihan
d dhanuś ciccheda bhīṣmasya navabhir daśadhā śaraiḥ
d saṃdhāya viśikhaṃ caiva śaraṃ lomapravāhinam
d unmamātha tatas tālaṃ dhvajaśīrṣaṃ mahātmanaḥ
d ketuṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya tanayās tava
d hataṃ bhīṣmam amanyanta śvetasya vaśam āgatam
d pāṇḍavāś cāpi saṃhṛṣṭā dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yutāḥ
d bhīṣmasya patitaṃ ketuṃ dṛṣṭvā tālaṃ mahātmanaḥ
d tato duryodhanaḥ krodhāt svam anīkam acodayat
d yatnād bhīṣmaṃ parīpsadhvaṃ rakṣamāṇāḥ samantataḥ
d mā naḥ prapaśyamānānāṃ śvetān mṛtyum avāpsyati
d bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ śūras tathā satyaṃ bravīmi vaḥ
d rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥ
d balena caturaṅgeṇa gāṅgeyam anvapālayan
d bāhlīkaḥ kṛtavarmā ca śalaḥ śalyaś ca bhārata
d jalasaṃdho vikarṇaś ca citraseno viviṃśatiḥ
d tvaramāṇās tvarākāle parivārya samantataḥ
d śastravṛṣṭiṃ sutumulāṃ śvetasyopary apātayan
d tān kruddho niśitair bāṇais tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
d avārayad ameyātmā darśayan pāṇilāghavam
d sa nivārya tu tān sarvān kesarī kuñjarān iva
d mahatā śaravarṣeṇa bhīṣmasya dhanur ācchinat
d tato 'nyad dhanur ādāya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhi
d śvetaṃ vivyādha rājendra kaṅkapatraiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tataḥ senāpatiḥ kruddho bhīṣmaṃ bahubhir āyasaiḥ
d vivyādha samare rājan sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
d tataḥ pravyathito rājā bhīṣmaṃ dṛṣṭvā nivāritam
d pravīraṃ sarvalokasya śvetena yudhi vai tadā
d niṣṭhānakaś ca sumahāṃs tava sainyasya cābhavat
d taṃ vīraṃ vāritaṃ dṛṣṭvā śvetena śaravikṣatam
d hataṃ śvetena manyante śvetasya vaśam āgatam
d tataḥ krodhavaśaṃ prāptaḥ pitā devavratas tava
d dhvajam unmathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ ca senāṃ nivāritām
d śvetaṃ prati mahārāja vyasṛjat sāyakān bahūn
d tān āvārya raṇe śveto bhīṣmasya rathināṃ varaḥ
d dhanuś ciccheda bhallena punar eva pitus tava
d utsṛjya kārmukaṃ rājan gāṅgeyaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
d anyat kārmukam ādāya vipulaṃ balavattaram
d tatra saṃdhāya vipulān bhallān sapta śilāśitān
d caturbhiś ca jaghānāśvāñ śvetasya pṛtanāpateḥ
d dhvajaṃ dvābhyāṃ tu ciccheda saptamena ca sāratheḥ
d śiraś ciccheda bhallena saṃkruddho laghuvikramaḥ
d hatāśvasūtāt sa rathād avaplutya mahābalaḥ
d amarṣavaśam āpanno vyākulaḥ samapadyata
d virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥ
d tāḍayām āsa niśitaiḥ śarasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥ
d sa tāḍyamānaḥ samare bhīṣmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
d svarathe dhanur utsṛjya śaktiṃ jagrāha kāñcanīm
d tataḥ śaktiṃ raṇe śveto jagrāhogrāṃ mahābhayām
d kāladaṇḍopamāṃ ghorāṃ mṛtyor iva svasāṃ śvasan
d abravīc ca tadā śveto bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ raṇe
d tiṣṭhedānīṃ susaṃrabdhaḥ paśya māṃ puruṣo bhava
d evam uktvā maheṣvāso bhīṣmaṃ yudhi parākramī
d tataḥ śaktim ameyātmā cikṣepa bhujagopamām
d pāṇḍavārthe parākrāntas tavānarthaṃ cikīrṣati
d hāhākāro mahān āsīt putrāṇāṃ te viśāṃ pate
d dṛṣṭvā śaktiṃ mahāghorāṃ mṛtyor daṇḍasamaprabhām
d śvetasya karanirmuktāṃ nirmuktoragasaṃnibhām
d apatat sahasā rājan maholkeva nabhastalāt
d jvalantīm antarikṣe tāṃ jvālābhir iva saṃvṛtām
d asaṃbhrāntas tadā rājan pitā devavratas tava
d aṣṭabhir navabhir bhīṣmaḥ śaktiṃ ciccheda patribhiḥ
d utkṛṣṭahemavikṛtāṃ nikṛttāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d uccukruśus tataḥ sarve tāvakā bharatarṣabha
d śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā vairāṭiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
d kālopahatacetās tu kartavyaṃ nābhyajānata
d krodhasaṃmūrchito rājan vairāṭiḥ prahasann iva
d gadāṃ jagrāha saṃhṛṣṭo bhīṣmasya nidhanaṃ prati
d krodhena raktanayano daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
d bhīṣmaṃ samabhidudrāva jalaugha iva parvatam
d tasya vegam asaṃvārya matvā bhīṣmaḥ pratāpavān
d prahāravipramokṣārthaṃ sahasā dharaṇīṃ gataḥ
d śvetaḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo bhrāmayitvā tu tāṃ gadām
d rathe bhīṣmasya cikṣepa yathā devo dhaneśvaraḥ
d tayā bhīṣmanipātinyā sa ratho bhasmasāt kṛtaḥ
d sadhvajaḥ saha sūtena sāśvaḥ sayugabandhuraḥ
d virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhīṣmaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathottamāḥ
d abhyadhāvanta sahitāḥ śalyaprabhṛtayo rathāḥ
d tato 'nyaṃ ratham āsthāya dhanur visphārya durmanāḥ
d śanakair abhyayāc chvetaṃ gāṅgeyaḥ prahasann iva
d etasminn antare bhīṣmaḥ śuśrāva vipulāṃ giram
d ākāśād īritāṃ divyām ātmano hitasaṃbhavām
d bhīṣma bhīṣma mahābāho śīghraṃ yatnaṃ kuruṣva vai
d eṣa hy asya jaye kālo nirdiṣṭo viśvayoninā
d etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ devadūtena bhāṣitam
d saṃprahṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā vadhe tasya mano dadhe
d virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā padātinam
d sahitās tv abhyavartanta parīpsanto mahārathāḥ
d sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
d kaikeyo dhṛṣṭaketuś ca abhimanyuś ca vīryavān
d etān āpatataḥ sarvān droṇaśalyakṛpaiḥ saha
d avārayad ameyātmā vārivegān ivācalaḥ
d sa niruddheṣu sarveṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
d śvetaḥ khaḍgam athākṛṣya bhīṣmasya dhanur ācchinat
d tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ tvaramāṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ
d devadūtavacaḥ śrutvā vadhe tasya mano dadhe
d tataḥ pracāramāṇas tu pitā devavratas tava
d anyat kārmukam ādāya tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
d kṣaṇena sajyam akaroc chakracāpasamaprabham
d pitā te bharataśreṣṭha śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahārathaiḥ
d vṛtaṃ taṃ manujavyāghrair bhīmasenapurogamaiḥ
d abhyavartata gāṅgeyaḥ śvetaṃ senāpatiṃ drutam
d āpatantaṃ tato bhīṣmo bhīmasenaṃ pratāpavān
d ājaghne viśikhaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā senānyaṃ sa mahārathaḥ
d abhimanyuṃ ca samare pitā devavratas tava
d ājaghne bharataśreṣṭhas tribhiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d sātyakiṃ ca śatenājau bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca viṃśatyā kaikeyaṃ cāpi pañcabhiḥ
d tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsān pitā devavratas tava
d vārayitvā śarair ghoraiḥ śvetam evābhidudruve
d tataḥ śaraṃ mṛtyusamaṃ bhārasādhanam uttamam
d vikṛṣya balavān bhīṣmaḥ samādhatta durāsadam
d brahmāstreṇa susaṃyuktaṃ taṃ śaraṃ lomavāhinam
d dadṛśur devagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ
d sa tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā hṛdayaṃ cāmitaujasaḥ
d jagāma dharaṇīṃ bāṇo mahāśanir iva jvalan
d astaṃ gacchan yathādityaḥ prabhām ādāya satvaraḥ
d evaṃ jīvitam ādāya śvetadehāj jagāma ha
d taṃ bhīṣmeṇa naravyāghraṃ tathā vinihataṃ yudhi
d prapatantam apaśyāma gireḥ śṛṅgam iva cyutam
d aśocan pāṇḍavās tatra kṣatriyāś ca mahārathāḥ
d prahṛṣṭāś ca sutās tubhyaṃ kuravaś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
d tato duḥśāsano rājañ śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā nipātitam
d vāditraninadair ghorair nṛtyati sma samantataḥ
d tasmin hate maheṣvāse bhīṣmeṇāhavaśobhinā
d prāvepanta maheṣvāsāḥ śikhaṇḍipramukhā rathāḥ
d tato dhanaṃjayo rājan vārṣṇeyaś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
d avahāraṃ śanaiś cakrur nihate vāhinīpatau
d tato 'vahāraḥ sainyānāṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
d tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nardatāṃ ca muhur muhuḥ
d pārthā vimanaso bhūtvā nyaviśanta mahārathāḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d cintayanto vadhaṃ ghoraṃ dvairathena paraṃtapāḥ
d śvete senāpatau tāta saṃgrāme nihate paraiḥ
d kim akurvan maheṣvāsāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
d senāpatiṃ samākarṇya śvetaṃ yudhi nipātitam
d tadarthaṃ yatatāṃ cāpi pareṣāṃ prapalāyinām
d manaḥ prīṇāti me vākyaṃ jayaṃ saṃjaya śṛṇvataḥ
d pratyupāyaṃ cintayantaḥ sajjanāḥ prasravanti me
d sa hi vīro 'nuraktaś ca vṛddhaḥ kurupatis tadā
d kṛtaṃ vairaṃ sadā tena pituḥ putreṇa dhīmatā
d tasyodvegabhayāc cāpi saṃśritaḥ pāṇḍavān purā
d sarvaṃ balaṃ parityajya durgaṃ saṃśritya tiṣṭhati
d pāṇḍavānāṃ pratāpena durgaṃ deśaṃ niveśya ca
d sapatnān satataṃ bādhann āryavṛttim anuṣṭhitaḥ
d āścaryaṃ vai sadā teṣāṃ purā rājñāṃ sudurmatiḥ
d tato yudhiṣṭhire bhaktaḥ kathaṃ saṃjaya sūditaḥ
d prakṣiptaḥ saṃmataḥ kṣudraḥ putro me puruṣādhamaḥ
d na yuddhaṃ rocayed bhīṣmo na cācāryaḥ kathaṃ cana
d na kṛpo na ca gāndhārī nāhaṃ saṃjaya rocaye
d na vāsudevo vārṣṇeyo dharmarājaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
d na bhīmo nārjunaś caiva na yamau puruṣarṣabhau
d vāryamāṇo mayā nityaṃ gāndhāryā vidureṇa ca
d jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa vyāsena ca mahātmanā
d duryodhano yudhyamāno nityam eva hi saṃjaya
d karṇasya matam āsthāya saubalasya ca pāpakṛt
d duḥśāsanasya ca tathā pāṇḍavān anvasūyata
d tasyāhaṃ vyasanaṃ ghoraṃ manye prāptaṃ tu saṃjaya
d śvetasya ca vināśena bhīṣmasya vijayena ca
d saṃkruddhaḥ kṛṣṇasahitaḥ pārthaḥ kim akarod yudhi
d arjunād dhi bhayaṃ bhūyas tan me tāta na śāmyati
d sa hi śūraś ca kaunteyaḥ kṣiprakārī ca pāṇḍavaḥ
d manye śaraiḥ śarīrāṇi pramathiṣyati vidviṣām
d aindrir indrānujasamo mahendrasadṛśo bale
d amoghakrodhasaṃkalpaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaḥ kim abhūn manaḥ
d tathaiva vedavic chūro jvalanārkasamadyutiḥ
d aindrāstravid ameyātmā prapatan samitiṃjayaḥ
d vajrasaṃsparśarūpāṇām astrāṇāṃ nyāsakāritā
d sa khaḍgākṣepahastas tu ghoṣaṃ cakre mahārathaḥ
d sa saṃjaya mahāprājño drupadasyātmajo balī
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kim akaroc chvete yudhi nipātite
d purā caivāparādhena vadhena ca camūpateḥ
d manye manaḥ prajajvāla pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
d teṣāṃ krodhaṃ cintayaṃs tu ahaḥsu ca niśāsu ca
d saṃjaya uvāca
d na śāntim adhigacchāmi sarvam ācakṣva saṃjaya
d gatapūrvāhṇabhūyiṣṭhe tasminn ahani dāruṇe
d tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca punar yuddham avartata
d śvetaṃ tu nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā virāṭasya camūpatim
d kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śalyam avasthitam
e śaṅkhaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla haviṣā havyavāḍ iva
a sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
c abhyadhāvaj jighāṃsan vai śalyaṃ madrādhipaṃ balī
a mahatā rathavaṃśena samantāt parivāritaḥ
c sṛjan bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ prāyāc chalyarathaṃ prati
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya mattavāraṇavikramam
c tāvakānāṃ rathāḥ sapta samantāt paryavārayan
e madrarājaṃ parīpsanto mṛtyor daṃṣṭrāntaraṃ gatam
a tato bhīṣmo mahābāhur vinadya jalado yathā
c tālamātraṃ dhanur gṛhya śaṅkham abhyadravad raṇe
a tam udyatam udīkṣyātha maheṣvāsaṃ mahābalam
c saṃtrastā pāṇḍavī senā vātavegahateva nauḥ
a tatrārjunaḥ saṃtvaritaḥ śaṅkhasyāsīt puraḥsaraḥ
c bhīṣmād rakṣyo 'yam adyeti tato yuddham avartata
a hāhākāro mahān āsīd yodhānāṃ yudhi yudhyatām
c tejas tejasi saṃpṛktam ity evaṃ vismayaṃ yayuḥ
a atha śalyo gadāpāṇir avatīrya mahārathāt
c śaṅkhasya caturo vāhān ahanad bharatarṣabha
a sa hatāśvād rathāt tūrṇaṃ khaḍgam ādāya vidrutaḥ
c bībhatsoḥ syandanaṃ prāpya tataḥ śāntim avindata
a tato bhīṣmarathāt tūrṇam utpatanti patatriṇaḥ
c yair antarikṣaṃ bhūmiś ca sarvataḥ samavastṛtam
d pāñcālān atha matsyaṃ ca drupadaṃ senayā vṛtam
a pāñcālān atha matsyāṃś ca kekayāṃś ca prabhadrakān
c bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pātayām āsa mārgaṇaiḥ
a utsṛjya samare tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ savyasācinam
c abhyadravata pāñcālyaṃ drupadaṃ senayā vṛtam
e priyaṃ saṃbandhinaṃ rājañ śarān avakiran bahūn
a agnineva pradagdhāni vanāni śiśirātyaye
c śaradagdhāny adṛśyanta sainyāni drupadasya ha
e atiṣṭhata raṇe bhīṣmo vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
a madhyaṃdine yathādityaṃ tapantam iva tejasā
c na śekuḥ pāṇḍaveyasya yodhā bhīṣmaṃ nirīkṣitum
a vīkṣāṃ cakruḥ samantāt te pāṇḍavā bhayapīḍitāḥ
c trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta gāvaḥ śītārditā iva
d sā tu yaudhiṣṭhirī senā gāṅgeyaśarapīḍitā
d siṃheneva vinirbhinnā śuklā gaur iva gopateḥ
a hatavipradrute sainye nirutsāhe vimardite
c hāhākāro mahān āsīt pāṇḍusainyeṣu bhārata
a tato bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo nityaṃ maṇḍalakārmukaḥ
c mumoca bāṇān dīptāgrān ahīn āśīviṣān iva
a śarair ekāyanīkurvan diśaḥ sarvā yatavrataḥ
c jaghāna pāṇḍavarathān ādiśyādiśya bhārata
a tataḥ sainyeṣu bhagneṣu mathiteṣu ca sarvaśaḥ
c prāpte cāstaṃ dinakare na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a bhīṣmaṃ ca samudīryantaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthā mahāhave
c avahāram akurvanta sainyānāṃ bharatarṣabha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a kṛte 'vahāre sainyānāṃ prathame bharatarṣabha
c bhīṣme ca yudhi saṃrabdhe hṛṣṭe duryodhane tathā
a dharmarājas tatas tūrṇam abhigamya janārdanam
c bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ sarvaiś caiva janeśvaraiḥ
a śucā paramayā yuktaś cintayānaḥ parājayam
c vārṣṇeyam abravīd rājan dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramam
a kṛṣṇa paśya maheṣvāsaṃ bhīṣmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
c śarair dahantaṃ sainyaṃ me grīṣme kakṣam ivānalam
d yudhiṣṭhiro mahārāja dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam athābravīt
a katham enaṃ mahātmānaṃ śakṣyāmaḥ prativīkṣitum
c lelihyamānaṃ sainyaṃ me haviṣmantam ivānalam
a etaṃ hi puruṣavyāghraṃ dhanuṣmantaṃ mahābalam
c dṛṣṭvā vipradrutaṃ sainyaṃ madīyaṃ mārgaṇāhatam
a śakyo jetuṃ yamaḥ kruddho vajrapāṇiś ca saṃyuge
c varuṇaḥ pāśabhṛc cāpi kubero vā gadādharaḥ
a na tu bhīṣmo mahātejāḥ śakyo jetuṃ mahābalaḥ
c so 'ham evaṃ gate magno bhīṣmāgādhajale 'plavaḥ
a ātmano buddhidaurbalyād bhīṣmam āsādya keśava
c vanaṃ yāsyāmi govinda śreyo me tatra jīvitum
a na tv imān pṛthivīpālān dātuṃ bhīṣmāya mṛtyave
c kṣapayiṣyati senāṃ me kṛṣṇa bhīṣmo mahāstravit
a yathānalaṃ prajvalitaṃ pataṃgāḥ samabhidrutāḥ
c vināśāyaiva gacchanti tathā me sainiko janaḥ
a kṣayaṃ nīto 'smi vārṣṇeya rājyahetoḥ parākramī
c bhrātaraś caiva me vīrāḥ karśitāḥ śarapīḍitāḥ
a matkṛte bhrātṛsauhārdād rājyād bhraṣṭās tathā sukhāt
c jīvitaṃ bahu manye 'haṃ jīvitaṃ hy adya durlabham
a jīvitasya hi śeṣeṇa tapas tapsyāmi duścaram
c na ghātayiṣyāmi raṇe mitrāṇīmāni keśava
a rathān me bahusāhasrān divyair astrair mahābalaḥ
c ghātayaty aniśaṃ bhīṣmaḥ pravarāṇāṃ prahāriṇām
a kiṃ nu kṛtvā kṛtaṃ me syād brūhi mādhava māciram
c madhyastham iva paśyāmi samare savyasācinam
a eko bhīmaḥ paraṃ śaktyā yudhyaty eṣa mahābhujaḥ
c kevalaṃ bāhuvīryeṇa kṣatradharmam anusmaran
a gadayā vīraghātinyā yathotsāhaṃ mahāmanāḥ
c karoty asukaraṃ karma gajāśvarathapattiṣu
a nālam eṣa kṣayaṃ kartuṃ parasainyasya māriṣa
c ārjavenaiva yuddhena vīra varṣaśatair api
a eko 'stravit sakhā te 'yaṃ so 'py asmān samupekṣate
c nirdahyamānān bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā
a divyāny astrāṇi bhīṣmasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
c dhakṣyanti kṣatriyān sarvān prayuktāni punaḥ punaḥ
a kṛṣṇa bhīṣmaḥ susaṃrabdhaḥ sahitaḥ sarvapārthivaiḥ
c kṣapayiṣyati no nūnaṃ yādṛśo 'sya parākramaḥ
a sa tvaṃ paśya maheṣvāsaṃ yogīṣvara mahāratham
c yo bhīṣmaṃ śamayet saṃkhye dāvāgniṃ jalado yathā
a tava prasādād govinda pāṇḍavā nihatadviṣaḥ
c svarājyam anusaṃprāptā modiṣyanti sabāndhavāḥ
a evam uktvā tataḥ pārtho dhyāyann āste mahāmanāḥ
c ciram antarmanā bhūtvā śokopahatacetanaḥ
a śokārtaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ jñātvā duḥkhena hatacetasam
c abravīt tatra govindo harṣayan sarvapāṇḍavān
a mā śuco bharataśreṣṭha na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi
c yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ sarvalokasya dhanvinaḥ
a ahaṃ ca priyakṛd rājan sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
a tathaiva sabalāḥ sarve rājāno rājasattama
c tvatprasādaṃ pratīkṣante tvadbhaktāś ca viśāṃ pate
a eṣa te pārṣato nityaṃ hitakāmaḥ priye rataḥ
c senāpatyam anuprāpto dhṛṣṭadyumno mahābalaḥ
e śikhaṇḍī ca mahābāho bhīṣmasya nidhanaṃ kila
f sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla śārdūlasamavikrama
f senāpatyena rājendra dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ niyojaya
a etac chrutvā tato rājā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāratham
c abravīt samitau tasyāṃ vāsudevasya śṛṇvataḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumna nibodhedaṃ yat tvā vakṣyāmi māriṣa
c nātikramyaṃ bhavet tac ca vacanaṃ mama bhāṣitam
a bhavān senāpatir mahyaṃ vāsudevena saṃmataḥ
c kārttikeyo yathā nityaṃ devānām abhavat purā
e tathā tvam api pāṇḍūnāṃ senānīḥ puruṣarṣabha
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla vikramya jahi kauravān
c ahaṃ ca tvānuyāsyāmi bhīmaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca māriṣa
a mādrīputrau ca sahitau draupadeyāś ca daṃśitāḥ
c ye cānye pṛthivīpālāḥ pradhānāḥ puruṣarṣabha
d etāvad uktvā nṛpatiḥ sahadevam abhāṣata
d abhiṣekasya saṃbhārān kṣipram ānaya vai javāt
d prādurāsīt tato dhaumyaḥ saṃbhārān gṛhya bhārata
d sahadevena sahitaḥ pāṇḍavāya nyavedayat
d tatas taṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ drupadasyātmajaṃ yudhi
d bhadrapīṭhe sukhaṃ nyasya abhiṣecayad acyutaḥ
d aśobhatābhiṣikto hi drupadasyātmajo balī
d yathā devāsure yuddhe kārttikeyo hy aśobhata
a tata uddharṣayan sarvān dhṛṣṭadyumno 'bhyabhāṣata
c ahaṃ droṇāntakaḥ pārtha vihitaḥ śaṃbhunā purā
a raṇe bhīṣmaṃ tathā droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ jayadratham
c sarvān adya raṇe dṛptān pratiyotsyāmi pārthiva
a athotkruṣṭaṃ maheṣvāsaiḥ pāṇḍavair yuddhadurmadaiḥ
b tac chrutvā jahṛṣuḥ pārthāḥ pārthivāś ca mahārathāḥ
c samudyate pārthivendre pārṣate śatrusūdane
a tam abravīt tataḥ pārthaḥ pārṣataṃ pṛtanāpatim
c vyūhaḥ krauñcāruṇo nāma sarvaśatrunibarhaṇaḥ
a yaṃ bṛhaspatir indrāya tadā devāsure 'bravīt
c taṃ yathāvat prativyūha parānīkavināśanam
e adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ rājānaḥ paśyantu kurubhiḥ saha
a tathoktaḥ sa nṛdevena viṣṇur vajrabhṛtā iva
c prabhāte sarvasainyānām agre cakre dhanaṃjayam
a ādityapathagaḥ ketus tasyādbhutamanoramaḥ
c śāsanāt puruhūtasya nirmito viśvakarmaṇā
a indrāyudhasavarṇābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtaḥ
c ākāśaga ivākāśe gandharvanagaropamaḥ
e nṛtyamāna ivābhāti rathacaryāsu māriṣa
a tena ratnavatā pārthaḥ sa ca gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
c babhūva paramopetaḥ svayaṃbhūr iva bhānunā
a śiro 'bhūd drupado rājā mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ
c kuntibhojaś ca caidyaś ca cakṣuṣy āstāṃ janeśvara
a dāśārṇakāḥ prayāgāś ca dāśerakagaṇaiḥ saha
c anūpagāḥ kirātāś ca grīvāyāṃ bharatarṣabha
a paṭaccaraiś ca huṇḍaiś ca rājan pauravakais tathā
c niṣādaiḥ sahitaś cāpi pṛṣṭham āsīd yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a pakṣau tu bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c draupadeyābhimanyuś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
a piśācā daradāś caiva puṇḍrāḥ kuṇḍīviṣaiḥ saha
c maḍakā laḍakāś caiva taṅgaṇāḥ parataṅgaṇāḥ
a bāhlikās tittirāś caiva colāḥ pāṇḍyāś ca bhārata
c ete janapadā rājan dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritāḥ
a agniveṣyā jagattuṇḍāḥ paladāśāś ca bhārata
c śabarās tumbupāś caiva vatsāś ca saha nākulaiḥ
e nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca vāmaṃ pārśvaṃ samāśritāḥ
a rathānām ayutaṃ pakṣau śiraś ca niyutaṃ tathā
c pṛṣṭham arbudam evāsīt sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ
e grīvāyāṃ niyutaṃ cāpi sahasrāṇi ca saptatiḥ
a pakṣakoṭiprapakṣeṣu pakṣānteṣu ca vāraṇāḥ
c jagmuḥ parivṛtā rājaṃś calanta iva parvatāḥ
a jaghanaṃ pālayām āsa virāṭaḥ saha kekayaiḥ
c kāśirājaś ca śaibyaś ca rathānām ayutais tribhiḥ
a evam etaṃ mahāvyūhaṃ vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ
c sūryodayanam icchantaḥ sthitā yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ
d śabdaś ca sumahāṃs tatra divaspṛg bharatottama
d evaṃ te puruṣavyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavā yuddhadurmadāḥ
d vyavasthitāḥ prativyūhya tava putrasya vāhinīm
d trasantīva hi cetāṃsi yodhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d dṛṣṭvāgrato bhīmasenaṃ gadāpāṇim avasthitam
d sūryodaye saṃjaya ke tu pūrvaṃ
d yuyutsavo hṛṣṭarūpās tathāsan
d kiṃ māmakā bhīṣmanetrāḥ samīyuḥ
d kiṃ pāṇḍavā bhīmanetrās tadānīm
d keṣāṃ jaghanyau somasūryau suvāyuḥ
d keṣāṃ senāṃ śvāpadā vyāhareyuḥ
d keṣāṃ yūnāṃ mukhavarṇāḥ prasannāḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d sarvaṃ hy etad brūhi tattvaṃ yathāvat
d ubhe sene tulyam evopapanne
d ubhe sene harṣarūpe tathaiva
d ubhe citre vanarājīprakāśe
d ubhe sene nāgarathāśvapūrṇe
d ubhe sene bhīmarūpe narendra
d tathā cobhe bhārata durviṣahye
d tathā cobhe svargajayāya tuṣṭe
d tathā cobhe satpuruṣopajuṣṭe
d paścānmukhāḥ kauravā dhārtarāṣṭrās
d tathā pāṇḍavāḥ prāṅmukhā yotsyamānāḥ
d daityendraseneva ca kauravāṇāṃ
d surendraseneva ca pāṇḍavānām
d vavau vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ
d tathā vāyuḥ sanmukhas tāvakānām
d gajendrāṇāṃ madagandhā   
d nna sehire tava putrasya nāgāḥ
d duryodhano dantivaraṃ padmavarṇaṃ
d suvarṇakakṣaṃ jātabalaṃ prabhinnam
d samāsthito madhyagataḥ kurūṇāṃ
d saṃstūyamāno rathibhir māgadhaiś ca
d candraprabhaṃ śvetam asyātapatraṃ
d tathā sauvarṇā srag bhrājate cottamāṅge
d taṃ sarvataḥ śakuniḥ pārvatīyaḥ
d sārdhaṃ gāndhāraiḥ pāti gāndhārarājaḥ
d bhīṣmo 'grataḥ sarvasainyasya vṛddhaḥ
d śvetacchatraḥ śvetakacaḥ saśaṅkhaḥ
d śvetoṣṇīṣaḥ pāṇḍureṇa dhvajena
d śveto rathaḥ śailasamaprakāśaḥ
d tadvat sainyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya sarve
d bāhlikānāṃ cātiratho mahātmā
d maheṣvāsā mahābhāgāḥ sthitā yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ
a teṣām ādityavarṇāni vimalāni mahānti ca
c śvetacchatrāṇy aśobhanta vāraṇeṣu ratheṣu ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a krauñcaṃ tato mahāvyūham abhedyaṃ tanayas tava
c vyūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāghoraṃ pārthenāmitatejasā
a ācāryam upasaṃgamya kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ ca māriṣa
c saumadattiṃ vikarṇaṃ ca aśvatthāmānam eva ca
a duḥśāsanādīn bhrātṝṃś ca sa sarvān eva bhārata
c anyāṃś ca subahūñ śūrān yuddhāya samupāgatān
a prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ kāle harṣayaṃs tanayas tava
c nānāśastrapraharaṇāḥ sarve śastrāstravedinaḥ
a ekaikaśaḥ samarthā hi yūyaṃ sarve mahārathāḥ
c pāṇḍuputrān raṇe hantuṃ sasainyān kim u saṃhatāḥ
a aparyāptaṃ tad asmākaṃ balaṃ bhīṣmābhirakṣitam
c paryāptaṃ tv idam eteṣāṃ balaṃ pārthivasattamāḥ
a saṃsthānāḥ śūrasenāś ca veṇikāḥ kukurās tathā
c ārevakās trigartāś ca madrakā yavanās tathā
a śatruṃjayena sahitās tathā duḥśāsanena ca
c vikarṇena ca vīreṇa tathā nandopanandakaiḥ
a citrasenena sahitāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇibhadrakaiḥ
c bhīṣmam evābhirakṣantu saha sainyapuraskṛtāḥ
a tato droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca tava putraś ca māriṣa
c avyūhanta mahāvyūhaṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ pratibādhane
a bhīṣmaḥ sainyena mahatā samantāt parivāritaḥ
c yayau prakarṣan mahatīṃ vāhinīṃ surarāḍ iva
a tam anvayān maheṣvāso bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c kuntalaiś ca daśārṇaiś ca māgadhaiś ca viśāṃ pate
a vidarbhair mekalaiś caiva karṇaprāvaraṇair api
c sahitāḥ sarvasainyena bhīṣmam āhavaśobhinam
a gāndhārāḥ sindhusauvīrāḥ śibayo 'tha vasātayaḥ
c śakuniś ca svasainyena bhāradvājam apālayat
a tato duryodhano rājā sahitaḥ sarvasodaraiḥ
c aśvātakair vikarṇaiś ca tathā śarmilakosalaiḥ
a daradaiś cūcupaiś caiva tathā kṣudrakamālavaiḥ
c abhyarakṣata saṃhṛṣṭaḥ saubaleyasya vāhinīm
a bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyo bhagadattaś ca māriṣa
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau vāmaṃ pārśvam apālayan
a saumadattiḥ suśarmā ca kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
c śatāyuś ca śrutāyuś ca dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvam āsthitāḥ
a aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ senāpṛṣṭhe vyavasthitāḥ
a pṛṣṭhagopās tu tasyāsan nānādeśyā janeśvarāḥ
c ketumān vasudānaś ca putraḥ kāśyasya cābhibhūḥ
a tatas te tāvakāḥ sarve hṛṣṭā yuddhāya bhārata
c dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yuktāḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca nādayan
a teṣāṃ śrutvā tu hṛṣṭānāṃ kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥ
c siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccaiḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau pratāpavān
a tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca peśyaś ca vividhāḥ paraiḥ
c ānakāś cābhyahanyanta sa śabdas tumulo 'bhavat
a tataḥ śvetair hayair yukte mahati syandane sthitau
c pradadhmatuḥ śaṅkhavarau hemaratnapariṣkṛtau
a pāñcajanyaṃ hṛṣīkeśo devadattaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c pauṇḍraṃ dadhmau mahāśaṅkhaṃ bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥ
a anantavijayaṃ rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sughoṣamaṇipuṣpakau
d yudhiṣṭhiraś ca dharmātmā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
d abhimanyuś ca vikrānta uttamaujāś ca vīryavān
a kāśirājaś ca śaibyaś ca śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumno virāṭaś ca sātyakiś ca mahāyaśāḥ
a pāñcālyaś ca maheṣvāso draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥ
c sarve dadhmur mahāśaṅkhān siṃhanādāṃś ca nedire
a sa ghoṣaḥ sumahāṃs tatra vīrais taiḥ samudīritaḥ
c nabhaś ca pṛthivīṃ caiva tumulo vyanunādayat
a evam ete mahārāja prahṛṣṭāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c punar yuddhāya saṃjagmus tāpayānāḥ parasparam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a evaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu māmakeṣv itareṣu ca
c kathaṃ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire
 saṃjaya uvāca
a samaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu saṃnaddhā ruciradhvajāḥ
b tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ yathāyudhyanta tac chṛṇu
c apāram iva saṃdṛśya sāgarapratimaṃ balam
a teṣāṃ madhye sthito rājā putro duryodhanas tava
c abravīt tāvakān sarvān yudhyadhvam iti daṃśitāḥ
a te manaḥ krūram āsthāya samabhityaktajīvitāḥ
c pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta sarva evocchritadhvajāḥ
a tato yuddhaṃ samabhavat tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca vyatiṣaktarathadvipam
a muktās tu rathibhir bāṇā rukmapuṅkhāḥ sutejanāḥ
c saṃnipetur akuṇṭhāgrā nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu ca
a tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme dhanur udyamya daṃśitaḥ
c abhipatya mahābāhur bhīṣmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
a saubhadre bhīmasene ca śaineye ca mahārathe
c kekaye ca virāṭe ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca pārṣate
a eteṣu naravīreṣu cedimatsyeṣu cābhitaḥ
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
a prākampata mahāvyūhas tasmin vīrasamāgame
c sarveṣām eva sainyānām āsīd vyatikaro mahān
a sāditadhvajanāgāś ca hatapravaravājinaḥ
c viprayātarathānīkāḥ samapadyanta pāṇḍavāḥ
a arjunas tu naravyāghro dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaṃ mahāratham
c vārṣṇeyam abravīt kruddho yāhi yatra pitāmahaḥ
a eṣa bhīṣmaḥ susaṃkruddho vārṣṇeya mama vāhinīm
c nāśayiṣyati suvyaktaṃ duryodhanahite rataḥ
a eṣa droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyo vikarṇaś ca janārdana
c dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca sahitā duryodhanapurogamāḥ
a pāñcālān nihaniṣyanti rakṣitā dṛḍhadhanvanā
c so 'haṃ bhīṣmaṃ gamiṣyāmi sainyahetor janārdana
a tam abravīd vāsudevo yatto bhava dhanaṃjaya
c eṣa tvā prāpaye vīra pitāmaharathaṃ prati
a evam uktvā tataḥ śaurī rathaṃ taṃ lokaviśrutam
c prāpayām āsa bhīṣmāya rathaṃ prati janeśvara
a cañcadbahupatākena balākāvarṇavājinā
c samucchritamahābhīmanadadvānaraketunā
d lāṅgūlāsphoṭaśabdena svanayāno nabhastalam
d piṅgākṣair dṛṣṭipātaiś ca bhīṣayann arisainikān
e mahatā meghanādena rathenādityavarcasā
a vinighnan kauravānīkaṃ śūrasenāṃś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c āyāc charān nudañ śīghraṃ suhṛcchoṣavināśanaḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ vegena prabhinnam iva vāraṇam
c trāsayānaṃ raṇe śūrān pātayantaṃ ca sāyakaiḥ
a saindhavapramukhair guptaḥ prācyasauvīrakekayaiḥ
c sahasā pratyudīyāya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'rjunam
a ko hi gāṇḍīvadhanvānam anyaḥ kurupitāmahāt
c droṇavaikartanābhyāṃ vā rathaḥ saṃyātum arhati
a tato bhīṣmo mahārāja kauravāṇāṃ pitāmahaḥ
c arjunaṃ saptasaptatyā nārācānāṃ samāvṛṇot
a droṇaś ca pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpaḥ pañcāśatā śaraiḥ
c duryodhanaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā śalyaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
d drauṇiḥ ṣaṣṭyā naravyāghro vikarṇaś ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a saindhavo navabhiś cāpi śakuniś cāpi pañcabhiḥ
c vikarṇo daśabhir bhallai rājan vivyādha pāṇḍavam
a sa tair viddho maheṣvāsaḥ samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c na vivyathe mahābāhur bhidyamāna ivācalaḥ
a sa bhīṣmaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c droṇaṃ ṣaṣṭyā naravyāghro vikarṇaṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
d śalyaṃ ca daśabhir bāṇais tāvadbhiś ca jayadratham
a ārtāyaniṃ tribhir bāṇai rājānaṃ cāpi pañcabhiḥ
c pratyavidhyad ameyātmā kirīṭī bharatarṣabha
a taṃ sātyakir virāṭaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c draupadeyābhimanyuś ca parivavrur dhanaṃjayam
a tato droṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ gāṅgeyasya priye ratam
c abhyavarṣata pāñcālyaḥ saṃyuktaḥ saha somakaiḥ
a bhīṣmas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭhas tūrṇaṃ vivyādha pāṇḍavam
c aśītyā niśitair bāṇais tato 'krośanta tāvakāḥ
a teṣāṃ tu ninadaṃ śrutvā prahṛṣṭānāṃ prahṛṣṭavat
c praviveśa tato madhyaṃ rathasiṃhaḥ pratāpavān
a teṣāṃ tu rathasiṃhānāṃ madhyaṃ prāpya dhanaṃjayaḥ
c cikrīḍa dhanuṣā rājaṃl lakṣyaṃ kṛtvā mahārathān
d kṣatriyāṇāṃ śirāṃsy ugraiḥ kṛntañ śastrair mahārathaḥ
d śūnyān kṛtvā rathopasthān vyacarat phalgunas tadā
a tato duryodhano rājā bhīṣmam āha janeśvaraḥ
c pīḍyamānaṃ svakaṃ sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthena saṃyuge
a eṣa pāṇḍusutas tāta kṛṣṇena sahito balī
c yatatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ mūlaṃ naḥ parikṛntati
e tvayi jīvati gāṅgeye droṇe ca rathināṃ vare
a tvatkṛte hy eṣa karṇo 'pi nyastaśastro mahārathaḥ
c na yudhyati raṇe pārthaṃ hitakāmaḥ sadā mama
a sa tathā kuru gāṅgeya yathā hanyeta phalgunaḥ
c evam uktas tato rājan pitā devavratas tava
e dhik kṣatradharmam ity uktvā yayau pārtharathaṃ prati
a ubhau śvetahayau rājan saṃsaktau dṛśya pārthivāḥ
c siṃhanādān bhṛśaṃ cakruḥ śaṅkhaśabdāṃś ca bhārata
a drauṇir duryodhanaś caiva vikarṇaś ca tavātmajaḥ
c parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ sthitā yuddhāya māriṣa
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parivārya dhanaṃjayam
c sthitā yuddhāya mahate tato yuddham avartata
a gāṅgeyas tu raṇe pārtham ānarchan navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c tam arjunaḥ pratyavidhyad daśabhir marmavedhibhiḥ
a tataḥ śarasahasreṇa suprayuktena pāṇḍavaḥ
c arjunaḥ samaraślāghī bhīṣmasyāvārayad diśaḥ
a śarajālaṃ tatas tat tu śarajālena kaurava
c vārayām āsa pārthasya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tathā
a ubhau paramasaṃhṛṣṭāv ubhau yuddhābhinandinau
c nirviśeṣam ayudhyetāṃ kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇau
a bhīṣmacāpavimuktāni śarajālāni saṃghaśaḥ
c śīryamāṇāny adṛśyanta bhinnāny arjunasāyakaiḥ
a tathaivārjunamuktāni śarajālāni bhāgaśaḥ
c gāṅgeyaśaranunnāni nyapatanta mahītale
a arjunaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā bhīṣmam ārcchac chitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c bhīṣmo 'pi samare pārthaṃ vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ
a anyonyasya hayān viddhvā dhvajau ca sumahābalau
c ratheṣāṃ rathacakre ca cikrīḍatur ariṃdamau
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
c vāsudevaṃ tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntare
a bhīṣmacāpacyutair bāṇair nirviddho madhusūdanaḥ
c virarāja raṇe rājan sapuṣpa iva kiṃśukaḥ
a tato 'rjuno bhṛśaṃ kruddho nirviddhaṃ prekṣya mādhavam
c gāṅgeyasārathiṃ saṃkhye nirbibheda tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a yatamānau tu tau vīrāv anyonyasya vadhaṃ prati
c nāśaknutāṃ tadānyonyam abhisaṃdhātum āhave
a maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi gatapratyāgatāni ca
c adarśayetāṃ bahudhā sūtasāmarthyalāghavāt
a antaraṃ ca prahāreṣu tarkayantau mahārathau
c rājann antaramārgasthau sthitāv āstāṃ muhur muhuḥ
a ubhau siṃharavonmiśraṃ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ pracakratuḥ
c tathaiva cāpanirghoṣaṃ cakratus tau mahārathau
a tayoḥ śaṅkhapraṇādena rathanemisvanena ca
c dāritā sahasā bhūmiś cakampa ca nanāda ca
a na tayor antaraṃ kaś cid dadṛśe bharatarṣabha
c balinau samare śūrāv anyonyasadṛśāv ubhau
a cihnamātreṇa bhīṣmaṃ tu prajajñus tatra kauravāḥ
c tathā pāṇḍusutāḥ pārthaṃ cihnamātreṇa jajñire
a tayor nṛvarayo rājan dṛśya tādṛk parākramam
c vismayaṃ sarvabhūtāni jagmur bhārata saṃyuge
a na tayor vivaraṃ kaś cid raṇe paśyati bhārata
c dharme sthitasya hi yathā na kaś cid vṛjinaṃ kva cit
a ubhau hi śarajālena tāv adṛśyau babhūvatuḥ
c prakāśau ca punas tūrṇaṃ babhūvatur ubhau raṇe
a tatra devāḥ sagandharvāś cāraṇāś ca saharṣibhiḥ
c anyonyaṃ pratyabhāṣanta tayor dṛṣṭvā parākramam
a na śakyau yudhi saṃrabdhau jetum etau mahārathau
c sadevāsuragandharvair lokair api kathaṃ cana
a āścaryabhūtaṃ lokeṣu yuddham etan mahādbhutam
c naitādṛśāni yuddhāni bhaviṣyanti kathaṃ cana
a nāpi śakyo raṇe jetuṃ bhīṣmaḥ pārthena dhīmatā
c sadhanuś ca rathasthaś ca pravapan sāyakān raṇe
a tathaiva pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe devair api durāsadam
c na vijetuṃ raṇe bhīṣma utsaheta dhanurdharam
d ālokād api yuddhaṃ tu samam etad bhaviṣyati
a iti sma vācaḥ śrūyante proccarantyas tatas tataḥ
c gāṅgeyārjunayoḥ saṃkhye stavayuktā viśāṃ pate
a tvadīyās tu tato yodhāḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca bhārata
c anyonyaṃ samare jaghnus tayos tatra parākrame
a śitadhārais tathā khaḍgair vimalaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
c śarair anyaiś ca bahubhiḥ śastrair nānāvidhair yudhi
e ubhayoḥ senayor vīrā nyakṛntanta parasparam
a vartamāne tathā ghore tasmin yuddhe sudāruṇe
c droṇapāñcālyayo rājan mahān āsīt samāgamaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālyaś cāpi pārṣataḥ
c raṇe samīyatur yattau tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a diṣṭam eva paraṃ manye pauruṣād api saṃjaya
c yatra śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo nātarad yudhi pāṇḍavam
a bhīṣmo hi samare kruddho hanyāl lokāṃś carācarān
c sa kathaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe nātarat saṃjayaujasā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan sthiro bhūtvā yuddham etat sudāruṇam
c na śakyaḥ pāṇḍavo jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ
a droṇas tu niśitair bāṇair dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayat
c sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apātayat
a tasyātha caturo vāhāṃś caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥ
c pīḍayām āsa saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnasya māriṣa
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato droṇaṃ navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyādha prahasan vīras tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa dhṛṣṭadyumnam amarṣaṇam
a ādade ca śaraṃ ghoraṃ pārṣatasya vadhaṃ prati
c śakrāśanisamasparśaṃ mṛtyudaṇḍam ivāparam
a hāhākāro mahān āsīt sarvasainyasya bhārata
c tam iṣuṃ saṃdhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāradvājena saṃyuge
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma dhṛṣṭadyumnasya pauruṣam
c yad ekaḥ samare vīras tasthau girir ivācalaḥ
a taṃ ca dīptaṃ śaraṃ ghoram āyāntaṃ mṛtyum ātmanaḥ
c ciccheda śaravṛṣṭiṃ ca bhāradvāje mumoca ha
a tata uccukruśuḥ sarve pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c dhṛṣṭadyumnena tat karma kṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā suduṣkaram
a tataḥ śaktiṃ mahāvegāṃ svarṇavaiḍūryabhūṣitām
c droṇasya nidhanākāṅkṣī cikṣepa sa parākramī
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śaktiṃ kanakabhūṣaṇām
c tridhā cikṣepa samare bhāradvājo hasann iva
a śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi droṇaṃ prati janeśvara
a śaravarṣaṃ tatas taṃ tu saṃnivārya mahāyaśāḥ
c droṇo drupadaputrasya madhye ciccheda kārmukam
a sa cchinnadhanvā samare gadāṃ gurvīṃ mahāyaśāḥ
c droṇāya preṣayām āsa girisāramayīṃ balī
a sā gadā vegavan muktā prāyād droṇajighāṃsayā
c tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bhāradvājasya vikramam
a lāghavād vyaṃsayām āsa gadāṃ hemavibhūṣitām
c vyaṃsayitvā gadāṃ tāṃ ca preṣayām āsa pārṣate
a bhallān suniśitān pītān svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
c te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave
a athānyad dhanur ādāya dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāmanāḥ
c droṇaṃ yudhi parākramya śarair vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
a rudhirāktau tatas tau tu śuśubhāte nararṣabhau
c vasantasamaye rājan puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
a amarṣitas tato rājan parākramya camūmukhe
c droṇo drupadaputrasya punaś ciccheda kārmukam
a athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c avākirad ameyātmā vṛṣṭyā megha ivācalam
d tad apy asya raṇe droṇaś ciccheda saśaraṃ dhanuḥ
a sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apātayat
c athāsya caturo vāhāṃś caturbhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a pātayām āsa samare siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca
c tato 'pareṇa bhallena hastāc cāpam athācchinat
a sa cchinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
c gadāpāṇir avārohat khyāpayan pauruṣaṃ mahat
a tām asya viśikhais tūrṇaṃ pātayām āsa bhārata
c rathād anavarūḍhasya tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tataḥ sa vipulaṃ carma śatacandraṃ ca bhānumat
c khaḍgaṃ ca vipulaṃ divyaṃ pragṛhya subhujo balī
a abhidudrāva vegena droṇasya vadhakāṅkṣayā
c āmiṣārthī yathā siṃho vane mattam iva dvipam
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bhāradvājasya pauruṣam
c lāghavaṃ cāstrayogaṃ ca balaṃ bāhvoś ca bhārata
a yad enaṃ śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa pārṣatam
c na śaśāka tato gantuṃ balavān api saṃyuge
a tatra sthitam apaśyāma dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāratham
c vārayāṇaṃ śaraughāṃś ca carmaṇā kṛtahastavat
a tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ sahasābhyapatad balī
c sāhāyyakārī samare pārṣatasya mahātmanaḥ
a sa droṇaṃ niśitair bāṇai rājan vivyādha saptabhiḥ
c pārṣataṃ ca tadā tūrṇam anyam āropayad ratham
a tato duryodhano rājā kaliṅgaṃ samacodayat
c sainyena mahatā yuktaṃ bhāradvājasya rakṣaṇe
a tataḥ sā mahatī senā kaliṅgānāṃ janeśvara
c bhīmam abhyudyayau tūrṇaṃ tava putrasya śāsanāt
a pāñcālyam abhisaṃtyajya droṇo 'pi rathināṃ varaḥ
c virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau yodhayām āsa saṃgatau
e dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi samare dharmarājaṃ samabhyayāt
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c kaliṅgānāṃ ca samare bhīmasya ca mahātmanaḥ
e jagataḥ prakṣayakaraṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a tathā pratisamādiṣṭaḥ kaliṅgo vāhinīpatiḥ
c katham adbhutakarmāṇaṃ bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
a carantaṃ gadayā vīraṃ daṇḍapāṇim ivāntakam
c yodhayām āsa samare kaliṅgaḥ saha senayā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a putreṇa tava rājendra sa tathokto mahābalaḥ
c mahatyā senayā guptaḥ prāyād bhīmarathaṃ prati
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā kaliṅgānāṃ mahācamūm
c rathanāgāśvakalilāṃ pragṛhītamahāyudhām
a bhīmasenaḥ kaliṅgānām ārchad bhārata vāhinīm
c ketumantaṃ ca naiṣādim āyāntaṃ saha cedibhiḥ
a tataḥ śrutāyuḥ saṃkruddho rājñā ketumatā saha
c āsasāda raṇe bhīmaṃ vyūḍhānīkeṣu cediṣu
a rathair anekasāhasraiḥ kaliṅgānāṃ janādhipaḥ
c ayutena gajānāṃ ca niṣādaiḥ saha ketumān
e bhīmasenaṃ raṇe rājan samantāt paryavārayat
a cedimatsyakarūṣāś ca bhīmasenapurogamāḥ
c abhyavartanta sahasā niṣādān saha rājabhiḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
b sarve kaliṅgakāś caiva saṃnivṛtteṣu cediṣu
b svabāhubalam āsthāya abhyavartanta pāṇḍavam
c prajānan na ca yodhān svān parasparajighāṃsayā
a ghoram āsīt tato yuddhaṃ bhīmasya sahasā paraiḥ
c yathendrasya mahārāja mahatyā daityasenayā
a tasya sainyasya saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya bhārata
c babhūva sumahāñ śabdaḥ sāgarasyeva garjataḥ
a anyonyasya tadā yodhā nikṛntanto viśāṃ pate
c mahīṃ cakruś citāṃ sarvāṃ śaśaśoṇitasaṃnibhām
a yodhāṃś ca svān parān vāpi nābhyajānañ jighāṃsayā
c svān apy ādadate svāś ca śūrāḥ samaradurjayāḥ
a vimardaḥ sumahān āsīd alpānāṃ bahubhiḥ saha
c kaliṅgaiḥ saha cedīnāṃ niṣādaiś ca viśāṃ pate
a kṛtvā puruṣakāraṃ tu yathāśakti mahābalāḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ parityajya saṃnyavartanta cedayaḥ
a sarvaiḥ kaliṅgair āsannaḥ saṃnivṛtteṣu cediṣu
c svabāhubalam āsthāya na nyavartata pāṇḍavaḥ
a na cacāla rathopasthād bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c śitair avākiran bāṇaiḥ kaliṅgānāṃ varūthinīm
a kaliṅgas tu maheṣvāsaḥ putraś cāsya mahārathaḥ
c śakradeva iti khyāto jaghnatuḥ pāṇḍavaṃ śaraiḥ
a tato bhīmo mahābāhur vidhunvan ruciraṃ dhanuḥ
c yodhayām āsa kāliṅgān svabāhubalam āśritaḥ
a śakradevas tu samare visṛjan sāyakān bahūn

a         ākṣipyānyāny apātayat
