c abhyavartanta rājānaḥ sahitāḥ savyasācinam
a uddhūtaṃ sahasā bhaumaṃ nāgāśvarathasādibhiḥ
c divākarapathaṃ prāpya rajas tīvram adṛśyata
a tāni nāgasahasrāṇi bhūmipālaśatāni ca
c tasya bāṇapathaṃ prāpya nābhyavartanta sarvaśaḥ
a praṇeduḥ sarvabhūtāni babhūvus timirā diśaḥ
c kurūṇām anayas tīvraḥ samadṛśyata dāruṇaḥ
a nāpy antarikṣaṃ na diśo na bhūmir na ca bhāskaraḥ
c prajajñe bharataśreṣṭha śarasaṃghaiḥ kirīṭinaḥ
a sāditadhvajanāgās tu hatāśvā rathino bhṛśam
c vipradrutarathāḥ ke cid dṛśyante rathayūthapāḥ
a virathā rathinaś cānye dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ
c tatra tatraiva dṛśyante sāyudhāḥ sāṅgadair bhujaiḥ
a hayārohā hayāṃs tyaktvā gajārohāś ca dantinaḥ
c arjunasya bhayād rājan samantād vipradudruvuḥ
a rathebhyaś ca gajebhyaś ca hayebhyaś ca narādhipāḥ
c patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca dṛśyante 'rjunatāḍitāḥ
a sagadān udyatān bāhūn sakhaḍgāṃś ca viśāṃ pate
c saprāsāṃś ca satūṇīrān saśarān saśarāsanān
a sāṅkuśān sapatākāṃś ca tatra tatrārjuno nṛṇām
c nicakarta śarair ugrai raudraṃ bibhrad vapus tadā
a parighāṇāṃ pravṛddhānāṃ mudgarāṇāṃ ca māriṣa
c prāsānāṃ bhiṇḍipālānāṃ nistriṃśānāṃ ca saṃyuge
a paraśvadhānāṃ tīkṣṇānāṃ tomarāṇāṃ ca bhārata
c varmaṇāṃ cāpaviddhānāṃ kavacānāṃ ca bhūtale
a dhvajānāṃ carmaṇāṃ caiva vyajanānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c chatrāṇāṃ hemadaṇḍānāṃ cāmarāṇāṃ ca bhārata
a pratodānāṃ kaśānāṃ ca yoktrāṇāṃ caiva māriṣa
c rāśayaś cātra dṛśyante vinikīrṇā raṇakṣitau
a nāsīt tatra pumān kaś cit tava sainyasya bhārata
c yo 'rjunaṃ samare śūraṃ pratyudyāyāt kathaṃ cana
a yo yo hi samare pārthaṃ patyudyāti viśāṃ pate
c sa sa vai viśikhais tīkṣṇaiḥ paralokāya nīyate
a teṣu vidravamāṇeṣu tava yodheṣu sarvaśaḥ
c arjuno vāsudevaś ca dadhmatur vārijottamau
d rorūyamāṇo dṛśyeta dhvajāgre vānareśvaraḥ
d dṛṣṭyā bhīṣayate śatrūn stabdhakarṇo mahākapiḥ
a tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitā devavratas tava
c abravīt samare śūraṃ bhāradvājaṃ smayann iva
a eṣa pāṇḍusuto vīraḥ kṛṣṇena sahito balī
c tathā karoti sainyāni yathā kuryād dhanaṃjayaḥ
a na hy eṣa samare śakyo jetum adya kathaṃ cana
c yathāsya dṛśyate rūpaṃ kālāntakayamopamam
a na nivartayituṃ cāpi śakyeyaṃ mahatī camūḥ
c anyonyaprekṣayā paśya dravatīyaṃ varūthinī
d vayaṃ ca śastribhir bhinnā nṛpair indrasamair yudhi
d bhīto vyūhasya sarvatra na sthātuṃ kaś cid icchati
d śaravrātāḥ pradṛśyanta pannagābhāḥ samantataḥ
d diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva vyāptā hy ārjunasāyakaiḥ
a eṣa cāstaṃ giriśreṣṭhaṃ bhānumān pratipadyate
c vapūṃṣi sarvalokasya saṃharann iva sarvathā
a tatrāvahāraṃ saṃprāptaṃ manye 'haṃ puruṣarṣabha
c śrāntā bhītāś ca no yodhā na yotsyanti kathaṃ cana
a evam uktvā tato bhīṣmo droṇam ācāryasattamam
c avahāram atho cakre tāvakānāṃ mahārathaḥ
d tataḥ sarathanāgāśvā jayaṃ prāpya sasomakāḥ
d pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva praṇeduś ca punaḥ punaḥ
d prayayuḥ śibirāyaiva dhanaṃjayapuraskṛtāḥ
d vāditraghoṣaiḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pranṛtyanto mahārathāḥ
a tato 'vahāraḥ sainyānāṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
c astaṃ gacchati sūrye 'bhūt saṃdhyākāle ca vartati
 saṃjaya uvāca
a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tataḥ
c anīkāny anusaṃyāne vyādideśātha bhārata
a gāruḍaṃ ca mahāvyūhaṃ cakre śāṃtanavas tadā
c putrāṇāṃ te jayākāṅkṣī bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
a garuḍasya svayaṃ tuṇḍe pitā devavratas tava
c cakṣuṣī ca bharadvājaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
a aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva śīrṣam āstāṃ yaśasvinau
c trigartair matsyakaikeyair vāṭadhānaiś ca saṃyutau
a bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyo bhagadattaś ca māriṣa
c madrakāḥ sindhusauvīrās tathā pañcanadāś ca ye
a jayadrathena sahitā grīvāyāṃ saṃniveśitāḥ
c pṛṣṭhe duryodhano rājā sodaraiḥ sānugair vṛtaḥ
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaś ca śakaiḥ saha
c puccham āsan mahārāja śūrasenāś ca sarvaśaḥ
a māgadhāś ca kaliṅgāś ca dāśerakagaṇaiḥ saha
c dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āsādya sthitā vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ
a kānanāś ca vikuñjāś ca muktāḥ puṇḍrāviṣas tathā
c bṛhadbalena sahitā vāmaṃ pakṣam upāśritāḥ
a vyūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu tat sainyaṃ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahitaḥ pratyavyūhata saṃyuge
d tāvakānāṃ tu taṃ vyūhaṃ pratyavyūhanta pāṇḍavāḥ
e ardhacandreṇa vyūhena vyūhaṃ tam atidāruṇam
a dakṣiṇaṃ śṛṅgam āsthāya bhīmaseno vyarocata
c nānāśastraughasaṃpannair nānādeśyair nṛpair vṛtaḥ
a tad anv eva virāṭaś ca drupadaś ca mahārathaḥ
c tadanantaram evāsīn nīlo nīlāyudhaiḥ saha
a nīlād anantaraṃ caiva dhṛṣṭaketur mahārathaḥ
c cedikāśikarūṣaiś ca pauravaiś cābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāñcālāś ca prabhadrakāḥ
c madhye sainyasya mahataḥ sthitā yuddhāya bhārata
a tathaiva dharmarājo 'pi gajānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
c tatas tu sātyakī rājan draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥ
a abhimanyus tatas tūrṇam irāvāṃś ca tataḥ param
c bhaimasenis tato rājan kekayāś ca mahārathāḥ
a tato 'bhūd dvipadāṃ śreṣṭho vāmaṃ pārśvam upāśritaḥ
c sarvasya jagato goptā goptā yasya janārdanaḥ
d tatrānu rathināṃ śreṣṭho vāmaśṛṅge vyavasthitaḥ
a evam etan mahāvyūhaṃ pratyavyūhanta pāṇḍavāḥ
c vadhārthaṃ tava putrāṇāṃ tatpakṣaṃ ye ca saṃgatāḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ vyatiṣaktarathadvipam
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nighnatām itaretaram
a hayaughāś ca rathaughāś ca tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
c saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante nighnamānāḥ parasparam
a dhāvatāṃ ca rathaughānāṃ nighnatāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak
c babhūva tumulaḥ śabdo vimiśro dundubhisvanaiḥ
a divaspṛṅ naravīrāṇāṃ nighnatām itaretaram
c saṃprahāre sutumule tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
d prāvartata nadī ghorā paralokāya bhārata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu tāvakeṣv itareṣu ca
c dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam avadhīt tava bhārata
e śarair atiratho yuddhe pātayan rathayūthapān
a te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kāleneva yugakṣaye
c dhārtarāṣṭrā raṇe yattāḥ pāṇḍavān pratyayodhayan
e prārthayānā yaśo dīptaṃ mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a ekāgramanaso bhūtvā pāṇḍavānāṃ varūthinīm
c babhañjur bahuśo rājaṃs te cābhajyanta saṃyuge
a dravadbhir atha bhagnaiś ca parivartadbhir eva ca
c pāṇḍavaiḥ kauravaiś caiva na prajñāyata kiṃ cana
a udatiṣṭhad rajo bhaumaṃ chādayānaṃ divākaram
c diśaḥ pratidiśo vāpi tatra jajñuḥ kathaṃ cana
a anumānena saṃjñābhir nāmagotraiś ca saṃyuge
c vartate sma tadā yuddhaṃ tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a na vyūho bhidyate tatra kauravāṇāṃ kathaṃ cana
c rakṣitaḥ satyasaṃdhena bhāradvājena dhīmatā
a tathaiva pāṇḍaveyānāṃ rakṣitaḥ savyasācinā
c nābhidhyata mahāvyūho bhīmena ca surakṣitaḥ
a senāgrād abhiniṣpatya prāyudhyaṃs tatra mānavāḥ
c ubhayoḥ senayo rājan vyatiṣaktarathadvipāḥ
a hayārohair hayārohāḥ pātyante sma mahāhave
c ṛṣṭibhir vimalāgrābhiḥ prāsair api ca saṃyuge
a rathī rathinam āsādya śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c pātayām āsa samare tasminn atibhayaṃkare
a gajārohā gajārohān nārācaśaratomaraiḥ
c saṃsaktāḥ pātayām āsus tava teṣāṃ ca saṃghaśaḥ
d kaś cid utpatya samare varavāraṇam āsthitaḥ
d keśapakṣe parāmṛśya jahāra samare śiraḥ
d anye dviradadantāgranirbhinnahṛdayā raṇe
d vemuś ca rudhiraṃ vīrā niḥśvasantaḥ samantataḥ
d kaś cit kariviṣāṇastho vīro raṇaviśāradaḥ
d prāvepac chaktinirbhinno gajaśikṣāstravedinā
a pattisaṃghā raṇe pattīn bhiṇḍipālaparaśvadhaiḥ
c nyapātayanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ parasparakṛtāgasaḥ
d rathī ca samare rājann āsādya gajayodhinam
d sagajaṃ pātayām āsa gajī ca rathinaṃ rathāt
d rathinaṃ ca hayārohaḥ prāsena bharatarṣabha
d pātayām āsa samare rathī ca hayasādinam
a padātī rathinaṃ saṃkhye rathī cāpi padātinam
c nyapātayac chitaiḥ śastraiḥ senayor ubhayor api
a gajārohā hayārohān pātayāṃ cakrire tadā
c hayārohā gajasthāṃś ca tad adbhutam ivābhavat
c   āplutyāplutya saṃyuge
c nistriṃśair niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ
a gajārohavaraiś cāpi tatra tatra padātayaḥ
c pātitāḥ samadṛśyanta taiś cāpi gajayodhinaḥ
a pattisaṃghā hayārohaiḥ sādisaṃghāś ca pattibhiḥ
c pātyamānā vyadṛśyanta śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a dhvajais tatrāpaviddhaiś ca kārmukais tomarais tathā
c prāsais tathā gadābhiś ca parighaiḥ kampanais tathā
a śaktibhiḥ kavacaiś citraiḥ kaṇapair aṅkuśair api
c nistriṃśair vimalaiś cāpi svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śarais tathā
a paristomaiḥ kuthābhiś ca kambalaiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
c bhūr bhāti bharataśreṣṭha sragdāmair iva citritā
a narāśvakāyaiḥ patitair dantibhiś ca mahāhave
c agamyarūpā pṛthivī māṃsaśoṇitakardamā
a praśaśāma rajo bhaumaṃ vyukṣitaṃ raṇaśoṇitaiḥ
c diśaś ca vimalāḥ sarvāḥ saṃbabhūvur janeśvara
a utthitāny agaṇeyāni kabandhāni samantataḥ
c cihnabhūtāni jagato vināśārthāya bhārata
a tasmin yuddhe mahāraudre vartamāne sudāruṇe
c pratyadṛśyanta rathino dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥ
a tato droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥ
c purumitro vikarṇaś ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
a ete samaradurdharṣāḥ siṃhatulyaparākramāḥ
c pāṇḍavānām anīkāni babhañjuḥ sma punaḥ punaḥ
a tathaiva bhīmaseno 'pi rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
c sātyakiś cekitānaś ca draupadeyāś ca bhārata
a tāvakāṃs tava putrāṃś ca sahitān sarvarājabhiḥ
c drāvayām āsur ājau te tridaśā dānavān iva
a tathā te samare 'nyonyaṃ nighnantaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
c raktokṣitā ghorarūpā virejur dānavā iva
a vinirjitya ripūn vīrāḥ senayor ubhayor api
c vyadṛśyanta mahāmātrā grahā iva nabhastale
a tato rathasahasreṇa putro duryodhanas tava
c abhyayāt pāṇḍavān yuddhe rākṣasaṃ ca ghaṭotkacam
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve mahatyā senayā saha
c droṇabhīṣmau raṇe śūrau pratyudyayur ariṃdamau
a kirīṭī tu yayau kruddhaḥ samarthān pārthivottamān
c ārjuniḥ sātyakiś caiva yayatuḥ saubalaṃ balam
a tataḥ pravavṛte bhūyaḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca samare vijigīṣatām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tatas te pārthivāḥ kruddhāḥ phalgunaṃ vīkṣya saṃyuge
c rathair anekasāhasraiḥ samantāt paryavārayan
a athainaṃ rathavṛndena koṣṭakīkṛtya bhārata
c śaraiḥ subahusāhasraiḥ samantād abhyavārayan
a śaktīś ca vimalās tīkṣṇā gadāś ca parighaiḥ saha
c prāsān paraśvadhāṃś caiva mudgarān musalān api
e cikṣipuḥ samare kruddhāḥ phalgunasya rathaṃ prati
a śastrāṇām atha tāṃ vṛṣṭiṃ śalabhānām ivāyatim
c rurodha sarvataḥ pārthaḥ śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
a tatra tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā bībhatsor atimānuṣam
c devadānavagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ
e sādhu sādhv iti rājendra phalgunaṃ pratyapūjayan
a sātyakiṃ cābhimanyuṃ ca mahatyā senayā saha
c gāndhārāḥ samare śūrā rurudhuḥ sahasaubalāḥ
a tatra saubalakāḥ kruddhā vārṣṇeyasya rathottamam
c tilaśaś cicchiduḥ krodhāc chastrair nānāvidhair yudhi
a sātyakis tu rathaṃ tyaktvā vartamāne mahābhaye
c abhimanyo rathaṃ tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ
a tāv ekarathasaṃyuktau saubaleyasya vāhinīm
c vyadhametāṃ śitais tūrṇaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a droṇabhīṣmau raṇe yattau dharmarājasya vāhinīm
c nāśayetāṃ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatraparicchadaiḥ
a tato dharmasuto rājā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c miṣatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ droṇānīkam upādravan
a tatrāsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c yathā devāsuraṃ yuddhaṃ pūrvam āsīt sudāruṇam
a kurvāṇau tu mahat karma bhīmasenaghaṭotkacau
b pitā putraś ca samare kurvāṇau karma duṣkaram
b rājānaṃ pratyudīyetāṃ bhīmasenaghaṭotkacau
c duryodhanas tato 'bhyetya tāv ubhāv abhyavārayat
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma haiḍimbasya parākramam
c atītya pitaraṃ yuddhe yad ayudhyata bhārata
a bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddho duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c hṛdy avidhyat pṛṣatkena prahasann iva pāṇḍavaḥ
a tato duryodhano rājā prahāravaramohitaḥ
c niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalaṃ ca jagāma ha
a taṃ visaṃjñam atho jñātvā tvaramāṇo 'sya sārathiḥ
c apovāha raṇād rājaṃs tataḥ sainyam abhidyata
a tatas tāṃ kauravīṃ senāṃ dravamāṇāṃ samantataḥ
c nighnan bhīmaḥ śarais tīkṣṇair anuvavrāja pṛṣṭhataḥ
a pārṣataś ca rathaśreṣṭho dharmaputraś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c droṇasya paśyataḥ sainyaṃ gāṅgeyasya ca paśyataḥ
e jaghnatur viśikhais tīkṣṇaiḥ parānīkaviśātanaiḥ
a dravamāṇaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ tava putrasya saṃyuge
c nāśaknutāṃ vārayituṃ bhīṣmadroṇau mahārathau
a vāryamāṇaṃ hi bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca viśāṃ pate
c vidravaty eva tat sainyaṃ paśyator droṇabhīṣmayoḥ
a tato rathasahasreṣu vidravatsu tatas tataḥ
c tāv āsthitāv ekarathaṃ saubhadraśinipuṃgavau
e saubalīṃ samare senāṃ śātayetāṃ samantataḥ
a śuśubhāte tadā tau tu śaineyakurupuṃgavau
c amāvāsyāṃ gatau yadvat somasūryau nabhastale
a arjunas tu tataḥ kruddhas tava sainyaṃ viśāṃ pate
c vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa dhārābhir iva toyadaḥ
a vadhyamānaṃ tatas tat tu śaraiḥ pārthasya saṃyuge
c dudrāva kauravaṃ sainyaṃ viṣādabhayakampitam
d vāryamāṇaṃ mahārāja bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādibhiḥ
a dravatas tān samālokya bhīṣmadroṇau mahārathau
c nyavārayetāṃ saṃrabdhau duryodhanahitaiṣiṇau
a tato duryodhano rājā samāśvasya viśāṃ pate
c nyavartayata tat sainyaṃ dravamāṇaṃ samantataḥ
a yatra yatra sutaṃ tubhyaṃ yo yaḥ paśyati bhārata
c tatra tatra nyavartanta kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahārathāḥ
a tān nivṛttān samīkṣyaiva tato 'nye 'pītare janāḥ
c anyonyaspardhayā rājaṃl lajjayānye 'vatasthire
a punarāvartatāṃ teṣāṃ vega āsīd viśāṃ pate
c pūryataḥ sāgarasyeva candrasyodayanaṃ prati
a saṃnivṛttāṃs tatas tāṃs tu dṛṣṭvā rājā suyodhanaḥ
c abravīt tvarito gatvā bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ vacaḥ
a pitāmaha nibodhedaṃ yat tvā vakṣyāmi bhārata
c nānurūpam ahaṃ manye tvayi jīvati kaurava
a droṇe cāstravidāṃ śreṣṭhe saputre sasuhṛjjane
c kṛpe caiva maheṣvāse dravatīyaṃ varūthinī
a na pāṇḍavāḥ pratibalās tava rājan kathaṃ cana
c tathā droṇasya saṃgrāme drauṇeś caiva kṛpasya ca
a anugrāhyāḥ pāṇḍusutā nūnaṃ tava pitāmaha
c yathemāṃ kṣamase vīra vadhyamānāṃ varūthinīm
a so 'smi vācyas tvayā rājan pūrvam eva samāgame
c na yotsye pāṇḍavān saṃkhye nāpi pārṣatasātyakī
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tubhyam ācāryasya kṛpasya ca
c karṇena sahitaḥ kṛtyaṃ cintayānas tadaiva hi
a yadi nāhaṃ parityājyo yuvābhyām iha saṃyuge
c vikrameṇānurūpeṇa yudhyetāṃ puruṣarṣabhau
a etac chrutvā vaco bhīṣmaḥ prahasan vai muhur muhuḥ
c abravīt tanayaṃ tubhyaṃ krodhād udvṛtya cakṣuṣī
a bahuśo hi mayā rājaṃs tathyam uktaṃ hitaṃ vacaḥ
c ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavā yuddhe devair api savāsavaiḥ
a yat tu śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ vṛddhenādya nṛpottama
c kariṣyāmi yathāśakti prekṣedānīṃ sabāndhavaḥ
a adya pāṇḍusutān sarvān sasainyān saha bandhubhiḥ
c miṣato vārayiṣyāmi sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
a evam ukte tu bhīṣmeṇa putrās tava janeśvara
c dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yuktā bherīś ca jaghnire bhṛśam
a pāṇḍavāpi tato rājañ śrutvā taṃ ninadaṃ mahat
c dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca bherīś ca murajāṃś ca vyanādayan
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a pratijñāte tu bhīṣmeṇa tasmin yuddhe sudāruṇe
b pāṇḍūn āvārayiṣyeti kathaṃ yuyudhire nṛpāḥ
c krodhito mama putreṇa duḥkhitena viśeṣataḥ
a bhīṣmaḥ kim akarot tatra pāṇḍaveyeṣu saṃjaya
c pitāmahe vā pāñcālās tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a gatapūrvāhṇabhūyiṣṭhe tasminn ahani bhārata
b paścimāṃ diśam āsthāya sthite cāpi divākare
c jayaṃ prāpteṣu hṛṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
a sarvadharmaviśeṣajñaḥ pitā devavratas tava
c abhyayāj javanair aśvaiḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
e mahatyā senayā guptas tava putraiś ca sarvaśaḥ
a prāvartata tato yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c asmākaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham anayāt tava bhārata
a dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ tatra talānāṃ cābhihanyatām
c mahān samabhavac chabdo girīṇām iva dīryatām
a tiṣṭha sthito 'smi viddhy enaṃ nivartasva sthiro bhava
c sthito 'smi praharasveti śabdāḥ śrūyanta sarvaśaḥ
a kāñcaneṣu tanutreṣu kirīṭeṣu dhvajeṣu ca
c śilānām iva śaileṣu patitānām abhūt svanaḥ
a patitāny uttamāṅgāni bāhavaś ca vibhūṣitāḥ
c vyaceṣṭanta mahīṃ prāpya śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a hṛtottamāṅgāḥ ke cit tu tathaivodyatakārmukāḥ
c pragṛhītāyudhāś cāpi tasthuḥ puruṣasattamāḥ
a prāvartata mahāvegā nadī rudhiravāhinī
c mātaṅgāṅgaśilāraudrā māṃsaśoṇitakardamā
a varāśvanaranāgānāṃ śarīraprabhavā tadā
c paralokārṇavamukhī gṛdhragomāyumodinī
a na dṛṣṭaṃ na śrutaṃ cāpi yuddham etādṛśaṃ nṛpa
c yathā tava sutānāṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārata
a nāsīd rathapathas tatra yodhair yudhi nipātitaiḥ
c gajaiś ca patitair nīlair giriśṛṅgair ivāvṛtam
a vikīrṇaiḥ kavacaiś citrair dhvajaiś chatraiś ca māriṣa
c śuśubhe tad raṇasthānaṃ śaradīva nabhastalam
a vinirbhinnāḥ śaraiḥ ke cid antapīḍāvikarṣiṇaḥ
c abhītāḥ samare śatrūn abhyadhāvanta daṃśitāḥ
a tāta bhrātaḥ sakhe bandho vayasya mama mātula
c mā māṃ parityajety anye cukruśuḥ patitā raṇe
a ādhāvābhyehi mā gaccha kiṃ bhīto 'si kva yāsyasi
c sthito 'haṃ samare mā bhair iti cānye vicukruśuḥ
a tatra bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo nityaṃ maṇḍalakārmukaḥ
c mumoca bāṇān dīptāgrān ahīn āśīviṣān iva
a śarair ekāyanīkurvan diśaḥ sarvā yatavrataḥ
c jaghāna pāṇḍavarathān ādiśyādiśya bhārata
a sa nṛtyan vai rathopasthe darśayan pāṇilāghavam
c alātacakravad rājaṃs tatra tatra sma dṛśyate
a tam ekaṃ samare śūraṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayās tathā
c anekaśatasāhasraṃ samapaśyanta lāghavāt
a māyākṛtātmānam iva bhīṣmaṃ tatra sma menire
c pūrvasyāṃ diśi taṃ dṛṣṭvā pratīcyāṃ dadṛśur janāḥ
a udīcyāṃ cainam ālokya dakṣiṇasyāṃ punaḥ prabho
c evaṃ sa samare vīro gāṅgeyaḥ pratyadṛśyata
a na cainaṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ kaś cic chaknoti vīkṣitum
c viśikhān eva paśyanti bhīṣmacāpacyutān bahūn
a kurvāṇaṃ samare karma sūdayānaṃ ca vāhinīm
c vyākrośanta raṇe tatra vīrā bahuvidhaṃ bahu
e amānuṣeṇa rūpeṇa carantaṃ pitaraṃ tava
a śalabhā iva rājānaḥ patanti vidhicoditāḥ
c bhīṣmāgnim abhi saṃkruddhaṃ vināśāya sahasraśaḥ
a na hi moghaḥ śaraḥ kaś cid āsīd bhīṣmasya saṃyuge
c naranāgāśvakāyeṣu bahutvāl laghuvedhinaḥ
a bhinatty ekena bāṇena sumuktena patatriṇā
c gajakaṅkaṭasaṃnāhaṃ vajreṇevācalottamam
a dvau trīn api gajārohān piṇḍitān varmitān api
c nārācena sutīkṣṇena nijaghāna pitā tava
a yo yo bhīṣmaṃ naravyāghram abhyeti yudhi kaś cana
c muhūrtadṛṣṭaḥ sa mayā pātito bhuvi dṛśyate
a evaṃ sā dharmarājasya vadhyamānā mahācamūḥ
c bhīṣmeṇātulavīryeṇa vyaśīryata sahasradhā
a prakīryata mahāsenā śaravarṣābhitāpitā
c paśyato vāsudevasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ
a yatamānāpi te vīrā dravamāṇān mahārathān
c nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ bhīṣmabāṇaprapīḍitāḥ
a mahendrasamavīryeṇa vadhyamānā mahācamūḥ
c abhajyata mahārāja na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥ
a āviddhanaranāgāśvaṃ patitadhvajakūbaram
c anīkaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ hāhābhūtam acetanam
a jaghānātra pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ tathā
c priyaṃ sakhāyaṃ cākrande sakhā daivabalātkṛtaḥ
a vimucya kavacān anye pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥ
c prakīrya keśān dhāvantaḥ pratyadṛśyanta bhārata
a tad gokulam ivodbhrāntam udbhrāntarathayūthapam
c dadṛśe pāṇḍuputrasya sainyam ārtasvaraṃ tadā
a prabhajyamānaṃ tat sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā devakinandanaḥ
c uvāca pārthaṃ bībhatsuṃ nigṛhya ratham uttamam
a ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pārtha yaḥ kāṅkṣitas tvayā
c praharāsmai naravyāghra na cen mohād vimuhyase
a yat tvayā kathitaṃ vīra purā rājñāṃ samāgame
c bhīṣmadroṇamukhān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikān
a sānubandhān haniṣyāmi ye māṃ yotsyanti saṃyuge
c iti tat kuru kaunteya satyaṃ vākyam ariṃdama
a bībhatso paśya sainyaṃ svaṃ bhajyamānaṃ samantataḥ
c dravataś ca mahīpālān sarvān yaudhiṣṭhire bale
a dṛṣṭvā hi samare bhīṣmaṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam
c bhayārtāḥ saṃpraṇaśyanti siṃhaṃ kṣudramṛgā iva
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca vāsudevaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c codayāśvān yato bhīṣmo vigāhyaitad balārṇavam
d pātayiṣyāmi durdharṣaṃ kuruvṛddhaṃ pitāmaham
a tato 'śvān rajataprakhyāṃś codayām āsa mādhavaḥ
c yato bhīṣmaratho rājan duṣprekṣyo raśmimān iva
a tatas tat punar āvṛttaṃ yudhiṣṭhirabalaṃ mahat
c dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ mahābāhuṃ bhīṣmāyodyantam āhave
a tato bhīṣmaḥ kuruśreṣṭhaḥ siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥ
c dhanaṃjayarathaṃ tūrṇaṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
a kṣaṇena sa rathas tasya sahayaḥ sahasārathiḥ
c śaravarṣeṇa mahatā saṃchanno na prakāśate
a vāsudevas tv asaṃbhrānto dhairyam āsthāya sattvavān
c codayām āsa tān aśvān vitunnān bhīṣmasāyakaiḥ
a tataḥ pārtho dhanur gṛhya divyaṃ jaladanisvanam
c pātayām āsa bhīṣmasya dhanuś chittvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a sa cchinnadhanvā kauravyaḥ punar anyan mahad dhanuḥ
c nimeṣāntaramātreṇa sajyaṃ cakre pitā tava
a vicakarṣa tato dorbhyāṃ dhanur jaladanisvanam
c athāsya tad api kruddhaś ciccheda dhanur arjunaḥ
a tasya tat pūjayām āsa lāghavaṃ śaṃtanoḥ sutaḥ
c sādhu pārtha mahābāho sādhu bho pāṇḍunandana
a tvayy evaitad yuktarūpaṃ mahat karma dhanaṃjaya
c prīto 'smi sudṛḍhaṃ putra kuru yuddhaṃ mayā saha
a iti pārthaṃ praśasyātha pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥ
c mumoca samare vīraḥ śarān pārtharathaṃ prati
a adarśayad vāsudevo hayayāne paraṃ balam
c moghān kurvañ śarāṃs tasya maṇḍalāny acaral laghu
a tathāpi bhīṣmaḥ sudṛḍhaṃ vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
c vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiḥ sarvagātreṣu māriṣa
a śuśubhāte naravyāghrau tau bhīṣmaśaravikṣatau
c govṛṣāv iva nardantau viṣāṇollikhitāṅkitau
a punaś cāpi susaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c kṛṣṇayor yudhi saṃrabdho bhīṣmo vyāvārayad diśaḥ
d pārtho 'pi samare kruddho bhīṣmasyāvārayad diśaḥ
d bhīṣmo 'pi rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pārthasyāvārayad diśaḥ
a vārṣṇeyaṃ ca śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kampayām āsa roṣitaḥ
c muhur abhyutsmayan bhīṣmaḥ prahasya svanavat tadā
a tataḥ kṛṣṇas tu samare dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaparākramam
c saṃprekṣya ca mahābāhuḥ pārthasya mṛduyuddhatām
a bhīṣmaṃ ca śaravarṣāṇi sṛjantam aniśaṃ yudhi
c pratapantam ivādityaṃ madhyam āsādya senayoḥ
a varān varān vinighnantaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya sainikān
c yugāntam iva kurvāṇaṃ bhīṣmaṃ yaudhiṣṭhire bale
a amṛṣyamāṇo bhagavān keśavaḥ paravīrahā
c acintayad ameyātmā nāsti yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ balam
a ekāhnā hi raṇe bhīṣmo nāśayed devadānavān
c kim u pāṇḍusutān yuddhe sabalān sapadānugān
a dravate ca mahat sainyaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
c ete ca kauravās tūrṇaṃ prabhagnān dṛśya somakān
e ādravanti raṇe hṛṣṭā harṣayantaḥ pitāmaham
a so 'haṃ bhīṣmaṃ nihanmy adya pāṇḍavārthāya daṃśitaḥ
c bhāram etaṃ vineṣyāmi pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
a arjuno 'pi śarais tīkṣṇair vadhyamāno hi saṃyuge
c kartavyaṃ nābhijānāti raṇe bhīṣmasya gauravāt
a tathā cintayatas tasya bhūya eva pitāmahaḥ
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ śarān pārtharathaṃ prati
a teṣāṃ bahutvād dhi bhṛśaṃ śarāṇāṃ
diśo 'tha sarvāḥ pihitā babhūvuḥ
c na cāntarikṣaṃ na diśo na bhūmir
na bhāskaro 'dṛśyata raśmimālī
e vavuś ca vātās tumulāḥ sadhūmā
diśaś ca sarvāḥ kṣubhitā babhūvuḥ
a droṇo vikarṇo 'tha jayadrathaś ca
bhūriśravāḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaś ca
c śrutāyur ambaṣṭhapatiś ca rājā
vindānuvindau ca sudakṣiṇaś ca
a prācyāś ca sauvīragaṇāś ca sarve
vasātayaḥ kṣudrakamālavāś ca
c kirīṭinaṃ tvaramāṇābhisasrur
nideśagāḥ śāṃtanavasya rājñaḥ
d tavāpi putrasya tu kopanasya
a taṃ vājipādātarathaughajālair
anekasāhasraśatair dadarśa
c kirīṭinaṃ saṃparivāryamāṇaṃ
śiner naptā vāraṇayūthapaiś ca
a tatas tu dṛṣṭvārjunavāsudevau
padātināgāśvarathaiḥ samantāt
c abhidrutau śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhau
śinipravīro 'bhisasāra tūrṇam
a sa tāny anīkāni mahādhanuṣmāñ
śinipravīraḥ sahasābhipatya
c cakāra sāhāyyam athārjunasya
viṣṇur yathā vṛtraniṣūdanasya
a viśīrṇanāgāśvarathadhvajaughaṃ
bhīṣmeṇa vitrāsitasarvayodham
c yudhiṣṭhirānīkam abhidravantaṃ
provāca saṃdṛśya śinipravīraḥ
a kva kṣatriyā yāsyatha naiṣa dharmaḥ
satāṃ purastāt kathitaḥ purāṇaiḥ
c mā svāṃ pratijñāṃ jahata pravīrāḥ
svaṃ vīradharmaṃ paripālayadhvam
a tān vāsavān antarajo niśamya
narendramukhyān dravataḥ samantāt
c pārthasya dṛṣṭvā mṛduyuddhatāṃ ca
bhīṣmaṃ ca saṃkhye samudīryamāṇam
a amṛṣyamāṇaḥ sa tato mahātmā
yaśasvinaṃ sarvadaśārhabhartā
c uvāca śaineyam abhipraśaṃsan
dṛṣṭvā kurūn āpatataḥ samantāt
a ye yānti yāntv eva śinipravīra
ye 'pi sthitāḥ sātvata te 'pi yāntu
c bhīṣmaṃ rathāt paśya nipātyamānaṃ
droṇaṃ ca saṃkhye sagaṇaṃ mayādya
a nāsau rathaḥ sātvata kauravāṇāṃ
kruddhasya mucyeta raṇe 'dya kaś cit
c tasmād ahaṃ gṛhya rathāṅgam ugraṃ
prāṇaṃ hariṣyāmi mahāvratasya
a nihatya bhīṣmaṃ sagaṇaṃ tathājau
droṇaṃ ca śaineya rathapravīram
c prītiṃ kariṣyāmi dhanaṃjayasya
rājñaś ca bhīmasya tathāśvinoś ca
a nihatya sarvān dhṛtarāṣṭraputrāṃs
tatpakṣiṇo ye ca narendramukhyāḥ
c rājyena rājānam ajātaśatruṃ
saṃpādayiṣyāmy aham adya hṛṣṭaḥ
d itīdam uktvā sa mahānubhāvaḥ
d sasmāra cakraṃ niśitaṃ purāṇam
d sudarśanaṃ cintitamātram eva
d tasyāgrahastaṃ svayam āruroha
a tataḥ sunābhaṃ vasudevaputraḥ
sūryaprabhaṃ vajrasamaprabhāvam
c kṣurāntam udyamya bhujena cakraṃ
rathād avaplutya visṛjya vāhān
a saṃkampayan gāṃ caraṇair mahātmā
vegena kṛṣṇaḥ prasasāra bhīṣmam
c madāndham ājau samudīrṇadarpaḥ
siṃho jighāṃsann iva vāraṇendram
a so 'bhyadravad bhīṣmam anīkamadhye
kruddho mahendrāvarajaḥ pramāthī
c vyālambipītāntapaṭaś cakāśe
ghano yathā khe 'cirabhāpinaddhaḥ
a sudarśanaṃ cāsya rarāja śaures
tac cakrapadmaṃ subhujorunālam
c yathādipadmaṃ taruṇārkavarṇaṃ
rarāja nārāyaṇanābhijātam
a tat kṛṣṇakopodayasūryabuddhaṃ
kṣurāntatīkṣṇāgrasujātapatram
c tasyaiva dehorusaraḥprarūḍhaṃ
rarāja nārāyaṇabāhunālam
a tam āttacakraṃ praṇadantam uccaiḥ
kruddhaṃ mahendrāvarajaṃ samīkṣya
c sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhṛśaṃ vineduḥ
kṣayaṃ kurūṇām iti cintayitvā
a sa vāsudevaḥ pragṛhītacakraḥ
saṃvartayiṣyann iva jīvalokam
c abhyutpataṃl lokagurur babhāse
bhūtāni dhakṣyann iva kālavahniḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ pragṛhītacakraṃ
samīkṣya devaṃ dvipadāṃ variṣṭham
c asaṃbhramāt kārmukabāṇapāṇī
rathe sthitaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bhyuvāca
d asaṃbhramaṃ tad vicakarṣa dorbhyāṃ
d mahādhanur gāṇḍivatulyaghoṣam
d uvāca bhīṣmas tam anantapauruṣaṃ
d govindam ājāv avimūḍhacetāḥ
a ehy ehi deveśa jagannivāsa
namo 'stu te śārṅgarathāṅgapāṇe
c prasahya māṃ pātaya lokanātha
rathottamād bhūtaśaraṇya saṃkhye
d mamogracakreṇa nikṛnta dehaṃ
a tvayā hatasyeha mamādya kṛṣṇa
śreyaḥ parasminn iha caiva loke
c saṃbhāvito 'smy andhakavṛṣṇinātha
lokais tribhir vīra tavābhiyānāt
d śrutvā vacaḥ śāṃtanavasya kṛṣṇo
d vegena dhāvaṃs tam athābhyuvāca
d tvaṃ mūlam asyeha bhuvi kṣayasya
d duryodhanaṃ cādya samuddhariṣyasi
d durdyūtadevī nṛpatir nivāryaḥ
d sumantriṇā dharmapathi sthitena
d tyājyo 'tha vā kālaparītabuddhir
d dharmātigo yaḥ kulapāṃsanaḥ syāt
d bhīṣmas tad ākarṇya yadupravīraṃ
d rājā paraṃ daivatam ity uvāca
d tyaktas tu kaṃso yadubhir hitārthe
d dharmāt kurūṇām adhipas tadānīm
d saṃbodhyamāno na bubodha rājā
d kleśāya daivād viparītabuddhiḥ
d śrotā hitaṃ yasya na kaś cid asti
d vaktā bhṛśaṃ syāt sa tu kiṃ bravītu
a rathād avaplutya tatas tvarāvān
pārtho 'py anudrutya yadupravīram
c jagrāha pīnottamalambabāhuṃ
bāhvor hariṃ vyāyatapīnabāhuḥ
a nigṛhyamāṇaś ca tadādidevo
bhṛśaṃ saroṣaḥ kila nāma yogī
c ādāya vegena jagāma viṣṇur
jiṣṇuṃ mahāvāta ivaikavṛkṣam
a pārthas tu viṣṭabhya balena pādau
bhīṣmāntikaṃ tūrṇam abhidravantam
c balān nijagrāha kirīṭamālī
pade 'tha rājan daśame kathaṃ cit
a avasthitaṃ ca praṇipatya kṛṣṇaṃ
prīto 'rjunaḥ kāñcanacitramālī
c uvāca kopaṃ pratisaṃhareti
gatir bhavān keśava pāṇḍavānām
a na hāsyate karma yathāpratijñaṃ
putraiḥ śape keśava sodaraiś ca
c antaṃ kariṣyāmi yathā kurūṇāṃ
tvayāham indrānuja saṃprayuktaḥ
a tataḥ pratijñāṃ samayaṃ ca tasmai
janārdanaḥ prītamanā niśamya
c sthitaḥ priye kauravasattamasya
rathaṃ sacakraḥ punar āruroha
d tataḥ pratijñāṃ samavāpya bhīṣmaḥ
d kṛtāñjaliḥ stutyam athākarod vai
d traivikrame yasya vapur babhāse

a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c duryodhanaṃ tribhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
a śalyaṃ ca pañcaviṃśatyā śarair vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥ
c rukmapuṅkhair maheṣvāsaḥ sa viddho vyapayād raṇāt
a pratyudyayus tato bhīmaṃ tava putrāś caturdaśa
c senāpatiḥ suṣeṇaś ca jalasaṃdhaḥ sulocanaḥ
a ugro bhīmaratho bhīmo bhīmabāhur alolupaḥ
c durmukho duṣpradharṣaś ca vivitsur vikaṭaḥ samaḥ
a visṛjanto bahūn bāṇān krodhasaṃraktalocanāḥ
c bhīmasenam abhidrutya vivyadhuḥ sahitā bhṛśam
a putrāṃs tu tava saṃprekṣya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c sṛkkiṇī vilihan vīraḥ paśumadhye vṛko yathā
d abhipatya mahābāhur garutmān iva vegitaḥ
e senāpateḥ kṣurapreṇa śiraś ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ
f saṃprahṛṣya ca hṛṣṭātmā tribhir bāṇair mahābhujaḥ
a jalasaṃdhaṃ vinirbhidya so 'nayad yamasādanam
c suṣeṇaṃ ca tato hatvā preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
d vicitraṃ ca tathā hatvā preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
a ugrasya saśirastrāṇaṃ śiraś candropamaṃ bhuvi
c pātayām āsa bhallena kuṇḍalābhyāṃ vibhūṣitam
a bhīmabāhuṃ ca saptatyā sāśvaketuṃ sasārathim
c nināya samare bhīmaḥ paralokāya māriṣa
a bhīmaṃ bhīmarathaṃ cobhau bhīmaseno hasann iva
c bhrātarau rabhasau rājann anayad yamasādanam
a tataḥ sulocanaṃ bhīmaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahāmṛdhe
c miṣatāṃ sarvasainyānām anayad yamasādanam
a putrās tu tava taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaparākramam
c śeṣā ye 'nye 'bhavaṃs tatra te bhīmasya bhayārditāḥ
e vipradrutā diśo rājan vadhyamānā mahātmanā
a tato 'bravīc chāṃtanavaḥ sarvān eva mahārathān
c eṣa bhīmo raṇe kruddho dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathān
a yathāprāgryān yathājyeṣṭhān yathāśūrāṃś ca saṃgatān
c nipātayaty ugradhanvā taṃ pramathnīta pārthivāḥ
a evam uktās tataḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃkruddhā bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
a bhagadattaḥ prabhinnena kuñjareṇa viśāṃ pate
c apatat sahasā tatra yatra bhīmo vyavasthitaḥ
a āpatann eva ca raṇe bhīmasenaṃ śilāśitaiḥ
c adṛśyaṃ samare cakre jīmūta iva bhāskaram
a abhimanyumukhās tatra nāmṛṣyanta mahārathāḥ
c bhīmasyācchādanaṃ saṃkhye svabāhubalam āśritāḥ
a ta enaṃ śaravarṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayan
c gajaṃ ca śaravṛṣṭyā taṃ bibhidus te samantataḥ
a sa śastravṛṣṭyābhihataḥ prādravad dviguṇaṃ padam
c prāgjyotiṣagajo rājan nānāliṅgaiḥ sutejanaiḥ
a saṃjātarudhirotpīḍaḥ prekṣaṇīyo 'bhavad raṇe
c gabhastibhir ivārkasya saṃsyūto jalado mahān
a sa codito madasrāvī bhagadattena vāraṇaḥ
c abhyadhāvata tān sarvān kālotsṛṣṭa ivāntakaḥ
e dviguṇaṃ javam āsthāya kampayaṃś caraṇair mahīm
a tasya tat sumahad rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve mahārathāḥ
c asahyaṃ manyamānās te nātipramanaso 'bhavan
a tatas tu nṛpatiḥ kruddho bhīmasenaṃ stanāntare
c ājaghāna naravyāghra śareṇa nataparvaṇā
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāsas tena rājñā mahārathaḥ
c mūrchayābhiparītāṅgo dhvajayaṣṭim upāśritaḥ
a tāṃs tu bhītān samālakṣya bhīmasenaṃ ca mūrchitam
c nanāda balavan nādaṃ bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
d bhīmo 'pi labdhasaṃjñas tu adravat sa tato raṇe
a tato ghaṭotkaco rājan prekṣya bhīmaṃ tathāgatam
c saṃkruddho rākṣaso ghoras tatraivāntaradhīyata
a sa kṛtvā dāruṇāṃ māyāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinīm
c adṛśyata nimeṣārdhād ghorarūpaṃ samāśritaḥ
a airāvataṃ samāruhya svayaṃ māyāmayaṃ kṛtam
b kailāsagirisaṃkāśaṃ vajrapāṇir ivābhyayāt
c tasya cānye 'pi diṅnāgā babhūvur anuyāyinaḥ
a añjano vāmanaś caiva mahāpadmaś ca suprabhaḥ
c traya ete mahānāgā rākṣasaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ
d madhye trigartāsic
n rākṣasyo labhante prasravanti ca
d kāmarūpadharāś caiva bhavanti bahurūpakāḥ
d praṇamya vikacaḥ pādāv agṛhṇāt pitaraṃ tadā
d mātuś ca parameṣvāsas tau ca nāmāsya cakratuḥ
d ghaṭotkacasyoktapūrvaṃ mātā taṃ pratyabhāṣata
d abravīt tena nāmāsya ghaṭotkaca iti sma ha
d sa hi sṛṣṭo maghavatā karṇahetor mahātmanā
d karṇasyāprativīryasya pratiyoddhā mahārathaḥ
a mahākāyās tridhā rājan prasravanto madaṃ bahu
c tejovīryabalopetā mahābalaparākramāḥ
d preṣitāś ca mahārāja rākṣasaiś ca caturdiśam
a ghaṭotkacas tu svaṃ nāgaṃ codayām āsa taṃ tataḥ
c sagajaṃ bhagadattaṃ tu hantukāmaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
a te cānye coditā nāgā rākṣasais tair mahābalaiḥ
c paripetuḥ susaṃrabdhāś caturdaṃṣṭrāś caturdiśam
e bhagadattasya taṃ nāgaṃ viṣāṇais te 'bhyapīḍayan
a saṃpīḍyamānas tair nāgair vedanārtaḥ śarāturaḥ
c so 'nadat sumahānādam indrāśanisamasvanam
d nyavartata mahāghoṣo bhīmasenaśarārditaḥ
d mṛditvā sarvasainyāni tava putrasya bhārata
a tasya taṃ nadato nādaṃ sughoraṃ bhīmanisvanam
c śrutvā bhīṣmo 'bravīd droṇaṃ rājānaṃ ca suyodhanam
a eṣa yudhyati saṃgrāme haiḍimbena durātmanā
c bhagadatto maheṣvāsaḥ kṛcchreṇa parivartate
a rākṣasaś ca mahāmāyaḥ sa ca rājātikopanaḥ
c tau sametau mahāvīryau kālamṛtyusamāv ubhau
a śrūyate hy eṣa hṛṣṭānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāsvanaḥ
c hastinaś caiva sumahān bhītasya ruvato dhvaniḥ
a tatra gacchāma bhadraṃ vo rājānaṃ parirakṣitum
c arakṣyamāṇaḥ samare kṣipraṃ prāṇān vimokṣyate
a te tvaradhvaṃ mahāvīryāḥ kiṃ cireṇa prayāmahe
c mahān hi vartate raudraḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
a bhaktaś ca kulaputraś ca śūraś ca pṛtanāpatiḥ
c yuktaṃ tasya paritrāṇaṃ kartum asmābhir acyutāḥ
a bhīṣmasya tad vacaḥ śrutvā bhāradvājapurogamāḥ
c sahitāḥ sarvarājāno bhagadattaparīpsayā
e uttamaṃ javam āsthāya prayayur yatra so 'bhavat
a tān prayātān samālokya yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥ
c pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayuḥ parān
a tāny anīkāny athālokya rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavān
c nanāda sumahānādaṃ visphoṭam aśaner iva
a tasya taṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā nāgāṃś ca yudhyataḥ
c bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bhūyo bhāradvājam abhāṣata
a na rocate me saṃgrāmo haiḍimbena durātmanā
c balavīryasamāviṣṭaḥ sasahāyaś ca sāṃpratam
a naiṣa śakyo yudhā jetum api vajrabhṛtā svayam
c labdhalakṣyaḥ prahārī ca vayaṃ ca śrāntavāhanāḥ
e pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiś ca divasaṃ kṣatavikṣatāḥ
f idānīṃ yudhi nirjetuṃ na śakyo 'sau sa rākṣasaḥ
f astam abhyeti savitā rātrau yoddhuṃ na śakyate
a tan na me rocate yuddhaṃ pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥ
c ghuṣyatām avahāro 'dya śvo yotsyāmaḥ paraiḥ saha
a pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā tathā cakruḥ sma kauravāḥ
c upāyenāpayānaṃ te ghaṭotkacabhayārditāḥ
a kauraveṣu nivṛtteṣu pāṇḍavā jitakāśinaḥ
c siṃhanādam akurvanta śaṅkhaveṇusvanaiḥ saha
a evaṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ divasaṃ bharatarṣabha
c pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca puraskṛtya ghaṭotkacam
a kauravās tu tato rājan prayayuḥ śibiraṃ svakam
c vrīḍamānā niśākāle pāṇḍaveyaiḥ parājitāḥ
a śaravikṣatagātrāś ca pāṇḍuputrā mahārathāḥ
c yuddhe sumanaso bhūtvā śibirāyaiva jagmire
a puraskṛtya mahārāja bhīmasenaghaṭotkacau
c pūjayantas tadānyonyaṃ mudā paramayā yutāḥ
a nadanto vividhān nādāṃs tūryasvanavimiśritān
c siṃhanādāṃś ca kurvāṇā vimiśrāñ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥ
a vinadanto mahātmānaḥ kampayantaś ca medinīm
c ghaṭṭayantaś ca marmāṇi tava putrasya māriṣa
d kampayantaś ca putrāṇāṃ tava cetāṃsi bhūmipa
d putrāś ca tava rājendra tathaiva śaravikṣatāḥ
e prayātāḥ śibirāyaiva niśākāle paraṃtapāḥ
a duryodhanas tu nṛpatir dīno bhrātṛvadhena ca
c muhūrtaṃ cintayām āsa bāṣpaśokasamākulaḥ
a tataḥ kṛtvā vidhiṃ sarvaṃ śibirasya yathāvidhi
c pradadhyau śokasaṃtapto bhrātṛvyasanakarśitaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a bhayaṃ me sumahaj jātaṃ vismayaś caiva saṃjaya
c śrutvā pāṇḍukumārāṇāṃ karma devaiḥ suduṣkaram
a putrāṇāṃ ca parābhavaṃ śrutvā saṃjaya sarvaśaḥ
c cintā me mahatī sūta bhaviṣyati kathaṃ tv iti
a dhruvaṃ viduravākyāni dhakṣyanti hṛdayaṃ mama
c yathā hi dṛśyate sarvaṃ daivayogena saṃjaya
a yatra bhīṣmamukhāñ śūrān astrajñān yodhasattamān
c pāṇḍavānām anīkāni yodhayanti prahāriṇaḥ
a kenāvadhyā mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍuputrā mahābalāḥ
c kena dattavarās tāta kiṃ vā jñānaṃ vidanti te
e yena kṣayaṃ na gacchanti divi tārāgaṇā iva
a punaḥ punar na mṛṣyāmi hataṃ sainyaṃ sma pāṇḍavaiḥ
c mayy eva daṇḍaḥ patati daivāt paramadāruṇaḥ
a yathāvadhyāḥ pāṇḍusutā yathā vadhyāś ca me sutāḥ
c etan me sarvam ācakṣva yathātattvena saṃjaya
a na hi pāraṃ prapaśyāmi duḥkhasyāsya kathaṃ cana
c samudrasyeva mahato bhujābhyāṃ prataran naraḥ
a putrāṇāṃ vyasanaṃ manye dhruvaṃ prāptaṃ sudāruṇam
c ghātayiṣyati me putrān sarvān bhīmo na saṃśayaḥ
a na hi paśyāmi taṃ vīraṃ yo me rakṣet sutān raṇe
c dhruvaṃ vināśaḥ samare putrāṇāṃ mama saṃjaya
a tasmān me kāraṇaṃ sūta yuktiṃ caiva viśeṣataḥ
c pṛcchato 'dya yathātattvaṃ sarvam ākhyātum arhasi
a duryodhano 'pi yac cakre dṛṣṭvā svān vimukhān raṇe
c bhīṣmadroṇau kṛpaś caiva saubaleyo jayadrathaḥ
e drauṇir vāpi maheṣvāso vikarṇo vā mahābalaḥ
a niścayo vāpi kas teṣāṃ tadā hy āsīn mahātmanām
c vimukheṣu mahāprājña mama putreṣu saṃjaya
d yad vṛttaṃ tatra saṃgrāme tad bhavān vaktum arhati
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājann avahitaḥ śrutvā caivāvadhāraya
c naiva mantrakṛtaṃ kiṃ cin naiva māyāṃ tathāvidhām
e na vai vibhīṣikāṃ kāṃ cid rājan kurvanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a yudhyanti te yathānyāyaṃ śaktimantaś ca saṃyuge
c dharmeṇa sarvakāryāṇi kīrtitānīti bhārata
e ārabhante sadā pārthāḥ prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥ
a na te yuddhān nivartante dharmopetā mahābalāḥ
c śriyā paramayā yuktā yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
e tenāvadhyā raṇe pārthā jayayuktāś ca pārthiva
a tava putrā durātmānaḥ pāpeṣv abhiratāḥ sadā
c niṣṭhurā hīnakarmāṇas tena hīyanti saṃyuge
a subahūni nṛśaṃsāni putrais tava janeśvara
c nikṛtānīha pāṇḍūnāṃ nīcair iva yathā naraiḥ
a sarvaṃ ca tad anādṛtya putrāṇāṃ tava kilbiṣam
c sāpahnavāḥ sadaivāsan pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvaja
e na cainān bahu manyante putrās tava viśāṃ pate
a tasya pāpasya satataṃ kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ
c saṃprāptaṃ sumahad ghoraṃ phalaṃ kiṃpākasaṃnibham
e sa tad bhuṅkṣva mahārāja saputraḥ sasuhṛjjanaḥ
a nāvabudhyasi yad rājan vāryamāṇaḥ suhṛjjanaiḥ
c vidureṇātha bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā
a tathā mayā cāpy asakṛd vāryamāṇo na gṛhṇasi
c vākyaṃ hitaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca martyaḥ pathyam ivauṣadham
e putrāṇāṃ matam āsthāya jitān manyasi pāṇḍavān
a śṛṇu bhūyo yathātattvaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
c kāraṇaṃ bharataśreṣṭha pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaṃ prati
e tat te 'haṃ kathayiṣyāmi yathāśrutam ariṃdama
a duryodhanena saṃpṛṣṭa etam arthaṃ pitāmahaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn raṇe sarvān nirjitān sumahārathān
a śokasaṃmūḍhahṛdayo niśākāle sma kauravaḥ
c pitāmahaṃ mahāprājñaṃ vinayenopagamya ha
e yad abravīt sutas te 'sau tan me śṛṇu janeśvara
 duryodhana uvāca
a tvaṃ ca droṇaś ca śalyaś ca kṛpo drauṇis tathaiva ca
c kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
a bhūriśravā vikarṇaś ca bhagadattaś ca vīryavān
c mahārathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥ
a trayāṇām api lokānāṃ paryāptā iti me matiḥ
c pāṇḍavānāṃ samastāś ca na tiṣṭhanti parākrame
a tatra me saṃśayo jātas tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
c yaṃ samāśritya kaunteyā jayanty asmān pade pade
 bhīṣma uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan vaco mahyaṃ yat tvāṃ vakṣyāmi kaurava
c bahuśaś ca mamokto 'si na ca me tattvayā kṛtam
a kriyatāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ śamo bharatasattama
c etat kṣamam ahaṃ manye pṛthivyās tava cābhibho
a bhuñjemāṃ pṛthivīṃ rājan bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sukhī
c durhṛdas tāpayan sarvān nandayaṃś cāpi bāndhavān
a na ca me krośatas tāta śrutavān asi vai purā
c tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ yat pāṇḍūn avamanyase
a yaś ca hetur avadhyatve teṣām akliṣṭakarmaṇām
c taṃ śṛṇuṣva mahārāja mama kīrtayataḥ prabho
a nāsti lokeṣu tad bhūtaṃ bhavitā no bhaviṣyati
c yo jayet pāṇḍavān saṃkhye pālitāñ śārṅgadhanvanā
a yat tu me kathitaṃ tāta munibhir bhāvitātmabhiḥ
c purāṇagītaṃ dharmajña tac chṛṇuṣva yathātatham
a purā kila surāḥ sarve ṛṣayaś ca samāgatāḥ
c pitāmaham upāseduḥ parvate gandhamādane
a madhye teṣāṃ samāsīnaḥ prajāpatir apaśyata
c vimānaṃ jājvalad bhāsā sthitaṃ pravaram ambare
a dhyānenāvedya taṃ brahmā kṛtvā ca niyato 'ñjalim
c namaścakāra hṛṣṭātmā paramaṃ parameśvaram
a ṛṣayas tv atha devāś ca dṛṣṭvā brahmāṇam utthitam
c sthitāḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve paśyanto mahad adbhutam
a yathāvac ca tam abhyarcya brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ
c jagāda jagataḥ sraṣṭā paraṃ paramadharmavit
a viśvāvasur viśvamūrtir viśveśo
viṣvakseno viśvakarmā vaśī ca
c viśveśvaro vāsudevo 'si tasmād
yogātmānaṃ daivataṃ tvām upaimi
d viśvāvāso viśvamūrtir viṣvakseno janārdanaḥ
d viśvakartā viśvapatir devadeva jagatpate
d yogeśvara namaste 'stu saṃsārārṇavatāraṇa
a jaya viśva mahādeva jaya lokahite rata
c jaya yogīśvara vibho jaya yogaparāvara
a padmagarbha viśālākṣa jaya lokeśvareśvara
c bhūtabhavyabhavan nātha jaya saumyātmajātmaja
a asaṃkhyeyaguṇājeya jaya sarvaparāyaṇa
c nārāyaṇa suduṣpāra jaya śārṅgadhanurdhara
a sarvaguhyaguṇopeta viśvamūrte nirāmaya
c viśveśvara mahābāho jaya lokārthatatpara
a mahoraga varāhādya harikeśa vibho jaya
c harivāsa viśāmīśa viśvāvāsāmitāvyaya
a vyaktāvyaktāmitasthāna niyatendriya sendriya
c asaṃkhyeyātmabhāvajña jaya gambhīra kāmada
a ananta viditaprajña nityaṃ bhūtavibhāvana
c kṛtakārya kṛtaprajña dharmajña vijayājaya
a guhyātman sarvabhūtātman sphuṭasaṃbhūtasaṃbhava
c bhūtārthatattva lokeśa jaya bhūtavibhāvana
a ātmayone mahābhāga kalpasaṃkṣepatatpara
c udbhāvana manodbhāva jaya brahmajanapriya
a nisargasargābhirata kāmeśa parameśvara
c amṛtodbhava sadbhāva yugāgne vijayaprada
a prajāpatipate deva padmanābha mahābala
c ātmabhūta mahābhūta karmātmañ jaya karmada
a pādau tava dharā devī diśo bāhur divaṃ śiraḥ
c mūrtis te 'haṃ surāḥ kāyaś candrādityau ca cakṣuṣī
a balaṃ tapaś ca satyaṃ ca dharmaḥ kāmātmajaḥ prabho
c tejo 'gniḥ pavanaḥ śvāsa āpas te svedasaṃbhavāḥ
a aśvinau śravaṇau nityaṃ devī jihvā sarasvatī
c vedāḥ saṃskāraniṣṭhā hi tvayīdaṃ jagad āśritam
a na saṃkhyāṃ na parīmāṇaṃ na tejo na parākramam
c na balaṃ yogayogīśa jānīmas te na saṃbhavam
a tvadbhaktiniratā deva niyamais tvā samāhitāḥ
c arcayāmaḥ sadā viṣṇo parameśaṃ maheśvaram
a ṛṣayo devagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ
c piśācā mānuṣāś caiva mṛgapakṣisarīsṛpāḥ
a evamādi mayā sṛṣṭaṃ pṛthivyāṃ tvatprasādajam
c padmanābha viśālākṣa kṛṣṇa duḥsvapnanāśana
a tvaṃ gatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tvaṃ netā tvaṃ jaganmukham
c tvatprasādena deveśa sukhino vibudhāḥ sadā
a pṛthivī nirbhayā deva tvatprasādāt sadābhavat
c tasmād bhava viśālākṣa yaduvaṃśavivardhanaḥ
a dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya daiteyānāṃ vadhāya ca
c jagato dhāraṇārthāya vijñāpyaṃ kuru me prabho
a yad etat paramaṃ guhyaṃ tvatprasādamayaṃ vibho
c vāsudeva tad etat te mayodgītaṃ yathātatham
a sṛṣṭvā saṃkarṣaṇaṃ devaṃ svayam ātmānam ātmanā
c kṛṣṇa tvam ātmanāsrākṣīḥ pradyumnaṃ cātmasaṃbhavam
a pradyumnāc cāniruddhaṃ tvaṃ yaṃ vidur viṣṇum avyayam
c aniruddho 'sṛjan māṃ vai brahmāṇaṃ lokadhāriṇam
a vāsudevamayaḥ so 'haṃ tvayaivāsmi vinirmitaḥ
b vāsudeveti taṃ vidyād yenāhaṃ nirmitaḥ prabho
b tasmād yācāmi lokeśa caturātmānam ātmanā
c vibhajya bhāgaśo ''tmānaṃ vraja mānuṣatāṃ vibho
a tatrāsuravadhaṃ kṛtvā sarvalokasukhāya vai
c dharmaṃ sthāpya yaśaḥ prāpya yogaṃ prāpsyasi tattvataḥ
a tvāṃ hi brahmarṣayo loke devāś cāmitavikrama
c tais taiś ca nāmabhir bhaktā gāyanti paramātmakam
d sarvabhūteśvaraṃ devaṃ yogaṃ yogeśvaraṃ prabhum
a sthitāś ca sarve tvayi bhūtasaṃghāḥ
kṛtvāśrayaṃ tvāṃ varadaṃ subāho
c anādimadhyāntam apārayogaṃ
lokasya setuṃ pravadanti viprāḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a tataḥ sa bhagavān devo lokānāṃ parameśvaraḥ
c brahmāṇaṃ pratyuvācedaṃ snigdhagambhīrayā girā
a viditaṃ tāta yogān me sarvam etat tavepsitam
c tathā tad bhavitety uktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata
a tato devarṣigandharvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥ
c kautūhalaparāḥ sarve pitāmaham athābruvan
a ko nv ayaṃ yo bhagavatā praṇamya vinayād vibho
c vāgbhiḥ stuto variṣṭhābhiḥ śrotum icchāma taṃ vayam
a evam uktas tu bhagavān pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ
c devabrahmarṣigandharvān sarvān madhurayā girā
a yat tatparaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca bhavitavyaṃ ca yat param
c bhūtātmā yaḥ prabhuś caiva brahma yac ca paraṃ padam
a tenāsmi kṛtasaṃvādaḥ prasannena surarṣabhāḥ
c jagato 'nugrahārthāya yācito me jagatpatiḥ
a mānuṣaṃ lokam ātiṣṭha vāsudeva iti śrutaḥ
c asurāṇāṃ vadhārthāya saṃbhavasva mahītale
c   vāsudeva iti śrutaḥ
c vāsudevagṛhe sākṣāt  
a saṃgrāme nihatā ye te daityadānavarākṣasāḥ
c ta ime nṛṣu saṃbhūtā ghorarūpā mahābalāḥ
a teṣāṃ vadhārthaṃ bhagavān nareṇa sahito vaśī
c mānuṣīṃ yonim āsthāya cariṣyati mahītale
a naranārāyaṇau yau tau purāṇāv ṛṣisattamau
c sahitau mānuṣe loke saṃbhūtāv amitadyutī
a ajeyau samare yattau sahitāv amarair api
c mūḍhās tv etau na jānanti naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
d jagataś cāgrajau vidmas tato devau surarṣabhāḥ
a tasyāham ātmajo brahmā sarvasya jagataḥ patiḥ
c vāsudevo 'rcanīyo vaḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ
a tathā manuṣyo 'yam iti kadā cit surasattamāḥ
c nāvajñeyo mahāvīryaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
d etat puruṣasaṃjñaṃ vai purāṇaṃ rūpam uttamam
a etat paramakaṃ guhyam etat paramakaṃ padam
c etat paramakaṃ brahma etat paramakaṃ yaśaḥ
a etad akṣaram avyaktam etat tac chāśvataṃ mahat
c etat puruṣasaṃjñaṃ vai gīyate jñāyate na ca
a etat paramakaṃ teja etat paramakaṃ sukham
c etat paramakaṃ satyaṃ kīrtitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
a tasmāt sarvaiḥ suraiḥ sendrair lokaiś cāmitavikramaḥ
c nāvajñeyo vāsudevo mānuṣo 'yam iti prabhuḥ
a yaś ca mānuṣamātro 'yam iti brūyāt sumandadhīḥ
c hṛṣīkeśam avajñānāt tam āhuḥ puruṣādhamam
a yoginaṃ taṃ mahātmānaṃ praviṣṭaṃ mānuṣīṃ tanum
c avamanyed vāsudevaṃ tam āhus tāmasaṃ janāḥ
a devaṃ carācarātmānaṃ śrīvatsāṅkaṃ suvarcasam
c padmanābhaṃ na jānāti tam āhus tāmasaṃ janāḥ
a kirīṭakaustubhadharaṃ mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaram
c avajānan mahātmānaṃ ghore tamasi majjati
a evaṃ viditvā tattvārthaṃ lokānām īśvareśvaraḥ
c vāsudevo namaskāryaḥ sarvalokaiḥ surottamāḥ
a evam uktvā sa bhagavān sarvān devagaṇān purā
c visṛjya sarvalokātmā jagāma bhavanaṃ svakam
a tato devāḥ sagandharvā munayo 'psaraso 'pi ca
c kathāṃ tāṃ brahmaṇā gītāṃ śrutvā prītā divaṃ yayuḥ
a etac chrutaṃ mayā tāta ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām
c vāsudevaṃ kathayatāṃ samavāye purātanam
a jāmadagnyasya rāmasya mārkaṇḍeyasya dhīmataḥ
c vyāsanāradayoś cāpi śrutaṃ śrutaviśārada
a etam arthaṃ ca vijñāya śrutvā ca prabhum avyayam
c vāsudevaṃ mahātmānaṃ lokānām īśvareśvaram
a yasyāsāv ātmajo brahmā sarvasya jagataḥ pitā
c kathaṃ na vāsudevo 'yam arcyaś cejyaś ca mānavaiḥ
a vārito 'si purā tāta munibhir vedapāragaiḥ
c mā gaccha saṃyugaṃ tena vāsudevena dhīmatā
e mā pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham iti tac ca mohān na budhyase
a manye tvāṃ rākṣasaṃ krūraṃ tathā cāsi tamovṛtaḥ
c yasmād dviṣasi govindaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
e naranārāyaṇau devau nānyo dviṣyād dhi mānavaḥ
a tasmād bravīmi te rājann eṣa vai śāśvato 'vyayaḥ
c sarvalokamayo nityaḥ śāstā dhātā dharo dhruvaḥ
a lokān dhārayate yas trīṃś carācaraguruḥ prabhuḥ
c yoddhā jayaś ca jetā ca sarvaprakṛtir īśvaraḥ
a rājan sattvamayo hy eṣa tamorāgavivarjitaḥ
c yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato dharmo yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a tasya māhātmyayogena yogenātmana eva ca
c dhṛtāḥ pāṇḍusutā rājañ jayaś caiṣāṃ bhaviṣyati
a śreyoyuktāṃ sadā buddhiṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ dadhāti yaḥ
c balaṃ caiva raṇe nityaṃ bhayebhyaś caiva rakṣati
a sa eṣa śāśvato devaḥ sarvaguhyamayaḥ śivaḥ
c vāsudeva iti jñeyo yan māṃ pṛcchasi bhārata
a brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaiḥ
c sevyate 'bhyarcyate caiva nityayuktaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ
a dvāparasya yugasyānte ādau kaliyugasya ca
c sātvataṃ vidhim āsthāya gītaḥ saṃkarṣaṇena yaḥ
a sa eṣa sarvāsuramartyalokaṃ
samudrakakṣyāntaritāḥ purīś ca
c yuge yuge mānuṣaṃ caiva vāsaṃ
punaḥ punaḥ sṛjate vāsudevaḥ
 duryodhana uvāca
a vāsudevo mahad bhūtaṃ sarvalokeṣu kathyate
c tasyāgamaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ ca jñātum icche pitāmaha
 bhīṣma uvāca
a vāsudevo mahad bhūtaṃ saṃbhūtaṃ saha daivataiḥ
c na paraṃ puṇḍarīkākṣād dṛśyate bharatarṣabha
d śrutaṃ me tāta rāmasya jāmadagnyasya jalpataḥ
d nāradasya ca devarṣeḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya ca
d asito devalaś cāpi vālakhilyās tapodhanāḥ
e mārkaṇḍeyaś ca govindaṃ kathayaty adbhutaṃ mahat
a sarvabhūtāni bhūtātmā mahātmā puruṣottamaḥ
c āpo vāyuś ca tejaś ca trayam etad akalpayat
a sa sṛṣṭvā pṛthivīṃ devaḥ sarvalokeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
c apsu vai śayanaṃ cakre mahātmā puruṣottamaḥ
e sarvatoyamayo devo yogāt suṣvāpa tatra ha
a mukhataḥ so 'gnim asṛjat prāṇād vāyum athāpi ca
c sarasvatīṃ ca vedāṃś ca manasaḥ sasṛje 'cyutaḥ
a eṣa lokān sasarjādau devāṃś carṣigaṇaiḥ saha
c nidhanaṃ caiva mṛtyuṃ ca prajānāṃ prabhavo 'vyayaḥ
a eṣa dharmaś ca dharmajño varadaḥ sarvakāmadaḥ
c eṣa kartā ca kāryaṃ ca pūrvadevaḥ svayaṃprabhuḥ
a bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca pūrvam etad akalpayat
c ubhe saṃdhye diśaḥ khaṃ ca niyamaṃ ca janārdanaḥ
a ṛṣīṃś caiva hi govindas tapaś caivānu kalpayat
c sraṣṭāraṃ jagataś cāpi mahātmā prabhur avyayaḥ
a agrajaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃkarṣaṇam akalpayat
b tasmān nārāyaṇo jajñe devadevaḥ sanātanaḥ
b nābhau padmaṃ babhūvāsya sarvalokasya saṃbhavaḥ
b tasmāt pitāmaho jātas tasmāj jātās tv imāḥ prajāḥ
c śeṣaṃ cākalpayad devam anantam iti yaṃ viduḥ
a yo dhārayati bhūtāni dharāṃ cemāṃ saparvatām
c dhyānayogena viprāś ca taṃ vadanti mahaujasam
a karṇasrotodbhavaṃ cāpi madhuṃ nāma mahāsuram
c tam ugram ugrakarmāṇam ugrāṃ buddhiṃ samāsthitam
d harantaṃ brahmaṇo vedāñ jaghāna brahmaṇaḥ pitā
e brahmaṇo 'pacitiṃ kurvañ jaghāna puruṣottamaḥ
a tasya tāta vadhād eva devadānavamānavāḥ
c madhusūdanam ity āhur ṛṣayaś ca janārdanam
e varāhaś caiva siṃhaś ca trivikramagatiḥ prabhuḥ
a eṣa mātā pitā caiva sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ hariḥ
c paraṃ hi puṇḍarīkākṣān na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
a mukhato 'sṛjad brāhmaṇān bāhubhyāṃ kṣatriyāṃs tathā
c vaiśyāṃś cāpy ūruto rājañ śūdrān padbhyāṃ tathaiva ca
e tapasā niyato devo nidhānaṃ sarvadehinām
a brahmabhūtam amāvāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tathaiva ca
c yogabhūtaṃ paricaran keśavaṃ mahad āpnuyāt
a keśavaḥ paramaṃ tejaḥ sarvalokapitāmahaḥ
c evam āhur hṛṣīkeśaṃ munayo vai narādhipa
a evam enaṃ vijānīhi ācāryaṃ pitaraṃ gurum
c kṛṣṇo yasya prasīdeta lokās tenākṣayā jitāḥ
a yaś caivainaṃ bhayasthāne keśavaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajet
c sadā naraḥ paṭhaṃś cedaṃ svastimān sa sukhī bhavet
a ye ca kṛṣṇaṃ prapadyante te na muhyanti mānavāḥ
c bhaye mahati ye magnāḥ pāti nityaṃ janārdanaḥ
a etad yudhiṣṭhiro jñātvā yāthātathyena bhārata
c sarvātmanā mahātmānaṃ keśavaṃ jagadīśvaram
e prapannaḥ śaraṇaṃ rājan yogānām īśvaraṃ prabhum
 bhīṣma uvāca
a śṛṇu cedaṃ mahārāja brahmabhūtastavaṃ mama
c brahmarṣibhiś ca devaiś ca yaḥ purā kathito bhuvi
a sādhyānām api devānāṃ devadeveśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
c lokabhāvanabhāvajña iti tvāṃ nārado 'bravīt
e bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyo 'bhyuvāca ha
a yajñānāṃ caiva yajñaṃ tvāṃ tapaś ca tapasām api
c devānām api devaṃ ca tvām āha bhagavān bhṛguḥ
e purāṇe bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ viṣṇo bhūtapateti vai
a vāsudevo vasūnāṃ tvaṃ śakraṃ sthāpayitā tathā
c devadevo 'si devānām iti dvaipāyano 'bravīt
a pūrve prajānisargeṣu dakṣam āhuḥ prajāpatim
c sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānām aṅgirās tvāṃ tato 'bravīt
a avyaktaṃ te śarīrotthaṃ vyaktaṃ te manasi sthitam
c devā vāksaṃbhavāś ceti devalas tv asito 'bravīt
a śirasā te divaṃ vyāptaṃ bāhubhyāṃ pṛthivī dhṛtā
c jaṭharaṃ te trayo lokāḥ puruṣo 'si sanātanaḥ
a evaṃ tvām abhijānanti tapasā bhāvitā narāḥ
c ātmadarśanatṛptānām ṛṣīṇāṃ cāpi sattamaḥ
a rājarṣīṇām udārāṇām āhaveṣv anivartinām
c sarvadharmapradhānānāṃ tvaṃ gatir madhusūdana
d iti nityaṃ yogavidbhir bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ
d sanatkumārapramukhaiḥ stūyate 'bhyarcyate hariḥ
d etad dvaipāyanaḥ prāha stutvā vai puruṣottamam
a eṣa te vistaras tāta saṃkṣepaś ca prakīrtitaḥ
c keśavasya yathātattvaṃ suprīto bhava keśave
d purāṇapuruṣasyeha yadarthaṃ nṛṣu saṃbhavaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a puṇyaṃ śrutvaitad ākhyānaṃ mahārāja sutas tava
c keśavaṃ bahu mene sa pāṇḍavāṃś ca mahārathān
a tam abravīn mahārāja bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punaḥ
c māhātmyaṃ te śrutaṃ rājan keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
d arjunasya māhātmyaṃ hi kathitaṃ tattvato mayā
d na jeṣyāmi mahāyuddhe vicarantaṃ naraṃ kva cit
d nārāyaṇaṃ ca saṃgrāme avadhyau tau yataḥ smṛtau
d dharmarājaś ca bhīmaś ca mādrīputraś ca pāṃḍavau
d ete 'py avadhyāḥ kathitāḥ purāṇe paramarṣiṇā
a narasya ca yathātattvaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
c yadarthaṃ nṛṣu saṃbhūtau naranārāyaṇāv ubhau
a avadhyau ca yathā vīrau saṃyugeṣv aparājitau
c yathā ca pāṇḍavā rājann agamyā yudhi kasya cit
a prītimān hi dṛḍhaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍaveṣu yaśasviṣu
c tasmād bravīmi rājendra śamo bhavatu pāṇḍavaiḥ
a pṛthivīṃ bhuṅkṣva sahito bhrātṛbhir balibhir vaśī
c naranārāyaṇau devāv avajñāya naśiṣyasi
d na cet kartāsi vacanaṃ saṃdigdhaṃ na tariṣyasi
a evam uktvā tava pitā tūṣṇīm āsīd viśāṃ pate
c vyasarjayac ca rājānaṃ śayanaṃ ca viveśa ha
a rājāpi śibiraṃ prāyāt praṇipatya mahātmane
c śiśye ca śayane śubhre tāṃ rātriṃ bharatarṣabha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vyuṣitāyāṃ ca śarvaryām udite ca divākare
c ubhe sene mahārāja yuddhāyaiva samīyatuḥ
d tasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ niryayuḥ kurupuṃgavāḥ
d puraskṛtya mahātmānaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yudhi
a abhyadhāvaṃś ca saṃkruddhāḥ parasparajigīṣavaḥ
c te sarve sahitā yuddhe samālokya parasparam
a pāṇḍavā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca rājan durmantrite tava
c vyūhau ca vyūhya saṃrabdhāḥ saṃprayuddhāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a arakṣan makaravyūhaṃ bhīṣmo rājan samantataḥ
c tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājann arakṣan vyūham ātmanaḥ
d ajātaśatruḥ śatrūṇāṃ manāṃsi samakampayat
d śyenavad vyūhya taṃ vyūhaṃ dhaumyasya vacanāt svayam
d sa hi tasya suvijñāta agnicityeṣu bhārata
d makaras tu mahāvyūhas tava putrasya dhīmataḥ
d svayaṃ sarveṇa sainyena droṇenānumatas tadā
d yathāvyūhaṃ śāṃtanavaḥ so 'nvavartata tat punaḥ
a sa niryayau rathānīkaṃ pitā devavratas tava
c mahatā rathavaṃśena saṃvṛto rathināṃ varaḥ
a itaretaram anvīyur yathābhāgam avasthitāḥ
c rathinaḥ pattayaś caiva dantinaḥ sādinas tathā
a tān dṛṣṭvā prodyatān saṃkhye pāṇḍavāś ca yaśasvinaḥ
c śyenena vyūharājena tenājayyena saṃyuge
a aśobhata mukhe tasya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c netre śikhaṇḍī durdharṣo dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
a śīrṣaṃ tasyābhavad vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
c vidhunvan gāṇḍivaṃ pārtho grīvāyām abhavat tadā
a akṣauhiṇyā samagrā yā vāmapakṣo 'bhavat tadā
c mahātmā drupadaḥ śrīmān saha putreṇa saṃyuge
a dakṣiṇaś cābhavat pakṣaḥ kaikeyo 'kṣauhiṇīpatiḥ
c pṛṣṭhato draupadeyāś ca saubhadraś cāpi vīryavān
a pṛṣṭhe samabhavac chrīmān svayaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhrātṛbhyāṃ sahito dhīmān yamābhyāṃ cāruvikramaḥ
a praviśya tu raṇe bhīmo makaraṃ mukhatas tadā
c bhīṣmam āsādya saṃgrāme chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a tato bhīṣmo mahāstrāṇi pātayām āsa bhārata
c mohayan pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ vyūḍhaṃ sainyaṃ mahāhave
a saṃmuhyati tadā sainye tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ śarasahasreṇa vivyādha raṇamūrdhani
a parisaṃvārya cāstrāṇi bhīṣmamuktāni saṃyuge
c svenānīkena hṛṣṭena yuddhāya samavasthitaḥ
a tato duryodhano rājā bhāradvājam abhāṣata
c pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭvā vadhaṃ ghoraṃ balasya balināṃ varaḥ
e bhrātṝṇāṃ ca vadhaṃ yuddhe smaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
a ācārya satataṃ tvaṃ hi hitakāmo mamānagha
c vayaṃ hi tvāṃ samāśritya bhīṣmaṃ caiva pitāmaham
a devān api raṇe jetuṃ prārthayāmo na saṃśayaḥ
c kim u pāṇḍusutān yuddhe hīnavīryaparākramān
d sa tathā kuru bhadraṃ te yathā vadhyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a evam uktas tato droṇas tava putreṇa māriṣa
b uvāca tatra rājānaṃ saṃkruddha iva niḥśvasan
b bāliśas tvaṃ na jānīṣe pāṇḍavānāṃ parākramam
b na śakyā hi yathā jetuṃ pāṇḍavā hi mahābalāḥ
b yathābalaṃ yathāvīryaṃ karma kuryām ahaṃ hi te
b ity uktvā te sutaṃ rājann abhyapadyata vāhinīm
c abhinat pāṇḍavānīkaṃ prekṣamāṇasya sātyakeḥ
a sātyakis tu tadā droṇaṃ vārayām āsa bhārata
c tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
a śaineyaṃ tu raṇe kruddho bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c avidhyan niśitair bāṇair jatrudeśe hasann iva
a bhīmasenas tataḥ kruddho bhāradvājam avidhyata
c saṃrakṣan sātyakiṃ rājan droṇāc chastrabhṛtāṃ varāt
a tato droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca tathā śalyaś ca māriṣa
c bhīmasenaṃ raṇe kruddhāś chādayāṃ cakrire śaraiḥ
a tatrābhimanyuḥ saṃkruddho draupadeyāś ca māriṣa
c vivyadhur niśitair bāṇaiḥ sarvāṃs tān udyatāyudhān
a bhīṣmadroṇau ca saṃkruddhāv āpatantau mahābalau
c pratyudyayau śikhaṇḍī tu maheṣvāso mahāhave
a pragṛhya balavad vīro dhanur jaladanisvanam
c abhyavarṣac charais tūrṇaṃ chādayāno divākaram
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ samāsādya bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥ
c avarjayata saṃgrāme strītvaṃ tasyānusaṃsmaran
a tato droṇo mahārāja abhyadravata taṃ raṇe
c rakṣamāṇas tato bhīṣmaṃ tava putreṇa coditaḥ
a śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya droṇaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c avarjayata saṃgrāme yugāntāgnim ivolbaṇam
a tato balena mahatā putras tava viśāṃ pate
c jugopa bhīṣmam āsādya prārthayāno mahad yaśaḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan puraskṛtya dhanaṃjayam
c bhīṣmam evābhyavartanta jaye kṛtvā dṛḍhāṃ matim
a tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ devānāṃ dānavair iva
c jayaṃ ca kāṅkṣatāṃ nityaṃ yaśaś ca paramādbhutam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a akarot tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadā
c bhīmasenabhayād icchan putrāṃs tārayituṃ tava
a pūrvāhṇe tan mahāraudraṃ rājñāṃ yuddham avartata
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca mukhyaśūravināśanam
a tasminn ākulasaṃgrāme vartamāne mahābhaye
c abhavat tumulaḥ śabdaḥ saṃspṛśan gaganaṃ mahat
a nadadbhiś ca mahānāgair heṣamāṇaiś ca vājibhiḥ
c bherīśaṅkhaninādaiś ca tumulaḥ samapadyata
a yuyutsavas te vikrāntā vijayāya mahābalāḥ
c anyonyam abhigarjanto goṣṭheṣv iva maharṣabhāḥ
a śirasāṃ pātyamānānāṃ samare niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c aśmavṛṣṭir ivākāśe babhūva bharatarṣabha
a kuṇḍaloṣṇīṣadhārīṇi jātarūpojjvalāni ca
c patitāni sma dṛśyante śirāṃsi bharatarṣabha
a viśikhonmathitair gātrair bāhubhiś ca sakārmukaiḥ
c sahastābharaṇaiś cānyair abhavac chāditā mahī
a kavacopahitair gātrair hastaiś ca samalaṃkṛtaiḥ
c mukhaiś ca candrasaṃkāśai raktāntanayanaiḥ śubhaiḥ
a gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ sarvagātraiś ca bhūpate
c āsīt sarvā samākīrṇā muhūrtena vasuṃdharā
a rajomeghaiś ca tumulaiḥ śastravidyutprakāśitaiḥ
c āyudhānāṃ ca nirghoṣaḥ stanayitnusamo 'bhavat
a sa saṃprahāras tumulaḥ kaṭukaḥ śoṇitodakaḥ
c prāvartata kurūṇāṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārata
a tasmin mahābhaye ghore tumule lomaharṣaṇe
c vavarṣuḥ śaravarṣāṇi kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ
a krośanti kuñjarās tatra śaravarṣapratāpitāḥ
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca saṃyuge bharatottama
d saṃrabdhānāṃ ca vīrāṇāṃ dhīrāṇām amitaujasām
d dhanurjyātalaśabdena na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
d utthiteṣu kabandheṣu sarvataḥ śoṇitodake
d samare paryadhāvanta nṛpā ripuvadhodyatāḥ
d śaraśaktigadābhis te khaḍgaiś cāmitatejasaḥ
d nijaghnuḥ samare śūrās te 'nyonyaṃ ca paraṃtapa
d babhramuḥ kuñjarāś cātra śarair viddhā niraṅkuśāḥ
e aśvāś ca paryadhāvanta hatārohā diśo daśa
a utpatya nipatanty anye śaraghātaprapīḍitāḥ
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca yodhānāṃ bharatarṣabha
d bahūnām uttamāṅgānāṃ kārmukāṇāṃ tathaiva ca
d gadānāṃ parighāṇāṃ ca hastānāṃ corubhiḥ saha
d pādānāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca keyūrāṇāṃ ca saṃghaśaḥ
d rāśayaḥ sma pradṛśyante bhīṣmabhīmaparākrame
a aśvānāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca rathānāṃ cātivartatām
c saṃghātāḥ sma pradṛśyante tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a gadābhir asibhiḥ prāsair bāṇaiś ca nataparvabhiḥ
c jaghnuḥ parasparaṃ tatra kṣatriyāḥ kālacoditāḥ
a apare bāhubhir vīrā niyuddhakuśalā yudhi
c bahudhā samasajjanta āyasaiḥ parighair iva
a muṣṭibhir jānubhiś caiva talaiś caiva viśāṃ pate
c anyonyaṃ jaghnire vīrās tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
d patitaiḥ pātyamānaiś ca viceṣṭadbhiś ca bhūtale
d ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe tatra tatra janeśvara
d duryodhanamate ghore akṣadyūtābhidevane
d bhīṣme yudhi parākrānte bhīmasenena bhārata
d prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇī
d madhye ca mahatī senā keśaśaivalaśādvalā
d hatārohā hayā rājan rathino virathā api
d vicerus tatra saṃgrāme nistriṃśavaradhāriṇaḥ
a virathā rathinaś cātra nistriṃśavaradhāriṇaḥ
c anyonyam abhidhāvanta parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
a tato duryodhano rājā kaliṅgair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c puraskṛtya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ pāṇḍavān abhyavartata
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parivārya vṛkodaram
c bhīṣmam abhyadravan kruddhā raṇe rabhasavāhanāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmeṇa saṃsaktān bhrātṝn anyāṃś ca pārthivān
c tam abhyadhāvad gāṅgeyam udyatāstro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaṃ dhanuṣo gāṇḍivasya ca
c dhvajaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā pārthasya sarvān no bhayam āviśat
d siṃhalāṅgūlam ākāśe jvalantam iva parvatam
a asajjamānaṃ vṛkṣeṣu dhūmaketum ivotthitam
c bahuvarṇaṃ ca citraṃ ca divyaṃ vānaralakṣaṇam
e apaśyāma mahārāja dhvajaṃ gāṇḍivadhanvanaḥ
a vidyutaṃ meghamadhyasthāṃ bhrājamānām ivāmbare
c dadṛśur gāṇḍivaṃ yodhā rukmapṛṣṭhaṃ mahārathe
a aśuśruma bhṛśaṃ cāsya śakrasyevābhigarjataḥ
c sughoraṃ talayoḥ śabdaṃ nighnatas tava vāhinīm
a caṇḍavāto yathā meghaḥ savidyutstanayitnumān
c diśaḥ saṃplāvayan sarvāḥ śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥ
a abhyadhāvata gāṅgeyaṃ bhairavāstro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c diśaṃ prācīṃ pratīcīṃ ca na jānīmo 'stramohitāḥ
a kāṃdigbhūtāḥ śrāntapatrā hatāstrā hatacetasaḥ
c anyonyam abhisaṃśliṣya yodhās te bharatarṣabha
a bhīṣmam evābhilīyanta saha sarvais tavātmajaiḥ
c teṣām ārtāyanam abhūd bhīṣmaḥ śaṃtanavo raṇe
a samutpatanta vitrastā rathebhyo rathinas tadā
c sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyo bhūmau cāpi padātayaḥ
d gajebhyo gajayodhāś ca vitrastā bhayamohitāḥ
d vihvalāḥ pratyadṛśyanta na jānanti diśo nṛpa
a śrutvā gāṇḍīvanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
c sarvasainyāni bhītāni vyavalīyanta bhārata
a atha kāmbojamukhyais tu bṛhadbhiḥ śīghragāmibhiḥ
c gopānāṃ bahusāhasrair balair govāsano vṛtaḥ
d tataḥ kāmbojamukhyāś ca te haṃsapathakarṇikāḥ
d gopāsanabalaughāś ca gopāsanapatis tathā
a madrasauvīragāndhārais trigartaiś ca viśāṃ pate
c sarvakāliṅgamukhyaiś ca kaliṅgādhipatir vṛtaḥ
a nāgā naragaṇaughāś ca duḥśāsanapuraḥsarāḥ
c jayadrathaś ca nṛpatiḥ sahitaḥ sarvarājabhiḥ
a hayārohavarāś caiva tava putreṇa coditāḥ
c caturdaśa sahasrāṇi saubalaṃ paryavārayan
a tatas te sahitāḥ sarve vibhaktarathavāhanāḥ
c pāṇḍavān samare jagmus tāvakā bharatarṣabha
d cedikāśipadātaiś ca rathaiḥ pāñcālasṛñjayaiḥ
d pāṇḍavāḥ sahitāḥ sarve dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
d tāvakān samare jagmur dharmaputreṇa coditāḥ
a rathibhir vāraṇair aśvaiḥ padātaiś ca samīritam
c ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe mahābhrasadṛśaṃ rajaḥ
a tomaraprāsanārācagajāśvarathayodhinām
c balena mahatā bhīṣmaḥ samasajjat kirīṭinā
a āvantyaḥ kāśirājena bhīmasenena saindhavaḥ
c ajātaśatrur madrāṇām ṛṣabheṇa yaśasvinā
e sahaputraḥ sahāmātyaḥ śalyena samasajjata
a vikarṇaḥ sahadevena citrasenaḥ śikhaṇḍinā
c matsyā duryodhanaṃ jagmuḥ śakuniṃ ca viśāṃ pate
a drupadaś cekitānaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c droṇena samasajjanta saputreṇa mahātmanā
e kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca dhṛṣṭaketum abhidrutau
a evaṃ prajavitāśvāni bhrāntanāgarathāni ca
c sainyāni samasajjanta prayuddhāni samantataḥ
a nirabhre vidyutas tīvrā diśaś ca rajasāvṛtāḥ
c prādurāsan maholkāś ca sanirghātā viśāṃ pate
a pravavau ca mahāvātaḥ pāṃsuvarṣaṃ papāta ca
c nabhasy antardadhe sūryaḥ sainyena rajasāvṛtaḥ
a pramohaḥ sarvasattvānām atīva samapadyata
b prakāśaṃ cakrur ākāśa udyatāsibhir uttamaiḥ
c rajasā cābhibhūtānām astrajālaiś ca tudyatām
a vīrabāhuvisṛṣṭānāṃ sarvāvaraṇabhedinām
c saṃghātaḥ śarajālānāṃ tumulaḥ samapadyata
a prakāśaṃ cakrur ākāśam udyatāni bhujottamaiḥ
c nakṣatravimalābhāni śastrāṇi bharatarṣabha
a ārṣabhāṇi vicitrāṇi rukmajālāvṛtāni ca
c saṃpetur dikṣu sarvāsu carmāṇi bharatarṣabha
a sūryavarṇaiś ca nistriṃśaiḥ pātyamānāni sarvaśaḥ
c dikṣu sarvāsv adṛśyanta śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca
a bhagnacakrākṣanīḍāś ca nipātitamahādhvajāḥ
c hatāśvāḥ pṛthivīṃ jagmus tatra tatra mahārathāḥ
a paripetur hayāś cātra ke cic chastrakṛtavraṇāḥ
c rathān viparikarṣanto hateṣu rathayodhiṣu
a śarāhatā bhinnadehā baddhayoktrā hayottamāḥ
c yugāni paryakarṣanta tatra tatra sma bhārata
a adṛśyanta sasūtāś ca sāśvāḥ sarathayodhinaḥ
c ekena balinā rājan vāraṇena hatā rathāḥ
a gandhahastimadasrāvam āghrāya bahavo raṇe
c saṃnipāte balaughānāṃ vītam ādadire gajāḥ
a satomaramahāmātrair nipatadbhir gatāsubhiḥ
c babhūvāyodhanaṃ channaṃ nārācābhihatair gajaiḥ
a saṃnipāte balaughānāṃ preṣitair varavāraṇaiḥ
c nipetur yudhi saṃbhagnāḥ sayodhāḥ sadhvajā rathāḥ
a nāgarājopamair hastair nāgair ākṣipya saṃyuge
c vyadṛśyanta mahārāja saṃbhagnā rathakūbarāḥ
a viśīrṇarathajālāś ca keśeṣv ākṣipya dantibhiḥ
c drumaśākhā ivāvidhya niṣpiṣṭā rathino raṇe
a ratheṣu ca rathān yuddhe saṃsaktān varavāraṇāḥ
c vikarṣanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃpetuḥ sarvaśabdagāḥ
a teṣāṃ tathā karṣatāṃ ca gajānāṃ rūpam ābabhau
c saraḥsu nalinījālaṃ viṣaktam iva karṣatām
a evaṃ saṃchāditaṃ tatra babhūvāyodhanaṃ mahat
c sādibhiś ca padātaiś ca sadhvajaiś ca mahārathaiḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śikhaṇḍī saha matsyena virāṭena viśāṃ pate
c bhīṣmam āśu maheṣvāsam āsasāda sudurjayam
a droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca maheṣvāsān mahābalān
c rājñaś cānyān raṇe śūrān bahūn ārchad dhanaṃjayaḥ
a saindhavaṃ ca maheṣvāsaṃ sāmātyaṃ saha bandhubhiḥ
c prācyāṃś ca dākṣiṇātyāṃś ca bhūmipān bhūmiparṣabha
a putraṃ ca te maheṣvāsaṃ duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c duḥsahaṃ caiva samare bhīmaseno 'bhyavartata
a sahadevas tu śakunim ulūkaṃ ca mahāratham
c pitāputrau maheṣvāsāv abhyavartata durjayau
a yudhiṣṭhiro mahārāja gajānīkaṃ mahārathaḥ
c samavartata saṃgrāme putreṇa nikṛtas tava
a mādrīputras tu nakulaḥ śūraḥ saṃkrandano yudhi
c trigartānāṃ rathodāraiḥ samasajjata pāṇḍavaḥ
a abhyavartanta durdharṣāḥ samare śālvakekayān
b nākuliś ca śatānīkaḥ samare rathapuṃgavaḥ
c sātyakiś cekitānaś ca saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥ
a dhṛṣṭaketuś ca samare rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
c putrāṇāṃ te rathānīkaṃ pratyudyātāḥ sudurjayāḥ
a senāpatir ameyātmā dhṛṣṭadyumno mahābalaḥ
c droṇena samare rājan samiyāyendrakarmaṇā
a evam ete maheṣvāsās tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c sametya samare śūrāḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire
a madhyaṃdinagate sūrye nabhasy ākulatāṃ gate
c kuravaḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca nijaghnur itaretaram
a dhvajino hemacitrāṅgā vicaranto raṇājire
c sapatākā rathā rejur vaiyāghraparivāraṇāḥ
a sametānāṃ ca samare jigīṣūṇāṃ parasparam
c babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ siṃhānām iva nardatām
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma saṃprahāraṃ sudāruṇam
c yam akurvan raṇe vīrāḥ sṛñjayāḥ kurubhiḥ saha
a naiva khaṃ na diśo rājan na sūryaṃ śatrutāpana
c vidiśo vāpy apaśyāma śarair muktaiḥ samantataḥ
a śaktīnāṃ vimalāgrāṇāṃ tomarāṇāṃ tathāsyatām
c nistriṃśānāṃ ca pītānāṃ nīlotpalanibhāḥ prabhāḥ
a kavacānāṃ vicitrāṇāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ prabhās tathā
c khaṃ diśaḥ pradiśaś caiva bhāsayām āsur ojasā
d vapurbhiś ca narendrāṇāṃ candrasūryasamaprabhaiḥ
e virarāja tadā rājaṃs tatra tatra raṇāṅgaṇam
a rathasiṃhāsanavyāghrāḥ samāyāntaś ca saṃyuge
c virejuḥ samare rājan grahā iva nabhastale
a bhīṣmas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭho bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
c avārayata saṃkruddhaḥ sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a tato bhīṣmavinirmuktā rukmapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
c abhyaghnan samare bhīmaṃ tailadhautāḥ sutejanāḥ
a tasya śaktiṃ mahāvegāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c kruddhāśīviṣasaṃkāśāṃ preṣayām āsa bhārata
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā rukmadaṇḍāṃ durāsadām
c ciccheda samare bhīṣmaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tato 'pareṇa bhallena pītena niśitena ca
c kārmukaṃ bhīmasenasya dvidhā ciccheda bhārata
d apāsya tu dhanuś chinnaṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
d śarair bahubhir ānarchad bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yudhi
a sātyakis tu tatas tūrṇaṃ bhīṣmam āsādya saṃyuge
b ākarṇaprahitais tīkṣṇair niśitais tigmatejanaiḥ
c śarair bahubhir ānarchat pitaraṃ te janeśvara
a tataḥ saṃdhāya vai tīkṣṇaṃ śaraṃ paramadāruṇam
c vārṣṇeyasya rathād bhīṣmaḥ pātayām āsa sārathim
a tasyāśvāḥ pradrutā rājan nihate rathasārathau
c tena tenaiva dhāvanti manomārutaraṃhasaḥ
a tataḥ sarvasya sainyasya nisvanas tumulo 'bhavat
c hāhākāraś ca saṃjajñe pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
a abhidravata gṛhṇīta hayān yacchata dhāvata
c ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdo yuyudhānarathaṃ prati
a etasminn eva kāle tu bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punaḥ
c vyahanat pāṇḍavīṃ senām āsurīm iva vṛtrahā
a te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ saha
c āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā bhīṣmam evābhidudruvuḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhāś cāpi pārthāḥ śāṃtanavaṃ raṇe
c abhyadhāvañ jigīṣantas tava putrasya vāhinīm
a tathaiva tāvakā rājan bhīṣmadroṇamukhāḥ parān
c abhyadhāvanta vegena tato yuddham avartata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a virāṭo 'tha tribhir bāṇair bhīṣmam ārchan mahāratham
c vivyādha turagāṃś cāsya tribhir bāṇair mahārathaḥ
a taṃ pratyavidhyad daśabhir bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ śaraiḥ
c rukmapuṅkhair maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtahasto mahābalaḥ
a drauṇir gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ bhīmadhanvā mahārathaḥ
c avidhyad iṣubhiḥ ṣaḍbhir dṛḍhahastaḥ stanāntare
a kārmukaṃ tasya ciccheda phalgunaḥ paravīrahā
c avidhyac ca bhṛśaṃ tīkṣṇaiḥ patribhiḥ śatrukarśanaḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya vegavat krodhamūrchitaḥ
c amṛṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena kārmukacchedam āhave
a avidhyat phalgunaṃ rājan navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vāsudevaṃ ca saptatyā vivyādha parameṣubhiḥ
a tataḥ krodhābhitāmrākṣaḥ saha kṛṣṇena phalgunaḥ
c dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya cintayitvā muhur muhuḥ
a dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇāmitrakarśanaḥ
c gāṇḍīvadhanvā saṃkruddhaḥ śitān saṃnataparvaṇaḥ
e jīvitāntakarān ghorān samādatta śilīmukhān
a tais tūrṇaṃ samare 'vidhyad drauṇiṃ balavatāṃ varam
c tasya te kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave
a na vivyathe ca nirbhinno drauṇir gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
c tathaiva śaravarṣāṇi pratimuñcann avihvalaḥ
e tasthau sa samare rājaṃs trātum icchan mahāvratam
a tasya tat sumahat karma śaśaṃsuḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c yat kṛṣṇābhyāṃ sametābhyāṃ nāpatrapata saṃyuge
d sa viddhaḥ phālgunenājau na papāta mahītale
a sa hi nityam anīkeṣu yudhyate 'bhayam āsthitaḥ
c astragrāmaṃ sasaṃhāraṃ droṇāt prāpya sudurlabham
a mamāyam ācāryasuto droṇasyātipriyaḥ sutaḥ
c brāhmaṇaś ca viśeṣeṇa mānanīyo mameti ca
a samāsthāya matiṃ vīro bībhatsuḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c kṛpāṃ cakre rathaśreṣṭho bhāradvājasutaṃ prati
a drauṇiṃ tyaktvā tato yuddhe kaunteyaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c yuyudhe tāvakān nighnaṃs tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
a duryodhanas tu daśabhir gārdhrapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ rukmapuṅkhaiḥ samarpayat
a bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddhaḥ parāsukaraṇaṃ dṛḍham
c citraṃ kārmukam ādatta śarāṃś ca niśitān daśa
a ākarṇaprahitais tīkṣṇair vegitais tigmatejanaiḥ
c avidhyat tūrṇam avyagraḥ kururājaṃ mahorasi
a tasya kāñcanasūtras tu śaraiḥ parivṛto maṇiḥ
c rarājorasi vai sūryo grahair iva samāvṛtaḥ
a putras tu tava tejasvī bhīmasenena tāḍitaḥ
c nāmṛṣyata yathā nāgas talaśabdaṃ samīritam
a tataḥ śarair mahārāja rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c bhīmaṃ vivyādha saṃkruddhas trāsayāno varūthinīm
a tau yudhyamānau samare bhṛśam anyonyavikṣatau
c putrau te devasaṃkāśau vyarocetāṃ mahābalau
a citrasenaṃ naravyāghraṃ saubhadraḥ paravīrahā
c avidhyad daśabhir bāṇaiḥ purumitraṃ ca saptabhiḥ
a satyavrataṃ ca saptatyā viddhvā śakrasamo yudhi
c nṛtyann iva raṇe vīra ārtiṃ naḥ samajījanat
a taṃ pratyavidyad daśabhiś citrasenaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
c satyavrataś ca navabhiḥ purumitraś ca saptabhiḥ
a sa viddho vikṣaran raktaṃ śatrusaṃvāraṇaṃ mahat
c ciccheda citrasenasya citraṃ kārmukam ārjuniḥ
e bhittvā cāsya tanutrāṇaṃ śareṇorasy atāḍayat
a tatas te tāvakā vīrā rājaputrā mahārathāḥ
c sametya yudhi saṃrabdhā vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e tāṃś ca sarvāñ śarais tīkṣṇair jaghāna paramāstravit
a tasya dṛṣṭvā tu tat karma parivavruḥ sutās tava
c dahantaṃ samare sainyaṃ tava kakṣaṃ yatholbaṇam
a apetaśiśire kāle samiddham iva pāvakaḥ
c atyarocata saubhadras tava sainyāni śātayan
a tat tasya caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā pautras tava viśāṃ pate
c lakṣmaṇo 'bhyapatat tūrṇaṃ sātvatīputram āhave
a abhimanyus tu saṃkruddho lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam
c vivyādha viśikhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tathaiva lakṣmaṇo rājan saubhadraṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c avidhyata mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sārathiṃ ca mahābalaḥ
c abhyadravata saubhadro lakṣmaṇaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a hatāśve tu rathe tuṣṭhaṃl lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c śaktiṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddhaḥ saubhadrasya rathaṃ prati
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā ghorarūpāṃ durāsadām
c abhimanyuḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiś ciccheda bhujagopamām
a tataḥ svaratham āropya lakṣmaṇaṃ gautamas tadā
c apovāha rathenājau sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a tataḥ samākule tasmin vartamāne mahābhaye
b hayo hayaṃ gajo nāgaṃ vīro vīraṃ viśāṃ pate
c abhyadravañ jighāṃsantaḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
a tāvakāś ca maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavāś ca mahārathāḥ
c juhvantaḥ samare prāṇān nijaghnur itaretaram
a muktakeśā vikavacā virathāś chinnakārmukāḥ
c bāhubhiḥ samayudhyanta sṛñjayāḥ kurubhiḥ saha
a tato bhīṣmo mahābāhuḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c senāṃ jaghāna saṃkruddho divyair astrair mahābalaḥ
a hateśvarair gajais tatra narair aśvaiś ca pātitaiḥ
c rathibhiḥ sādibhiś caiva samāstīryata medinī
 saṃjaya uvāca
a atha rājan mahābāhuḥ sātyakir yuddhadurmadaḥ
c vikṛṣya cāpaṃ samare bhārasādhanam uttamam
d yat tat sakhyus tu pūrveṇa arjunād upaśikṣitam
a prāmuñcat puṅkhasaṃyuktāñ śarān āśīviṣopamān
c prakāśaṃ laghu citraṃ ca darśayann astralāghavam
a tasya vikṣipataś cāpaṃ śarān anyāṃś ca muñcataḥ
c ādadānasya bhūyaś ca saṃdadhānasya cāparān
a kṣipataś ca śarān asya raṇe śatrūn vinighnataḥ
c dadṛśe rūpam atyarthaṃ meghasyeva pravarṣataḥ
a tam udīryantam ālokya rājā duryodhanas tataḥ
c rathānām ayutaṃ tasya preṣayām āsa bhārata
a tāṃs tu sarvān maheṣvāsān sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
c jaghāna parameṣvāso divyenāstreṇa vīryavān
a sa kṛtvā dāruṇaṃ karma pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥ
c āsasāda tato vīro bhūriśravasam āhave
a sa hi saṃdṛśya senāṃ tāṃ yuyudhānena pātitām
c abhyadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥ
a indrāyudhasavarṇaṃ tat sa visphārya mahad dhanuḥ
c vyasṛjad vajrasaṃkāśāñ śarān āśīviṣopamān
e sahasraśo mahārāja darśayan pāṇilāghavam
a śarāṃs tān mṛtyusaṃsparśān sātyakes tu padānugāḥ
c na viṣehus tadā rājan dudruvus te samantataḥ
e vihāya samare rājan sātyakiṃ yuddhadurmadam
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā yuyudhānasya sutā daśa mahābalāḥ
c mahārathāḥ samākhyātāś citravarmāyudhadhvajāḥ
a samāsādya maheṣvāsaṃ bhūriśravasam āhave
c ūcuḥ sarve susaṃrabdhā yūpaketuṃ mahāraṇe
d yudhyasva samare cādya paśyāmas tava pauruṣam
a bho bho kauravadāyāda sahāsmābhir mahābala
c ehi yudhyasva saṃgrāme samastaiḥ pṛthag eva vā
a asmān vā tvaṃ parājitya yaśaḥ prāpnuhi saṃyuge
c vayaṃ vā tvāṃ parājitya prītiṃ dāsyāmahe pituḥ
a evam uktas tadā śūrais tān uvāca mahābalaḥ
c vīryaślāghī naraśreṣṭhas tān dṛṣṭvā samupasthitān
a sādhv idaṃ kathyate vīrā yad evaṃ matir adya vaḥ
c yudhyadhvaṃ sahitā yattā nihaniṣyāmi vo raṇe
a evam uktā maheṣvāsās te vīrāḥ kṣiprakāriṇaḥ
c mahatā śaravarṣeṇa abhyavarṣann ariṃdamam
a aparāhṇe mahārāja saṃgrāmas tumulo 'bhavat
c ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca sametānāṃ raṇājire
a tam ekaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śaravarṣair avākiran
c prāvṛṣīva mahāśailaṃ siṣicur jaladā nṛpa
a tais tu muktāñ śaraughāṃs tān yamadaṇḍāśaniprabhān
c asaṃprāptān asaṃprāptāṃś cicchedāśu mahārathaḥ
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma saumadatteḥ parākramam
c yad eko bahubhir yuddhe samasajjad abhītavat
a visṛjya śaravṛṣṭiṃ tāṃ daśa rājan mahārathāḥ
c parivārya mahābāhuṃ nihantum upacakramuḥ
a saumadattis tataḥ kruddhas teṣāṃ cāpāni bhārata
c ciccheda daśabhir bāṇair nimeṣeṇa mahārathaḥ
a athaiṣāṃ chinnadhanuṣāṃ bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c ciccheda samare rājañ śirāṃsi niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e te hatā nyapatan bhūmau vajrabhagnā iva drumāḥ
a tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān vīrān raṇe putrān mahābalān
c vārṣṇeyo vinadan rājan bhūriśravasam abhyayāt
a rathaṃ rathena samare pīḍayitvā mahābalau
c tāv anyonyasya samare nihatya rathavājinaḥ
e virathāv abhivalgantau sameyātāṃ mahārathau
a pragṛhītamahākhaḍgau tau carmavaradhāriṇau
c śuśubhāte naravyāghrau yuddhāya samavasthitau
d asahyam asiyuddhāya bhūriśravasam āhave
d matvā vṛkodaras tūrṇam abhiplutya mahārathaḥ
a tataḥ sātyakim abhyetya nistriṃśavaradhāriṇam
c bhīmasenas tvaran rājan ratham āropayat tadā
a tavāpi tanayo rājan bhūriśravasam āhave
c āropayad rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne raṇe bhīṣmaṃ mahāratham
c ayodhayanta saṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabha
a lohitāyati cāditye tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥ
c pañcaviṃśatisāhasrān nijaghāna mahārathān
a te hi duryodhanādiṣṭās tadā pārthanibarhaṇe
c saṃprāpyaiva gatā nāśaṃ śalabhā iva pāvakam
a tato matsyāḥ kekayāś ca dhanurvedaviśāradāḥ
c parivavrus tadā pārthaṃ sahaputraṃ mahāratham
a etasminn eva kāle tu sūrye 'stam upagacchati
c sarveṣām eva sainyānāṃ pramohaḥ samajāyata
a avahāraṃ tataś cakre pitā devavratas tava
c saṃdhyākāle mahārāja sainyānāṃ śrāntavāhanaḥ
a pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca parasparasamāgame
c te sene bhṛśasaṃvigne yayatuḥ svaṃ niveśanam
a tataḥ svaśibiraṃ gatvā nyaviśaṃs tatra bhārata
c pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ sārdhaṃ kuravaś ca yathāvidhi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vihṛtya ca tato rājan sahitāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c vyatītāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ punar yuddhāya niryayuḥ
a tatra śabdo mahān āsīt tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
c yujyatāṃ rathamukhyānāṃ kalpyatāṃ caiva dantinām
a saṃnahyatāṃ padātīnāṃ hayānāṃ caiva bhārata
c śaṅkhadundubhinādaś ca tumulaḥ sarvato 'bhavat
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā dhṛṣṭadyumnam abhāṣata
c vyūhaṃ vyūha mahābāho makaraṃ śatrutāpanam
a evam uktas tu pārthena dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
c vyādideśa mahārāja rathino rathināṃ varaḥ
a śiro 'bhūd drupadas tasya pāṇḍavaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
c cakṣuṣī sahadevaś ca nakulaś ca mahārathaḥ
e tuṇḍam āsīn mahārāja bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
a saubhadro draupadeyāś ca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
c sātyakir dharmarājaś ca vyūhagrīvāṃ samāsthitāḥ
a pṛṣṭham āsīn mahārāja virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahito mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ
a kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca vāmaṃ pārśvaṃ samāśritāḥ
c dhṛṣṭaketur naravyāghraḥ karakarṣaś ca vīryavān
e dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā vyūhasya rakṣaṇe
a pādayos tu mahārāja sthitaḥ śrīmān mahārathaḥ
c kuntibhojaḥ śatānīko mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ
a śikhaṇḍī tu maheṣvāsaḥ somakaiḥ saṃvṛto balī
c irāvāṃś ca tataḥ pucche makarasya vyavasthitau
a evam etan mahāvyūhaṃ vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ
c sūryodaye mahārāja punar yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ
a kauravān abhyayus tūrṇaṃ hastyaśvarathapattibhiḥ
c samucchritair dhvajaiś citraiḥ śastraiś ca vimalaiḥ śitaiḥ
a vyūhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu tat sainyaṃ pitā devavratas tava
c krauñcena mahatā rājan pratyavyūhata vāhinīm
a tasya tuṇḍe maheṣvāso bhāradvājo vyarocata
c aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva cakṣur āstāṃ nareśvara
a kṛtavarmā tu sahitaḥ kāmbojāraṭṭabāhlikaiḥ
c śirasy āsīn naraśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a grīvāyāṃ śūrasenas tu tava putraś ca māriṣa
c duryodhano mahārāja rājabhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ
a prāgjyotiṣas tu sahitaḥ madrasauvīrakekayaiḥ
c urasy abhūn naraśreṣṭha mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ
d pṛṣṭhe cāstāṃ maheṣvāsāv āvantyau sapadānugau
a svasenayā ca sahitaḥ suśarmā prasthalādhipaḥ
c vāmaṃ pakṣaṃ samāśritya daṃśitaḥ samavasthitaḥ
a tuṣārā yavanāś caiva śakāś ca saha cūcupaiḥ
c dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā vyūhasya bhārata
a śrutāyuś ca śatāyuś ca saumadattiś ca māriṣa
c vyūhasya jaghane tasthū rakṣamāṇāḥ parasparam
a tato yuddhāya saṃjagmuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kauravaiḥ saha
c sūryodaye mahārāja tato yuddham abhūn mahat
a pratīyū rathino nāgān nāgāś ca rathino yayuḥ
c hayārohā hayārohān rathinaś cāpi sādinaḥ
a sārathiṃ ca rathī rājan kuñjarāṃś ca mahāraṇe
c hastyārohā rathārohān rathinaś cāpi sādinaḥ
a rathinaḥ pattibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sādinaś cāpi pattibhiḥ
c anyonyaṃ samare rājan pratyadhāvann amarṣitāḥ
a bhīmasenārjunayamair guptā cānyair mahārathaiḥ
c śuśubhe pāṇḍavī senā nakṣatrair iva śarvarī
a tathā bhīṣmakṛpadroṇaśalyaduryodhanādibhiḥ
c tavāpi vibabhau senā grahair dyaur iva saṃvṛtā
a bhīmasenas tu kaunteyo droṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā parākramī
c abhyayāj javanair aśvair bhāradvājasya vāhinīm
a droṇas tu samare kruddho bhīmaṃ navabhir āyasaiḥ
c vivyādha samare rājan marmāṇy uddiśya vīryavān
a dṛḍhāhatas tato bhīmo bhāradvājasya saṃyuge
c sārathiṃ preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanaṃ prati
a sa saṃgṛhya svayaṃ vāhān bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c vyadhamat pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ tūlarāśim ivānalaḥ
a te vadhyamānā droṇena bhīṣmeṇa ca narottama
c sṛñjayāḥ kekayaiḥ sārdhaṃ palāyanaparābhavan
a tathaiva tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ bhīmārjunaparikṣatam
c muhyate tatra tatraiva samadeva varāṅganā
a abhidyetāṃ tato vyūhau tasmin vīravarakṣaye
c āsīd vyatikaro ghoras tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
a tad adbhutam apaśyāma tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ saha
c ekāyanagatāḥ sarve yad ayudhyanta bhārata
a pratisaṃvārya cāstrāṇi te 'nyonyasya viśāṃ pate
c yuyudhuḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva kauravāś ca mahārathāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a evaṃ bahuguṇaṃ sainyam evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ param
c vyūḍham evaṃ yathāśāstram amoghaṃ caiva saṃjaya
a puṣṭam asmākam atyantam abhikāmaṃ ca naḥ sadā
c prahvam avyasanopetaṃ purastād dṛṣṭavikramam
a nātivṛddham abālaṃ ca na kṛśaṃ na ca pīvaram
c laghuvṛttāyataprāyaṃ sāragātram anāmayam
a āttasaṃnāhaśastraṃ ca bahuśastraparigraham
c asiyuddhe niyuddhe ca gadāyuddhe ca kovidam
a prāsarṣṭitomareṣv ājau parigheṣv āyaseṣu ca
c bhiṇḍipāleṣu śaktīṣu musaleṣu ca sarvaśaḥ
a kampaneṣu ca cāpeṣu kaṇapeṣu ca sarvaśaḥ
c kṣepaṇīṣu ca citrāsu muṣṭiyuddheṣu kovidam
a aparokṣaṃ ca vidyāsu vyāyāmeṣu kṛtaśramam
c śastragrahaṇavidyāsu sarvāsu pariniṣṭhitam
a ārohe paryavaskande saraṇe sāntaraplute
c samyakpraharaṇe yāne vyapayāne ca kovidam
a nāgāśvarathayāneṣu bahuśaḥ suparīkṣitam
c parīkṣya ca yathānyāyaṃ vetanenopapāditam
a na goṣṭhyā nopacāreṇa na ca bandhunimittataḥ
c na sauhṛdabalaiś cāpi nākulīnaparigrahaiḥ
a samṛddhajanam āryaṃ ca tuṣṭasatkṛtabāndhavam
c kṛtopakārabhūyiṣṭhaṃ yaśasvi ca manasvi ca
a sajayaiś ca narair mukhyair bahuśo mukhyakarmabhiḥ
c lokapālopamais tāta pālitaṃ lokaviśrutaiḥ
a bahubhiḥ kṣatriyair guptaṃ pṛthivyāṃ lokasaṃmataiḥ
c asmān abhigataiḥ kāmāt sabalaiḥ sapadānugaiḥ
a mahodadhim ivāpūrṇam āpagābhiḥ samantataḥ
c apakṣaiḥ pakṣasaṃkāśai rathair nāgaiś ca saṃvṛtam
a nānāyodhajalaṃ bhīmaṃ vāhanormitaraṅgiṇam
c kṣepaṇyasigadāśaktiśaraprāsasamākulam
a dhvajabhūṣaṇasaṃbādhaṃ ratnapaṭṭena saṃcitam
c vāhanaiḥ parisarpadbhir vāyuvegavikampitam
a apāram iva garjantaṃ sāgarapratimaṃ mahat
c droṇabhīṣmābhisaṃguptaṃ guptaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇā
a kṛpaduḥśāsanābhyāṃ ca jayadrathamukhais tathā
c bhagadattavikarṇābhyāṃ drauṇisaubalabāhlikaiḥ
a guptaṃ pravīrair lokasya sāravadbhir mahātmabhiḥ
c yad ahanyata saṃgrāme diṣṭam etat purātanam
a naitādṛśaṃ samudyogaṃ dṛṣṭavanto 'tha mānuṣāḥ
c ṛṣayo vā mahābhāgāḥ purāṇā bhuvi saṃjaya
a īdṛśo hi balaughas tu yuktaḥ śastrāstrasaṃpadā
c vadhyate yatra saṃgrāme kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a viparītam idaṃ sarvaṃ pratibhāti sma saṃjaya
c yatredṛśaṃ balaṃ ghoraṃ nātarad yudhi pāṇḍavān
a atha vā pāṇḍavārthāya devās tatra samāgatāḥ
c yudhyante māmakaṃ sainyaṃ yad avadhyanta saṃjaya
a ukto hi vidureṇeha hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca saṃjaya
c na ca gṛhṇāti tan mandaḥ putro duryodhano mama
a tasya manye matiḥ pūrvaṃ sarvajñasya mahātmanaḥ
c āsīd yathāgataṃ tāta yena dṛṣṭam idaṃ purā
a atha vā bhāvyam evaṃ hi saṃjayaitena sarvathā
c purā dhātrā yathā sṛṣṭaṃ tat tathā na tad anyathā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ātmadoṣāt tvayā rājan prāptaṃ vyasanam īdṛśam
c na hi duryodhanas tāni paśyate bharatarṣabha
e yāni tvaṃ dṛṣṭavān rājan dharmasaṃkarakārite
a tava doṣāt purā vṛttaṃ dyūtam etad viśāṃ pate
c tava doṣeṇa yuddhaṃ ca pravṛttaṃ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
e tvam evādya phalaṃ bhuṅkṣva kṛtvā kilbiṣam ātmanā
a ātmanā hi kṛtaṃ karma ātmanaivopabhujyate
c iha vā pretya vā rājaṃs tvayā prāptaṃ yathātatham
a tasmād rājan sthiro bhūtvā prāpyedaṃ vyasanaṃ mahat
c śṛṇu yuddhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ śaṃsato mama māriṣa
a bhīmasenas tu niśitair bāṇair bhittvā mahācamūm
c āsasāda tato vīraḥ sarvān duryodhanānujān
a duḥśāsanaṃ durviṣahaṃ duḥsahaṃ durmadaṃ jayam
c jayatsenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca citrasenaṃ sudarśanam
a cārucitraṃ suvarmāṇaṃ duṣkarṇaṃ karṇam eva ca
c etān anyāṃś ca subahūn samīpasthān mahārathān
a dhārtarāṣṭrān susaṃkruddhān dṛṣṭvā bhīmo mahābalaḥ
c bhīṣmeṇa samare guptāṃ praviveśa mahācamūm
a athāhvayanta te 'nyonyam ayaṃ prāpto vṛkodaraḥ
b athālokya praviṣṭaṃ tam ūcus te sarva eva tu
c jīvagrāhaṃ nigṛhṇīmo vayam enaṃ narādhipāḥ
a sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ pārtho bhrātṛbhiḥ kṛtaniścayaiḥ
c prajāsaṃharaṇe sūryaḥ krūrair iva mahāgrahaiḥ
a saṃprāpya madhyaṃ vyūhasya na bhīḥ pāṇḍavam āviśat
c yathā devāsure yuddhe mahendraḥ prāpya dānavān
a tataḥ śatasahasrāṇi rathināṃ sarvaśaḥ prabho
c chādayānaṃ śarair ghorais tam ekam anuvavrire
a sa teṣāṃ pravarān yodhān hastyaśvarathasādinaḥ
c jaghāna samare śūro dhārtarāṣṭrān acintayan
a teṣāṃ vyavasitaṃ jñātvā bhīmaseno jighṛkṣatām
c samastānāṃ vadhe rājan matiṃ cakre mahāmanāḥ
a tato rathaṃ samutsṛjya gadām ādāya pāṇḍavaḥ
b uvāca sārathiṃ bhīmaḥ sthīyatām iti bhārata
b yāvad enān haniṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭrān sahānugān
b ity uktvā bhīmasenas tu praviśya mahatīṃ camūm
c jaghāna dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ taṃ balaughamahārṇavam
d gadayā bhīmasenena tāḍitā vāraṇottamāḥ
d bhinnakumbhā mahākāyā bhinnapṛṣṭhās tathaiva ca
