d bhinnagātrāḥ sahārohāḥ śerate parvatā iva
d rathāś ca bhagnās tilaśaḥ sayodhāḥ śataśo raṇe
d aśvāś ca sādinaś caiva pādātaiḥ saha bhārata
d tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bhīmasenasya vikramam
d yad ekaḥ samare rājan bahubhiḥ samayodhayat
d antakāle prajāḥ sarvā daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
a bhīmasene praviṣṭe tu dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi pārṣataḥ
c droṇam utsṛjya tarasā prayayau yatra saubalaḥ
a vidārya mahatīṃ senāṃ tāvakānāṃ nararṣabhaḥ
c āsasāda rathaṃ śūnyaṃ bhīmasenasya saṃyuge
d rathaṃ ca śūnyaṃ saṃprekṣya bhīmaṃ prati vicetanaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā viśokaṃ samare bhīmasenasya sārathim
c dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja durmanā gatacetanaḥ
a apṛcchad bāṣpasaṃruddho nisvanāṃ vācam īrayan
c mama prāṇaiḥ priyatamaḥ kva bhīma iti duḥkhitaḥ
a viśokas tam uvācedaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
c saṃsthāpya mām iha balī pāṇḍaveyaḥ pratāpavān
a praviṣṭo dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām etad balamahārṇavam
c mām uktvā puruṣavyāghra prītiyuktam idaṃ vacaḥ
a pratipālaya māṃ sūta niyamyāśvān muhūrtakam
c yāvad etān nihanmy āśu ya ime madvadhodyatāḥ
d abhyadhāvad gadāpāṇis tad balaṃ sa mahābalaḥ
a tato dṛṣṭvā gadāhastaṃ pradhāvantaṃ mahābalam
c sarveṣām eva sainyānāṃ saṃgharṣaḥ samajāyata
a tasmiṃs tu tumule yuddhe vartamāne bhayānake
c bhittvā rājan mahāvyūhaṃ praviveśa sakhā tava
a viśokasya vacaḥ śrutvā dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi pārṣataḥ
c pratyuvāca tataḥ sūtaṃ raṇamadhye mahābalaḥ
a na hi me vidyate sūta jīvite 'dya prayojanam
c bhīmasenaṃ raṇe hitvā sneham utsṛjya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a yadi yāmi vinā bhīmaṃ kiṃ māṃ kṣatraṃ vadiṣyati
c ekāyanagate bhīme mayi cāvasthite yudhi
a asvasti tasya kurvanti devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
c yaḥ sahāyān parityajya svastimān āvrajed gṛhān
d dhikkṛtasya ca kṣatreṇa nirarthaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet
d raurave narake majjed aplave dustare nṛbhiḥ
a mama bhīmaḥ sakhā caiva saṃbandhī ca mahābalaḥ
c bhakto 'smān bhaktimāṃś cāhaṃ tam apy ariniṣūdanam
a so 'haṃ tatra gamiṣyāmi yatra yāto vṛkodaraḥ
c nighnantaṃ mām arīn paśya dānavān iva vāsavam
a evam uktvā tato vīro yayau madhyena bhāratīm
c bhīmasenasya mārgeṣu gadāpramathitair gajaiḥ
a sa dadarśa tato bhīmaṃ dahantaṃ ripuvāhinīm
c vātaṃ vṛkṣān iva balāt prabhañjantaṃ raṇe nṛpān
a te hanyamānāḥ samare rathinaḥ sādinas tathā
c pādātā dantinaś caiva cakrur ārtasvaraṃ mahat
a hāhākāraś ca saṃjajñe tava sainyasya māriṣa
c vadhyato bhīmasenena kṛtinā citrayodhinā
a tataḥ kṛtāstrās te sarve parivārya vṛkodaram
c abhītāḥ samavartanta śastravṛṣṭyā samantataḥ
a abhidrutaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃ
samantataḥ pāṇḍavaṃ lokavīraiḥ
b abhidrutaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃ ca samantataḥ
b lokapālasamaṃ vīra lokavīraiś ca pāṇḍavam
c sainyena ghoreṇa susaṃgatena
dṛṣṭvā balī pārṣato bhīmasenam
a athopagacchac charavikṣatāṅgaṃ
padātinaṃ krodhaviṣaṃ vamantam
c āśvāsayan pārṣato bhīmasenaṃ
gadāhastaṃ kālam ivāntakāle
a niḥśalyam enaṃ ca cakāra tūrṇam
āropayac cātmarathaṃ mahātmā
c bhṛśaṃ pariṣvajya ca bhīmasenam
āśvāsayām āsa ca śatrumadhye
d tathā tasmin vartamāne 'tivegaṃ
d bhīmo tatho pretya ca yājñasenam sic
a bhrātṝn athopetya tavāpi putras
tasmin vimarde mahati pravṛtte
b dṛṣṭvā raṇe vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe
c ayaṃ durātmā drupadasya putraḥ
samāgato bhīmasenena sārdham
e taṃ yāta sarve sahitā nihantuṃ
mā vo ripuḥ prārthayatām anīkam
f ārchann etaṃ kṣudrakarmātihīnaṃ
f sainyaṃ ca vidhvaṃsayate pṛṣatkaiḥ
a śrutvā tu vākyaṃ tam amṛṣyamāṇā
jyeṣṭhājñayā coditā dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ
c vadhāya niṣpetur udāyudhās te
yugakṣaye ketavo yadvad ugrāḥ
a pragṛhya citrāṇi dhanūṃṣi vīrā
jyānemighoṣaiḥ pravikampayantaḥ
c śarair avarṣan drupadasya putraṃ
yathāmbudā bhūdharaṃ vārijālaiḥ
e nihatya tāṃś cāpi śaraiḥ sutīkṣṇair
na vivyathe samare citrayodhī
a samabhyudīrṇāṃś ca tavātmajāṃs tathā
niśāmya vīrān abhitaḥ sthitān raṇe
c jighāṃsur ugraṃ drupadātmajo yuvā
pramohanāstraṃ yuyuje mahārathaḥ
e kruddho bhṛśaṃ tava putreṣu rājan
daityeṣu yadvat samare mahendraḥ
f sa vai tato 'straṃ sumahāprabhāvaṃ
f pramohanaṃ droṇadattaṃ mahātmā
f prayojayām āsa udārakarmā
f tasmin raṇe tava sainyasya rājan
a tato vyamuhyanta raṇe nṛvīrāḥ
pramohanāstrāhatabuddhisattvāḥ
c pradudruvuḥ kuravaś caiva sarve
savājināgāḥ sarathāḥ samantāt
e parītakālān iva naṣṭasaṃjñān
mohopetāṃs tava putrān niśamya
f etasminn eva kāle tu bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
f viśramya ca tadā rājan pītvāmṛtarasaṃ jalam
f punaḥ saṃnahya sahasā yodhayām āsa saṃyuge
f dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahitaḥ kālayām āsa bhārata
a etasminn eva kāle tu droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c drupadaṃ tribhir āsādya śarair vivyādha dāruṇaiḥ
a so 'tividdhas tadā rājan raṇe droṇena pārthivaḥ
c apāyād drupado rājan pūrvavairam anusmaran
a jitvā tu drupadaṃ droṇaḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau pratāpavān
c tasya śaṅkhasvanaṃ śrutvā vitresuḥ sarvasomakāḥ
a atha śuśrāva tejasvī droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c pramohanāstreṇa raṇe mohitān ātmajāṃs tava
a tato droṇo rājagṛddhī tvarito 'bhiyayau raṇāt
c tatrāpaśyan maheṣvāso bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
e dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca vicarantau mahāraṇe
a mohāviṣṭāṃś ca te putrān apaśyat sa mahārathaḥ
c tataḥ prajñāstram ādāya mohanāstraṃ vyaśātayat
a atha pratyāgataprāṇās tava putrā mahārathāḥ
c punar yuddhāya samare prayayur bhīmapārṣatau
a tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prāha samāhūya svasainikān
c gacchantu padavīṃ śaktyā bhīmapārṣatayor yudhi
a saubhadrapramukhā vīrā rathā dvādaśa daṃśitāḥ
c pravṛttim adhigacchantu na hi śudhyati me manaḥ
d pravṛttiṃ bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca saṃyuge
d vijñāya samare śīghraṃ praviśadhvaṃ rathārṇavam
d gacchantu parayā śaktyā bhavanta iti me matiḥ
a ta evaṃ samanujñātāḥ śūrā vikrāntayodhinaḥ
c bāḍham ity evam uktvā tu sarve puruṣamāninaḥ
e madhyaṃdinagate sūrye prayayuḥ sarva eva hi
a kekayā draupadeyāś ca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavān
c abhimanyuṃ puraskṛtya mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ
a te kṛtvā samare vyūhaṃ sūcīmukham ariṃdamāḥ
c bibhidur dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ tad rathānīkam āhave
a tān prayātān maheṣvāsān abhimanyupurogamān
c bhīmasenabhayāviṣṭā dhṛṣṭadyumnavimohitā
a na saṃdhārayituṃ śaktā tava senā janādhipa
c madamūrchānvitātmānaṃ pramadevādhvani sthitā
a te 'bhiyātā maheṣvāsāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥ
c parīpsanto 'bhyadhāvanta dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarau
a tau ca dṛṣṭvā maheṣvāsān abhimanyupurogamān
c babhūvatur mudā yuktau nighnantau tava vāhinīm
d droṇam iṣvastrakuśalaṃ sarvavidyāsu pāragam
a dṛṣṭvā ca sahasāyāntaṃ pāñcālyo gurum ātmanaḥ
c nāśaṃsata vadhaṃ vīraḥ putrāṇāṃ tava pārṣataḥ
a tato rathaṃ samāropya kekayasya vṛkodaram
c abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddho droṇam iṣvastrapāragam
a tasyābhipatatas tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c kruddhaś ciccheda bhallena dhanuḥ śatruniṣūdanaḥ
a anyāṃś ca śataśo bāṇān preṣayām āsa pārṣate
c duryodhanahitārthāya bhartṛpiṇḍam anusmaran
a athānyad dhanur ādāya pārṣataḥ paravīrahā
c droṇaṃ vivyādha saptatyā rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
a tasya droṇaḥ punaś cāpaṃ cicchedāmitrakarśanaḥ
c hayāṃś ca caturas tūrṇaṃ caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥ
a vaivasvatakṣayaṃ ghoraṃ preṣayām āsa vīryavān
c sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
d dharmarājapuraṃ rājan preṣayām āsa vai dvijaḥ
a hatāśvāt sa rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥ
c āruroha mahābāhur abhimanyor mahāratham
a tataḥ sarathanāgāśvā samakampata vāhinī
c paśyato bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca paśyataḥ
a tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā droṇenāmitatejasā
c nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ samastās te mahārathāḥ
a vadhyamānaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ droṇena niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vyabhramat tatra tatraiva kṣobhyamāṇa ivārṇavaḥ
a tathā dṛṣṭvā ca tat sainyaṃ jahṛṣe ca balaṃ tava
c dṛṣṭvācāryaṃ ca saṃkruddhaṃ dahantaṃ ripuvāhinīm
e cukruśuḥ sarvato yodhāḥ sādhu sādhv iti bhārata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato duryodhano rājā mohāt pratyāgatas tadā
c śaravarṣaiḥ punar bhīmaṃ pratyavārayad acyutam
a ekībhūtāḥ punaś caiva tava putrā mahārathāḥ
c sametya samare bhīmaṃ yodhayām āsur udyatāḥ
a bhīmaseno 'pi samare saṃprāpya svarathaṃ punaḥ
c samāruhya mahābāhur yayau yena tavātmajaḥ
a pragṛhya ca mahāvegaṃ parāsukaraṇaṃ dṛḍham
c citraṃ śarāsanaṃ saṃkhye śarair vivyādha te sutān
a tato duryodhano rājā bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
c nārācena sutīkṣṇena bhṛśaṃ marmaṇy atāḍayat
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāsas tava putreṇa dhanvinā
c krodhasaṃraktanayano vegenotkṣipya kārmukam
a duryodhanaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayat
c sa tathābhihato rājā nācalad girirāḍ iva
a tau dṛṣṭvā samare kruddhau vinighnantau parasparam
c duryodhanānujāḥ sarve śūrāḥ saṃtyaktajīvitāḥ
a saṃsmṛtya mantritaṃ pūrvaṃ nigrahe bhīmakarmaṇaḥ
c niścayaṃ manasā kṛtvā nigrahītuṃ pracakramuḥ
a tān āpatata evājau bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c pratyudyayau mahārāja gajaḥ pratigajān iva
a bhṛśaṃ kruddhaś ca tejasvī nārācena samarpayat
c citrasenaṃ mahārāja tava putraṃ mahāyaśāḥ
a tathetarāṃs tava sutāṃs tāḍayām āsa bhārata
c śarair bahuvidhaiḥ saṃkhye rukmapuṅkhaiḥ suvegitaiḥ
a tataḥ saṃsthāpya samare svāny anīkāni sarvaśaḥ
c abhimanyuprabhṛtayas te dvādaśa mahārathāḥ
a preṣitā dharmarājena bhīmasenapadānugāḥ
c pratyudyayur mahārāja tava putrān mahābalān
a dṛṣṭvā rathasthāṃs tāñ śūrān sūryāgnisamatejasaḥ
c sarvān eva maheṣvāsān bhrājamānāñ śriyā vṛtān
a mahāhave dīpyamānān suvarṇakavacojjvalān
c tatyajuḥ samare bhīmaṃ tava putrā mahābalāḥ
a tān nāmṛṣyata kaunteyo jīvamānā gatā iti
c anvīya ca punaḥ sarvāṃs tava putrān apīḍayat
a athābhimanyuṃ samare bhīmasenena saṃgatam
c pārṣatena ca saṃprekṣya tava sainye mahārathāḥ
c   kekayā draupadīsutāḥ
c tān dṛṣṭvā samare kruddhās
a duryodhanaprabhṛtayaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥ
c bhṛśam aśvaiḥ prajavitaiḥ prayayur yatra te rathāḥ
a aparāhṇe tato rājan prāvartata mahān raṇaḥ
c tāvakānāṃ ca balināṃ pareṣāṃ caiva bhārata
a abhimanyur vikarṇasya hayān hatvā mahājavān
c athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samācinot
a hatāśvaṃ ratham utsṛjya vikarṇas tu mahārathaḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ rājaṃś citrasenasya bhāsvaram
a sthitāv ekarathe tau tu bhrātarau kuruvardhanau
c ārjuniḥ śarajālena chādayām āsa bhārata
a durjayo 'tha vikarṇaś ca kārṣṇiṃ pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
c vivyadhāte na cākampat kārṣṇir merur ivācalaḥ
a duḥśāsanas tu samare kekayān pañca māriṣa
c yodhayām āsa rājendra tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a draupadeyā raṇe kruddhā duryodhanam avārayan
c ekaikas tribhir ānarchat putraṃ tava viśāṃ pate
a putro 'pi tava durdharṣo draupadyās tanayān raṇe
c sāyakair niśitai rājann ājaghāna pṛthak pṛthak
a taiś cāpi viddhaḥ śuśubhe rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ
c giriprasravaṇair yadvad girir dhātuvimiśritaiḥ
a bhīṣmo 'pi samare rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c kālayām āsa balavān pālaḥ paśugaṇān iva
a tato gāṇḍīvanirghoṣaḥ prādurāsīd viśāṃ pate
c dakṣiṇena varūthinyāḥ pārthasyārīn vinighnataḥ
a uttasthuḥ samare tatra kabandhāni samantataḥ
c kurūṇāṃ cāpi sainyeṣu pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārata
a śoṇitodaṃ rathāvartaṃ gajadvīpaṃ hayormiṇam
c rathanaubhir naravyāghrāḥ prateruḥ sainyasāgaram
a chinnahastā vikavacā videhāś ca narottamāḥ
c patitās tatra dṛśyante śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a nihatair mattamātaṅgaiḥ śoṇitaughapariplutaiḥ
c bhūr bhāti bharataśreṣṭha parvatair ācitā yathā
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
c na tatrāsīt pumān kaś cid yo yoddhuṃ nābhikāṅkṣati
a evaṃ yuyudhire vīrāḥ prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥ
c tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ kāṅkṣamāṇā jayaṃ yudhi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato duryodhano rājā lohitāyati bhāskare
c saṃgrāmarabhaso bhīmaṃ hantukāmo 'bhyadhāvata
a tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya nṛvīraṃ dṛḍhavairiṇam
c bhīmasenaḥ susaṃkruddha idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto varṣapūgābhikāṅkṣitaḥ
c adya tvāṃ nihaniṣyāmi yadi notsṛjase raṇam
a adya kuntyāḥ parikleśaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ
c draupadyāś ca parikleśaṃ praṇotsyāmi hate tvayi
a yat tvaṃ durodaro bhūtvā pāṇḍavān avamanyase
c tasya pāpasya gāndhāre paśya vyasanam āgatam
a karṇasya matam ājñāya saubalasya ca yat purā
c acintya pāṇḍavān kāmād yatheṣṭaṃ kṛtavān asi
a yācamānaṃ ca yan mohād dāśārham avamanyase
c ulūkasya samādeśaṃ yad dadāsi ca hṛṣṭavat
a adya tvā nihaniṣyāmi sānubandhaṃ sabāndhavam
c samīkariṣye tat pāpaṃ yat purā kṛtavān asi
a evam uktvā dhanur ghoraṃ vikṛṣyodbhrāmya cāsakṛt
c samādāya śarān ghorān mahāśanisamaprabhān
a ṣaḍviṃśat tarasā kruddho mumocāśu suyodhane
c jvalitāgniśikhākārān vajrakalpān ajihmagān
a tato 'sya kārmukaṃ dvābhyāṃ sūtaṃ dvābhyāṃ ca vivyadhe
c caturbhir aśvāñ javanān anayad yamasādanam
a dvābhyāṃ ca suvikṛṣṭābhyāṃ śarābhyām arimardanaḥ
c chatraṃ ciccheda samare rājñas tasya rathottamāt
a tribhiś ca tasya ciccheda jvalantaṃ dhvajam uttamam
b tribhir anyair maheṣvāsaś cicchedāsya dhvajaṃ tathā
c chittvā taṃ ca nanādoccais tava putrasya paśyataḥ
a rathāc ca sa dhvajaḥ śrīmān nānāratnavibhūṣitaḥ
c papāta sahasā bhūmiṃ vidyuj jaladharād iva
a jvalantaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ nāgaṃ maṇimayaṃ śubham
c dhvajaṃ kurupateś chinnaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
a athainaṃ daśabhir bāṇais tottrair iva mahāgajam
c ājaghāna raṇe bhīmaḥ smayann iva mahārathaḥ
d sa tathābhihato rājā smayann iva mahārathaḥ
a tatas tu rājā sindhūnāṃ rathaśreṣṭho jayadrathaḥ
c duryodhanasya jagrāha pārṣṇiṃ satpuruṣocitām
a kṛpaś ca rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kauravyam amitaujasam
c āropayad rathaṃ rājan duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
a sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c niṣasāda rathopasthe rājā duryodhanas tadā
a parivārya tato bhīmaṃ hantukāmo jayadrathaḥ
c rathair anekasāhasrair bhīmasyāvārayad diśaḥ
a dhṛṣṭaketus tato rājann abhimanyuś ca vīryavān
c kekayā draupadeyāś ca tava putrān ayodhayan
a citrasenaḥ sucitraś ca citrāśvaś citradarśanaḥ
c cārucitraḥ sucāruś ca tathā nandopanandakau
a aṣṭāv ete maheṣvāsāḥ sukumārā yaśasvinaḥ
c abhimanyurathaṃ rājan samantāt paryavārayan
a ājaghāna tatas tūrṇam abhimanyur mahāmanāḥ
c ekaikaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
e vajramṛtyupratīkāśair vicitrāyudhaniḥsṛtaiḥ
a amṛṣyamāṇās te sarve saubhadraṃ rathasattamam
c vavarṣur mārgaṇais tīkṣṇair giriṃ merum ivāmbudāḥ
a sa pīḍyamānaḥ samare kṛtāstro yuddhadurmadaḥ
c abhimanyur mahārāja tāvakān samakampayat
e yathā devāsure yuddhe vajrapāṇir mahāsurān
a vikarṇasya tato bhallān preṣayām āsa bhārata
c caturdaśa rathaśreṣṭho ghorān āśīviṣopamān
d sa tair vikarṇasya rathāt pātayām āsa vīryavān
e dhvajaṃ sūtaṃ hayāṃś cāsya chittvā nṛtyann ivāhave
a punaś cānyāñ śarān pītān akuṇṭhāgrāñ śilāśitān
c preṣayām āsa saubhadro vikarṇāya mahābalaḥ
a te vikarṇaṃ samāsādya kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥ
c bhittvā dehaṃ gatā bhūmiṃ jvalanta iva pannagāḥ
a te śarā hemapuṅkhāgrā vyadṛśyanta mahītale
c vikarṇarudhiraklinnā vamanta iva śoṇitam
a vikarṇaṃ vīkṣya nirbhinnaṃ tasyaivānye sahodarāḥ
c abhyadravanta samare saubhadrapramukhān rathān
a abhiyātvā tathaivāśu rathasthān sūryavarcasaḥ
c avidhyan samare 'nyonyaṃ saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥ
a durmukhaḥ śrutakarmāṇaṃ viddhvā saptabhir āśugaiḥ
c dhvajam ekena ciccheda sārathiṃ cāsya saptabhiḥ
a aśvāñ jāmbūnadair jālaiḥ pracchannān vātaraṃhasaḥ
c jaghāna ṣaḍbhir āsādya sārathiṃ cābhyapātayat
a sa hatāśve rathe tiṣṭhañ śrutakarmā mahārathaḥ
c śaktiṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddho maholkāṃ jvalitām iva
a sā durmukhasya vipulaṃ varma bhittvā yaśasvinaḥ
c vidārya prāviśad bhūmiṃ dīpyamānā sutejanā
d durmukho vihvalas tatra niṣasāda rathe vibho
d visaṃjñaṃ prekṣya te sarve bhrātaraḥ paryavārayan
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā virathaṃ tatra sutasomo mahābalaḥ
c paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ ratham āropayat svakam
a śrutakīrtis tathā vīro jayatsenaṃ sutaṃ tava
c abhyayāt samare rājan hantukāmo yaśasvinam
a tasya vikṣipataś cāpaṃ śrutakīrter mahātmanaḥ
c ciccheda samare rājañ jayatsenaḥ sutas tava
e kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena prahasann iva bhārata
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā chinnadhanvānaṃ śatānīkaḥ sahodaram
c abhyapadyata tejasvī siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥ
a śatānīkas tu samare dṛḍhaṃ visphārya kārmukam
b nanāda sumahānādaṃ prabhinna iva vāraṇaḥ
c vivyādha daśabhis tūrṇaṃ jayatsenaṃ śilīmukhaiḥ
a athānyena sutīkṣṇena sarvāvaraṇabhedinā
c śatānīko jayatsenaṃ vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam
a tathā tasmin vartamāne duṣkarṇo bhrātur antike
b mumocāsmai śitān bāṇāṃs tīkṣṇān āśīviṣopamān
c ciccheda samare cāpaṃ nākuleḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya bhārasādhanam uttamam
c samādatta śitān bāṇāñ śatānīko mahābalaḥ
a tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cāmantrya duṣkarṇaṃ bhrātur agrataḥ
c mumoca niśitān bāṇāñ jvalitān pannagān iva
a tato 'sya dhanur ekena dvābhyāṃ sūtaṃ ca māriṣa
c ciccheda samare tūrṇaṃ taṃ ca vivyādha saptabhiḥ
a aśvān manojavāṃś cāsya kalmāṣān vītakalmaṣaḥ
c jaghāna niśitais tūrṇaṃ sarvān dvādaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a athāpareṇa bhallena sumuktena nipātinā
c duṣkarṇaṃ samare kruddho vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam
d sa papāta tato bhūmau vajrarugṇa iva drumaḥ
d sa vihvalo rathopasthe niṣasāda sutas tava
a duṣkarṇaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā pañca rājan mahārathāḥ
c jighāṃsantaḥ śatānīkaṃ sarvataḥ paryavārayan
a chādyamānaṃ śaravrātaiḥ śatānīkaṃ yaśasvinam
c abhyadhāvanta saṃrabdhāḥ kekayāḥ pañca sodarāḥ
a tān abhyāpatataḥ prekṣya tava putrā mahārathāḥ
c pratyudyayur mahārāja gajā iva mahāgajān
a durmukho durjayaś caiva tathā durmarṣaṇo yuvā
c śatruṃjayaḥ śatrusahaḥ sarve kruddhā yaśasvinaḥ
e pratyudyātā mahārāja kekayān bhrātaraḥ samam
a rathair nagarasaṃkāśair hayair yuktair manojavaiḥ
c nānāvarṇavicitrābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtaiḥ
a varacāpadharā vīrā vicitrakavacadhvajāḥ
c viviśus te paraṃ sainyaṃ siṃhā iva vanād vanam
a teṣāṃ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ vyatiṣaktarathadvipam
c avartata mahāraudraṃ nighnatām itaretaram
e anyonyāgaskṛtāṃ rājan yamarāṣṭravivardhanam
a muhūrtāstamite sūrye cakrur yuddhaṃ sudāruṇam
c rathinaḥ sādinaś caiva vyakīryanta sahasraśaḥ
a tataḥ śāṃtanavaḥ kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c nāśayām āsa senāṃ vai bhīṣmas teṣāṃ mahātmanām
e pāñcālānāṃ ca sainyāni śarair ninye yamakṣayam
a evaṃ bhittvā maheṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c kṛtvāvahāraṃ sainyānāṃ yayau svaśibiraṃ nṛpa
d nāśayām āsatur vīrau dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarau
d kauravāṇām anīkāni śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a dharmarājo 'pi saṃprekṣya dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarau
c mūrdhni caitāv upāghrāya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śibiraṃ yayau
d arjuno vāsudevaś ca kauravāṇām anīkinīm
d hatvā vidrāvya ca śaraiḥ śibirāyaiva jagmatuḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a atha śūrā mahārāja parasparakṛtāgasaḥ
c jagmuḥ svaśibirāṇy eva rudhireṇa samukṣitāḥ
a viśramya ca yathānyāyaṃ pūjayitvā parasparam
c saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta bhūyo yuddhacikīrṣayā
a tatas tava suto rājaṃś cintayābhipariplutaḥ
c visravac choṇitāktāṅgaḥ papracchedaṃ pitāmaham
a sainyāni raudrāṇi bhayānakāni
vyūḍhāni samyag bahuladhvajāni
c vidārya hatvā ca nipīḍya śūrās
te pāṇḍavānāṃ tvaritā rathaughāḥ
a saṃmohya sarvān yudhi kīrtimanto
vyūhaṃ ca taṃ makaraṃ vajrakalpam
c praviśya bhīmena nibarhito 'smi
ghoraiḥ śarair mṛtyudaṇḍaprakāśaiḥ
a kruddhaṃ tam udvīkṣya bhayena rājan
saṃmūrchito nālabhaṃ śāntim adya
c icche prasādāt tava satyasaṃdha
prāptuṃ jayaṃ pāṇḍaveyāṃś ca hantum
a tenaivam uktaḥ prahasan mahātmā
duryodhanaṃ jātamanyuṃ viditvā
c taṃ pratyuvācāvimanā manasvī
gaṅgāsutaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
a pareṇa yatnena vigāhya senāṃ
sarvātmanāhaṃ tava rājaputra
c icchāmi dātuṃ vijayaṃ sukhaṃ ca
na cātmānaṃ chādaye 'haṃ tvadarthe
a ete tu raudrā bahavo mahārathā
yaśasvinaḥ śūratamāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ
c ye pāṇḍavānāṃ samare sahāyā
jitaklamāḥ krodhaviṣaṃ vamanti
a te neha śakyāḥ sahasā vijetuṃ
vīryonnaddhāḥ kṛtavairās tvayā ca
c ahaṃ hy etān pratiyotsyāmi rājan
sarvātmanā jīvitaṃ tyajya vīra
a raṇe tavārthāya mahānubhāva
na jīvitaṃ rakṣyatamaṃ mamādya
c sarvāṃs tavārthāya sadevadaityāṃl
lokān daheyaṃ kim u śatrūṃs taveha
a tat pāṇḍavān yodhayiṣyāmi rājan
priyaṃ ca te sarvam ahaṃ kariṣye
c śrutvaiva caitat paramapratīto
duryodhanaḥ prītamanā babhūva
a sarvāṇi sainyāni tataḥ prahṛṣṭo
nirgacchatety āha nṛpāṃś ca sarvān
c tadājñayā tāni viniryayur drutaṃ
rathāśvapādātagajāyutāni
a praharṣayuktāni tu tāni rājan
mahānti nānāvidhaśastravanti
c sthitāni nāgāśvapadātimanti
virejur ājau tava rājan balāni
a vṛndaiḥ sthitāś cāpi susaṃprayuktāś
cakāśire dantigaṇāḥ samantāt
c śastrāstravidbhir naradeva yodhair
adhiṣṭhitāḥ sainyagaṇās tvadīyāḥ
a rathaiś ca pādātagajāśvasaṃghaiḥ
prayādbhir ājau vidhivat praṇunnaiḥ
c samuddhataṃ vai taruṇārkavarṇaṃ
rajo babhau chādayat sūryaraśmīn
a rejuḥ patākā rathadantisaṃsthā
vāteritā bhrāmyamāṇāḥ samantāt
c nānāraṅgāḥ samare tatra rājan
meghair yuktā vidyutaḥ khe yathaiva
a dhanūṃṣi visphārayatāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ
babhūva śabdas tumulo 'tighoraḥ
c vimathyato devamahāsuraughair
yathārṇavasyādiyuge tadānīm
a tad ugranādaṃ bahurūpavarṇaṃ
tavātmajānāṃ samudīrṇam evam
c babhūva sainyaṃ ripusainyahantṛ
yugāntameghaughanibhaṃ tadānīm
 saṃjaya uvāca
a athātmajaṃ tava punar gāṅgeyo dhyānam āsthitam
c abravīd bharataśreṣṭhaḥ saṃpraharṣakaraṃ vacaḥ
a ahaṃ droṇaś ca śalyaś ca kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca somadatto 'tha saindhavaḥ
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau bāhlikaḥ saha bāhlikaiḥ
c trigartarājaś ca balī māgadhaś ca sudurjayaḥ
a bṛhadbalaś ca kausalyaś citraseno viviṃśatiḥ
b kṛpaś ca saha sodaryais tava rājan padānugaiḥ
c rathāś ca bahusāhasrāḥ śobhamānā mahādhvajāḥ
a deśajāś ca hayā rājan svārūḍhā hayasādibhiḥ
c gajendrāś ca madodvṛttāḥ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥ
a padātāś ca tathā śūrā nānāpraharaṇāyudhāḥ
c nānādeśasamutpannās tvadarthe yoddhum udyatāḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavas tvadarthe tyaktajīvitāḥ
c devān api raṇe jetuṃ samarthā iti me matiḥ
a avaśyaṃ tu mayā rājaṃs tava vācyaṃ hitaṃ sadā
c aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ
e vāsudevasahāyāś ca mahendrasamavikramāḥ
a sarvathāhaṃ tu rājendra kariṣye vacanaṃ tava
c pāṇḍavān vā raṇe jeṣye māṃ vā jeṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a evam uktvā dadau cāsmai viśalyakaraṇīṃ śubhām
c oṣadhīṃ vīryasaṃpannāṃ viśalyaś cābhavat tadā
a tataḥ prabhāte vimale svenānīkena vīryavān
c avyūhata svayaṃ vyūhaṃ bhīṣmo vyūhaviśāradaḥ
a maṇḍalaṃ manujaśreṣṭha nānāśastrasamākulam
c saṃpūrṇaṃ yodhamukhyaiś ca tathā dantipadātibhiḥ
a rathair anekasāhasraiḥ samantāt parivāritam
c aśvavṛndair mahadbhiś ca ṛṣṭitomaradhāribhiḥ
a nāge nāge rathāḥ sapta sapta cāśvā rathe rathe
c anv aśvaṃ daśa dhānuṣkā dhānuṣke sapta carmiṇaḥ
a evaṃvyūhaṃ mahārāja tava sainyaṃ mahārathaiḥ
c sthitaṃ raṇāya mahate bhīṣmeṇa yudhi pālitam
a daśāśvānāṃ sahasrāṇi dantināṃ ca tathaiva ca
c rathānām ayutaṃ cāpi putrāś ca tava daṃśitāḥ
e citrasenādayaḥ śūrā abhyarakṣan pitāmaham
a rakṣyamāṇaś ca taiḥ śūrair gopyamānāś ca tena te
c saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta rājānaś ca mahābalāḥ
a duryodhanas tu samare daṃśito ratham āsthitaḥ
c vyabhrājata śriyā juṣṭo yathā śakras triviṣṭape
a tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīt putrāṇāṃ tava bhārata
c rathaghoṣaś ca tumulo vāditrāṇāṃ ca nisvanaḥ
a bhīṣmeṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ vyūḍhaḥ pratyaṅmukho yudhi
c maṇḍalaḥ sumahāvyūho durbhedyo 'mitraghātinām
e sarvataḥ śuśubhe rājan raṇe 'rīṇāṃ durāsadaḥ
a maṇḍalaṃ tu samālokya vyūhaṃ paramadāruṇam
c svayaṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā vyūhaṃ vajram athākarot
a tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu yathāsthānam avasthitāḥ
c rathinaḥ sādinaś caiva siṃhanādam athānadan
a bibhitsavas tato vyūhaṃ niryayur yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c itaretarataḥ śūrāḥ sahasainyāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a bhāradvājo yayau matsyaṃ drauṇiś cāpi śikhaṇḍinam
c svayaṃ duryodhano rājā pārṣataṃ samupādravat
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca rājan madreśam īyatuḥ
c vindānuvindāv āvantyāv irāvantam abhidrutau
a sarve nṛpās tu samare dhanaṃjayam ayodhayan
c bhīmaseno raṇe yatto hārdikyaṃ samavārayat
a citrasenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca tathā durmarṣaṇaṃ vibho
c ārjuniḥ samare rājaṃs tava putrān ayodhayat
a prāgjyotiṣaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ haiḍimbo rākṣasottamaḥ
c abhidudrāva vegena matto mattam iva dvipam
a alambusas tato rājan sātyakiṃ yuddhadurmadam
c sasainyaṃ samare kruddho rākṣasaḥ samabhidravat
a bhūriśravā raṇe yatto dhṛṣṭaketum ayodhayat
c śrutāyuṣaṃ tu rājānaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a cekitānas tu samare kṛpam evānvayodhayat
c śeṣāḥ pratiyayur yattā bhīmam eva mahāratham
a tato rājasahasrāṇi parivavrur dhanaṃjayam
c śaktitomaranārācagadāparighapāṇayaḥ
a arjuno 'tha bhṛśaṃ kruddho vārṣṇeyam idam abravīt
c paśya mādhava sainyāni dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃyuge
e vyūḍhāni vyūhaviduṣā gāṅgeyena mahātmanā
a yuddhābhikāmāñ śūrāṃś ca paśya mādhava daṃśitān
c trigartarājaṃ sahitaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ paśya keśava
a adyaitān pātayiṣyāmi paśyatas te janārdana
c ya ime māṃ yaduśreṣṭha yoddhukāmā raṇājire
a evam uktvā tu kaunteyo dhanurjyām avamṛjya ca
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi narādhipagaṇān prati
a te 'pi taṃ parameṣvāsāḥ śaravarṣair apūrayan
c taḍāgam iva dhārābhir yathā prāvṛṣi toyadā
a hāhākāro mahān āsīt tava sainye viśāṃ pate
c chādyamānau bhṛśaṃ kṛṣṇau śarair dṛṣṭvā mahāraṇe
a devā devarṣayaś caiva gandharvāś ca mahoragāḥ
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmur dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇau tathāgatau
a tataḥ kruddho 'rjuno rājann aindram astram udīrayat
c tatrādbhutam apaśyāma vijayasya parākramam
a śastravṛṣṭiṃ parair muktāṃ śaraughair yad avārayat
c na ca tatrāpy anirbhinnaḥ kaś cid āsīd viśāṃ pate
a teṣāṃ rājasahasrāṇāṃ hayānāṃ dantināṃ tathā
c dvābhyāṃ tribhiḥ śaraiś cānyān pārtho vivyādha māriṣa
a te hanyamānāḥ pārthena bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yayuḥ
c agādhe majjamānānāṃ bhīṣmas trātābhavat tadā
a āpatadbhis tu tais tatra prabhagnaṃ tāvakaṃ balam
c saṃcukṣubhe mahārāja vātair iva mahārṇavaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme nivṛtte ca suśarmaṇi
c prabhagneṣu ca vīreṣu pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
a kṣubhyamāṇe bale tūrṇaṃ sāgarapratime tava
c pratyudyāte ca gāṅgeye tvaritaṃ vijayaṃ prati
a dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājan raṇe pārthasya vikramam
c tvaramāṇaḥ samabhyetya sarvāṃs tān abravīn nṛpān
a teṣāṃ ca pramukhe śūraṃ suśarmāṇaṃ mahābalam
c madhye sarvasya sainyasya bhṛśaṃ saṃharṣayan vacaḥ
a eṣa bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yoddhukāmo dhanaṃjayam
c sarvātmanā kuruśreṣṭhas tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
a taṃ prayāntaṃ parānīkaṃ sarvasainyena bhāratam
c saṃyattāḥ samare sarve pālayadhvaṃ pitāmaham
a bāḍham ity evam uktvā tu tāny anīkāni sarvaśaḥ
c narendrāṇāṃ mahārāja samājagmuḥ pitāmaham
a tataḥ prayātaḥ sahasā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'rjunam
c raṇe bhāratam āyāntam āsasāda mahābalam
a mahāśvetāśvayuktena bhīmavānaraketunā
c mahatā meghanādena rathenāti virājata
a samare sarvasainyānām upayātaṃ dhanaṃjayam
c abhavat tumulo nādo bhayād dṛṣṭvā kirīṭinam
a abhīśuhastaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭvādityam ivāparam
c madhyaṃdinagataṃ saṃkhye na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum
a tathā śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śvetāśvaṃ śvetakārmukam
c na śekuḥ pāṇḍavā draṣṭuṃ śvetagraham ivoditam
a sa sarvataḥ parivṛtas trigartaiḥ sumahātmabhiḥ
c bhrātṛbhis tava putraiś ca tathānyaiś ca mahārathaiḥ
a bhāradvājas tu samare matsyaṃ vivyādha patriṇā
c dhvajaṃ cāsya śareṇājau dhanuś caikena cicchide
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
c anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhārasahaṃ dṛḍham
e śarāṃś cāśīviṣākārāñ jvalitān pannagān iva
a droṇaṃ tribhiḥ pravivyādha caturbhiś cāsya vājinaḥ
c dhvajam ekena vivyādha sārathiṃ cāsya pañcabhiḥ
e dhanur ekeṣuṇāvidhyat tatrākrudhyad dvijarṣabhaḥ
a tasya droṇo 'vadhīd aśvāñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c aṣṭābhir bharataśreṣṭha sūtam ekena patriṇā
a sa hatāśvād avaplutya syandanād dhatasārathiḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ śaṅkhasya rathināṃ varaḥ
a tatas tu tau pitāputrau bhāradvājaṃ rathe sthitau
c mahatā śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsatur balāt
a bhāradvājas tataḥ kruddhaḥ śaram āśīviṣopamam
c cikṣepa samare tūrṇaṃ śaṅkhaṃ prati janeśvara
a sa tasya hṛdayaṃ bhittvā pītvā śoṇitam āhave
c jagāma dharaṇiṃ bāṇo lohitārdrīkṛtacchaviḥ
a sa papāta rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājaśarāhataḥ
c dhanus tyaktvā śarāṃś caiva pitur eva samīpataḥ
a hataṃ svam ātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā virāṭaḥ prādravad bhayāt
c utsṛjya samare droṇaṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam
a bhāradvājas tatas tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūm
c dārayām āsa samare śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a śikhaṇḍy api mahārāja drauṇim āsādya saṃyuge
c ājaghāna bhruvor madhye nārācais tribhir āśugaiḥ
a sa babhau naraśārdūlo lalāṭe saṃsthitais tribhiḥ
c śikharaiḥ kāñcanamayair merus tribhir ivocchritaiḥ
a aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddho nimeṣārdhāc chikhaṇḍinaḥ
c sūtaṃ dhvajam atho rājaṃs turagān āyudhaṃ tathā
e śarair bahubhir uddiśya pātayām āsa saṃyuge
a sa hatāśvād avaplutya rathād vai rathināṃ varaḥ
c khaḍgam ādāya niśitaṃ vimalaṃ ca śarāvaram
e śyenavad vyacarat kruddhaḥ śikhaṇḍī śatrutāpanaḥ
a sakhaḍgasya mahārāja caratas tasya saṃyuge
c nāntaraṃ dadṛśe drauṇis tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi bahūni bharatarṣabha
c preṣayām āsa samare drauṇiḥ paramakopanaḥ
a tām āpatantīṃ samare śaravṛṣṭiṃ sudāruṇām
c asinā tīkṣṇadhāreṇa ciccheda balināṃ varaḥ
a tato 'sya vimalaṃ drauṇiḥ śatacandraṃ manoramam
c carmācchinad asiṃ cāsya khaṇḍayām āsa saṃyuge
e śitaiḥ subahuśo rājaṃs taṃ ca vivyādha patribhiḥ
a śikhaṇḍī tu tataḥ khaḍgaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ tena sāyakaiḥ
c āvidhya vyasṛjat tūrṇaṃ jvalantam iva pannagam
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā kālānalasamaprabham
c ciccheda samare drauṇir darśayan pāṇilāghavam
e śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca vivyādha śarair bahubhir āyasaiḥ
a śikhaṇḍī tu bhṛśaṃ rājaṃs tāḍyamānaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ mādhavasya mahātmanaḥ
a sātyakis tu tataḥ kruddho rākṣasaṃ krūram āhave
c alambusaṃ śarair ghorair vivyādha balinaṃ balī
a rākṣasendras tatas tasya dhanuś ciccheda bhārata
c ardhacandreṇa samare taṃ ca vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
e māyāṃ ca rākṣasīṃ kṛtvā śaravarṣair avākirat
f athānyad dhanur ādāya bhārasādhanam uttamam
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma śaineyasya parākramam
c nāsaṃbhramad yat samare vadhyamānaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a aindram astraṃ ca vārṣṇeyo yojayām āsa bhārata
c vijayād yad anuprāptaṃ mādhavena yaśasvinā
a tad astraṃ bhasmasāt kṛtvā māyāṃ tāṃ rākṣasīṃ tadā
c alambusaṃ śarair ghorair abhyākirata sarvaśaḥ
e parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ
a tat tathā pīḍitaṃ tena mādhavena mahātmanā
c pradudrāva bhayād rakṣo hitvā sātyakim āhave
a tam ajeyaṃ rākṣasendraṃ saṃkhye maghavatā api
c śaineyaḥ prāṇadaj jitvā yodhānāṃ tava paśyatām
a nyahanat tāvakāṃś cāpi sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
c niśitair bahubhir bāṇais te 'dravanta bhayārditāḥ
a etasminn eva kāle tu drupadasyātmajo balī
c dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja tava putraṃ janeśvaram
e chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a saṃchādyamāno viśikhair dhṛṣṭadyumnena bhārata
c vivyathe na ca rājendra tava putro janeśvaraḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca samare tūrṇaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
c ṣaṣṭyā ca triṃśatā caiva tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tasya senāpatiḥ kruddho dhanuś ciccheda māriṣa
c hayāṃś ca caturaḥ śīghraṃ nijaghāna mahārathaḥ
e śaraiś cainaṃ suniśitaiḥ kṣipraṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥ
a sa hatāśvān mahābāhur avaplutya rathād balī
c padātir asim udyamya prādravat pārṣataṃ prati
a śakunis taṃ samabhyetya rājagṛddhī mahābalaḥ
c rājānaṃ sarvalokasya ratham āropayat svakam
a tato nṛpaṃ parājitya pārṣataḥ paravīrahā
c nyahanat tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vajrapāṇir ivāsuram
a kṛtavarmā raṇe bhīmaṃ śarair ārchan mahāratham
c pracchādayām āsa ca taṃ mahāmegho raviṃ yathā
a tataḥ prahasya samare bhīmasenaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ sāyakān kṛtavarmaṇe
a tair ardyamāno 'tirathaḥ sātvataḥ śastrakovidaḥ
c nākampata mahārāja bhīmaṃ cārchac chitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c sārathiṃ pātayām āsa dhvajaṃ ca supariṣkṛtam
a śarair bahuvidhaiś cainam ācinot paravīrahā
c śakalīkṛtasarvāṅgaḥ śvāvidvat samadṛśyata
a hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇaṃ vṛṣakasya rathaṃ yayau
c syālasya te mahārāja tava putrasya paśyataḥ
a bhīmaseno 'pi saṃkruddhas tava sainyam upādravat
c nijaghāna ca saṃkruddho daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a bahūnīha vicitrāṇi dvairathāni sma saṃjaya
c pāṇḍūnāṃ māmakaiḥ sārdham aśrauṣaṃ tava jalpataḥ
a na caiva māmakaṃ kaṃ cid dhṛṣṭaṃ śaṃsasi saṃjaya
c nityaṃ pāṇḍusutān hṛṣṭān abhagnāṃś caiva śaṃsasi
a jīyamānān vimanaso māmakān vigataujasaḥ
c vadase saṃyuge sūta diṣṭam etad asaṃśayam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yathāśakti yathotsāhaṃ yuddhe ceṣṭanti tāvakāḥ
c darśayānāḥ paraṃ śaktyā pauruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabha
a gaṅgāyāḥ suranadyā vai svādubhūtaṃ yathodakam
c mahodadhiguṇābhyāsāl lavaṇatvaṃ nigacchati
a tathā tat pauruṣaṃ rājaṃs tāvakānāṃ mahātmanām
c prāpya pāṇḍusutān vīrān vyarthaṃ bhavati saṃyuge
a ghaṭamānān yathāśakti kurvāṇān karma duṣkaram
c na doṣeṇa kuruśreṣṭha kauravān gantum arhasi
a tavāparādhāt sumahān saputrasya viśāṃ pate
c pṛthivyāḥ prakṣayo ghoro yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
a ātmadoṣāt samutpannaṃ śocituṃ nārhase nṛpa
c na hi rakṣanti rājānaḥ sarvārthān nāpi jīvitam
a yuddhe sukṛtināṃ lokān icchanto vasudhādhipāḥ
c camūṃ vigāhya yudhyante nityaṃ svargaparāyaṇāḥ
a pūrvāhṇe tu mahārāja prāvartata janakṣayaḥ
c tan mamaikamanā bhūtvā śṛṇu devāsuropamam
a āvantyau tu maheṣvāsau mahātmānau mahābalau
c irāvantam abhiprekṣya sameyātāṃ raṇotkaṭau
e teṣāṃ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
a irāvāṃs tu susaṃkruddho bhrātarau devarūpiṇau
c vivyādha niśitais tūrṇaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
e tāv enaṃ pratyavidhyetāṃ samare citrayodhinau
a yudhyatāṃ hi tathā rājan viśeṣo na vyadṛśyata
c yatatāṃ śatrunāśāya kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇām
a irāvāṃs tu tato rājann anuvindasya sāyakaiḥ
c caturbhiś caturo vāhān anayad yamasādanam
a bhallābhyāṃ ca sutīkṣṇābhyāṃ dhanuḥ ketuṃ ca māriṣa
c ciccheda samare rājaṃs tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tyaktvānuvindo 'tha rathaṃ vindasya ratham āsthitaḥ
c dhanur gṛhītvā navamaṃ bhārasādhanam uttamam
a tāv ekasthau raṇe vīrāv āvantyau rathināṃ varau
c śarān mumucatus tūrṇam irāvati mahātmani
a tābhyāṃ muktā mahāvegāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
c divākarapathaṃ prāpya chādayām āsur ambaram
a irāvāṃs tu tataḥ kruddho bhrātarau tau mahārathau
c vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa sārathiṃ cāpy apātayat
a tasmin nipatite bhūmau gatasattve 'tha sārathau
c rathaḥ pradudrāva diśaḥ samudbhrāntahayas tataḥ
a tau sa jitvā mahārāja nāgarājasutāsutaḥ
c pauruṣaṃ khyāpayaṃs tūrṇaṃ vyadhamat tava vāhinīm
a sā vadhyamānā samare dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥ
c vegān bahuvidhāṃś cakre viṣaṃ pītveva mānavaḥ
a haiḍimbo rākṣasendras tu bhagadattaṃ samādravat
c rathenādityavarṇena sadhvajena mahābalaḥ
a tataḥ prāgjyotiṣo rājā nāgarājaṃ samāsthitaḥ
c yathā vajradharaḥ pūrvaṃ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye
a tatra devāḥ sagandharvā ṛṣayaś ca samāgatāḥ
c viśeṣaṃ na sma vividur haiḍimbabhagadattayoḥ
a yathā surapatiḥ śakras trāsayām āsa dānavān
c tathaiva samare rājaṃs trāsayām āsa pāṇḍavān
a tena vidrāvyamāṇās te pāṇḍavāḥ sarvatodiśam
c trātāraṃ nābhyavindanta sveṣv anīkeṣu bhārata
a bhaimaseniṃ rathasthaṃ tu tatrāpaśyāma bhārata
c śeṣā vimanaso bhūtvā prādravanta mahārathāḥ
a nivṛtteṣu tu pāṇḍūnāṃ punaḥ sainyeṣu bhārata
b naiṣṭhikīṃ buddhim āsthāya svargāya bharatottamāḥ
c āsīn niṣṭānako ghoras tava sainyeṣu saṃyuge
a ghaṭotkacas tato rājan bhagadattaṃ mahāraṇe
c śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa meruṃ girim ivāmbudaḥ
a nihatya tāñ śarān rājā rākṣasasya dhanuścyutān
c bhaimaseniṃ raṇe tūrṇaṃ sarvamarmasv atāḍayat
a sa tāḍyamāno bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c na vivyathe rākṣasendro bhidyamāna ivācalaḥ
a tasya prāgjyotiṣaḥ kruddhas tomarān sa caturdaśa
c preṣayām āsa samare tāṃś ca ciccheda rākṣasaḥ
a sa tāṃś chittvā mahābāhus tomarān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c bhagadattaṃ ca vivyādha saptatyā kaṅkapatribhiḥ
a tataḥ prāgjyotiṣo rājan prahasann iva bhārata
c tasyāśvāṃś caturaḥ saṃkhye pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a sa hatāśve rathe tiṣṭhan rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavān
c śaktiṃ cikṣepa vegena prāgjyotiṣagajaṃ prati
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā hemadaṇḍāṃ suvegitām
c tridhā ciccheda nṛpatiḥ sā vyakīryata medinīm
a śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā haiḍimbaḥ prādravad bhayāt
c yathendrasya raṇāt pūrvaṃ namucir daityasattamaḥ
a taṃ vijitya raṇe śūraṃ vikrāntaṃ khyātapauruṣam
c ajeyaṃ samare rājan yamena varuṇena ca
a pāṇḍavīṃ samare senāṃ saṃmamarda sakuñjaraḥ
c yathā vanagajo rājan mṛdnaṃś carati padminīm
a madreśvaras tu samare yamābhyāṃ saha saṃgataḥ
c svasrīyau chādayāṃ cakre śaraughaiḥ pāṇḍunandanau
a sahadevas tu samare mātulaṃ vīkṣya saṃgatam
c avārayac charaugheṇa megho yadvad divākaram
a chādyamānaḥ śaraugheṇa hṛṣṭarūpataro 'bhavat
c tayoś cāpy abhavat prītir atulā mātṛkāraṇāt
a tataḥ prahasya samare nakulasya mahārathaḥ
b dhvajaṃ ciccheda bāṇena dhanuś caikena māriṣa
b athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ chādayann iva bhārata
b nijaghāna raṇe taṃ tu sūtaṃ cāsya nyapātayat
c aśvān vai caturo rājaṃś caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥ
e preṣayām āsa samare yamasya sadanaṃ prati
a hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥ
c āruroha tato yānaṃ bhrātur eva yaśasvinaḥ
a ekasthau tu raṇe śūrau dṛḍhe vikṣipya kārmuke
c madrarājarathaṃ kruddhau chādayām āsatuḥ kṣaṇāt
a sa cchādyamāno bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c svasrīyābhyāṃ naravyāghro nākampata yathācalaḥ
e prahasann iva tāṃ cāpi śaravṛṣṭiṃ jaghāna ha
f pṛṣatkānāṃ sahasrāṇi prahasann iva tāv api
f sṛjan rurodha samare megho vṛṣṭyā yathācalam
a sahadevas tataḥ kruddhaḥ śaram udyamya vīryavān
c madrarājam abhiprekṣya preṣayām āsa bhārata
a sa śaraḥ preṣitas tena garutmān iva vegavān
c madrarājaṃ vinirbhidya nipapāta mahītale
a sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopasthe mahārathaḥ
c niṣasāda mahārāja kaśmalaṃ ca jagāma ha
a taṃ visaṃjñaṃ nipatitaṃ sūtaḥ saṃprekṣya saṃyuge
c apovāha rathenājau yamābhyām abhipīḍitam
a dṛṣṭvā madreśvararathaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukham
c sarve vimanaso bhūtvā nedam astīty acintayan
a nirjitya mātulaṃ saṃkhye mādrīputrau mahārathau
c dadhmatur muditau śaṅkhau siṃhanādaṃ vinedatuḥ
a abhidudruvatur hṛṣṭau tava sainyaṃ viśāṃ pate
c yathā daityacamūṃ rājann indropendrāv ivāmarau
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā madhyaṃ prāpte divākare
c śrutāyuṣam abhiprekṣya codayām āsa vājinaḥ
a abhyadhāvat tato rājā śrutāyuṣam ariṃdamam
c vinighnan sāyakais tīkṣṇair navabhir nataparvabhiḥ
a sa saṃvārya raṇe rājā preṣitān dharmasūnunā
c śarān sapta maheṣvāsaḥ kaunteyāya samarpayat
a te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave
c asūn iva vicinvanto dehe tasya mahātmanaḥ
a pāṇḍavas tu bhṛśaṃ viddhas tena rājñā mahātmanā
c raṇe varāhakarṇena rājānaṃ hṛdi vivyadhe
a athāpareṇa bhallena ketuṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ
c rathaśreṣṭho rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhūmau pārtho nyapātayat
a ketuṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutāyuḥ sa tu pārthivaḥ
c pāṇḍavaṃ viśikhais tīkṣṇai rājan vivyādha saptabhiḥ
a tataḥ krodhāt prajajvāla dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c yathā yugānte bhūtāni dhakṣyann iva hutāśanaḥ
a kruddhaṃ tu pāṇḍavaṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvarākṣasāḥ
c pravivyathur mahārāja vyākulaṃ cāpy abhūj jagat
a sarveṣāṃ caiva bhūtānām idam āsīn manogatam

a ṛṣayaś caiva devāś ca cakruḥ svastyayanaṃ mahat
c lokānāṃ nṛpa śāntyarthaṃ krodhite pāṇḍave tadā
a sa ca krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ sṛkkiṇī parilelihan
c dadhārātmavapur ghoraṃ yugāntādityasaṃnibham

c nirāśāny abhavaṃs tatra jīvitaṃ prati bhārata
a sa tu dhairyeṇa taṃ kopaṃ saṃnivārya mahāyaśāḥ
c śrutāyuṣaḥ praciccheda muṣṭideśe mahad dhanuḥ
a athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ nārācena stanāntare
c nirbibheda raṇe rājā sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a satvaraṃ caraṇe rājaṃs tasya vāhān mahātmanaḥ
c nijaghāna śaraiḥ kṣipraṃ sūtaṃ ca sumahābalaḥ
a hatāśvaṃ tu rathaṃ tyaktvā dṛṣṭvā rājñas tu pauruṣam

c duryodhanabalaṃ rājan sarvam āsīt parāṅmukham
a etat kṛtvā mahārāja dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c vyāttānano yathā kālas tava sainyaṃ jaghāna ha
a cekitānas tu vārṣṇeyo gautamaṃ rathināṃ varam
c prekṣatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ

a athāpareṇa bhallena dhanuś ciccheda māriṣa
c sārathiṃ cāsya samare kṣiprahasto nyapātayat

a so 'vaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāṃ jagrāha sātvataḥ
c sa tayā vīraghātinyā gadayā gadināṃ varaḥ
e gautamasya hayān hatvā sārathiṃ ca nyapātayat
a bhūmiṣṭho gautamas tasya śarāṃś cikṣepa ṣoḍaśa
c te śarāḥ sātvataṃ bhittvā prāviśanta dharātalam
a cekitānas tataḥ kruddhaḥ punaś cikṣepa tāṃ gadām
c gautamasya vadhākāṅkṣī vṛtrasyeva puraṃdaraḥ
a tām āpatantīṃ vimalām aśmagarbhāṃ mahāgadām
c śarair anekasāhasrair vārayām āsa gautamaḥ
a cekitānas tataḥ khaḍgaṃ kośād uddhṛtya bhārata

c vegena mahatā rājaṃś cekitānam upādravat

c nistriṃśābhyāṃ sutīkṣṇābhyām anyonyaṃ saṃtatakṣatuḥ
a nistriṃśavegābhihatau tatas tau puruṣarṣabhau

c āropayad rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ gautamaṃ rathināṃ varam

c āruroha tato yānaṃ śatānīkasya māriṣa

a tato rājñāṃ bahuśatair gajāśvarathayāyibhiḥ

a evam uktaḥ sa vārṣṇeyaḥ kaunteyenāmitaujasā
b satvaraṃ bālarakṣārthaṃ gacchāv eti dhanaṃjayaḥ

a niṣṭānako mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣa

c suśarmāṇam atho rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīt

b tatas tvaṃ samare yoddhuṃ rājabhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c paryāyasyādya saṃprāptaṃ phalaṃ paśya sudāruṇam
e adya te darśayiṣyāmi pūrvapretān pitāmahān
a evaṃ saṃjalpatas tasya bībhatsoḥ śatrughātinaḥ

e na cainam abravīt kiṃ cic chubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
a abhi gatvārjunaṃ vīraṃ rājabhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ

a parivāryārjunaṃ saṃkhye tava putraiḥ sahānagha
c śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa meghair iva divākaram

c tāvakānāṃ ca samare pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a sa tudyamānas tu śarair dhanaṃjayaḥ
padā hato nāga iva śvasan balī
c bāṇena bāṇena mahārathānāṃ
ciccheda cāpāni raṇe prasahya
a saṃchidya cāpāni ca tāni rājñāṃ
teṣāṃ raṇe vīryavatāṃ kṣaṇena
c vivyādha bāṇair yugapan mahātmā
niḥśeṣatāṃ teṣv atha manyamānaḥ
a nipetur ājau rudhirapradigdhās
te tāḍitāḥ śakrasutena rājan
c vibhinnagātrāḥ patitottamāṅgā

a mahīṃ gatāḥ pārthabalābhibhūtā
vicitrarūpā yugapad vineśuḥ
c dṛṣṭvā hatāṃs tān yudhi rājaputrāṃs
trigartarājaḥ prayayau kṣaṇena
a teṣāṃ rathānām atha pṛṣṭhagopā
dvātriṃśad anye 'byapatanta pārtham
c tathaiva te saṃparivārya pārthaṃ
vikṛṣya cāpāni mahāravāṇi

a saṃpīḍyamānas tu śaraughavṛṣṭyā
dhanaṃjayas tān yudhi jātaroṣaḥ
c ṣaṣṭyā śaraiḥ saṃyati tailadhautair

a ṣaṣṭiṃ rathāṃs tān avajitya saṃkhye

a trigartarājo nihatān samīkṣya

c raṇe puraskṛtya narādhipāṃs tāñ
jagāma pārthaṃ tvarito vadhāya
a abhidrutaṃ cāstrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃ

c abhyudyayus te śitaśastrahastā

a pārtho 'pi tān āpatataḥ samīkṣya
trigartarājñā sahitān nṛvīrān
c vidhvaṃsayitvā samare dhanuṣmān
gāṇḍīvamuktair niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
e bhīṣmaṃ yiyāsur yudhi saṃdadarśa
duryodhanaṃ saindhavādīṃś ca rājñaḥ
a āvārayiṣṇūn abhisaṃprayāya
muhūrtam āyodhya balena vīraḥ
c utsṛjya rājānam anantavīryo
jayadrathādīṃś ca nṛpān mahaujāḥ
e yayau tato bhīmabalo manasvī

f bhīṣmo 'pi dṛṣṭvā samare kṛtāstrān

a yudhiṣṭhiraś cograbalo mahātmā

c madrādhipaṃ samabhityajya saṃkhye

e sārdhaṃ sa mādrīsutabhīmasenair
bhīṣmaṃ yayau śāṃtanavaṃ raṇāya
a taiḥ saṃprayuktaḥ sa mahārathāgryair
gaṅgāsutaḥ samare citrayodhī
c na vivyathe śāṃtanavo mahātmā
samāgataiḥ pāṇḍusutaiḥ samastaiḥ
a athaitya rājā yudhi satyasaṃdho
jayadratho 'tyugrabalo manasvī
c ciccheda cāpāni mahārathānāṃ

pārthaṃ tathā yudhi saṃjātakopaḥ
c duryodhanaḥ krodhaviṣo mahātmā
jaghāna bāṇair analaprakāśaiḥ
a kṛpeṇa śalyena śalena caiva
tathā vibho citrasenena cājau
b te vāridhārāś ca yathādrirājaṃ

a uktvā tathā tvaṃ pitur agrato mām

a prekṣasva bhīṣmaṃ yudhi bhīmavegaṃ

c vihāya bandhūn atha sodarāṃś ca

a dṛṣṭvā hi bhīṣmaṃ tam anantavīryaṃ

a ājñāyamāne 'pi dhanaṃjayena

c āvārayām āsa hi śalya enaṃ

a sa cāpi dṛṣṭvā samudīryamāṇam
astraṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabhāvam
c nāsau vyamuhyad drupadasya putro
rājan mahendrapratimaprabhāvaḥ
a tasthau ca tatraiva mahādhanuṣmāñ
śarais tad astraṃ pratibādhamānaḥ
c athādade vāruṇam anyad astraṃ
śikhaṇḍy athograṃ pratighātāya tasya
e tad astram astreṇa vidāryamāṇaṃ
khasthāḥ surā dadṛśuḥ pārthivāś ca
a bhīṣmas tu rājan samare mahātmā

d jayadratho bhagnavāhaṃ rathaṃ taṃ

 saṃjaya uvāca

c sarveṣām eva sainyānām āsīd vyatikaro mahān
a bhinneṣu teṣu vyūheṣu kṣatriyā itaretaram
c ekam ekaṃ samāhūya yuddhāyaivopatasthire
a śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bharatānāṃ pitāmaham
c abhidudrāva vegena tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a anādṛtya tato bhīṣmas taṃ śikhaṇḍinam āhave
c prayayau sṛñjayān kruddhaḥ strītvaṃ cintya śikhaṇḍinaḥ
a sṛñjayās tu tato hṛṣṭā dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaṃ mahāratham
c siṃhanādān bahuvidhāṃś cakruḥ śaṅkhavimiśritān
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ vyatiṣaktarathadvipam
c aparāṃ diśam āsthāya sthite savitari prabho
a dhṛṣṭadyumno 'tha pāñcālyaḥ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c pīḍayantau bhṛśaṃ sainyaṃ śaktitomaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
e śastraiś ca bahubhī rājañ jaghnatus tāvakān raṇe
a te hanyamānāḥ samare tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabha
c āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā na tyajanti sma saṃyugam
e yathotsāhaṃ ca samare jaghnur lokaṃ mahārathāḥ
a tatrākrando mahān āsīt tāvakānāṃ mahātmanām
c vadhyatāṃ samare rājan pārṣatena mahātmanā
a taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ tāvakānāṃ mahārathau
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau pārṣataṃ patyupasthitau
a tau tasya turagān hatvā tvaramāṇau mahārathau
c chādayām āsatur ubhau śaravarṣeṇa pārṣatam
a avaplutyātha pāñcālyo rathāt tūrṇaṃ mahābalaḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ sātyakeḥ sumahātmanaḥ
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ
c āvantyau samare kruddhāv abhyayāt sa paraṃtapau
a tathaiva tava putro 'pi sarvodyogena māriṣa
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau parivāryopatasthivān
a arjunaś cāpi saṃkruddhaḥ kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabha
c ayodhayata saṃgrāme vajrapāṇir ivāsurān
a droṇaś ca samare kruddhaḥ putrasya priyakṛt tava
c vyadhamat sarvapāñcālāṃs tūlarāśim ivānalaḥ
a duryodhanapurogās tu putrās tava viśāṃ pate
c parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ yuyudhuḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
a tato duryodhano rājā lohitāyati bhāskare
c abravīt tāvakān sarvāṃs tvaradhvam iti bhārata
a yudhyatāṃ tu tathā teṣāṃ kurvatāṃ karma duṣkaram
c astaṃ girim athārūḍhe naprakāśati bhāskare
a prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇī
c gomāyugaṇasaṃkīrṇā kṣaṇena rajanīmukhe
a śivābhir aśivābhiś ca ruvadbhir bhairavaṃ ravam
c ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe bhūtasaṃghasamākulam
a rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca tathānye piśitāśanāḥ
c samantato vyadṛśyanta śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
d mattā rudhiragandhena piśitena ca te nṛpāḥ
d āsvādyāsvādya nṛtyante nādaṃ muñcanti bhīṣaṇam
d kabandhāni ca nṛtyanti dhanur hastāni saṃyuge
d prāsam ālambya niśitaṃ nistriṃśaṃ nirmalaṃ mahat
a arjuno 'tha suśarmādīn rājñas tān sapadānugān
c vijitya pṛtanāmadhye yayau svaśibiraṃ prati
a yudhiṣṭhiro 'pi kauravyo bhrātṛbhyāṃ sahitas tadā
c yayau svaśibiraṃ rājā niśāyāṃ senayā vṛtaḥ
a bhīmaseno 'pi rājendra duryodhanamukhān rathān
c avajitya tataḥ saṃkhye yayau svaśibiraṃ prati
a duryodhano 'pi nṛpatiḥ parivārya mahāraṇe
c bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ tūrṇaṃ prayātaḥ śibiraṃ prati
a droṇo drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c parivārya camūṃ sarvāṃ prayayuḥ śibiraṃ prati
a tathaiva sātyakī rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c parivārya raṇe yodhān yayatuḥ śibiraṃ prati
a evam ete mahārāja tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c paryavartanta sahitā niśākāle paraṃtapāḥ
a tataḥ svaśibiraṃ gatvā pāṇḍavāḥ kuravas tathā
c nyaviśanta mahārāja pūjayantaḥ parasparam
a rakṣāṃ kṛtvātmanaḥ śūrā nyasya gulmān yathāvidhi
c apanīya ca śalyāṃs te snātvā ca vividhair jalaiḥ
a kṛtasvastyayanāḥ sarve saṃstūyantaś ca bandibhiḥ
c gītavāditraśabdena vyakrīḍanta yaśasvinaḥ
a muhūrtam iva tat sarvam abhavat svargasaṃnibham
c na hi yuddhakathāṃ kāṃ cit tatra cakrur mahārathāḥ
a te prasupte bale tatra pariśrāntajane nṛpa
c hastyaśvabahule rājan prekṣaṇīye babhūvatuḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a pariṇāmya niśāṃ tāṃ tu sukhasuptā janeśvarāḥ
c kuravaḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva punar yuddhāya niryayuḥ
a tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīt senayor ubhayor api
c nirgacchamānayoḥ saṃkhye sāgarapratimo mahān
a tato duryodhano rājā citraseno viviṃśatiḥ
c bhīṣmaś ca rathināṃ śreṣṭho bhāradvājaś ca vai dvijaḥ
a ekībhūtāḥ susaṃyattāḥ kauravāṇāṃ mahācamūḥ
c vyūhāya vidadhū rājan pāṇḍavān prati daṃśitāḥ
a bhīṣmaḥ kṛtvā mahāvyūhaṃ pitā tava viśāṃ pate
c sāgarapratimaṃ ghoraṃ vāhanormitaraṅgiṇam
a agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yayau
c mālavair dākṣiṇātyaiś ca āvantyaiś ca samanvitaḥ
a tato 'nantaram evāsīd bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c pulindaiḥ pāradaiś caiva tathā kṣudrakamālavaiḥ
a droṇād anantaraṃ yatto bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
c māgadhaiś ca kaliṅgaiś ca piśācaiś ca viśāṃ pate
a prāgjyotiṣād anu nṛpaḥ kausalyo 'tha bṛhadbalaḥ
c mekalais traipuraiś caiva cicchilaiś ca samanvitaḥ
a bṛhadbalāt tataḥ śūras trigartaḥ prasthalādhipaḥ
c kāmbojair bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ yavanaiś ca sahasraśaḥ
a drauṇis tu rabhasaḥ śūras trigartād anu bhārata
c prayayau siṃhanādena nādayāno dharātalam
a tathā sarveṇa sainyena rājā duryodhanas tadā
c drauṇer anantaraṃ prāyāt sodaryaiḥ parivāritaḥ
a duryodhanād anu kṛpas tataḥ śāradvato yayau
c evam eṣa mahāvyūhaḥ prayayau sāgaropamaḥ
a rejus tatra patākāś ca śvetacchatrāṇi cābhibho
c aṅgadāny atha citrāṇi mahārhāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca
a taṃ tu dṛṣṭvā mahāvyūhaṃ tāvakānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiro 'bravīt tūrṇaṃ pārṣataṃ pṛtanāpatim
a paśya vyūhaṃ maheṣvāsa nirmitaṃ sāgaropamam
c prativyūhaṃ tvam api hi kuru pārṣata māciram
a tataḥ sa pārṣataḥ śūro vyūhaṃ cakre sudāruṇam
c śṛṅgāṭakaṃ mahārāja paravyūhavināśanam
a śṛṅgebhyo bhīmasenaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c rathair anekasāhasrais tathā hayapadātibhiḥ
a nābhyām abhūn naraśreṣṭhaḥ śvetāśvo vānaradhvajaḥ
c madhye yudhiṣṭhiro rājā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
a athetare maheṣvāsāḥ sahasainyā narādhipāḥ
c vyūhaṃ taṃ pūrayām āsur vyūhaśāstraviśāradāḥ
a abhimanyus tataḥ paścād virāṭaś ca mahārathaḥ
c draupadeyāś ca saṃhṛṣṭā rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
a evam etaṃ mahāvyūhaṃ vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ
c atiṣṭhan samare śūrā yoddhukāmā jayaiṣiṇaḥ
a bherīśabdāś ca tumulā vimiśrāḥ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥ
c kṣveḍitāsphoṭitotkruṣṭaiḥ subhīmāḥ sarvatodiśam
a tataḥ śūrāḥ samāsādya samare te parasparam
c netrair animiṣai rājann avaikṣanta prakopitāḥ
a manobhis te manuṣyendra pūrvaṃ yodhāḥ parasparam
c yuddhāya samavartanta samāhūyetaretaram
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvaham
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nighnatām itaretaram
a nārācā niśitāḥ saṃkhye saṃpatanti sma bhārata
c vyāttānanā bhayakarā uragā iva saṃghaśaḥ
a niṣpetur vimalāḥ śaktyas tailadhautāḥ sutejanāḥ
c ambudebhyo yathā rājan bhrājamānāḥ śatahradāḥ
a gadāś ca vimalaiḥ paṭṭaiḥ pinaddhāḥ svarṇabhūṣitāḥ
c patantyas tatra dṛśyante giriśṛṅgopamāḥ śubhāḥ
e nistriṃśāś ca vyarājanta vimalāmbarasaṃnibhāḥ
a ārṣabhāṇi ca carmāṇi śatacandrāṇi bhārata
c aśobhanta raṇe rājan patamānāni sarvaśaḥ
d meghāntare yathā vidyuj jvalamāneva dṛśyate
a te 'nyonyaṃ samare sene yudhyamāne narādhipa
c aśobhetāṃ yathā daityadevasene samudyate
e abhyadravanta samare te 'nyonyaṃ vai samantataḥ
a rathās tu rathibhis tūrṇaṃ preṣitāḥ paramāhave
c yugair yugāni saṃśliṣya yuyudhuḥ pārthivarṣabhāḥ
a dantināṃ yudhyamānānāṃ saṃgharṣāt pāvako 'bhavat
c danteṣu bharataśreṣṭha sadhūmaḥ sarvatodiśam
a prāsair abhihatāḥ ke cid gajayodhāḥ samantataḥ
c patamānāḥ sma dṛśyante giriśṛṅgān nagā iva
a pādātāś cāpy adṛśyanta nighnanto hi parasparam
c citrarūpadharāḥ śūrā nakharaprāsayodhinaḥ
a anyonyaṃ te samāsādya kurupāṇḍavasainikāḥ
c śastrair nānāvidhair ghorai raṇe ninyur yamakṣayam
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo rathaghoṣeṇa nādayan
c abhyāgamad raṇe pāṇḍūn dhanuḥśabdena mohayan
a pāṇḍavānāṃ rathāś cāpi nadanto bhairavasvanam
c abhyadravanta saṃyattā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
c narāśvarathanāgānāṃ vyatiṣaktaṃ parasparam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bhīṣmaṃ tu samare kruddhaṃ pratapantaṃ samantataḥ
c na śekuḥ pāṇḍavā draṣṭuṃ tapantam iva bhāskaram
a tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni dharmaputrasya śāsanāt
c abhyadravanta gāṅgeyaṃ mardayantaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a sa tu bhīṣmo raṇaślāghī somakān sahasṛñjayān
c pāñcālāṃś ca maheṣvāsān pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ saha
c bhīṣmam evābhyayus tūrṇaṃ tyaktvā mṛtyukṛtaṃ bhayam
a sa teṣāṃ rathināṃ vīro bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhi
c ciccheda sahasā rājan bāhūn atha śirāṃsi ca
a virathān rathinaś cakre pitā devavratas tava
c patitāny uttamāṅgāni hayebhyo hayasādinām
a nirmanuṣyāṃś ca mātaṅgāñ śayānān parvatopamān
c apaśyāma mahārāja bhīṣmāstreṇa pramohitān
a na tatrāsīt pumān kaś cit pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c anyatra rathināṃ śreṣṭhād bhīmasenān mahābalāt
a sa hi bhīṣmaṃ samāsādya tāḍayām āsa saṃyuge
c tato niṣṭānako ghoro bhīṣmabhīmasamāgame
a babhūva sarvasainyānāṃ ghorarūpo bhayānakaḥ
c tathaiva pāṇḍavā hṛṣṭāḥ siṃhanādam athānadan
a tato duryodhano rājā sodaryaiḥ parivāritaḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ jugopa samare vartamāne janakṣaye
a bhīmas tu sārathiṃ hatvā bhīṣmasya rathināṃ varaḥ
c vidrutāśve rathe tasmin dravamāṇe samantataḥ
e sunābhasya śareṇāśu śiraś ciccheda cārihā
a kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena sa hato nyapatad bhuvi
c hate tasmin mahārāja tava putre mahārathe
e nāmṛṣyanta raṇe śūrāḥ sodaryāḥ sapta saṃyuge
a ādityaketur bahvāśī kuṇḍadhāro mahodaraḥ
c aparājitaḥ paṇḍitako viśālākṣaḥ sudurjayaḥ
a pāṇḍavaṃ citrasaṃnāhā vicitrakavacadhvajāḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃgrāme yoddhukāmārimardanāḥ
a mahodaras tu samare bhīmaṃ vivyādha patribhiḥ
c navabhir vajrasaṃkāśair namuciṃ vṛtrahā yathā
a ādityaketuḥ saptatyā bahvāśī cāpi pañcabhiḥ
c navatyā kuṇḍadhāras tu viśālākṣaś ca saptabhiḥ
a aparājito mahārāja parājiṣṇur mahārathaḥ
c śarair bahubhir ānarchad bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
a raṇe paṇḍitakaś cainaṃ tribhir bāṇaiḥ samardayat
c sa tan na mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ śatrubhir vadham āhave
a dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇāmitrakarśanaḥ
b aparājitasya rājendra bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c śiraś ciccheda samare śareṇa nataparvaṇā
a aparājitasya sunasaṃ tava putrasya saṃyuge
c parājitasya bhīmena nipapāta śiro mahīm
a athāpareṇa bhallena kuṇḍadhāraṃ mahāratham
c prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā prasaṃdhāya śilīmukham
c preṣayām āsa samare paṇḍitaṃ prati bhārata
a sa śaraḥ paṇḍitaṃ hatvā viveśa dharaṇītalam
c yathā naraṃ nihatyāśu bhujagaḥ kālacoditaḥ
a viśālākṣaśiraś chittvā pātayām āsa bhūtale
c tribhiḥ śarair adīnātmā smaran kleśaṃ purātanam
a mahodaraṃ maheṣvāsaṃ nārācena stanāntare
c vivyādha samare rājan sa hato nyapatad bhuvi
a ādityaketoḥ ketuṃ ca chittvā bāṇena saṃyuge
c bhallena bhṛśatīkṣṇena śiraś ciccheda cārihā
a bahvāśinaṃ tato bhīmaḥ śareṇa nataparvaṇā
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho yamasya sadanaṃ prati
a pradudruvus tatas te 'nye putrās tava viśāṃ pate
c manyamānā hi tat satyaṃ sabhāyāṃ tasya bhāṣitam
a tato duryodhano rājā bhrātṛvyasanakarśitaḥ
c abravīt tāvakān yodhān bhīmo 'yaṃ yudhi vadhyatām
a evam ete maheṣvāsāḥ putrās tava viśāṃ pate
b nihatā bhīmasenena mahāvīryeṇa saṃyuge
c bhrātṝn saṃdṛśya nihatān prāsmaraṃs te hi tad vacaḥ
a yad uktavān mahāprājñaḥ kṣattā hitam anāmayam
c tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ divyadarśinaḥ
a lobhamohasamāviṣṭaḥ putraprītyā janādhipa
c na budhyase purā yat tat tathyam uktaṃ vaco mahat
a tathaiva hi vadhārthāya putrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavo balī
c nūnaṃ jāto mahābāhur yathā hanti sma kauravān
a tato duryodhano rājā bhīṣmam āsādya māriṣa
c duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo vilalāpātikarśitaḥ
a nihatā bhrātaraḥ śūrā bhīmasenena me yudhi
c yatamānās tathānye 'pi hanyante sarvasainikāḥ
a bhavāṃś ca madhyasthatayā nityam asmān upekṣate
c so 'haṃ kāpatham ārūḍhaḥ paśya daivam idaṃ mama
a etac chrutvā vacaḥ krūraṃ pitā devavratas tava
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam abravīt sāśrulocanam
a uktam etan mayā pūrvaṃ droṇena vidureṇa ca
c gāndhāryā ca yaśasvinyā tattvaṃ tāta na buddhavān
a samayaś ca mayā pūrvaṃ kṛto vaḥ śatrukarśana
c nāhaṃ yudhi vimoktavyo nāpy ācāryaḥ kathaṃ cana
a yaṃ yaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ bhīmo drakṣyati saṃyuge
c haniṣyati raṇe taṃ taṃ satyam etad bravīmi te
a sa tvaṃ rājan sthiro bhūtvā dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā raṇe matim
c yodhayasva raṇe pārthān svargaṃ kṛtvā parāyaṇam
a na śakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
c tasmād yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā sthirāṃ yudhyasva bhārata
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a dṛṣṭvā mama hatān putrān bahūn ekena saṃjaya
c bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaś caiva kim akurvata saṃyuge
a ahany ahani me putrāḥ kṣayaṃ gacchanti saṃjaya
c manye 'haṃ sarvathā sūta daivenopahatā bhṛśam
a yatra me tanayāḥ sarve jīyante na jayanty uta
c yatra bhīṣmasya droṇasya kṛpasya ca mahātmanaḥ
a saumadatteś ca vīrasya bhagadattasya cobhayoḥ
c aśvatthāmnas tathā tāta śūrāṇāṃ sumahātmanām
a anyeṣāṃ caiva vīrāṇāṃ madhyagās tanayā mama
c yad ahanyanta saṃgrāme kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
a na hi duryodhano mandaḥ purā proktam abudhyata
c vāryamāṇo mayā tāta bhīṣmeṇa vidureṇa ca
a gāndhāryā caiva durmedhāḥ satataṃ hitakāmyayā
c nāvabudhyat purā mohāt tasya prāptam idaṃ phalam
a yad bhīmasenaḥ samare putrān mama vicetasaḥ
c ahany ahani saṃkruddho nayate yamasādanam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a idaṃ tat samanuprāptaṃ kṣattur vacanam uttamam
c na buddhavān asi vibho procyamānaṃ hitaṃ tadā
a nivāraya sutān dyūtāt pāṇḍavān mā druheti ca
c suhṛdāṃ hitakāmānāṃ bruvatāṃ tat tad eva ca
a na śuśrūṣasi yad vākyaṃ martyaḥ pathyam ivauṣadham
c tad eva tvām anuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ sādhu bhāṣitam
a viduradroṇabhīṣmāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ hitaiṣiṇām
c akṛtvā vacanaṃ pathyaṃ kṣayaṃ gacchanti kauravāḥ
a tad etat samatikrāntaṃ pūrvam eva viśāṃ pate
c tasmān me śṛṇu tattvena yathā yuddham avartata
a madhyāhne sumahāraudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata
c lokakṣayakaro rājaṃs tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
a tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni dharmaputrasya śāsanāt
c saṃrabdhāny abhyadhāvanta bhīṣmam eva jighāṃsayā
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c yuktānīkā mahārāja bhīṣmam eva samabhyayuḥ
d virāṭo drupadaś caiva sahitāḥ sarvasomakaiḥ
d abhyadravanta saṃgrāme bhīṣmam eva mahārathāḥ
d kekayā dhṛṣṭaketuś ca kuntibhojaś ca daṃśitaḥ
d yuktānīkā mahārāja bhīṣmam eva samabhyayuḥ
a arjuno draupadeyāś ca cekitānaś ca saṃyuge
c duryodhanasamādiṣṭān rājñaḥ sarvān samabhyayuḥ
a abhimanyus tathā vīro haiḍimbaś ca mahārathaḥ
c bhīmasenaś ca saṃkruddhas te 'bhyadhāvanta kauravān
a tridhābhūtair avadhyanta pāṇḍavaiḥ kauravā yudhi
c tathaiva kaurave rājann avadhyanta pare raṇe
a droṇas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ somakān sṛñjayaiḥ saha
c abhyadravata saṃkruddhaḥ preṣayiṣyan yamakṣayam
a tatrākrando mahān āsīt sṛñjayānāṃ mahātmanām
c vadhyatāṃ samare rājan bhāradvājena dhanvinā
a droṇena nihatās tatra kṣatriyā bahavo raṇe
c viveṣṭantaḥ sma dṛśyante vyādhikliṣṭā narā iva
a kūjatāṃ krandatāṃ caiva stanatāṃ caiva saṃyuge
c aniśaṃ śrūyate śabdaḥ kṣutkṛśānāṃ nṛṇām iva
a tathaiva kauraveyāṇāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c cakāra kadanaṃ ghoraṃ kruddhaḥ kāla ivāparaḥ
a vadhyatāṃ tatra sainyānām anyonyena mahāraṇe
c prāvartata nadī ghorā rudhiraughapravāhinī
a sa saṃgrāmo mahārāja ghorarūpo 'bhavan mahān
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
a tato bhīmo raṇe kruddho rabhasaś ca viśeṣataḥ
c gajānīkaṃ samāsādya preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
a tatra bhārata bhīmena nārācābhihatā gajāḥ
c petuḥ seduś ca neduś ca diśaś ca paribabhramuḥ
a chinnahastā mahānāgāś chinnapādāś ca māriṣa
c krauñcavad vyanadan bhītāḥ pṛthivīm adhiśiśyire
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca hayānīkam abhidrutau
c te hayāḥ kāñcanāpīḍā rukmabhāṇḍaparicchadāḥ
e vadhyamānā vyadṛśyanta śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a patadbhiś ca hayai rājan samāstīryata medinī
c nirjihvaiś ca śvasadbhiś ca kūjadbhiś ca gatāsubhiḥ
e hayair babhau naraśreṣṭha nānārūpadharair dharā
a arjunena hataiḥ saṃkhye tathā bhārata vājibhiḥ
c prababhau vasudhā ghorā tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a rathair bhagnair dhvajaiś chinnaiś chatraiś ca sumahāprabhaiḥ
c hārair niṣkaiḥ sakeyūraiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
d cāmaravyajanaiś chinnair nikṛttaiś ca mahāyudhaiḥ
d pratodaiś ca tathā chinnair vikṛtaiś ca mahāyudhaiḥ
a uṣṇīṣair apaviddhaiś ca patākābhiś ca sarvaṣaḥ
c anukarṣaiḥ śubhai rājan yoktraiś cavyasuraśmibhiḥ
e saṃchannā vasudhā bhāti vasante kusumair iva
a evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ pāṇḍūnām api bhārata
c kruddhe śāṃtanave bhīṣme droṇe ca rathasattame
a aśvatthāmni kṛpe caiva tathaiva kṛtavarmaṇi
c tathetareṣu kruddheṣu tāvakānām api kṣayaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vartamāne tathā raudre rājan vīravarakṣaye
c śakuniḥ saubalaḥ śrīmān pāṇḍavān samupādravat
a tathaiva sātvato rājan hārdikyaḥ paravīrahā
c abhyadravata saṃgrāme pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a tataḥ kāmbojamukhyānāṃ nadījānāṃ ca vājinām
c āraṭṭānāṃ mahījānāṃ sindhujānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a vanāyujānāṃ śubhrāṇāṃ tathā parvatavāsinām
b vājināṃ bahubhiḥ saṃkhye samantāt paryavārayan
c ye cāpare tittirajā javanā vātaraṃhasaḥ
a suvarṇālaṃkṛtair etair varmavadbhiḥ sukalpitaiḥ
c hayair vātajavair mukhyaiḥ pāṇḍavasya suto balī
e abhyavartata tat sainyaṃ hṛṣṭarūpaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
a arjunasyātha dāyāda irāvān nāma vīryavān
c sutāyāṃ nāgarājasya jātaḥ pārthena dhīmatā
a airāvatena sā dattā anapatyā mahātmanā
c patyau hate suparṇena kṛpaṇā dīnacetanā
a bhāryārthaṃ tāṃ ca jagrāha pārthaḥ kāmavaśānugām
c evam eṣa samutpannaḥ parakṣetre 'rjunātmajaḥ
a sa nāgaloke saṃvṛddho mātrā ca parirakṣitaḥ
c pitṛvyeṇa parityaktaḥ pārthadveṣād durātmanā
a rūpavān vīryasaṃpanno guṇavān satyavikramaḥ
c indralokaṃ jagāmāśu śrutvā tatrārjunaṃ gatam
a so 'bhigamya mahātmānaṃ pitaraṃ satyavikramam
b uvāca vacanaṃ rājann ulūpītanayas tadā
c abhyavādayad avyagro vinayena kṛtāñjaliḥ
d nyavedayata cātmānam arjunasya mahātmanaḥ
e irāvān asmi bhadraṃ te putraś cāhaṃ tavābhibho
a mātuḥ samāgamo yaś ca tat sarvaṃ pratyavedayat
c tac ca sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam anusasmāra pāṇḍavaḥ
a pariṣvajya sutaṃ cāpi so ''tmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ guṇaiḥ
c prītimān abhavat pārtho devarājaniveśane
a so 'rjunena samājñapto devaloke tadā nṛpa
c prītipūrvaṃ mahābāhuḥ svakāryaṃ prati bhārata
d sa cāpi naraśārdūlaḥ śārdūlasamavikramaḥ
d abravīc ca tadā pārtham ayam asmi tadā vibho
d sthitaḥ preṣyaś ca putraś ca sarvathā hy anuśādhi mām
d kiṃ karomi ca te kāmaṃ kaṃ vā kāmaṃ tvam icchasi
d pariṣvajya sutaṃ premṇā vāsaviḥ pratyuvāca tam
d prītipūrvaṃ ca kāryaṃ ca kāryaṃ prati ca mānada
e yuddhakāle tvayāsmākaṃ sāhyaṃ deyam iti prabho
a bāḍham ity evam uktvā ca yuddhakāla upāgataḥ
c kāmavarṇajavair aśvaiḥ saṃvṛto bahubhir nṛpa
a te hayāḥ kāñcanāpīḍā nānāvarṇā manojavāḥ
c utpetuḥ sahasā rājan haṃsā iva mahodadhau
a te tvadīyān samāsādya hayasaṃghān mahājavān
c kroḍaiḥ kroḍān abhighnanto ghoṇābhiś ca parasparam
e nipetuḥ sahasā rājan suvegābhihatā bhuvi
a nipatadbhis tathā taiś ca hayasaṃghaiḥ parasparam
c śuśruve dāruṇaḥ śabdaḥ suparṇapatane yathā
a tathaiva ca mahārāja sametyānyonyam āhave
c parasparavadhaṃ ghoraṃ cakrus te hayasādinaḥ
a tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃkule tumule bhṛśam
c ubhayor api saṃśāntā hayasaṃghāḥ samantataḥ
a prakṣīṇasāyakāḥ śūrā nihatāśvāḥ śramāturāḥ
c vilayaṃ samanuprāptās takṣamāṇāḥ parasparam
a tataḥ kṣīṇe hayānīke kiṃciccheṣe ca bhārata
c saubalasyātmajāḥ śūrā nirgatā raṇamūrdhani
a vāyuvegasamasparśā jave vāyusamāṃs tathā
c āruhya śīlasaṃpannān vayaḥsthāṃs turagottamān
a gajo gavākṣo vṛṣakaś carmavān ārjavaḥ śukaḥ
c ṣaḍ ete balasaṃpannā niryayur mahato balāt
a vāryamāṇāḥ śakuninā svaiś ca yodhair mahābalaiḥ
c saṃnaddhā yuddhakuśalā raudrarūpā mahābalāḥ
a tad anīkaṃ mahābāho bhittvā paramadurjayam
c balena mahatā yuktāḥ svargāya vijayaiṣiṇaḥ
e viviśus te tadā hṛṣṭā gāndhārā yuddhadurmadāḥ
a tān praviṣṭāṃs tadā dṛṣṭvā irāvān api vīryavān
c abravīt samare yodhān vicitrābharaṇāyudhān
a yathaite dhārtarāṣṭrasya yodhāḥ sānugavāhanāḥ
c hanyante samare sarve tathā nītir vidhīyatām
a bāḍham ity evam uktvā te sarve yodhā irāvataḥ
c jaghnus te vai parānīkaṃ durjayaṃ samare paraiḥ
a tad anīkam anīkena samare vīkṣya pātitam
c amṛṣyamāṇās te sarve subalasyātmajā raṇe
e irāvantam abhidrutya sarvataḥ paryavārayan
a tāḍayantaḥ śitaiḥ prāsaiś codayantaḥ parasparam
c te śūrāḥ paryadhāvanta kurvanto mahad ākulam
a irāvān atha nirbhinnaḥ prāsais tīkṣṇair mahātmabhiḥ
c sravatā rudhireṇāktas tottrair viddha iva dvipaḥ
a urasy api ca pṛṣṭhe ca pārśvayoś ca bhṛśāhataḥ
c eko bahubhir atyarthaṃ dhairyād rājan na vivyathe
a irāvān atha saṃkruddhaḥ sarvāṃs tān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c mohayām āsa samare viddhvā parapuraṃjayaḥ
a prāsān uddhṛtya sarvāṃś ca svaśarīrād ariṃdamaḥ
c tair eva tāḍayām āsa subalasyātmajān raṇe
a nikṛṣya niśitaṃ khaḍgaṃ gṛhītvā ca śarāvaram
c padātis tūrṇam āgacchaj jighāṃsuḥ saubalān yudhi
a tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇāḥ sarve te subalātmajāḥ
c bhūyaḥ krodhasamāviṣṭā irāvantam athādravan
a irāvān api khaḍgena darśayan pāṇilāghavam
c abhyavartata tān sarvān saubalān baladarpitaḥ
a lāghavenātha carataḥ sarve te subalātmajāḥ
c antaraṃ nādhyagacchanta carantaḥ śīghragāminaḥ
a bhūmiṣṭham atha taṃ saṃkhye saṃpradṛśya tataḥ punaḥ
c parivārya bhṛśaṃ sarve grahītum upacakramuḥ
a athābhyāśagatānāṃ sa khaḍgenāmitrakarśanaḥ
c upahastāvahastābhyāṃ teṣāṃ gātrāṇy akṛntata
a āyudhāni ca sarveṣāṃ bāhūn api ca bhūṣitān
c apatanta nikṛttāṅgā gatā bhūmiṃ gatāsavaḥ
a vṛṣakas tu mahārāja bahudhā parivikṣataḥ
c amucyata mahāraudrāt tasmād vīrāvakartanāt
a tān sarvān patitān dṛṣṭvā bhīto duryodhanas tataḥ
c abhyabhāṣata saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ ghoradarśanam
a ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ māyāvinam ariṃdamam
c vairiṇaṃ bhīmasenasya pūrvaṃ bakavadhena vai
a paśya vīra yathā hy eṣa phalgunasya suto balī
c māyāvī vipriyaṃ ghoram akārṣīn me balakṣayam
a tvaṃ ca kāmagamas tāta māyāstre ca viśāradaḥ
c kṛtavairaś ca pārthena tasmād enaṃ raṇe jahi
a bāḍham ity evam uktvā tu rākṣaso ghoradarśanaḥ
c prayayau siṃhanādena yatrārjunasuto yuvā
a svārūḍhair yuddhakuśalair vimalaprāsayodhibhiḥ
c vīraiḥ prahāribhir yuktaḥ svair anīkaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
d hataśeṣair mahārāja dvisāhasrair hayottamaiḥ
e nihantukāmaḥ samare irāvantaṃ mahābalam
a irāvān api saṃkruddhas tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
c hantukāmam amitraghno rākṣasaṃ pratyavārayat
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya rākṣasaḥ sumahābalaḥ
c tvaramāṇas tato māyāṃ prayoktum upacakrame
a tena māyāmayāḥ kḷptā hayās tāvanta eva hi
c svārūḍhā rākṣasair ghoraiḥ śūlapaṭṭiśapāṇibhiḥ
a te saṃrabdhāḥ samāgamya dvisāhasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c acirād gamayām āsuḥ pretalokaṃ parasparam
a tasmiṃs tu nihate sainye tāv ubhau yuddhadurmadau
c saṃgrāme vyavatiṣṭhetāṃ yathā vai vṛtravāsavau
a ādravantam abhiprekṣya rākṣasaṃ yuddhadurmadam
c irāvān krodhasaṃrabdhaḥ pratyadhāvan mahābalaḥ
a samabhyāśagatasyājau tasya khaḍgena durmateḥ
c ciccheda kārmukaṃ dīptaṃ śarāvāpaṃ ca pañcakam
a sa nikṛttaṃ dhanur dṛṣṭvā khaṃ javena samāviśat
c irāvantam abhikruddhaṃ mohayann iva māyayā
a tato 'ntarikṣam utpatya irāvān api rākṣasam
c vimohayitvā māyābhis tasya gātrāṇi sāyakaiḥ
e ciccheda sarvamarmajñaḥ kāmarūpo durāsadaḥ
a tathā sa rākṣasaśreṣṭhaḥ śaraiḥ kṛttaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
c saṃbabhūva mahārāja samavāpa ca yauvanam
a māyā hi sahajā teṣāṃ vayo rūpaṃ ca kāmajam
c evaṃ tad rākṣasasyāṅgaṃ chinnaṃ chinnaṃ vyarohata
a irāvān api saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahābalam
c paraśvadhena tīkṣṇena ciccheda ca punaḥ punaḥ
a sa tena balinā vīraś chidyamāna iva drumaḥ
c rākṣaso vyanadad ghoraṃ sa śabdas tumulo 'bhavat
a paraśvadhakṣataṃ rakṣaḥ susrāva rudhiraṃ bahu
c tataś cukrodha balavāṃś cakre vegaṃ ca saṃyuge
a ārśyaśṛṅgis tato dṛṣṭvā samare śatrum ūrjitam
c kṛtvā ghoraṃ mahad rūpaṃ grahītum upacakrame
d arjunasya sutaṃ vīram irāvantaṃ yaśasvinam
e saṃgrāmaśiraso madhye sarveṣāṃ tatra paśyatām
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛśīṃ māyāṃ rākṣasasya mahātmanaḥ
c irāvān api saṃkruddho māyāṃ sraṣṭuṃ pracakrame
a tasya krodhābhibhūtasya saṃyugeṣv anivartinaḥ
c yo 'nvayo mātṛkas tasya sa enam abhipedivān
a sa nāgair bahuśo rājan sarvataḥ saṃvṛto raṇe
c dadhāra sumahad rūpam ananta iva bhogavān
e tato bahuvidhair nāgaiś chādayām āsa rākṣasam
a chādyamānas tu nāgaiḥ sa dhyātvā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥ
c sauparṇaṃ rūpam āsthāya bhakṣayām āsa pannagān
a māyayā bhakṣite tasminn anvaye tasya mātṛke
c vimohitam irāvantam asinā rākṣaso 'vadhīt
a sakuṇḍalaṃ samukuṭaṃ padmendusadṛśaprabham
c irāvataḥ śiro rakṣaḥ pātayām āsa bhūtale
a tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre rākṣasenārjunātmaje
c viśokāḥ samapadyanta dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥ
a tasmin mahati saṃgrāme tādṛśe bhairave punaḥ
c mahān vyatikaro ghoraḥ senayoḥ samapadyata
a hayā gajāḥ padātāś ca vimiśrā dantibhir hatāḥ
c rathāś ca dantinaś caiva pattibhis tatra sūditāḥ
a tathā pattirathaughāś ca hayāś ca bahavo raṇe
c rathibhir nihatā rājaṃs tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkule
a ajānann arjunaś cāpi nihataṃ putram aurasam
c jaghāna samare śūrān rājñas tān bhīṣmarakṣiṇaḥ
a tathaiva tāvakā rājan sṛñjayāś ca mahābalāḥ
c juhvataḥ samare prāṇān nijaghnur itaretaram
a muktakeśā vikavacā virathāś chinnakārmukāḥ
c bāhubhiḥ samayudhyanta samavetāḥ parasparam
a tathā marmātigair bhīṣmo nijaghāna mahārathān
c kampayan samare senāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahābalaḥ
a tena yaudhiṣṭhire sainye bahavo mānavā hatāḥ
c dantinaḥ sādinaś caiva rathino 'tha hayās tathā
a tatra bhārata bhīṣmasya raṇe dṛṣṭvā parākramam
c atyadbhutam apaśyāma śakrasyeva parākramam
a tathaiva bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca bhārata
c raudram āsīt tadā yuddhaṃ sātvatasya ca dhanvinaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā droṇasya vikrāntaṃ pāṇḍavān bhayam āviśat
c eka eva raṇe śakto hantum asmān sasainikān
a kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivīśūrair yodhavrātaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
c ity abruvan mahārāja raṇe droṇena pīḍitāḥ
a vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme bharatarṣabha
c ubhayoḥ senayoḥ śūrā nāmṛṣyanta parasparam
a āviṣṭā iva yudhyante rakṣobhūtā mahābalāḥ
c tāvakāḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca saṃrabdhās tāta dhanvinaḥ
a na sma paśyāmahe kaṃ cid yaḥ prāṇān parirakṣati
c saṃgrāme daityasaṃkāśe tasmin yoddhā narādhipa
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a irāvantaṃ tu nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthā mahārathāḥ
c saṃgrāme kim akurvanta tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a irāvantaṃ tu nihataṃ saṃgrāme vīkṣya rākṣasaḥ
c vyanadat sumahānādaṃ bhaimasenir ghaṭotkacaḥ
a nadatas tasya śabdena pṛthivī sāgarāmbarā
c saparvatavanā rājaṃś cacāla subhṛśaṃ tadā
e antarikṣaṃ diśaś caiva sarvāś ca pradiśas tathā
f celuś ca sahasā tatra tena nādena nāditāḥ
a taṃ śrutvā sumahānādaṃ tava sainyasya bhārata
c ūrustambhaḥ samabhavad vepathuḥ sveda eva ca
a sarva eva ca rājendra tāvakā dīnacetasaḥ
c sarpavat samaveṣṭanta siṃhabhītā gajā iva
a ninadat sumahānādaṃ nirghātam iva rākṣasaḥ
c jvalitaṃ śūlam udyamya rūpaṃ kṛtvā vibhīṣaṇam
a nānāpraharaṇair ghorair vṛto rākṣasapuṃgavaiḥ
c ājagāma susaṃkruddhaḥ kālāntakayamopamaḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya saṃkruddhaṃ bhīmadarśanam
c svabalaṃ ca bhayāt tasya prāyaśo vimukhīkṛtam
a tato duryodhano rājā ghaṭotkacam upādravat
c pragṛhya vipulaṃ cāpaṃ siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥ
a pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayau cainaṃ sravadbhiḥ parvatopamaiḥ
c kuñjarair daśasāhasrair vaṅgānām adhipaḥ svayam
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya gajānīkena saṃvṛtam
c putraṃ tava mahārāja cukopa sa niśācaraḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c rākṣasānāṃ ca rājendra duryodhanabalasya ca
a gajānīkaṃ ca saṃprekṣya meghavṛndam ivodyatam
c abhyadhāvanta saṃkruddhā rākṣasāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ
a nadanto vividhān nādān meghā iva savidyutaḥ
c śaraśaktyṛṣṭinārācair nighnanto gajayodhinaḥ
a bhiṇḍipālais tathā śūlair mudgaraiḥ saparaśvadhaiḥ
c parvatāgraiś ca vṛkṣaiś ca nijaghnus te mahāgajān
a bhinnakumbhān virudhirān bhinnagātrāṃś ca vāraṇān
c apaśyāma mahārāja vadhyamānān niśācaraiḥ
a teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu bhagneṣu gajayodhiṣu
c duryodhano mahārāja rākṣasān samupādravat
a amarṣavaśam āpannas tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
c mumoca niśitān bāṇān rākṣaseṣu mahābalaḥ
a jaghāna ca maheṣvāsaḥ pradhānāṃs tatra rākṣasān
c saṃkruddho bharataśreṣṭha putro duryodhanas tava
a vegavantaṃ mahāraudraṃ vidyujjihvaṃ pramāthinam
c śaraiś caturbhiś caturo nijaghāna mahārathaḥ
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā śaravarṣaṃ durāsadam
c mumoca bharataśreṣṭha niśācarabalaṃ prati
a tat tu dṛṣṭvā mahat karma putrasya tava māriṣa
c krodhenābhiprajajvāla bhaimasenir mahābalaḥ
a visphārya ca mahac cāpam indrāśanisamasvanam
c abhidudrāva vegena duryodhanam ariṃdamam
a tam āpatantam udvīkṣya kālasṛṣṭam ivāntakam
c na vivyathe mahārāja putro duryodhanas tava
a athainam abravīt kruddhaḥ krūraḥ saṃraktalocanaḥ
b adyānṛṇyaṃ gamiṣyāmi pitṝṇāṃ mātur eva ca
c ye tvayā sunṛśaṃsena dīrghakālaṃ pravāsitāḥ
e yac ca te pāṇḍavā rājaṃś chaladyūte parājitāḥ
a yac caiva draupadī kṛṣṇā ekavastrā rajasvalā
c sabhām ānīya durbuddhe bahudhā kleśitā tvayā
d asya pāpasya durbuddhe phalaṃ prāpnuhi durmate
a tava ca priyakāmena āśramasthā durātmanā
c saindhavena parikliṣṭā paribhūya pitṝn mama
a eteṣām avamānānām anyeṣāṃ ca kulādhama
c antam adya gamiṣyāmi yadi notsṛjase raṇam
a evam uktvā tu haiḍimbo mahad visphārya kārmukam
c saṃdaśya daśanair oṣṭhaṃ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihan
a śaravarṣeṇa mahatā duryodhanam avākirat
c parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tatas tad bāṇavarṣaṃ tu duḥsahaṃ dānavair api
c dadhāra yudhi rājendro yathā varṣaṃ mahādvipaḥ
a tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo niḥśvasann iva pannagaḥ
c saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ prāptaḥ putras te bharatarṣabha
a mumoca niśitāṃs tīkṣṇān nārācān pañcaviṃśatim
c te 'patan sahasā rājaṃs tasmin rākṣasapuṃgave
e āśīviṣā iva kruddhāḥ parvate gandhamādane
a sa tair viddhaḥ sravan raktaṃ prabhinna iva kuñjaraḥ
c dadhre matiṃ vināśāya rājñaḥ sa piśitāśanaḥ
e jagrāha ca mahāśaktiṃ girīṇām api dāraṇīm
a saṃpradīptāṃ maholkābhām aśanīṃ maghavān iva
c samudyacchan mahābāhur jighāṃsus tanayaṃ tava
a tām udyatām abhiprekṣya vaṅgānām adhipas tvaran
c kuñjaraṃ girisaṃkāśaṃ rākṣasaṃ pratyacodayat
a sa nāgapravareṇājau balinā śīghragāminā
c yato duryodhanarathas taṃ mārgaṃ pratyapadyata
e rathaṃ ca vārayām āsa kuñjareṇa sutasya te
a mārgam āvāritaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājñā vaṅgena dhīmatā
c ghaṭotkaco mahārāja krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
e udyatāṃ tāṃ mahāśaktiṃ tasmiṃś cikṣepa vāraṇe
a sa tayābhihato rājaṃs tena bāhuvimuktayā
c saṃjātarudhirotpīḍaḥ papāta ca mamāra ca
a pataty atha gaje cāpi vaṅgānām īśvaro balī
c javena samabhidrutya jagāma dharaṇītalam
a duryodhano 'pi saṃprekṣya pātitaṃ varavāraṇam
c prabhagnaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā jagāma paramāṃ vyathām
d aśaktaḥ pratiyoddhuṃ vai dṛṣṭvā tasya parākramam
a kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya ātmanaś cābhimānitām
c prāpte 'pakramaṇe rājā tasthau girir ivācalaḥ
a saṃdhāya ca śitaṃ bāṇaṃ kālāgnisamatejasam

a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya bāṇam indrāśaniprabham
c lāghavād vañcayām āsa mahākāyo ghaṭotkacaḥ
a bhūya eva nanādograḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
c trāsayan sarvabhūtāni yugānte jalado yathā
a taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ tasya bhīṣmasya rakṣasaḥ
c ācāryam upasaṃgamya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bravīt
a yathaiṣa ninado ghoraḥ śrūyate rākṣaseritaḥ
c haiḍimbo yudhyate nūnaṃ rājñā duryodhanena ha
a naiṣa śakyo hi saṃgrāme jetuṃ bhūtena kena cit
c tatra gacchata bhadraṃ vo rājānaṃ parirakṣata
a abhidrutaṃ mahābhāgaṃ rākṣasena durātmanā
c etad dhi paramaṃ kṛtyaṃ sarveṣāṃ naḥ paraṃtapāḥ
a pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥ
c uttamaṃ javam āsthāya prayayur yatra kauravaḥ
a droṇaś ca somadattaś ca bāhlikaś ca jayadrathaḥ
c kṛpo bhūriśravāḥ śalyaś citraseno viviṃśatiḥ
a aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca āvantyaś ca bṛhadbalaḥ
c rathāś cānekasāhasrā ye teṣām anuyāyinaḥ
e abhidrutaṃ parīpsantaḥ putraṃ duryodhanaṃ tava
a tad anīkam anādhṛṣyaṃ pālitaṃ lokasattamaiḥ
c ātatāyinam āyāntaṃ prekṣya rākṣasasattamaḥ
e nākampata mahābāhur maināka iva parvataḥ
a pragṛhya vipulaṃ cāpaṃ jñātibhiḥ parivāritaḥ
c śūlamudgarahastaiś ca nānāpraharaṇair api
a tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c rākṣasānāṃ ca mukhyasya duryodhanabalasya ca
a dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ śabdaḥ sarvatas tumulo 'bhavat
c aśrūyata mahārāja vaṃśānāṃ dahyatām iva
a śastrāṇāṃ pātyamānānāṃ kavaceṣu śarīriṇām
c śabdaḥ samabhavad rājann adrīṇām iva dīryatām
a vīrabāhuvisṛṣṭānāṃ tomarāṇāṃ viśāṃ pate
c rūpam āsīd viyatsthānāṃ sarpāṇāṃ sarpatām iva
a tataḥ paramasaṃkruddho visphārya sumahad dhanuḥ
c rākṣasendro mahābāhur vinadan bhairavaṃ ravam
a ācāryasyārdhacandreṇa kruddhaś ciccheda kārmukam
c somadattasya bhallena dhvajam unmathya cānadat
a bāhlikaṃ ca tribhir bāṇair abhyavidhyat stanāntare
c kṛpam ekena vivyādha citrasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena samyak praṇihitena ca
c jatrudeśe samāsādya vikarṇaṃ samatāḍayat
e nyaṣīdat sa rathopasthe śoṇitena pariplutaḥ
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā nārācān daśa pañca ca
c bhūriśravasi saṃkruddhaḥ prāhiṇod bharatarṣabha
e te varma bhittvā tasyāśu prāviśan medinītalam
a viviṃśateś ca drauṇeś ca yantārau samatāḍayat
c tau petatū rathopasthe raśmīn utsṛjya vājinām
a sindhurājño 'rdhacandreṇa vārāhaṃ svarṇabhūṣitam
c unmamātha mahārāja dvitīyenācchinad dhanuḥ
a caturbhir atha nārācair āvantyasya mahātmanaḥ
c jaghāna caturo vāhān krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
a pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena pītena niśitena ca
c nirbibheda mahārāja rājaputraṃ bṛhadbalam
e sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśat
a bhṛśaṃ krodhena cāviṣṭo rathastho rākṣasādhipaḥ
c cikṣepa niśitāṃs tīkṣṇāñ śarān āśīviṣopamān
e bibhidus te mahārāja śalyaṃ yuddhaviśāradam
f prāviśan bhūtalaṃ rājan valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vimukhīkṛtya tān sarvāṃs tāvakān yudhi rākṣasaḥ
c jighāṃsur bharataśreṣṭha duryodhanam upādravat
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya rājānaṃ prati vegitam
c abhyadhāvaj jighāṃsantas tāvakā yuddhadurmadāḥ
a tālamātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣanto mahābalāḥ
c tam ekam abhyadhāvanta nadantaḥ siṃhasaṃghavat
a athainaṃ śaravarṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayan
c parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ śaradīva balāhakāḥ
a sa gāḍhaviddho vyathitas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥ
c utpapāta tadākāśaṃ samantād vainateyavat
a vyanadat sumahānādaṃ jīmūta iva śāradaḥ
c diśaḥ khaṃ pradiśaś caiva nādayan bhairavasvanaḥ
a rākṣasasya tu taṃ śabdaṃ śrutvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c uvāca bharataśreṣṭho bhīmasenam idaṃ vacaḥ
a yudhyate rākṣaso nūnaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrair mahārathaiḥ
c yathāsya śrūyate śabdo nadato bhairavaṃ svanam
e atibhāraṃ ca paśyāmi tatra tāta samāhitam
a pitāmahaś ca saṃkruddhaḥ pāñcālān hantum udyataḥ
c teṣāṃ ca rakṣaṇārthāya yudhyate phalgunaḥ paraiḥ
a etac chrutvā mahābāho kāryadvayam upasthitam
c gaccha rakṣasva haiḍimbaṃ saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gatam

c prayayau siṃhanādena trāsayan sarvapārthivān
e vegena mahatā rājan parvakāle yathodadhiḥ
a tam anvayāt satyadhṛtiḥ saucittir yuddhadurmadaḥ
c śreṇimān vasudānaś ca putraḥ kāśyasya cābhibhūḥ
a abhimanyumukhāś caiva draupadeyā mahārathāḥ
c kṣatradevaś ca vikrāntaḥ kṣatradharmā tathaiva ca
a anūpādhipatiś caiva nīlaḥ svabalam āsthitaḥ
c mahatā rathavaṃśena haiḍimbaṃ paryavārayan
a kuñjaraiś ca sadā mattaiḥ ṣaṭsahasraiḥ prahāribhiḥ
c abhyarakṣanta sahitā rākṣasendraṃ ghaṭotkacam
a siṃhanādena mahatā nemighoṣeṇa caiva hi
c khuraśabdaninādaiś ca kampayanto vasuṃdharām
a teṣām āpatatāṃ śrutvā śabdaṃ taṃ tāvakaṃ balam

c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinām

c anyonyam abhidhāvantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire

a hayā gajaiḥ samājagmuḥ pādātā rathibhiḥ saha
b rathā rathaiḥ samāgacchan nāgā nāgaiś ca saṃyuge
c anyonyaṃ samare rājan prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥ
a sahasā cābhavat tīvraṃ saṃnipātān mahad rajaḥ
c rathāśvagajapattīnāṃ padanemisamuddhatam
a dhūmrāruṇaṃ rajas tīvraṃ raṇabhūmiṃ samāvṛṇot
c naiva sve na pare rājan samajānan parasparam
a pitā putraṃ na jānīte putro vā pitaraṃ tathā
c nirmaryāde tathā bhūte vaiśase lomaharṣaṇe
a śastrāṇāṃ bharataśreṣṭha manuṣyāṇāṃ ca garjatām
c sumahān abhavac chabdo vaṃśānām iva dahyatām
a gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ śoṇitāntrataraṅgiṇī
c prāvartata nadī tatra keśaśaivalaśādvalā

c śuśruve sumahāñ śabdaḥ patatām aśmanām iva
a viśiraskair manuṣyaiś ca chinnagātraiś ca vāraṇaiḥ
c aśvaiḥ saṃbhinnadehaiś ca saṃkīrṇābhūd vasuṃdharā
a nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjanto mahārathāḥ
c anyonyam abhidhāvantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire
a hayā hayān samāsādya preṣitā hayasādibhiḥ
c samāhatya raṇe 'nyonyaṃ nipetur gatajīvitāḥ
a narā narān samāsādya krodharaktekṣaṇā bhṛśam
c urāṃsy urobhir anyonyaṃ samāśliṣya nijaghnire
a preṣitāś ca mahāmātrair vāraṇāḥ paravāraṇāḥ
c abhighnanti viṣāṇāgrair vāraṇān eva saṃyuge
a te jātarudhirāpīḍāḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtāḥ
c saṃsaktāḥ pratyadṛśyanta meghā iva savidyutaḥ
a ke cid bhinnā viṣāṇāgrair bhinnakumbhāś ca tomaraiḥ
c vinadanto 'bhyadhāvanta garjanto jaladā iva
a ke cid dhastair dvidhā chinnaiś chinnagātrās tathāpare
c nipetus tumule tasmiṃś chinnapakṣā ivādrayaḥ
a pārśvais tu dāritair anye vāraṇair varavāraṇāḥ
c mumucuḥ śoṇitaṃ bhūri dhātūn iva mahīdharāḥ
a nārācābhihatās tv anye tathā viddhāś ca tomaraiḥ
c hatārohā vyadṛśyanta viśṛṅgā iva parvatāḥ
a ke cit krodhasamāviṣṭā madāndhā niravagrahāḥ
c rathān hayān padātāṃś ca mamṛduḥ śataśo raṇe

c tena tenābhyavartanta kurvanto vyākulā diśaḥ
a rathino rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥ
c parāṃ śaktiṃ samāsthāya cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavat

c prārthayānā yaśo rājan svargaṃ vā yuddhaśālinaḥ
a tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇe

a ardhacandraṃ ca saṃdhāya sutīkṣṇaṃ lomavāhinam
c bhīmasenasya ciccheda cāpaṃ krodhasamanvitaḥ
a tadantaraṃ ca saṃprekṣya tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
c saṃdadhe niśitaṃ bāṇaṃ girīṇām api dāraṇam

c saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ prāptaṃ majjantaṃ vyasanārṇave

c bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya duryodhanam upadrutāḥ
a nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjanto jaye ratāḥ
c nadanto bhairavān nādāṃs trāsayantaś ca bhūm imām

c citraseno vikarṇaś ca saindhavo 'tha bṛhadbalaḥ

a evam uktvā mahābāhur mahad visphārya kārmukam

c parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ śaradīva balāhakaḥ

c samudyamya gadāṃ gurvīṃ yamadaṇḍopamāṃ raṇe

a bhāradvājamukhāḥ sarve bhīmasenajighāṃsayā
c nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi bhīmasyorasy apātayan
