a taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃśayaṃ prāptaṃ pīḍyamānaṃ mahāratham
c abhimanyuprabhṛtayaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
e abhyadhāvan parīpsantaḥ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā sudustyajān
a anūpādhipatiḥ śūro bhīmasya dayitaḥ sakhā
c nīlo nīlāmbudaprakhyaḥ saṃkruddho drauṇim abhyayāt
e spardhate hi maheṣvāso nityaṃ droṇasutena yaḥ
a sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ drauṇiṃ vivyādha patriṇā
c yathā śakro mahārāja purā vivyādha dānavam
a vipracittiṃ durādharṣaṃ devatānāṃ bhayaṃkaram
c yena lokatrayaṃ krodhāt trāsitaṃ svena tejasā
d sa rudreṇa jitaḥ pūrvaṃ nihato mātariśvanā
a tathā nīlena nirbhinnaḥ sumukhena patatriṇā
c saṃjātarudhirotpīḍo drauṇiḥ krodhasamanvitaḥ
a sa visphārya dhanuś citram indrāśanisamasvanam
c dadhre nīlavināśāya matiṃ matimatāṃ varaḥ
a tataḥ saṃdhāya vimalān bhallān karmārapāyitān
c jaghāna caturo vāhān pātayām āsa ca dhvajam
d tataḥ ṣaṣṭhena bhallena rathāt sūtam apātayat
d sūtaṃ caikena bhallena rathanīḍād apāharat
a saptamena ca bhallena nīlaṃ vivyādha vakṣasi
c sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśat
a mohitaṃ vīkṣya rājānaṃ nīlam abhracayopamam
c ghaṭotkaco 'pi saṃkruddho bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a abhidudrāva vegena drauṇim āhavaśobhinam
c tathetare abhyadhāvan rākṣasā yuddhadurmadāḥ
d bhīmaseno 'pi samare nīlaṃ nīlāñjanaprabham
d āropya svarathaṃ vīro duryodhanam upādravat
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya rākṣasaṃ ghoradarśanam
c abhyadhāvata tejasvī bhāradvājātmajas tvaran
a nijaghāna ca saṃkruddho rākṣasān bhīmadarśanān
c yo 'bhavann agrataḥ kruddhā rākṣasasya puraḥsarāḥ
a vimukhāṃś caiva tān dṛṣṭvā drauṇicāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
c akrudhyata mahākāyo bhaimasenir ghaṭotkacaḥ
a prāduścakre mahāmāyāṃ ghorarūpāṃ sudāruṇām
c mohayan samare drauṇiṃ māyāvī rākṣasādhipaḥ
a tatas te tāvakāḥ sarve māyayā vimukhīkṛtāḥ
c anyonyaṃ samapaśyanta nikṛttān medinītale
e viceṣṭamānān kṛpaṇāñ śoṇitena samukṣitān
a droṇaṃ duryodhanaṃ śalyam aśvatthāmānam eva ca
c prāyaśaś ca maheṣvāsā ye pradhānāś ca kauravāḥ
a vidhvastā rathinaḥ sarve gajāś ca vinipātitāḥ
c hayāś ca sahayārohā vinikṛttāḥ sahasraśaḥ
a tad dṛṣṭvā tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vidrutaṃ śibiraṃ prati
c mama prākrośato rājaṃs tathā devavratasya ca
a yudhyadhvaṃ mā palāyadhvaṃ māyaiṣā rākṣasī raṇe
c ghaṭotkacaprayukteti nātiṣṭhanta vimohitāḥ
e naiva te śraddadhur bhītā vadator āvayor vacaḥ
a tāṃś ca pradravato dṛṣṭvā jayaṃ prāptāś ca pāṇḍavāḥ
c ghaṭotkacena sahitāḥ siṃhanādān pracakrire
e śaṅkhadundubhighoṣāś ca samantāt sasvanur bhṛśam
a evaṃ tava balaṃ sarvaṃ haiḍimbena durātmanā
c sūryāstamanavelāyāṃ prabhagnaṃ vidrutaṃ diśaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tasmin mahati saṃkrande rājā duryodhanas tadā
b parājayaṃ rākṣasena nāmṛṣyata paraṃtapa
c gāṅgeyam upasaṃgamya vinayenābhivādya ca
a tasya sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam ākhyātum upacakrame
c ghaṭotkacasya vijayam ātmanaś ca parājayam
a kathayām āsa durdharṣo viniḥśvasya punaḥ punaḥ
c abravīc ca tadā rājan bhīṣmaṃ kurupitāmaham
a bhavantaṃ samupāśritya vāsudevaṃ yathā paraiḥ
c pāṇḍavair vigraho ghoraḥ samārabdho mayā prabho
a ekādaśa samākhyātā akṣauhiṇyaś ca yā mama
c nideśe tava tiṣṭhanti mayā sārdhaṃ paraṃtapa
a so 'haṃ bharataśārdūla bhīmasenapurogamaiḥ
c ghaṭotkacaṃ samāśritya pāṇḍavair yudhi nirjitaḥ
a tan me dahati gātrāṇi śuṣkavṛkṣam ivānalaḥ
c tad icchāmi mahābhāga tvatprasādāt paraṃtapa
a rākṣasāpasadaṃ hantuṃ svayam eva pitāmaha
c tvāṃ samāśritya durdharṣaṃ tan me kartuṃ tvam arhasi
a etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ rājño bharatasattama
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bravīt
a śṛṇu rājan mama vaco yat tvā vakṣyāmi kaurava
c yathā tvayā mahārāja vartitavyaṃ paraṃtapa
a ātmā rakṣyo raṇe tāta sarvāvasthāsv ariṃdama
c dharmarājena saṃgrāmas tvayā kāryaḥ sadānagha
a arjunena yamābhyāṃ vā bhīmasenena vā punaḥ
b na tu kāryas tvayā rājan haiḍimbena durātmanā
c rājadharmaṃ puraskṛtya rājā rājānam ṛcchati
a ahaṃ droṇaḥ kṛpo drauṇiḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c śalyaś ca saumadattiś ca vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
a tava ca bhrātaraḥ śūrā duḥśāsanapurogamāḥ
c tvadarthaṃ pratiyotsyāmo rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahābalam
a tasmin raudre rākṣasendre yadi te hṛcchayo mahān
c ayaṃ vā gacchatu raṇe tasya yuddhāya durmateḥ
e bhagadatto mahīpālaḥ puraṃdarasamo yudhi
a etāvad uktvā rājānaṃ bhagadattam athābravīt
c samakṣaṃ pārthivendrasya vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
a gaccha śīghraṃ mahārāja haiḍimbaṃ yuddhadurmadam
c vārayasva raṇe yatto miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
e rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ yathendras tārakaṃ purā
a tava divyāni cāstrāṇi vikramaś ca paraṃtapa
c samāgamaś ca bahubhiḥ purābhūd asuraiḥ saha
a tvaṃ tasya rājaśārdūla pratiyoddhā mahāhave
c svabalena vṛto rājañ jahi rākṣasapuṃgavam
a etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ bhīṣmasya pṛtanāpateḥ
c prayayau siṃhanādena parān abhimukho drutam
a tam ādravantaṃ saṃprekṣya garjantam iva toyadam
c abhyavartanta saṃkruddhāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
a bhimaseno 'bhimanyuś ca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
c draupadeyāḥ satyadhṛtiḥ kṣatradevaś ca māriṣa
a cedipo vasudānaś ca daśārṇādhipatis tathā
c supratīkena tāṃś cāpi bhagadatto 'py upādravat
a tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
c pāṇḍūnāṃ bhagadattena yamarāṣṭravivardhanam
a pramuktā rathibhir bāṇā bhīmavegāḥ sutejanāḥ
c te nipetur mahārāja nāgeṣu ca ratheṣu ca
a prabhinnāś ca mahānāgā vinītā hastisādibhiḥ
c parasparaṃ samāsādya saṃnipetur abhītavat
a madāndhā roṣasaṃrabdhā viṣāṇāgrair mahāhave
c bibhidur dantamusalaiḥ samāsādya parasparam
a hayāś ca cāmarāpīḍāḥ prāsapāṇibhir āsthitāḥ
c coditāḥ sādibhiḥ kṣipraṃ nipetur itaretaram
a pādātāś ca padātyoghais tāḍitāḥ śaktitomaraiḥ
c nyapatanta tadā bhūmau śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a rathinaś ca tathā rājan karṇinālīkasāyakaiḥ
c nihatya samare vīrān siṃhanādān vinedire
a tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇe
c bhagadatto maheṣvāso bhīmasenam athādravat
a kuñjareṇa prabhinnena saptadhā sravatā madam
c parvatena yathā toyaṃ sravamāṇena sarvataḥ
a kirañ śarasahasrāṇi supratīkaśirogataḥ
c airāvatastho maghavān vāridhārā ivānagha
a sa bhīmaṃ śaradhārābhis tāḍayām āsa pārthivaḥ
c parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ
a bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddhaḥ pādarakṣān paraḥśatān
c nijaghāna maheṣvāsaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān kruddho bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
c codayām āsa nāgendraṃ bhīmasenarathaṃ prati
a sa nāgaḥ preṣitas tena bāṇo jyācodito yathā
c abhyadhāvata vegena bhīmasenam ariṃdamam
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c abhyavartanta vegena bhīmasenapurogamāḥ
a kekayāś cābhimanyuś ca draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c daśārṇādhipatiḥ śūraḥ kṣatradevaś ca māriṣa
e cedipaś citraketuś ca saṃkruddhāḥ sarva eva te
a uttamāstrāṇi divyāni darśayanto mahābalāḥ
c tam ekaṃ kuñjaraṃ kruddhāḥ samantāt paryavārayan
a sa viddho bahubhir bāṇair vyarocata mahādvipaḥ
c saṃjātarudhirotpīḍo dhātucitra ivādrirāṭ
a daśārṇādhipatiś cāpi gajaṃ bhūmidharopamam
c samāsthito 'bhidudrāva bhagadattasya vāraṇam
a tam āpatantaṃ samare gajaṃ gajapatiḥ sa ca
c dadhāra supratīko 'pi veleva makarālayam
d dadhāra supratīkaṃ taṃ kṣatradharmā gajena tu
a vāritaṃ prekṣya nāgendraṃ daśārṇasya mahātmanaḥ
c sādhu sādhv iti sainyāni pāṇḍaveyāny apūjayan
a tataḥ prāgjyotiṣaḥ kruddhas tomarān vai caturdaśa
c prāhiṇot tasya nāgasya pramukhe nṛpasattama
a tasya varma mukhatrāṇaṃ śātakumbhapariṣkṛtam
c vidārya prāviśan kṣipraṃ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
a sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito nāgo bharatasattama
c upāvṛttamadaḥ kṣipraṃ sa nyavartata vegataḥ
a pradudrāva ca vegena praṇadan bhairavaṃ svanam
c sa mardamānaḥ svabalaṃ vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasā
a tasmin parājite nāge pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccair yuddhāyaivopatasthire
a tato bhīmaṃ puraskṛtya bhagadattam upādravan
c kiranto vividhān bāṇāñ śastrāṇi vividhāni ca
a teṣām āpatatāṃ rājan saṃkruddhānām amarṣiṇām
c śrutvā sa ninadaṃ ghoram amarṣād gatasādhvasaḥ
e bhagadatto maheṣvāsaḥ svanāgaṃ pratyacodayat
a aṅkuśāṅguṣṭhanuditaḥ sa gajapravaro yudhi
c tasmin kṣaṇe samabhavat saṃvartaka ivānalaḥ
a rathasaṃghāṃs tathā nāgān hayāṃś ca saha sādibhiḥ
c pādātāṃś ca susaṃkruddhaḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
e amṛdnāt samare rājan saṃpradhāvaṃs tatas tataḥ
a tena saṃloḍyamānaṃ tu pāṇḍūnāṃ tad balaṃ mahat
c saṃcukoca mahārāja carmevāgnau samāhitam
a bhagnaṃ tu svabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagadattena dhīmatā
c ghaṭotkaco 'tha saṃkruddho bhagadattam upādravat
a vikaṭaḥ puruṣo rājan dīptāsyo dīptalocanaḥ
c rūpaṃ vibhīṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā roṣeṇa prajvalann iva
a jagrāha vipulaṃ śūlaṃ girīṇām api dāraṇam
c nāgaṃ jighāṃsuḥ sahasā cikṣepa ca mahābalaḥ
e saviṣphuliṅgajvālābhiḥ samantāt pariveṣṭitam
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā dṛṣṭvā jvālākulaṃ raṇe
c cikṣepa ruciraṃ tīkṣṇam ardhacandraṃ sa pārthivaḥ
e ciccheda sumahac chūlaṃ tena bāṇena vegavat
a nipapāta dvidhā chinnaṃ śūlaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam
c mahāśanir yathā bhraṣṭā śakramuktā nabhogatā
a śūlaṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā dvidhā kṛttaṃ sa pārthivaḥ
c rukmadaṇḍāṃ mahāśaktiṃ jagrāhāgniśikhopamām
e cikṣepa tāṃ rākṣasasya tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a tām āpatantīṃ saṃprekṣya viyatsthām aśanīm iva
c utpatya rākṣasas tūrṇaṃ jagrāha ca nanāda ca
a babhañja caināṃ tvarito jānuny āropya bhārata
c paśyataḥ pārthivendrasya tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tad avekṣya kṛtaṃ karma rākṣasena balīyasā
c divi devāḥ sagandharvā munayaś cāpi vismitāḥ
a pāṇḍavāś ca maheṣvāsā bhīmasenapurogamāḥ
c sādhu sādhv iti nādena pṛthivīm anunādayan
a taṃ tu śrutvā mahānādaṃ prahṛṣṭānāṃ mahātmanām
c nāmṛṣyata maheṣvāso bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
a sa visphārya mahac cāpam indrāśanisamasvanam
c abhidudrāva vegena pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathān
e visṛjan vimalāṃs tīkṣṇān nārācāñ jvalanaprabhān
a bhīmam ekena vivyādha rākṣasaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c abhimanyuṃ tribhiś caiva kekayān pañcabhis tathā
a pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena svarṇapuṅkhena patriṇā
c bibheda dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ kṣatradevasya cāhave
e papāta sahasā tasya saśaraṃ dhanur uttamam
a draupadeyāṃs tataḥ pañca pañcabhiḥ samatāḍayat
c bhīmasenasya ca krodhān nijaghāna turaṃgamān
a dhvajaṃ kesariṇaṃ cāsya ciccheda viśikhais tribhiḥ
c nirbibheda tribhiś cānyaiḥ sārathiṃ cāsya patribhiḥ
a sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśat
c viśoko bharataśreṣṭha bhagadattena saṃyuge
a tato bhīmo mahārāja viratho rathināṃ varaḥ
c gadāṃ pragṛhya vegena pracaskanda mahārathāt
a tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā saśṛṅgam iva parvatam
c tāvakānāṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ samapadyata bhārata
a etasminn eva kāle tu pāṇḍavaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c ājagāma mahārāja nighnañ śatrūn sahasraśaḥ
a yatra tau puruṣavyāghrau pitāputrau paraṃtapau
c prāgjyotiṣeṇa saṃsaktau bhīmasenaghaṭotkacau
a dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavo rājan yudhyamānān mahārathān
c tvarito bharataśreṣṭha tatrāyād vikirañ śarān
a tato duryodhano rājā tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
c senām acodayat kṣipraṃ rathanāgāśvasaṃkulām
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā kauravāṇāṃ mahācamūm
c abhidudrāva vegena pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
a bhagadatto 'pi samare tena nāgena bhārata
c vimṛdnan pāṇḍavabalaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat
a tadāsīt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ bhagadattasya māriṣa
c pāñcālaiḥ sṛñjayaiś caiva kekayaiś codyatāyudhaiḥ
a bhīmaseno 'pi samare tāv ubhau keśavārjunau
c āśrāvayad yathāvṛttam irāvad vadham uttamam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a putraṃ tu nihataṃ śrutvā irāvantaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo niḥśvasan pannago yathā
a abravīt samare rājan vāsudevam idaṃ vacaḥ
c idaṃ nūnaṃ mahāprājño viduro dṛṣṭavān purā
a kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca kṣayaṃ ghoraṃ mahāmatiḥ
c tato nivārayitavān dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram
a avadhyā bahavo vīrāḥ saṃgrāme madhusūdana
c nihatāḥ kauravaiḥ saṃkhye tathāsmābhiś ca te hatāḥ
a arthahetor naraśreṣṭha kriyate karma kutsitam
c dhig arthān yatkṛte hy evaṃ kriyate jñātisaṃkṣayaḥ
a adhanasya mṛtaṃ śreyo na ca jñātivadhād dhanam
c kiṃ nu prāpsyāmahe kṛṣṇa hatvā jñātīn samāgatān
a duryodhanāparādhena śakuneḥ saubalasya ca
c kṣatriyā nidhanaṃ yānti karṇadurmantritena ca
a idānīṃ ca vijānāmi sukṛtaṃ madhusūdana
c kṛtaṃ rājñā mahābāho yācatā sma suyodhanam
e rājyārdhaṃ pañca vā grāmān nākārṣīt sa ca durmatiḥ
a dṛṣṭvā hi kṣatriyāñ śūrāñ śayānān dharaṇītale
c nindāmi bhṛśam ātmānaṃ dhig astu kṣatrajīvikām
a aśaktam iti mām ete jñāsyanti kṣatriyā raṇe
c yuddhaṃ mamaibhirucitaṃ jñātibhir madhusūdana
a saṃcodaya hayān kṣipraṃ dhārtarāṣṭracamūṃ prati
c pratariṣye mahāpāraṃ bhujābhyāṃ samarodadhim
e nāyaṃ klībayituṃ kālo vidyate mādhava kva cit
a evam uktas tu pārthena keśavaḥ paravīrahā
c codayām āsa tān aśvān pāṇḍurān vātaraṃhasaḥ
a atha śabdo mahān āsīt tava sainyasya bhārata
c mārutoddhūtavegasya sāgarasyeva parvaṇi
d rathaṃ saṃprerayām āsa vegena tvaritojjvalam
a aparāhṇe mahārāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata
c parjanyasamanirghoṣo bhīṣmasya saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
a tato rājaṃs tava sutā bhīmasenam upādravan
c parivārya raṇe droṇaṃ vasavo vāsavaṃ yathā
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaś ca rathināṃ varaḥ
c bhagadattaḥ suśarmā ca dhanaṃjayam upādravan
a hārdikyo bāhlikaś caiva sātyakiṃ samabhidrutau
c ambaṣṭhakas tu nṛpatir abhimanyum avārayat
a śeṣās tv anye mahārāja śeṣān eva mahārathān
c tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvaham
a bhīmasenas tu saṃprekṣya putrāṃs tava janeśvara
c prajajvāla raṇe kruddho haviṣā havyavāḍ iva
a putrās tu tava kaunteyaṃ chādayāṃ cakrire śaraiḥ
c prāvṛṣīva mahārāja jaladāḥ parvataṃ yathā
a sa cchādyamāno bahudhā putrais tava viśāṃ pate
c sṛkkiṇī vilihan vīraḥ śārdūla iva darpitaḥ
a vyūḍhoraskaṃ tato bhīmaḥ pātayām āsa pārthiva
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena so 'bhavad gatajīvitaḥ
c   sumuktena mahāraṇe
c tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ  
a apareṇa tu bhallena pītena niśitena ca
c apātayat kuṇḍalinaṃ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā
a tataḥ suniśitān pītān samādatta śilīmukhān
b subahūn preṣayām āsa kopayāno mahābalaḥ
b tatas tu samare kruddho bhīmasenaḥ śilīmukhān
c sa sapta tvarayā yuktaḥ putrāṃs te prāpya māriṣa
a preṣitā bhīmasenena śarās te dṛḍhadhanvanā
c apātayanta putrāṃs te rathebhyaḥ sumahārathān
a anādhṛṣṭiṃ kuṇḍabhedaṃ vairāṭaṃ dīrghalocanam
c dīrghabāhuṃ subāhuṃ ca tathaiva kanakadhvajam
a prapatanta sma te vīrā virejur bharatarṣabha
c vasante puṣpaśabalāś cūtāḥ prapatitā iva
a tataḥ pradudruvuḥ śeṣāḥ putrās tava viśāṃ pate
c taṃ kālam iva manyanto bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
a droṇas tu samare vīraṃ nirdahantaṃ sutāṃs tava
b saṃdadhāra mahābāhur bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
c yathādriṃ vāridhārābhiḥ samantād vyakirac charaiḥ
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma kuntīputrasya pauruṣam
c droṇena vāryamāṇo 'pi nijaghne yat sutāṃs tava
a yathā hi govṛṣo varṣaṃ saṃdhārayati khāt patat
c bhīmas tathā droṇamuktaṃ śaravarṣam adīdharat
d nimīlya netre gṛhṇīyāt tathā jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥ
d droṇacāpasamudbhūtaṃ śaravarṣaṃ durāsadam
d nimīlya nayane 'gṛhṇāt tathā bāṇān vṛkodaraḥ
a adbhutaṃ ca mahārāja tatra cakre vṛkodaraḥ
c yat putrāṃs te 'vadhīt saṃkhye droṇaṃ caiva nyayodhayat
a putreṣu tava vīreṣu cikrīḍārjunapūrvajaḥ
c mṛgeṣv iva mahārāja caran vyāghro mahābalaḥ
a yathā vā paśumadhyastho drāvayeta paśūn vṛkaḥ
c vṛkodaras tava sutāṃs tathā vyadrāvayad raṇe
a gāṅgeyo bhagadattaś ca gautamaś ca mahārathaḥ
c pāṇḍavaṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe vārayām āsur arjunam
a astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya teṣāṃ so 'tiratho raṇe
c pravīrāṃs tava sainyeṣu preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
a abhimanyuś ca rājānam ambaṣṭhaṃ lokaviśrutam
c virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a viratho vadhyamānaḥ sa saubhadreṇa yaśasvinā
c avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ savrīḍo manujādhipaḥ
a asiṃ cikṣepa samare saubhadrasya mahātmanaḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ caiva hārdikyasya mahātmanaḥ
a āpatantaṃ tu nistriṃśaṃ yuddhamārgaviśāradaḥ
c lāghavād vyaṃsayām āsa saubhadraḥ paravīrahā
a vyaṃsitaṃ vīkṣya nistriṃśaṃ saubhadreṇa raṇe tadā
c sādhu sādhv iti sainyānāṃ praṇādo 'bhūd viśāṃ pate
d nirāyudham athātmānaṃ sa saṃvīkṣya janādhipa
a dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhās tv anye tava sainyam ayodhayan
c tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve pāṇḍusainyam ayodhayan
a tatrākrando mahān āsīt tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
c nighnatāṃ bhṛśam anyonyaṃ kurvatāṃ karma duṣkaram
d pravartam iva hārdikyaṃ ghoraṃ yuddham abhūt tataḥ
a anyonyaṃ hi raṇe śūrāḥ keśeṣv ākṣipya māriṣa
c nakhair dantair ayudhyanta muṣṭibhir jānubhis tathā
a bāhubhiś ca talaiś caiva nistriṃśaiś ca susaṃśitaiḥ
c vivaraṃ prāpya cānyonyam anayan yamasādanam
a nyahanac ca pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ raṇe
c vyākulīkṛtasaṃkalpā yuyudhus tatra mānavāḥ
a raṇe cārūṇi cāpāni hemapṛṣṭhāni bhārata
c hatānām apaviddhāni kalāpāś ca mahādhanāḥ
a jātarūpamayaiḥ puṅkhai rājataiś ca śitāḥ śarāḥ
c tailadhautā vyarājanta nirmuktabhujagopamāḥ
a hastidantatsarūn khaḍgāñ jātarūpapariṣkṛtān
c carmāṇi cāpaviddhāni rukmapṛṣṭhāni dhanvinām
a suvarṇavikṛtaprāsān paṭṭiśān hemabhūṣitān
c jātarūpamayāś carṣṭīḥ śaktyaś ca kanakojjvalāḥ
a apakṛttāś ca patitā musalāni gurūṇi ca
c parighān paṭṭiśāṃś caiva bhiṇḍipālāṃś ca māriṣa
a patitāṃs tomarāṃś cāpi citrā hemapariṣkṛtāḥ
c kuthāś ca bahudhākārāś cāmaravyajanāni ca
a nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjya patitā narāḥ
c jīvanta iva dṛśyante gatasattvā mahārathāḥ
a gadāvimathitair gātrair musalair bhinnamastakāḥ
c gajavājirathakṣuṇṇāḥ śerate sma narāḥ kṣitau
a tathaivāśvanṛnāgānāṃ śarīrair ābabhau tadā
c saṃchannā vasudhā rājan parvatair iva sarvataḥ
a samare patitaiś caiva śaktyṛṣṭiśaratomaraiḥ
c nistriṃśaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsair ayaskuntaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
a parighair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca śataghnībhis tathaiva ca
c śarīraiḥ śastrabhinnaiś ca samāstīryata medinī
a niḥśabdair alpaśabdaiś ca śoṇitaughapariplutaiḥ
c gatāsubhir amitraghna vibabhau saṃvṛtā mahī
a satalatraiḥ sakeyūrair bāhubhiś candanokṣitaiḥ
b sudhṛtair lakuṭaiś caiva saṃvṛtā tatra medinī
c hastihastopamaiś chinnair ūrubhiś ca tarasvinām
d sāṅgadaiś ca bhujaiś caiva vipraviddhair alaṃkṛtaiḥ
a baddhacūḍāmaṇidharaiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
c patitair vṛṣabhākṣāṇāṃ babhau bhārata medinī
a kavacaiḥ śoṇitādigdhair viprakīrṇaiś ca kāñcanaiḥ
c rarāja subhṛśaṃ bhūmiḥ śāntārcibhir ivānalaiḥ
a vipraviddhaiḥ kalāpaiś ca patitaiś ca śarāsanaiḥ
c viprakīrṇaiḥ śaraiś cāpi rukmapuṅkhaiḥ samantataḥ
a rathaiś ca bahubhir bhagnaiḥ kiṅkiṇījālamālibhiḥ
c vājibhiś ca hataiḥ kīrṇaiḥ srastajihvaiḥ saśoṇitaiḥ
a anukarṣaiḥ patākābhir upāsaṅgair dhvajair api
c pravīrāṇāṃ mahāśaṅkhair viprakīrṇaiś ca pāṇḍuraiḥ
a srastahastaiś ca mātaṅgaiḥ śayānair vibabhau mahī
b śuśubhe dharaṇī rājan pradīptair iva parvataiḥ
b srastair ābharaṇaiś caiva vibabhau tu tadā mahī
c nānārūpair alaṃkāraiḥ pramadevābhyalaṃkṛtā
a dantibhiś cāparais tatra saprāsair gāḍhavedanaiḥ
c karaiḥ śabdaṃ vimuñcadbhiḥ śīkaraṃ ca muhur muhuḥ
e vibabhau tad raṇasthānaṃ dhamyamānair ivācalaiḥ
a nānārāgaiḥ kambalaiś ca paristomaiś ca dantinām
b vivāritavicitrābhiḥ kuthābhiś ca samantataḥ
c vaiḍūryamaṇidaṇḍaiś ca patitair aṅkuśaiḥ śubhaiḥ
a ghaṇṭābhiś ca gajendrāṇāṃ patitābhiḥ samantataḥ
c vighāṭitavicitrābhiḥ kuthābhī rāṅkavais tathā
a graiveyaiś citrarūpaiś ca rukmakakṣyābhir eva ca
c yantraiś ca bahudhā chinnais tomaraiś ca sakampanaiḥ
d rarāja subhṛśaṃ bhūmis tatra viśāṃ pate
a aśvānāṃ reṇukapilai rukmacchannair uraśchadaiḥ
c sādināṃ ca bhujaiś chinnaiḥ patitaiḥ sāṅgadais tathā
a prāsaiś ca vimalais tīkṣṇair vimalābhis tatharṣṭibhiḥ
c uṣṇīṣaiś ca tathā chinnaiḥ praviddhaiś ca tatas tataḥ
a vicitrair ardhacandraiś ca jātarūpapariṣkṛtaiḥ
c aśvāstaraparistomai rāṅkavair mṛditais tathā
a narendracūḍāmaṇibhir vicitraiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
c chatrais tathāpaviddhaiś ca cāmaravyajanair api
a padmendudyutibhiś caiva vadanaiś cārukuṇḍalaiḥ
c kḷptaśmaśrubhir atyarthaṃ vīrāṇāṃ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ
a apaviddhair mahārāja suvarṇojjvalakuṇḍalaiḥ
c grahanakṣatraśabalā dyaur ivāsīd vasuṃdharā
a evam ete mahāsene mṛdite tatra bhārata
c parasparaṃ samāsādya tava teṣāṃ ca saṃyuge
a teṣu śrānteṣu bhagneṣu mṛditeṣu ca bhārata
c rātriḥ samabhavad ghorā nāpaśyāma tato raṇam
a tato 'vahāraṃ sainyānāṃ pracakruḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c ghore niśāmukhe raudre vartamāne sudāruṇe
a avahāraṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sahitāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c nyaviśanta yathākālaṃ gatvā svaśibiraṃ tadā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato duryodhano rājā śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
c duḥśāsanaś ca putras te sūtaputraś ca durjayaḥ
a samāgamya mahārāja mantraṃ cakrūr vivakṣitam
c kathaṃ pāṇḍusutā yuddhe jetavyāḥ sagaṇā iti
a tato duryodhano rājā sarvāṃs tān āha mantriṇaḥ
c sūtaputraṃ samābhāṣya saubalaṃ ca mahābalam
a droṇo bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ saumadattiś ca saṃyuge
c na pārthān pratibādhante na jāne tatra kāraṇam
a avadhyamānās te cāpi kṣapayanti balaṃ mama
c so 'smi kṣīṇabalaḥ karṇa kṣīṇaśastraś ca saṃyuge
d droṇasya pramukhe vīrā hatās te bhrātaro mama
d bhīmasenena rādheya mama caiva ca paśyataḥ
a nikṛtaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūrair avadhyair daivatair api
c so 'haṃ saṃśayam āpannaḥ prakariṣye kathaṃ raṇam
d mahābala mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśārada
d mantrajño mantravān dakṣo nītimān nītikovidaḥ
d sa śūraḥ sa ca vikrāntaḥ sūryaputraḥ pratāpavān
d etan mahābhītikaraṃ pratariṣye raṇaṃ katham
a tam abravīn mahārāja sūtaputro narādhipam
c mā śuco bharataśreṣṭha prakariṣye priyaṃ tava
a bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tūrṇam apayātu mahāraṇāt
c nivṛtte yudhi gāṅgeye nyastaśastre ca bhārata
a ahaṃ pārthān haniṣyāmi sanitān sarvasomakaiḥ
c paśyato yudhi bhīṣmasya śape satyena te nṛpa
a pāṇḍaveṣu dayāṃ rājan sadā bhīṣmaḥ karoti vai
c aśaktaś ca raṇe bhīṣmo jetum etān mahārathān
a abhimānī raṇe bhīṣmo nityaṃ cāpi raṇapriyaḥ
c sa kathaṃ pāṇḍavān yuddhe jeṣyate tāta saṃgatān
a sa tvaṃ śīghram ito gatvā bhīṣmasya śibiraṃ prati
c anumānya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ śastraṃ nyāsaya bhārata
a nyastaśastre tato bhīṣme nihatān paśya pāṇḍavān
c mayaikena raṇe rājan sasuhṛdgaṇabāndhavān
a evam uktas tu karṇena putro duryodhanas tava
c abravīd bhrātaraṃ tatra duḥśāsanam idaṃ vacaḥ
a anuyātraṃ yathā sajjaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati sarvataḥ
c duḥśāsana tathā kṣipraṃ sarvam evopapādaya
a evam uktvā tato rājan karṇam āha janeśvaraḥ
c anumānya raṇe bhīṣmam ito 'haṃ dvipadāṃ varam
a āgamiṣye tataḥ kṣipraṃ tvatsakāśam ariṃdama
c tatas tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra prakariṣyasi saṃyugam
a niṣpapāta tatas tūrṇaṃ putras tava viśāṃ pate
c sahito bhrātṛbhiḥ sarvair devair iva śatakratuḥ
a tatas taṃ nṛpaśārdūlaṃ śārdūlasamavikramam
c ārohayad dhayaṃ tūrṇaṃ bhrātā duḥśāsanas tadā
a aṅgadī baddhamukuṭo hastābharaṇavān nṛpaḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭro mahārāja vibabhau sa mahendravat
a bhāṇḍīpuṣpanikāśena tapanīyanibhena ca
c anuliptaḥ parārdhyena candanena sugandhinā
a arajombarasaṃvītaḥ siṃhakhelagatir nṛpaḥ
c śuśubhe vimalārciṣmañ śaradīva divākaraḥ
a taṃ prayāntaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmasya śibiraṃ prati
c anujagmur maheṣvāsāḥ sarvalokasya dhanvinaḥ
e bhrātaraś ca maheṣvāsās tridaśā iva vāsavam
a hayān anye samāruhya gajān anye ca bhārata
c rathair anye naraśreṣṭhāḥ parivavruḥ samantataḥ
d padātayaś ca tvaritā nakharaprāsayodhinaḥ
d parivavrur maheṣvāsaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahāratham
a āttaśastrāś ca suhṛdo rakṣaṇārthaṃ mahīpateḥ
c prādurbabhūvuḥ sahitāḥ śakrasyevāmarā divi
a saṃpūjyamānaḥ kurubhiḥ kauravāṇāṃ mahārathaḥ
c prayayau sadanaṃ rājan gāṅgeyasya yaśasvinaḥ
e anvīyamānaḥ sahitaiḥ sodaraiḥ sarvato nṛpaḥ
a dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇaḥ kāle saṃbhṛtya svabhujaṃ tadā
c hastihastopamaṃ śaikṣaṃ sarvaśatrunibarhaṇam
a pragṛhṇann añjalīn nṝṇām udyatān sarvatodiśam
c śuśrāva madhurā vāco nānādeśanivāsinām
a saṃstūyamānaḥ sūtaiś ca māgadhaiś ca mahāyaśāḥ
c pūjayānaś ca tān sarvān sarvalokeśvareśvaraḥ
a pradīpaiḥ kāñcanais tatra gandhatailāvasecanaiḥ
c parivavrur mahātmānaṃ prajvaladbhiḥ samantataḥ
d devāsure yathendro 'sau saṃgrāme ca bhayaṃkare
a sa taiḥ parivṛto rājā pradīpaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ śubhaiḥ
c śuśubhe candramā yukto dīptair iva mahāgrahaiḥ
a kañcukoṣṇīṣiṇas tatra vetrajharjharapāṇayaḥ
c protsārayantaḥ śanakais taṃ janaṃ sarvatodiśam
a saṃprāpya tu tato rājā bhīṣmasya sadanaṃ śubham
c avatīrya hayāc cāpi bhīṣmaṃ prāpya janeśvaraḥ
a abhivādya tato bhīṣmaṃ niṣaṇṇaḥ paramāsane
c kāñcane sarvatobhadre spardhyāstaraṇasaṃvṛte
e uvāca prāñjalir bhīṣmaṃ bāṣpakaṇṭho 'śrulocanaḥ
a tvāṃ vayaṃ samupāśritya saṃyuge śatrusūdana
c utsahema raṇe jetuṃ sendrān api surāsurān
a kim u pāṇḍusutān vīrān sasuhṛdgaṇabāndhavān
c tasmād arhasi gāṅgeya kṛpāṃ kartuṃ mayi prabho
e jahi pāṇḍusutān vīrān mahendra iva dānavān
a pūrvam uktaṃ mahābāho nihaniṣyāmi somakān
c pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ karūṣāṃś ceti bhārata
a tad vacaḥ satyam evāstu jahi pārthān samāgatān
c somakāṃś ca maheṣvāsān satyavāg bhava bhārata
a dayayā yadi vā rājan dveṣyabhāvān mama prabho
c mandabhāgyatayā vāpi mama rakṣasi pāṇḍavān
a anujānīhi samare karṇam āhavaśobhinam
c sa jeṣyati raṇe pārthān sasuhṛdgaṇabāndhavān
a etāvad uktvā nṛpatiḥ putro duryodhanas tava
c novāca vacanaṃ kiṃ cid bhīṣmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vākśalyais tava putreṇa so 'tividdhaḥ pitāmahaḥ
c duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo novācāpriyam aṇv api
a sa dhyātvā suciraṃ kālaṃ duḥkharoṣasamanvitaḥ
c śvasamāno yathā nāgaḥ praṇunno vai śalākayā
a udvṛtya cakṣuṣī kopān nirdahann iva bhārata
c sadevāsuragandharvaṃ lokaṃ lokavidāṃ varaḥ
e abravīt tava putraṃ tu sāmapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
a kiṃ nu duryodhanaivaṃ māṃ vākśalyair upavidhyasi
c ghaṭamānaṃ yathāśakti kurvāṇaṃ ca tava priyam
e juhvānaṃ samare prāṇāṃs tavaiva hitakāmyayā
a yadā tu pāṇḍavaḥ śūraḥ khāṇḍave 'gnim atarpayat
c parājitya raṇe śakraṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a yadā ca tvāṃ mahābāho gandharvair hṛtam ojasā
c amocayat pāṇḍusutaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a dravamāṇeṣu śūreṣu sodareṣu tathābhibho
c sūtaputre ca rādheye paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a yac ca naḥ sahitān sarvān virāṭanagare tadā
c eka eva samudyātaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a droṇaṃ ca yudhi saṃrabdhaṃ māṃ ca nirjitya saṃyuge
c karṇaṃ ca tvāṃ ca drauṇiṃ ca kṛpaṃ ca sumahāratham
e vāsāṃsi sa samādatta paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
f tathā drauṇiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ śāradvatam athāpi ca
f gograhe jitavān pūrvaṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
f vijitya ca yadā karṇaṃ sadā puruṣamāninam
f uttarāyai dadau vastraṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a nivātakavacān yuddhe vāsavenāpi durjayān
c jitavān samare pārthaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
d avaśyaṃ hitakāmena pārṣatena ca dhīmatā
a ko hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ pāṇḍavaṃ rabhasaṃ raṇe
b yasya goptā jagadgoptā śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
b vāsudevo 'nantaśaktiḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ
b sarveśvaro devadevaḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ
b ukto 'si bahuśo rājan nāradādyair maharṣibhiḥ
c tvaṃ tu mohān na jānīṣe vācyāvācyaṃ suyodhana
a mumūrṣur hi naraḥ sarvān vṛkṣān paśyati kāñcanān
c tathā tvam api gāndhāre viparītāni paśyasi
a svayaṃ vairaṃ mahat kṛtvā pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥ
c yudhyasva tān adya raṇe paśyāmaḥ puruṣo bhava
d aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ
a ahaṃ tu somakān sarvān sapāñcālān samāgatān
c nihaniṣye naravyāghra varjayitvā śikhaṇḍinam
a tair vāhaṃ nihataḥ saṃkhye gamiṣye yamasādanam
c tān vā nihatya saṃgrāme prītiṃ dāsyāmi vai tava
a pūrvaṃ hi strī samutpannā śikhaṇḍī rājaveśmani
c varadānāt pumāñ jātaḥ saiṣā vai strī śikhaṇḍinī
a tām ahaṃ na haniṣyāmi prāṇatyāge 'pi bhārata
c yāsau prāṅ nirmitā dhātrā saiṣā vai strī śikhaṇḍinī
a sukhaṃ svapihi gāndhāre śvo 'smi kartā mahāraṇam
c yaj janāḥ kathayiṣyanti yāvat sthāsyati medinī
a evam uktas tava suto nirjagāma janeśvara
c abhivādya guruṃ mūrdhnā prayayau svaṃ niveśanam
a āgamya tu tato rājā visṛjya ca mahājanam
c praviveśa tatas tūrṇaṃ kṣayaṃ śatrukṣayaṃkaraḥ
e praviṣṭaḥ sa niśāṃ tāṃ ca gamayām āsa pārthivaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ prātar utthāya vai nṛpaḥ
c rājñaḥ samājñāpayata senāṃ yojayateti ha
e adya bhīṣmo raṇe kruddho nihaniṣyati somakān
a duryodhanasya tac chrutvā rātrau vilapitaṃ bahu
c manyamānaḥ sa taṃ rājan pratyādeśam ivātmanaḥ
a nirvedaṃ paramaṃ gatvā vinindya paravācyatām
c dīrghaṃ dadhyau śāṃtanavo yoddhukāmo 'rjunaṃ raṇe
a iṅgitena tu taj jñātvā gāṅgeyena vicintitam
c duryodhano mahārāja duḥśāsanam acodayat
a duḥśāsana rathās tūrṇaṃ yujyantāṃ bhīṣmarakṣiṇaḥ
c dvātriṃśat tvam anīkāni sarvāṇy evābhicodaya
a idaṃ hi samanuprāptaṃ varṣapūgābhicintitam
c pāṇḍavānāṃ sasainyānāṃ vadho rājyasya cāgamaḥ
a tatra kāryam ahaṃ manye bhīṣmasyaivābhirakṣaṇam
c sa no guptaḥ sukhāya syād dhanyāt pārthāṃś ca saṃyuge
a abravīc ca viśuddhātmā nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinam
c strīpūrvako hy asau jātas tasmād varjyo raṇe mayā
a lokas tad veda yad ahaṃ pituḥ priyacikīrṣayā
c rājyaṃ sphītaṃ mahābāho striyaś ca tyaktavān purā
a naiva cāhaṃ striyaṃ jātu na strīpūrvaṃ kathaṃ cana
c hanyāṃ yudhi naraśreṣṭha satyam etad bravīmi te
a ayaṃ strīpūrvako rājañ śikhaṇḍī yadi te śrutaḥ
c udyoge kathitaṃ yat tat tathā jātā śikhaṇḍinī
a kanyā bhūtvā pumāñ jātaḥ sa ca yotsyati bhārata
c tasyāhaṃ pramukhe bāṇān na muñceyaṃ kathaṃ cana
a yuddhe tu kṣatriyāṃs tāta pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaiṣiṇaḥ
c sarvān anyān haniṣyāmi saṃprāptān bāṇagocarān
a evaṃ māṃ bharataśreṣṭho gāṅgeyaḥ prāha śāstravit
c tatra sarvātmanā manye bhīṣmasyaivābhipālanam
a arakṣyamāṇaṃ hi vṛko hanyāt siṃhaṃ mahāvane
c mā vṛkeṇeva śārdūlaṃ ghātayema śikhaṇḍinā
d mā siṃham iva kākena hataṃ bhīṣmaṃ śikhaṇḍinā
d paśyema puruṣavyāghra tathā nītir vidhīyatām
a mātulaḥ śakuniḥ śalyaḥ kṛpo droṇo viviṃśatiḥ
c yattā rakṣantu gāṅgeyaṃ tasmin gupte dhruvo jayaḥ
a etac chrutvā tu rājāno duryodhanavacas tadā
c sarvato rathavaṃśena gāṅgeyaṃ paryavārayan
a putrāś ca tava gāṅgeyaṃ parivārya yayur mudā
c kampayanto bhuvaṃ dyāṃ ca kṣobhayantaś ca pāṇḍavān
a tai rathaiś ca susaṃyuktair dantibhiś ca mahārathāḥ
c parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ daṃśitāḥ samavasthitāḥ
a yathā devāsure yuddhe tridaśā vajradhāriṇam
c sarve te sma vyatiṣṭhanta rakṣantas taṃ mahāratham
a tato duryodhano rājā punar bhrātaram abravīt
c savyaṃ cakraṃ yudhāmanyur uttamaujāś ca dakṣiṇam
e goptārāv arjunasyaitāv arjuno 'pi śikhaṇḍinaḥ
a sa rakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena tathāsmābhir vivarjitaḥ
c yathā bhīṣmaṃ na no hanyād duḥśāsana tathā kuru
a bhrātus tad vacanaṃ śrutvā putro duḥśāsanas tava
c bhīṣmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtvā prayayau senayā saha
a bhīṣmaṃ tu rathavaṃśena dṛṣṭvā tam abhisaṃvṛtam
c arjuno rathināṃ śreṣṭho dhṛṣṭadyumnam uvāca ha
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ naravyāghra bhīṣmasya pramukhe 'nagha
c sthāpayasvādya pāñcālya tasya goptāham apy uta
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo niryayau senayā saha
c vyūhaṃ cāvyūhata mahat sarvatobhadram āhave
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca śaibyaś caiva mahārathaḥ
c śakuniḥ saindhavaś caiva kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
a bhīṣmeṇa sahitāḥ sarve putraiś ca tava bhārata
c agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ vyūhasya pramukhe sthitāḥ
a droṇo bhūriśravāḥ śalyo bhagadattaś ca māriṣa
c dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ
a aśvatthāmā somadatta āvantyau ca mahārathau
c mahatyā senayā yuktā vāmaṃ pakṣam apālayan
a duryodhano mahārāja trigartaiḥ sarvato vṛtaḥ
c vyūhamadhye sthito rājan pāṇḍavān prati bhārata
a alambuso rathaśreṣṭhaḥ śrutāyuś ca mahārathaḥ
c pṛṣṭhataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ sthitau vyūhasya daṃśitau
a evam ete tadā vyūhaṃ kṛtvā bhārata tāvakāḥ
c saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta pratapanta ivāgnayaḥ
a tathā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca mādrīputrāv ubhāv api
e agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ sthitā vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumno virāṭaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c sthitāḥ sainyena mahatā parānīkavināśanāḥ
d anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
d nānāvidhāyudhā vīrā nānāśastropaśobhitāḥ
a śikhaṇḍī vijayaś caiva rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
c cekitāno mahābāhuḥ kuntibhojaś ca vīryavān
e sthitā raṇe mahārāja mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ
a abhimanyur maheṣvāso drupadaś ca mahārathaḥ
b yuyudhāno maheṣvāso yudhāmanyuś ca vīryavān
c kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca sthitā yuddhāya daṃśitāḥ
a evaṃ te 'pi mahāvyūhaṃ prativyūhya sudurjayam
c pāṇḍavāḥ samare śūrāḥ sthitā yuddhāya māriṣa
a tāvakās tu raṇe yattāḥ sahasenā narādhipāḥ
c abhyudyayū raṇe pārthān bhīṣmaṃ kṛtvāgrato nṛpa
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan bhīmasenapurogamāḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ yuddhapariprepsuṃ saṃgrāme vijigīṣavaḥ
a kṣveḍāḥ kilikilāśabdān krakacān goviṣāṇikāḥ
c bherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavān nādayantaś ca puṣkarān
e pāṇḍavā abhyadhāvanta nadanto bhairavān ravān
a bherīmṛdaṅgaśaṅkhānāṃ dundubhīnāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c utkruṣṭasiṃhanādaiś ca valgitaiś ca pṛthagvidhaiḥ
a vayaṃ pratinadantas tān abhyagacchāma satvarāḥ
c sahasaivābhisaṃkruddhās tadāsīt tumulaṃ mahat
a tato 'nyonyaṃ pradhāvantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire
c tataḥ śabdena mahatā pracakampe vasuṃdharā
a pakṣiṇaś ca mahāghoraṃ vyāharanto vibabhramuḥ
c saprabhaś coditaḥ sūryo niṣprabhaḥ samapadyata
a vavuś ca tumulā vātāḥ śaṃsantaḥ sumahad bhayam
c ghorāś ca ghoranirhrādāḥ śivās tatra vavāśire
e vedayantyo mahārāja mahad vaiśasam āgatam
a diśaḥ prajvalitā rājan pāṃsuvarṣaṃ papāta ca
c rudhireṇa samunmiśram asthivarṣaṃ tathaiva ca
a rudatāṃ vāhanānāṃ ca netrebhyaḥ prāpataj jalam
c susruvuś ca śakṛnmūtraṃ pradhyāyanto viśāṃ pate
a antarhitā mahānādāḥ śrūyante bharatarṣabha
c rakṣasāṃ puruṣādānāṃ nadatāṃ bhairavān ravān
a saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante gomāyubakavāyasāḥ
c śvānaś ca vividhair nādair bhaṣantas tatra tasthire
a jvalitāś ca maholkā vai samāhatya divākaram
c nipetuḥ sahasā bhūmau vedayānā mahad bhayam
a mahānty anīkāni mahāsamucchraye
samāgame pāṇḍavadhārtarāṣṭrayoḥ
c prakāśire śaṅkhamṛdaṅganisvanaiḥ
prakampitānīva vanāni vāyunā
a narendranāgāśvasamākulānām
abhyāyatīnām aśive muhūrte
c babhūva ghoṣas tumulaś camūnāṃ
vātoddhutānām iva sāgarāṇām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a abhimanyū rathodāraḥ piśaṅgais turagottamaiḥ
c abhidudrāva tejasvī duryodhanabalaṃ mahat
e vikirañ śaravarṣāṇi vāridhārā ivāmbudaḥ
a na śekuḥ samare kruddhaṃ saubhadram arisūdanam
c śastraughiṇaṃ gāhamānaṃ senāsāgaram akṣayam
e nivārayitum apy ājau tvadīyāḥ kurupuṃgavāḥ
a tena muktā raṇe rājañ śarāḥ śatrunibarhaṇāḥ
c kṣatriyān anayañ śūrān pretarājaniveśanam
a yamadaṇḍopamān ghorāñ jvalanāśīviṣopamān
c saubhadraḥ samare kruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa sāyakān
a rathinaṃ ca rathāt tūrṇaṃ hayapṛṣṭhāc ca sādinam
c gajārohāṃś ca sagajān pātayām āsa phālguniḥ
a tasya tat kurvataḥ karma mahat saṃkhye 'dbhutaṃ nṛpāḥ
c pūjayāṃ cakrire hṛṣṭāḥ praśaśaṃsuś ca phālgunim
a tāny anīkāni saubhadro drāvayan bahv aśobhata
c tūlarāśim ivādhūya mārutaḥ sarvatodiśam
a tena vidrāvyamāṇāni tava sainyāni bhārata
c trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta paṅke magnā iva dvipāḥ
a vidrāvya sarvasainyāni tāvakāni narottamaḥ
c abhimanyuḥ sthito rājan vidhūmo 'gnir iva jvalan
a na cainaṃ tāvakāḥ sarve viṣehur arighātinam
c pradīptaṃ pāvakaṃ yadvat pataṃgāḥ kālacoditāḥ
a praharan sarvaśatrubhyaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c adṛśyata maheṣvāsaḥ savajra iva vajrabhṛt
a hemapṛṣṭhaṃ dhanuś cāsya dadṛśe carato diśaḥ
c toyadeṣu yathā rājan bhrājamānāḥ śatahvadāḥ
a śarāś ca niśitāḥ pītā niścaranti sma saṃyuge
c vanāt phulladrumād rājan bhramarāṇām iva vrajāḥ
a tathaiva caratas tasya saubhadrasya mahātmanaḥ
c rathena meghaghoṣeṇa dadṛśur nāntaraṃ janāḥ
a mohayitvā kṛpaṃ droṇaṃ drauṇiṃ ca sa bṛhadbalam
c saindhavaṃ ca maheṣvāsaṃ vyacaral laghu suṣṭhu ca
a maṇḍalīkṛtam evāsya dhanuḥ paśyāma māriṣa
c sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśaṃ tapatas tava vāhinīm
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ pratapantaṃ śarārcibhiḥ
c dviphalgunam imaṃ lokaṃ menire tasya karmabhiḥ
a tenārditā mahārāja bhāratī sā mahācamūḥ
c babhrāma tatra tatraiva yoṣin madavaśād iva
a drāvayitvā ca tat sainyaṃ kampayitvā mahārathān
c nandayām āsa suhṛdo mayaṃ jitveva vāsavaḥ
a tena vidrāvyamāṇāni tava sainyāni saṃyuge
c cakrur ārtasvaraṃ ghoraṃ parjanyaninadopamam
a taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ tava sainyasya māriṣa
c mārutoddhūtavegasya samudrasyeva parvaṇi
e duryodhanas tadā rājā ārśyaśṛṅgim abhāṣata
a eṣa kārṣṇir maheṣvāso dvitīya iva phalgunaḥ
c camūṃ drāvayate krodhād vṛtro devacamūm iva
a tasya nānyaṃ prapaśyāmi saṃyuge bheṣajaṃ mahat
c ṛte tvāṃ rākṣasaśreṣṭha sarvavidyāsu pāragam
a sa gatvā tvaritaṃ vīraṃ jahi saubhadram āhave
c vayaṃ pārthān haniṣyāmo bhīṣmadroṇapuraḥsarāḥ
a sa evam ukto balavān rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavān
c prayayau samare tūrṇaṃ tava putrasya śāsanāt
e nardamāno mahānādaṃ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ
a tasya śabdena mahatā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
c prācalat sarvato rājan pūryamāṇa ivārṇavaḥ
a bahavaś ca narā rājaṃs tasya nādena bhīṣitāḥ
c priyān prāṇān parityajya nipetur dharaṇītale
a kārṣṇiś cāpi mudā yuktaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥ
c nṛtyann iva rathopasthe tad rakṣaḥ samupādravat
a tataḥ sa rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ saṃprāpyaivārjuniṃ raṇe
c nātidūre sthitas tasya drāvayām āsa vai camūm
a sā vadhyamānā samare pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūḥ
b nādhyagacchata vai trāṇaṃ pīḍyamānā durātmanā
c pratyudyayau raṇe rakṣo devasenā yathā balim
a vimardaḥ sumahān āsīt tasya sainyasya māriṣa
c rakṣasā ghorarūpeṇa vadhyamānasya saṃyuge
a tataḥ śarasahasrais tāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūm
c vyadrāvayad raṇe rakṣo darśayad vai parākramam
a sā vadhyamānā ca tathā pāṇḍavānām anīkinī
c rakṣasā ghorarūpeṇa pradudrāva raṇe bhayāt
a tāṃ pramṛdya tataḥ senāṃ padminīṃ vāraṇo yathā
c tato 'bhidudrāva raṇe draupadeyān mahābalān
a te tu kruddhā maheṣvāsā draupadeyāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c rākṣasaṃ dudruvuḥ sarve grahāḥ pañca yathā ravim
a vīryavadbhis tatas tais tu pīḍito rākṣasottamaḥ
c yathā yugakṣaye ghore candramāḥ pañcabhir grahaiḥ
a prativindhyas tato rakṣo bibheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c sarvapāraśavais tūrṇam akuṇṭhāgrair mahābalaḥ
a sa tair bhinnatanutrāṇaḥ śuśubhe rākṣasottamaḥ
c marīcibhir ivārkasya saṃsyūto jalado mahān
a viṣaktaiḥ sa śaraiś cāpi tapanīyaparicchadaiḥ
c ārśyaśṛṅgir babhau rājan dīptaśṛṅga ivācalaḥ
a tatas te bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasendraṃ mahāhave
c vivyadhur niśitair bāṇais tapanīyavibhūṣitaiḥ
a sa nirbhinnaḥ śarair ghorair bhujagaiḥ kopitair iva
c alambuso bhṛśaṃ rājan nāgendra iva cukrudhe
d nirbhiṇṇas tu śarair ghorair dīpyamānaḥ samantataḥ
d alaṃbuso bhṛśaṃ bhāti ulkābhir iva kuñjaraḥ
a so 'tividdho mahārāja muhūrtam atha māriṣa
c praviveśa tamo dīrghaṃ pīḍitas tair mahārathaiḥ
a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ krodhena dviguṇīkṛtaḥ
c ciccheda sāyakais teṣāṃ dhvajāṃś caiva dhanūṃṣi ca
a ekaikaṃ ca tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna smayann iva
c alambuso rathopasthe nṛtyann iva mahārathaḥ
a tvaramāṇaś ca saṃkruddho hayāṃs teṣāṃ mahātmanām
c jaghāna rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ sārathīṃś ca mahābalaḥ
a bibheda ca susaṃhṛṣṭaḥ punaś cainān susaṃśitaiḥ
c śarair bahuvidhākāraiḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a virathāṃś ca maheṣvāsān kṛtvā tatra sa rākṣasaḥ
c abhidudrāva vegena hantukāmo niśācaraḥ
a tān arditān raṇe tena rākṣasena durātmanā
c dṛṣṭvārjunasutaḥ saṃkhye rākṣasaṃ samupādravat
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ vṛtravāsavayor iva
c dadṛśus tāvakāḥ sarve pāṇḍavāś ca mahārathāḥ
a tau sametau mahāyuddhe krodhadīptau parasparam
b udvṛtya cakṣuṣī rājan krodhāt prasphuritādharau
c mahābalau mahārāja krodhasaṃraktalocanau
e parasparam avekṣetāṃ kālānalasamau yudhi
f āśīviṣāv iva kruddhau netrābhyām itaretaram
a tayoḥ samāgamo ghoro babhūva kaṭukodayaḥ
c yathā devāsure yuddhe śakraśambarayor iva
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ārjuniṃ samare śūraṃ vinighnantaṃ mahāratham
c alambusaḥ kathaṃ yuddhe pratyayudhyata saṃjaya
a ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ kathaṃ cāpi saubhadraḥ paravīrahā
c tan mamācakṣva tattvena yathā vṛttaṃ sma saṃyuge
a dhanaṃjayaś ca kiṃ cakre mama sainyeṣu saṃjaya
c bhīmo vā balināṃ śreṣṭho rākṣaso vā ghaṭotkacaḥ
a nakulaḥ sahadevo vā sātyakir vā mahārathaḥ
c etad ācakṣva me sarvaṃ kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hanta te 'haṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃgrāmaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c yathābhūd rākṣasendrasya saubhadrasya ca māriṣa
a arjunaś ca yathā saṃkhye bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca raṇe cakruḥ parākramam
a tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve bhīṣmadroṇapurogamāḥ
c adbhutāni vicitrāṇi cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavat
a alambusas tu samare abhimanyuṃ mahāratham
c vinadya sumahānādaṃ tarjayitvā muhur muhuḥ
e abhidudrāva vegena tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a saubhadro 'pi raṇe rājan siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥ
c ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ pitur atyantavairiṇam
a tataḥ sameyatuḥ saṃkhye tvaritau nararākṣasau
c rathābhyāṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhau yathā vai devadānavau
e māyāvī rākṣasaśreṣṭho divyāstrajñaś ca phālguniḥ
a tataḥ kārṣṇir mahārāja niśitaiḥ sāyakais tribhiḥ
c ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ raṇe viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
a alambuso 'pi saṃkruddhaḥ kārṣṇiṃ navabhir āśugaiḥ
c hṛdi vivyādha vegena tottrair iva mahādvipam
a tataḥ śarasahasreṇa kṣiprakārī niśācaraḥ
c arjunasya sutaṃ saṃkhye pīḍayām āsa bhārata
a abhimanyus tataḥ kruddho navatiṃ nataparvaṇām
c cikṣepa niśitān bāṇān rākṣasasya mahorasi
a te tasya viviśus tūrṇaṃ kāyaṃ nirbhidya marmaṇi
c sa tair vibhinnasarvāṅgaḥ śuśubhe rākṣasottamaḥ
e puṣpitaiḥ kiṃśukai rājan saṃstīrṇa iva parvataḥ
a sa dhārayañ śarān hemapuṅkhān api mahābalaḥ
c vibabhau rākṣasaśreṣṭhaḥ sajvāla iva parvataḥ
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja ārśyaśṛṅgir mahābalaḥ
c mahendrapratimaṃ kārṣṇiṃ chādayām āsa patribhiḥ
a tena te viśikhā muktā yamadaṇḍopamāḥ śitāḥ
c abhimanyuṃ vinirbhidya prāviśan dharaṇītalam
a tathaivārjuninirmuktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
c alambusaṃ vinirbhidya prāviśanta dharātalam
a saubhadras tu raṇe rakṣaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c cakre vimukham āsādya mayaṃ śakra ivāhave
a vimukhaṃ ca tato rakṣo vadhyamānaṃ raṇe 'riṇā
c prāduścakre mahāmāyāṃ tāmasīṃ paratāpanaḥ
a tatas te tamasā sarve hṛtā hy āsan mahītale
c nābhimanyum apaśyanta naiva svān na parān raṇe
a abhimanyuś ca tad dṛṣṭvā ghorarūpaṃ mahat tamaḥ
c prāduścakre 'stram atyugraṃ bhāskaraṃ kurunandanaḥ
a tataḥ prakāśam abhavaj jagat sarvaṃ mahīpate
c tāṃ cāpi jaghnivān māyāṃ rākṣasasya durātmanaḥ
a saṃkruddhaś ca mahāvīryo rākṣasendraṃ narottamaḥ
c chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a bahvīs tathānyā māyāś ca prayuktās tena rakṣasā
c sarvāstravid ameyātmā vārayām āsa phālguniḥ
a hatamāyaṃ tato rakṣo vadhyamānaṃ ca sāyakaiḥ
c rathaṃ tatraiva saṃtyajya prādravan mahato bhayāt
a tasmin vinirjite tūrṇaṃ kūṭayodhini rākṣase
b saubhadraś ca mahābāhuḥ samare ca jitaśramaḥ
b parākramī mahātejāḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥ
c ārjuniḥ samare sainyaṃ tāvakaṃ saṃmamarda ha
e madāndho vanyanāgendraḥ sapadmāṃ padminīm iva
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvābhividrutam
c mahatā rathavaṃśena saubhadraṃ paryavārayat
a koṣṭhakīkṛtya taṃ vīraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā mahārathāḥ
c ekaṃ subahavo yuddhe tatakṣuḥ sāyakair dṛḍham
a sa teṣāṃ rathināṃ vīraḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥ
c sadṛśo vāsudevasya vikrameṇa balena ca
a ubhayoḥ sadṛśaṃ karma sa pitur mātulasya ca
c raṇe bahuvidhaṃ cakre sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a tato dhanaṃjayo rājan vinighnaṃs tava sainikān
c āsasāda raṇe bhīṣmaṃ putraprepsur amarṣaṇaḥ
a tathaiva samare rājan pitā devavratas tava
c āsasāda raṇe pārthaṃ svarbhānur iva bhāskaram
a tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ putrās tava viśāṃ pate
c parivavrū raṇe bhīṣmaṃ jugupuś ca samantataḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan parivārya dhanaṃjayam
c raṇāya mahate yuktā daṃśitā bharatarṣabha
a śāradvatas tato rājan bhīṣmasya pramukhe sthitam
c arjunaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānāṃ samācinot
a patyudgamyātha vivyādha sātyakis taṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c pāṇḍavapriyakāmārthaṃ śārdūla iva kuñjaram
a gautamo 'pi tvarāyukto mādhavaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c hṛdi vivyādha saṃkruddhaḥ kaṅkapatraparicchadaiḥ
a śaineyo 'pi tataḥ kruddho bhṛśaṃ viddho mahārathaḥ
c gautamāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ samādatta śilīmukham
a tam āpatantaṃ vegena śakrāśanisamadyutim
c dvidhā ciccheda saṃkruddho drauṇiḥ paramakopanaḥ
a samutsṛjyātha śaineyo gautamaṃ rathināṃ varam
c abhyadravad raṇe drauṇiṃ rāhuḥ khe śaśinaṃ yathā
a tasya droṇasutaś cāpaṃ dvidhā ciccheda bhārata
c athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ tāḍayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya śatrughnaṃ bhārasādhanam
c drauṇiṃ ṣaṣṭyā mahārāja bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a sa viddho vyathitaś caiva muhūrtaṃ kaśmalāyutaḥ
c niṣasāda rathopasthe dhvajayaṣṭim upāśritaḥ
a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān
c vārṣṇeyaṃ samare kruddho nārācena samardayat
a śaineyaṃ sa tu nirbhidya prāviśad dharaṇītalam
c vasantakāle balavān bilaṃ sarpaśiśur yathā
a tato 'pareṇa bhallena mādhavasya dhvajottamam
c ciccheda samare drauṇiḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca
a punaś cainaṃ śarair ghoraiś chādayām āsa bhārata
c nidāghānte mahārāja yathā megho divākaram
a sātyakiś ca mahārāja śarajālaṃ nihatya tat
c drauṇim abhyapatat tūrṇaṃ śarajālair anekadhā
a tāpayām āsa ca drauṇiṃ śaineyaḥ paravīrahā
c vimukto meghajālena yathaiva tapanas tathā
a śarāṇāṃ ca sahasreṇa punar enaṃ samudyatam
c sātyakiś chādayām āsa nanāda ca mahābalaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā putraṃ tathā grastaṃ rāhuṇeva niśākaram
c abhyadravata śaineyaṃ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
a vivyādha ca pṛṣatkena sutīkṣṇena mahāmṛdhe
c parīpsan svasutaṃ rājan vārṣṇeyenābhitāpitam
a sātyakis tu raṇe jitvā guruputraṃ mahāratham
c droṇaṃ vivyādha viṃśatyā sarvapāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tadantaram ameyātmā kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
c abhyadravad raṇe kruddho droṇaṃ prati mahārathaḥ
a tato droṇaś ca pārthaś ca sameyātāṃ mahāmṛdhe
c yathā budhaś ca śukraś ca mahārāja nabhastale
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
c samīyatū raṇe śūrau tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a priyo hi pāṇḍavo nityaṃ bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ
c ācāryaś ca raṇe nityaṃ priyaḥ pārthasya saṃjaya
a tāv ubhau rathinau saṃkhye dṛptau siṃhāv ivotkaṭau
c kathaṃ samīyatur yuddhe bhāradvājadhanaṃjayau
 saṃjaya uvāca
a na droṇaḥ samare pārthaṃ jānīte priyam ātmanaḥ
c kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya pārtho vā gurum āhave
d tathaiva pāṇḍavo droṇaṃ vetty eva priyam ātmanaḥ
d kṣatradharmarato nityaṃ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyate
a na kṣatriyā raṇe rājan varjayanti parasparam
c nirmaryādaṃ hi yudhyante pitṛbhir bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
a raṇe bhārata pārthena droṇo viddhas tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c nācintayata tān bāṇān pārthacāpacyutān yudhi
a śaravṛṣṭyā punaḥ pārthaś chādayām āsa taṃ raṇe
c prajajvāla ca roṣeṇa gahane 'gnir ivotthitaḥ
a tato 'rjunaṃ raṇe droṇaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c vārayām āsa rājendra nacirād iva bhārata
a tato duryodhano rājā suśarmāṇam acodayat
c droṇasya samare rājan pārṣṇigrahaṇakāraṇāt
a trigartarāḍ api kruddho bhṛśam āyamya kārmukam
c chādayām āsa samare pārthaṃ bāṇair ayomukhaiḥ
a tābhyāṃ muktāḥ śarā rājann antarikṣe virejire
c haṃsā iva mahārāja śaratkāle nabhastale
a te śarāḥ prāpya kaunteyaṃ samastā viviśuḥ prabho
c phalabhāranataṃ yadvat svāduvṛkṣaṃ vihaṃgamāḥ
a arjunas tu raṇe nādaṃ vinadya rathināṃ varaḥ
c trigartarājaṃ samare saputraṃ vivyadhe śaraiḥ
a te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kāleneva yugakṣaye
c pārtham evābhyavartanta maraṇe kṛtaniścayāḥ
e mumucuḥ śaravṛṣṭiṃ ca pāṇḍavasya rathaṃ prati
a śaravṛṣṭiṃ tatas tāṃ tu śaravarṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ
c pratijagrāha rājendra toyavṛṣṭim ivācalaḥ
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bībhatsor hastalāghavam
c vimuktāṃ bahubhiḥ śūraiḥ śastravṛṣṭiṃ durāsadām
a yad eko vārayām āsa māruto 'bhragaṇān iva
c karmaṇā tena pārthasya tutuṣur devadānavāḥ
a atha kruddho raṇe pārthas trigartān prati bhārata
c mumocāstraṃ mahārāja vāyavyaṃ pṛtanāmukhe
a prādurāsīt tato vāyuḥ kṣobhayāṇo nabhastalam
c pātayan vai tarugaṇān vinighnaṃś caiva sainikān
a tato droṇo 'bhivīkṣyaiva vāyavyāstraṃ sudāruṇam
c śailam anyan mahārāja ghoram astraṃ mumoca ha
a droṇena yudhi nirmukte tasminn astre mahāmṛdhe
c praśaśāma tato vāyuḥ prasannāś cābhavan diśaḥ
a tataḥ pāṇḍusuto vīras trigartasya rathavrajān
c nirutsāhān raṇe cakre vimukhān viparākramān
a tato duryodhano rājā kṛpaś ca rathināṃ varaḥ
c aśvatthāmā tataḥ śalyaḥ kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau bāhlikaś ca sabāhlikaḥ
c mahatā rathavaṃśena pārthasyāvārayan diśaḥ
a tathaiva bhagadattaś ca śrutāyuś ca mahābalaḥ
c gajānīkena bhīmasya tāv avārayatāṃ diśaḥ
a bhūriśravāḥ śalaś caiva saubalaś ca viśāṃ pate
c śaraughair vividhais tūrṇaṃ mādrīputrāv avārayan
a bhīṣmas tu sahitaḥ sarvair dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikaiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samāsādya sarvataḥ paryavārayat
a āpatantaṃ gajānīkaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārtho vṛkodaraḥ
c lelihan sṛkkiṇī vīro mṛgarāḍ iva kānane
a tatas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭho gadāṃ gṛhya mahāhave
c avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ tava sainyam abhīṣayat
d   giryagrād iva kesarī
d tasthau sa sagado bhīmaḥ saśṛṅga iva parvataḥ
d siṃho dṛṣṭvā mṛgaṃ yadvat
a tam udvīkṣya gadāhastaṃ tatas te gajasādinaḥ
c parivavrū raṇe yattā bhīmasenaṃ samantataḥ
a gajamadhyam anuprāptaḥ pāṇḍavaś ca vyarājata
c meghajālasya mahato yathā madhyagato raviḥ
a vyadhamat sa gajānīkaṃ gadayā pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
c mahābhrajālam atulaṃ mātariśveva saṃtatam
a te vadhyamānā balinā bhīmasenena dantinaḥ
c ārtanādaṃ raṇe cakrur garjanto jaladā iva
a bahudhā dāritaś caiva viṣāṇais tatra dantibhiḥ
c phullāśokanibhaḥ pārthaḥ śuśubhe raṇamūrdhani
d sādināṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ ca vyadhamad gadayā tataḥ
d vāyuvegasamāyukto vyacarat pāṇḍavo yudhi
d viṣāṇollikhitair gātrair viṣāṇābhihato bhṛśam
a viṣāṇe dantinaṃ gṛhya nirviṣāṇam athākarot
c viṣāṇena ca tenaiva kumbhe 'bhyāhatya dantinam
e pātayām āsa samare daṇḍahasta ivāntakaḥ
a śoṇitāktāṃ gadāṃ bibhran medomajjākṛtacchaviḥ
c kṛtāṅgadaḥ śoṇitena rudravat pratyadṛśyata
a evaṃ te vadhyamānās tu hataśeṣā mahāgajāḥ
c prādravanta diśo rājan vimṛdnantaḥ svakaṃ balam
a dravadbhis tair mahānāgaiḥ samantād bharatarṣabha
c duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukham
 saṃjaya uvāca
a madhyāhne tu mahārāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata
c lokakṣayakaro raudro bhīṣmasya saha somakaiḥ
a gāṅgeyo rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c vyadhaman niśitair bāṇaiḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a saṃmamarda ca tat sainyaṃ pitā devavratas tava
c dhānyānām iva lūnānāṃ prakaraṃ gogaṇā iva
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca virāṭo drupadas tathā
c bhīṣmam āsādya samare śarair jaghnur mahāratham
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato viddhvā virāṭaṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c drupadasya ca nārācaṃ preṣayām āsa bhārata
a tena viddhā maheṣvāsā bhīṣmeṇāmitrakarśinā
c cukrudhuḥ samare rājan pādaspṛṣṭā ivoragāḥ
a śikhaṇḍī taṃ ca vivyādha bharatānāṃ pitāmaham
c strīmayaṃ manasā dhyātvā nāsmai prāharad acyutaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare krodhād agnir iva jvalan
c pitāmahaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a drupadaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā virāṭo daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c śikhaṇḍī pañcaviṃśatyā bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
a so 'tividdho mahārāja bhīṣmaḥ saṃkhye mahātmabhiḥ
c vasante puṣpaśabalo raktāśoka ivābabhau
a tān pratyavidhyad gāṅgeyas tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥ
c drupadasya ca bhallena dhanuś ciccheda māriṣa
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
c sārathiṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiḥ suśitai raṇamūrdhani
a tato bhīmo mahārāja draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥ
c kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca sātyakiś caiva sātvataḥ
a abhyadravanta gāṅgeyaṃ yudhiṣṭhirahitepsayā
c rirakṣiṣantaḥ pāñcālyaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhan raṇe
a tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve bhīṣmarakṣārtham udyatāḥ
c pratyudyayuḥ pāṇḍusenāṃ sahasainyā narādhipa
a tatrāsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkulam
c narāśvarathanāgānāṃ yamarāṣṭravivardhanam
a rathī rathinam āsādya prāhiṇod yamasādanam
c tathetarān samāsādya naranāgāśvasādinaḥ
a anayan paralokāya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c astraiś ca vividhair ghorais tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
a rathāś ca rathibhir hīnā hatasārathayas tathā
c vipradrutāśvāḥ samare diśo jagmuḥ samantataḥ
a mardamānā narān rājan hayāṃś ca subahūn raṇe
c vātāyamānā dṛśyante gandharvanagaropamāḥ
a rathinaś ca rathair hīnā varmiṇas tejasā yutāḥ
c kuṇḍaloṣṇīṣiṇaḥ sarve niṣkāṅgadavibhūṣitāḥ
a devaputrasamā rūpe śaurye śakrasamā yudhi
c ṛddhyā vaiśravaṇaṃ cāti nayena ca bṛhaspatim
a sarvalokeśvarāḥ śūrās tatra tatra viśāṃ pate
c vipradrutā vyadṛśyanta prākṛtā iva mānavāḥ
a dantinaś ca naraśreṣṭha vihīnā varasādibhiḥ
c mṛdnantaḥ svāny anīkāni saṃpetuḥ sarvaśabdagāḥ
a varmabhiś cāmaraiś chatraiḥ patākābhiś ca māriṣa
c kakṣyābhir atha tottraiś ca ghaṇṭābhis tomarais tathā
a viśīrṇair vipradhāvanto dṛśyante sma diśo daśa
c nagameghapratīkāśair jaladodayanisvanaiḥ
a tathaiva dantibhir hīnān gajārohān viśāṃ pate
c pradhāvanto 'nvapaśyāma tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkule
a nānādeśasamutthāṃś ca turagān hemabhūṣitān
c vātāyamānān adrākṣaṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a aśvārohān hatair aśvair gṛhītāsīn samantataḥ
c dravamāṇān apaśyāma drāvyamāṇāṃś ca saṃyuge
d tato 'ntare mahārāja bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
d cakāra sumahad yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ bhayānakam
a gajo gajaṃ samāsādya dravamāṇaṃ mahāraṇe
c yayau vimṛdnaṃs tarasā padātīn vājinas tathā
d aśvān aśvaiś ca saṃmardya rathaiś ca rathinas tathā
a tathaiva ca rathān rājan saṃmamarda raṇe gajaḥ
c rathaś caiva samāsādya padātiṃ turagaṃ tathā
a vyamṛdnāt samare rājaṃs turagāṃś ca narān raṇe
c evaṃ te bahudhā rājan pramṛdnantaḥ parasparam
d dṛśyante sma mahābāho tatra tatra mahābalāḥ
a tasmin raudre tathā yuddhe vartamāne mahābhaye
c prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitāntrataraṅgiṇī
a asthisaṃcayasaṃghāṭā keśaśaivalaśādvalā
c rathahradā śarāvartā hayamīnā durāsadā
a śīrṣopalasamākīrṇā hastigrāhasamākulā
c kavacoṣṇīṣaphenāḍhyā dhanurdvīpāsikacchapā
d śaṅkhacakraughasaṃpūrṇā chatrakūrmā rathoḍupā
a patākādhvajavṛkṣāḍhyā martyakūlāpahāriṇī
c kravyādasaṃghasaṃkīrṇā yamarāṣṭravivardhinī
a tāṃ nadīṃ kṣatriyāḥ śūrā hayanāgarathaplavaiḥ
c praterur bahavo rājan bhayaṃ tyaktvā mahāhave
a apovāha raṇe bhīrūn kaśmalenābhisaṃvṛtān
c yathā vaitaraṇī pretān pretarājapuraṃ prati
a prākrośan kṣatriyās tatra dṛṣṭvā tad vaiśasaṃ mahat
c duryodhanāparādhena kṣayaṃ gacchanti kauravāḥ
a guṇavatsu kathaṃ dveṣaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
c kṛtavān pāṇḍuputreṣu pāpātmā lobhamohitaḥ
a evaṃ bahuvidhā vācaḥ śrūyante smātra bhārata
c pāṇḍavastavasaṃyuktāḥ putrāṇāṃ te sudāruṇāḥ
a tā niśamya tadā vācaḥ sarvayodhair udāhṛtāḥ
c āgaskṛt sarvalokasya putro duryodhanas tava
a bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ caiva śalyaṃ covāca bhārata
c yudhyadhvam anahaṃkārāḥ kiṃ ciraṃ kurutheti ca
d iti duryodhanotsṛṣṭāḥ sarve yuyudhire nṛpāḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c akṣadyūtakṛtaṃ rājan sughoraṃ vaiśasaṃ tadā
a yat purā na nigṛhṇīṣe vāryamāṇo mahātmabhiḥ
c vaicitravīrya tasyedaṃ phalaṃ paśya tathāvidham
a na hi pāṇḍusutā rājan sasainyāḥ sapadānugāḥ
b ayudhyanta mahāraṅge madhyaṃ prāpte divākare
b sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
b nākampayata śaineyo satyavān satyakovidaḥ
c rakṣanti samare prāṇān kauravā vā viśāṃ pate
a etasmāt kāraṇād ghoro vartate sma janakṣayaḥ
c daivād vā puruṣavyāghra tava cāpanayān nṛpa
 saṃjaya uvāca
a arjunas tu naravyāghra suśarmapramukhān nṛpān
c anayat pretarājasya bhavanaṃ sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ
a suśarmāpi tato bāṇaiḥ pārthaṃ vivyādha saṃyuge
c vāsudevaṃ ca saptatyā pārthaṃ ca navabhiḥ punaḥ
a tān nivārya śaraugheṇa śakrasūnur mahārathaḥ
c suśarmaṇo raṇe yodhān prāhiṇod yamasādanam
a te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kāleneva yugakṣaye
c vyadravanta raṇe rājan bhaye jāte mahārathāḥ
a utsṛjya turagān ke cid rathān ke cic ca māriṣa
c gajān anye samutsṛjya prādravanta diśo daśa
a apare tudyamānās tu vājināgarathā raṇāt
c tvarayā parayā yuktāḥ prādravanta viśāṃ pate
d kaśābhis tāḍayām āsuḥ pārṣṇibhiś ca mahur muhuḥ
d hayārohā dravanty eva codayanto hayottamān
d tathā tottranipātaiś ca aṅkuśānāṃ ca vibhramaiḥ
d gajārohā gajāṃs tūrṇaṃ tvarayantaḥ pradudruvuḥ
d rathinaś ca pratodaiś ca vāgbhiś caiva punaḥ punaḥ
d bhartsayanto hayān rājan prādravanti diśo daśa
a pādātāś cāpi śastrāṇi samutsṛjya mahāraṇe
c nirapekṣā vyadhāvanta tena tena sma bhārata
a vāryamāṇāḥ sma bahuśas traigartena suśarmaṇā
c tathānyaiḥ pārthivaśreṣṭhair na vyatiṣṭhanta saṃyuge
d putrāṃś ca patitān bhūmau mātulāṃś ca pitṝṃs tathā
d sodarāṃś cāvamardantaḥ pradrutās tatra tatra vai
a tad balaṃ pradrutaṃ dṛṣṭvā putro duryodhanas tava
c puraskṛtya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ sarvasainyapuraskṛtam
a sarvodyogena mahatā dhanaṃjayam upādravat
c trigartādhipater arthe jīvitasya viśāṃ pate
a sa ekaḥ samare tasthau kiran bahuvidhāñ śarān
c bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ śeṣā vipradrutā narāḥ
a tathaiva paṇḍavā rājan sarvodyogena daṃśitāḥ
c prayayuḥ phalgunārthāya yatra bhīṣmo vyavasthitaḥ
a jānanto 'pi raṇe śauryaṃ ghoraṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c hāhākārakṛtotsāhā bhīṣmaṃ jagmuḥ samantataḥ
a tatas tāladhvajaḥ śūraḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a ekībhūtās tataḥ sarve kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c ayudhyanta mahārāja madhyaṃ prāpte divākare
a sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
c atiṣṭhad āhave śūraḥ kiran bāṇān sahasraśaḥ
a tathaiva drupado rājā droṇaṃ viddhvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c punar vivyādha saptatyā sārathiṃ cāsya saptabhiḥ
a bhīmasenas tu rājānaṃ bāhlikaṃ prapitāmaham
c viddhvānadan mahānādaṃ śārdūla iva kānane
a ārjuniś citrasenena viddho bahubhir āśugaiḥ
c citrasenaṃ tribhir bāṇair vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśam
a samāgatau tau tu raṇe mahāmātrau vyarocatām
c yathā divi mahāghorau rājan budhaśanaiścarau
a tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sūtaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c nanāda balavan nādaṃ saubhadraḥ paravīrahā
a hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ durmukhasya viśāṃ pate
a droṇaś ca drupadaṃ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c sārathiṃ cāsya vivyādha tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
a pīḍyamānas tato rājā drupado vāhinīmukhe
c apāyāj javanair aśvaiḥ pūrvavairam anusmaran
a bhīmasenas tu rājānaṃ muhūrtād iva bāhlikam
c vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a sasaṃbhramo mahārāja saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ
c avaplutya tato vāhād bāhlikaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
e āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ lakṣmaṇasya mahārathaḥ
a sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ vārayitvā mahārathaḥ
c śarair bahuvidhai rājann āsasāda pitāmaham
a sa viddhvā bhārataṃ ṣaṣṭyā niśitair lomavāhibhiḥ
c nanarteva rathopasthe vidhunvāno mahad dhanuḥ
a tasyāyasīṃ mahāśaktiṃ cikṣepātha pitāmahaḥ
c hemacitrāṃ mahāvegāṃ nāgakanyopamāṃ śubhām
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā mṛtyukalpāṃ sutejanām
c dhvaṃsayām āsa vārṣṇeyo lāghavena mahāyaśāḥ
a anāsādya tu vārṣṇeyaṃ śaktiḥ paramadāruṇā
c nyapatad dharaṇīpṛṣṭhe maholkeva gataprabhā
a vārṣṇeyas tu tato rājan svāṃ śaktiṃ ghoradarśanām
c vegavad gṛhya cikṣepa pitāmaharathaṃ prati
a vārṣṇeyabhujavegena praṇunnā sā mahāhave
c abhidudrāva vegena kālarātrir yathā naram
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā dvidhā ciccheda bhārata
c kṣuraprābhyāṃ sutīkṣṇābhyāṃ sānvakīryata bhūtale
a chittvā tu śaktiṃ gāṅgeyaḥ sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghānorasi kruddhaḥ prahasañ śatrukarśanaḥ
a tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvaja
c parivavrū raṇe bhīṣmaṃ mādhavatrāṇakāraṇāt
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca samare vijayaiṣiṇām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ pāṇḍavair abhisaṃvṛtam
c yathā meghair mahārāja tapānte divi bhāskaram
a duryodhano mahārāja duḥśāsanam abhāṣata
c eṣa śūro maheṣvāso bhīṣmaḥ śatruniṣūdanaḥ
a chāditaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samantād bharatarṣabha
c tasya kāryaṃ tvayā vīra rakṣaṇaṃ sumahātmanaḥ
a rakṣyamāṇo hi samare bhīṣmo 'smākaṃ pitāmahaḥ
c nihanyāt samare yattān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
a tatra kāryam ahaṃ manye bhīṣmasyaivābhirakṣaṇam
c goptā hy eṣa maheṣvāso bhīṣmo 'smākaṃ pitāmahaḥ
a sa bhavān sarvasainyena parivārya pitāmaham
c samare duṣkaraṃ karma kurvāṇaṃ parirakṣatu
a evam uktas tu samare putro duḥśāsanas tava
c parivārya sthito bhīṣmaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
a tataḥ śatasahasreṇa hayānāṃ subalātmajaḥ
c vimalaprāsahastānām ṛṣṭitomaradhāriṇām
a darpitānāṃ suvegānāṃ balasthānāṃ patākinām
c śikṣitair yuddhakuśalair upetānāṃ narottamaiḥ
d nānāśastrasamākīrṇo yuddhāyaivābhidaṃśitaḥ
a nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca dharmarājaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
c nyavārayan naraśreṣṭhaṃ parivārya samantataḥ
a tato duryodhano rājā śūrāṇāṃ hayasādinām
c ayutaṃ preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavānāṃ nivāraṇe
a taiḥ praviṣṭair mahāvegair garutmadbhir ivāhave
c khurāhatā dharā rājaṃś cakampe ca nanāda ca
a khuraśabdaś ca sumahān vājināṃ śuśruve tadā
c mahāvaṃśavanasyeva dahyamānasya parvate
a utpatadbhiś ca tais tatra samuddhūtaṃ mahad rajaḥ
c divākarapathaṃ prāpya chādayām āsa bhāskaram
a vegavadbhir hayais tais tu kṣobhitaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ balam
c nipatadbhir mahāvegair haṃsair iva mahat saraḥ
e heṣatāṃ caiva śabdena na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
f antardadhe mahāñ śabdas tena śabdena mohitaḥ
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c pratyaghnaṃs tarasā vegaṃ samare hayasādinām
a udvṛttasya mahārāja prāvṛṭkālena pūryataḥ
c paurṇamāsyām ambuvegaṃ yathā velā mahodadheḥ
a tatas te rathino rājañ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c nyakṛntann uttamāṅgāni kāyebhyo hayasādinām
a te nipetur mahārāja nihatā dṛḍhadhanvibhiḥ
c nāgair iva mahānāgā yathā syur girigahvare
a te 'pi prāsaiḥ suniśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c nyakṛntann uttamāṅgāni vicaranto diśo daśa
a atyāsannā hayārohā ṛṣṭibhir bharatarṣabha
c acchinann uttamāṅgāni phalānīva mahādrumāt
a sasādino hayā rājaṃs tatra tatra niṣūditāḥ
c patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a vadhyamānā hayās te tu prādravanta bhayārditāḥ
c yathā siṃhān samāsādya mṛgāḥ prāṇaparāyaṇāḥ
d evaṃ tu saubalaṃ sainyaṃ prabhagnaṃ sarvatodiśam
a pāṇḍavās tu mahārāja jitvā śatrūn mahāhave
c dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca bherīś ca tāḍayām āsur āhave
a tato duryodhano dṛṣṭvā dīnaṃ sainyam avasthitam
c abravīd bharataśreṣṭha madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥ
d uvāca madrādhipatiṃ rājā duryodhanas tadā
a eṣa pāṇḍusuto jyeṣṭho jitvā mātula māmakān
c paśyatāṃ no mahābāho senāṃ drāvayate balī
a taṃ vāraya mahābāho veleva makarālayam
c tvaṃ hi saṃśrūyase 'tyartham asahyabalavikramaḥ
a putrasya tava tad vākyaṃ śrutvā śalyaḥ pratāpavān
c prayayau rathavaṃśena yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tad āpatad vai sahasā śalyasya sumahad balam
c mahaughavegaṃ samare vārayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
a madrarājaṃ ca samare dharmarājo mahārathaḥ
c daśabhiḥ sāyakais tūrṇam ājaghāna stanāntare
e nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥ
a madrarājo 'pi tān sarvān ājaghāna tribhis tribhiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ punaḥ ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e mādrīputrau ca saṃrabdhau dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām atāḍayat
a tato bhīmo mahābāhur dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhave
c madrarājavaśaṃ prāptaṃ mṛtyor āsyagataṃ yathā
e abhyadravata saṃgrāme yudhiṣṭhiram amitrajit
f āpatann eva bhīmas tu madrarājam atāḍayat
f sarvapāraśavais tīkṣṇair nārācair marmabhedibhiḥ
f tato bhīṣmaś ca droṇaś ca sainyena mahatā vṛtau
f rājānam abhyapadyetām añjasā śaravarṣiṇau
f dhṛṣṭadyumnas tribhir viddhvā rājānam abhyapadyata
a tato yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ prāvartata sudāruṇam
c aparāṃ diśam āsthāya dyotamāne divākare
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ pitā tava kruddho niśitaiḥ sāyakottamaiḥ
c ājaghāna raṇe pārthān sahasenān samantataḥ
a bhīmaṃ dvādaśabhir viddhvā sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c nakulaṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiḥ sahadevaṃ ca saptabhiḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dvādaśabhir bāhvor urasi cārpayat
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato viddhvā vinanāda mahābalaḥ
a taṃ dvādaśārdhair nakulo mādhavaś ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
b sahadevaś ca saptatyā pārthaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca saptatyā bhīmasenaś ca pañcabhiḥ
e yudhiṣṭhiro dvādaśabhiḥ pratyavidhyat pitāmaham
a droṇas tu sātyakiṃ viddhvā bhīmasenam avidhyata
a   niśitair navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a nakulaṃ ca tribhir viddhvā
c ekaikaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair yamadaṇḍopamaiḥ śitaiḥ
a tau ca taṃ pratyavidhyetāṃ tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥ
c tottrair iva mahānāgaṃ droṇaṃ brāhmaṇapuṃgavam
a sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcyodīcyamālavāḥ
c abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayo 'tha vasātayaḥ
e saṃgrāme nājahur bhīṣmaṃ vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tathaivānye vadhyamānāḥ pāṇḍaveyair mahātmabhiḥ
c pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
e tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan parivavruḥ pitāmaham
a sa samantāt parivṛto rathaughair aparājitaḥ
c gahane 'gnir ivotsṛṣṭaḥ prajajvāla dahan parān
a rathāgnyagāraś cāpārcir asiśaktigadendhanaḥ
c śarasphuliṅgo bhīṣmāgnir dadāha kṣatriyarṣabhān
d yathā hi sumahān agniḥ kakṣe carati sānilaḥ
d tathā bhīṣmo mahārāja divyam astram udīrayan
a suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhir gārdhrapakṣaiḥ sutejanaiḥ
c karṇinālīkanārācaiś chādayām āsa tad balam
a apātayad dhvajāṃś caiva rathinaś ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c muṇḍatālavanānīva cakāra sa rathavrajān
a nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan gajān aśvāṃś ca saṃyuge
c akarot sa mahābāhuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
c niśamya sarvabhūtāni samakampanta bhārata
a amoghā hy apatan bāṇāḥ pitus te bharatarṣabha
c nāsajjanta tanutreṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥ
a hatavīrān rathān rājan saṃyuktāñ javanair hayaiḥ
c apaśyāma mahārāja hriyamāṇān raṇājire
d matsyapāñcālakaikeyān pātayām āsa saṃyuge
a cedikāśikarūṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
c mahārathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥ
e aparāvartinaḥ sarve suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥ
a saṃgrāme bhīṣmam āsādya vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
c nimagnāḥ paralokāya savājirathakuñjarāḥ
a bhagnākṣopaskarān kāṃś cid bhagnacakrāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
c apaśyāma rathān rājañ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a savarūthai rathair bhagnai rathibhiś ca nipātitaiḥ
c śaraiḥ sukavacaiś chinnaiḥ paṭṭiśaiś ca viśāṃ pate
a gadābhir musalaiś caiva nistriṃśaiś ca śilīmukhaiḥ
c anukarṣair upāsaṅgaiś cakrair bhagnaiś ca māriṣa
a bāhubhiḥ kārmukaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
c talatrair aṅgulitraiś ca dhvajaiś ca vinipātitaiḥ
e cāpaiś ca bahudhā chinnaiḥ samāstīryata medinī
a hatārohā gajā rājan hayāś ca hatasādinaḥ
c paripetur drutaṃ tatra śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a yatamānāś ca te vīrā dravamāṇān mahārathān
c nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ bhīṣmabāṇaprapīḍitān
a mahendrasamavīryeṇa vadhyamānā mahācamūḥ
c abhajyata mahārāja na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥ
a āviddharathanāgāśvaṃ patitadhvajakūbaram
c anīkaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ hāhābhūtam acetanam
a jaghānātra pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ tathā
c priyaṃ sakhāyaṃ cākrande sakhā daivabalātkṛtaḥ
a vimucya kavacān anye pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥ
c prakīrya keśān dhāvantaḥ pratyadṛśyanta bhārata
a tad gokulam ivodbhrāntam udbhrāntarathakuñjaram
c dadṛśe pāṇḍuputrasya sainyam ārtasvaraṃ tadā
a prabhajyamānaṃ sainyaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā yādavanandanaḥ
c uvāca pārthaṃ bībhatsuṃ nigṛhya ratham uttamam
a ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pārtha yaḥ kāṅkṣitas tava
c praharāsmai naravyāghra na cen mohāt pramuhyase
a yat purā kathitaṃ vīra tvayā rājñāṃ samāgame
c virāṭanagare pārtha saṃjayasya samīpataḥ
a bhīṣmadroṇamukhān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikān
c sānubandhān haniṣyāmi ye māṃ yotsyanti saṃyuge
a iti tat kuru kaunteya satyaṃ vākyam ariṃdama
c kṣatradharmam anusmṛtya yudhyasva bharatarṣabha
a ity ukto vāsudevena tiryagdṛṣṭir adhomukhaḥ
c akāma iva bībhatsur idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a avadhyānāṃ vadhaṃ kṛtvā rājyaṃ vā narakottaram
c duḥkhāni vanavāse vā kiṃ nu me sukṛtaṃ bhavet
a codayāśvān yato bhīṣmaḥ kariṣye vacanaṃ tava
c pātayiṣyāmi durdharṣaṃ vṛddhaṃ kurupitāmaham
a tato 'śvān rajataprakhyāṃś codayām āsa mādhavaḥ
c yato bhīṣmas tato rājan duṣprekṣyo raśmivān iva
a tatas tat punar āvṛttaṃ yudhiṣṭhirabalaṃ mahat
c dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ mahābāhuṃ bhīṣmāyodyantam āhave
a tato bhīṣmaḥ kuruśreṣṭhaḥ siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥ
c dhanaṃjayarathaṃ śīghraṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
a kṣaṇena sa rathas tasya sahayaḥ sahasārathiḥ
c śaravarṣeṇa mahatā na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a vāsudevas tv asaṃbhrānto dhairyam āsthāya sātvataḥ
c codayām āsa tān aśvān vitunnān bhīṣmasāyakaiḥ
a tataḥ pārtho dhanur gṛhya divyaṃ jaladanisvanam
c pātayām āsa bhīṣmasya dhanuś chittvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a sa cchinnadhanvā kauravyaḥ punar anyan mahad dhanuḥ
c nimeṣāntaramātreṇa sajyaṃ cakre pitā tava
a vicakarṣa tato dorbhyāṃ dhanur jaladanisvanam
c athāsya tad api kruddhaś ciccheda dhanur arjunaḥ
a tasya tat pūjayām āsa lāghavaṃ śaṃtanoḥ sutaḥ
c sādhu pārtha mahābāho sādhu kuntīsuteti ca
a samābhāṣyainam aparaṃ pragṛhya ruciraṃ dhanuḥ
c mumoca samare bhīṣmaḥ śarān pārtharathaṃ prati
a adarśayad vāsudevo hayayāne paraṃ balam
c moghān kurvañ śarāṃs tasya maṇḍalāni vidarśayan
a śuśubhāte naravyāghrau bhīṣmapārthau śarakṣatau
c govṛṣāv iva saṃrabdhau viṣāṇollikhitāṅkitau
d tataḥ pravavṛte raudraḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
d pāṇḍavānāṃ ca mukhyasya kurūṇāṃ pravarasya ca
d tālamātre vikarṣantau tāv ubhau raṇakarkaśau
d dhanuṣī dṛḍhamuṣṭī tāv ubhau pautrapitāmahau
d śyāmasya palitenāsau saṃgamaḥ pratyaśobhata
d gaṅgāyamunayor yadvaj jalayoḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ
d pārthanāmāṅkitā bāṇāḥ petur bhīṣmasya vakṣasi
d nirguṇānāṃ kṛtaghnānāṃ manāṃsīva hi sādhuṣu
d bhīṣmasyāpi tato bāṇāḥ petur arjunavakṣasi
d mahādevapariprāptadhanurvidyāṃ jigīṣavaḥ
a vāsudevas tu saṃprekṣya pārthasya mṛduyuddhatām
c bhīṣmaṃ ca śaravarṣāṇi sṛjantam aniśaṃ yudhi
a pratapantam ivādityaṃ madhyam āsādya senayoḥ
c varān varān vinighnantaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya sainikān
a yugāntam iva kurvāṇaṃ bhīṣmaṃ yaudhiṣṭhire bale
c nāmṛṣyata mahābāhur mādhavaḥ paravīrahā
d vāsudevas tu saṃkruddho roṣāj jajvāla saṃyuge
a utsṛjya rajataprakhyān hayān pārthasya māriṣa
c kruddho nāma mahāyogī pracaskanda mahārathāt
e abhidudrāva bhīṣmaṃ sa bhujapraharaṇo balī
a pratodapāṇis tejasvī siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥ
c dārayann iva padbhyāṃ sa jagatīṃ jagatīśvaraḥ
a krodhatāmrekṣaṇaḥ kṛṣṇo jighāṃsur amitadyutiḥ
c grasann iva ca cetāṃsi tāvakānāṃ mahāhave
a dṛṣṭvā mādhavam ākrande bhīṣmāyodyantam āhave

e krośantaḥ prādravan sarve vāsudevabhayān narāḥ
a pītakauśeyasaṃvīto maṇiśyāmo janārdanaḥ
c śuśubhe vidravan bhīṣmaṃ vidyunmālī yathāmbudaḥ
a sa siṃha iva mātaṅgaṃ yūtharṣabha ivarṣabham
c abhidudrāva tejasvī vinadan yādavarṣabhaḥ
d pratodapāṇir bhagavāñ śuśubhe yādavarṣabhaḥ
d yathāṃśunārdayac candram amāvāsyāṃ divākaraḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya puṇḍarīkākṣam āhave

f praharasva yatheṣṭaṃ vai dāso 'smi tava cānagha
f nirguṇenāpi tottreṇa vāsudeva kṛtaṃ mama
f yo yogibhiś ca duṣprāpyaḥ sa ghātārtham ihāgataḥ
a anvag eva tataḥ pārthas tam anudrutya keśavam
c nijagrāha mahābāhur bāhubhyāṃ parigṛhya vai
a nigṛhyamāṇaḥ pārthena kṛṣṇo rājīvalocanaḥ
c jagāma cainam ādāya vegena puruṣottamaḥ
a pārthas tu viṣṭabhya balāc caraṇau paravīrahā
c nijaghrāha hṛṣīkeśaṃ kathaṃ cid daśame pade
a tata enam uvācārtaḥ krodhaparyākulekṣaṇam
c niḥśvasantaṃ yathā nāgam arjunaḥ paravīrahā

a mithyāvādīti lokas tvāṃ kathayiṣyati mādhava

a śape mādhava sakhyena satyena sukṛtena ca
c antaṃ yathā gamiṣyāmi śatrūṇāṃ śatrukarśana
a adyaiva paśya durdharṣaṃ pātyamānaṃ mahāvratam
c tārāpatim ivāpūrṇam antakāle yadṛcchayā
a mādhavas tu vacaḥ śrutvā phalgunasya mahātmanaḥ
b abhavat paramaprīto jñātvā pārthasya vikramam
c nakiṃcid uktvā sakrodha āruroha rathaṃ punaḥ
a tau rathasthau naravyāghrau bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punaḥ
c vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa megho vṛṣṭyā yathācalau
a prāṇāṃś cādatta yodhānāṃ pitā devavratas tava
c gabhastibhir ivādityas tejāṃsi śiśirātyaye
a yathā kurūṇāṃ sainyāni babhañja yudhi pāṇḍavaḥ
c tathā pāṇḍavasainyāni babhañja yudhi te pitā
a hatavidrutasainyās tu nirutsāhā vicetasaḥ
c nirīkṣituṃ na śekus te bhīṣmam apratimaṃ raṇe
d kurvāṇaṃ samare karmāṇy atimānuṣavikramam
e madhyaṃ gatam ivādityaṃ pratapantaṃ svatejasā
a te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa kāleneva yugakṣaye
c vīkṣāṃ cakrur mahārāja pāṇḍavā bhayapīḍitāḥ
d tathā pāṇḍavasainyāni drāvyamāṇāni bhārata
d vadhyamānā raṇe cāpi bhīṣmeṇāmitrakarśinā
a trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta gāvaḥ paṅkagatā iva
c pipīlikā iva kṣuṇṇā durbalā balinā raṇe
d tathaiva yodhā rājendra bhīṣmeṇāmitraghātinā
d samare mṛditāḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ
a mahārathaṃ bhārata duṣpradharṣaṃ
śaraughiṇaṃ pratapantaṃ narendrān
c bhīṣmaṃ na śekuḥ prativīkṣituṃ te
śarārciṣaṃ sūryam ivātapantam
a vimṛdnatas tasya tu pāṇḍusenām
astaṃ jagāmātha sahasraraśmiḥ
b tato 'pi bhīṣmaḥ sabalaḥ sasainyān
b nyavārayat pāṇḍusutāñ śaraughaiḥ
b jaghāna caitān subhṛśaṃ mahābalo
b mahāvrataḥ pāṇḍusutān mahātmā
b raṇe karūśādhipacedipair balair
b vṛtān sadā cakradharasya paśyataḥ
c tato balānāṃ śramakarśitānāṃ
mano 'vahāraṃ prati saṃbabhūva
d udayagiritaṭasthaḥ padminīṃ bodhayitvā
d mṛdutarakiraṇāgrais tāḥ svayaṃ copabhujya
d malinamadhupasaṅgāt tāsu saṃjātakopaḥ
d kṛtaruciravirocir bhānum astaṃ prayātaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yudhyatām eva teṣāṃ tu bhāskare 'stam upāgate
c saṃdhyā samabhavad ghorā nāpaśyāma tato raṇam
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā saṃdhyāṃ saṃdṛśya bhārata
c vadhyamānaṃ balaṃ cāpi bhīṣmeṇāmitraghātinā
a muktaśastraṃ parāvṛttaṃ palāyanaparāyaṇam
c bhīṣmaṃ ca yudhi saṃrabdham anuyāntaṃ mahārathān
a somakāṃś ca jitān dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān mahārathān
b niśāmukhaṃ ca saṃprekṣya ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
c cintayitvā ciraṃ dhyātvā avahāram arocayat
a tato 'vahāraṃ sainyānāṃ cakre rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c tathaiva tava sainyānām avahāro hy abhūt tadā
a tato 'vahāraṃ sainyānāṃ kṛtvā tatra mahārathāḥ
c nyaviśanta kuruśreṣṭha saṃgrāme kṣatavikṣatāḥ
a bhīṣmasya samare karma cintayānās tu pāṇḍavāḥ
c nālabhanta tadā śāntiṃ bhṛśaṃ bhīṣmeṇa pīḍitāḥ
a bhīṣmo 'pi samare jitvā pāṇḍavān saha sṛñjayaiḥ
c pūjyamānas tava sutair vandyamānaś ca bhārata
a nyaviśat kurubhiḥ sārdhaṃ hṛṣṭarūpaiḥ samantataḥ
c tato rātriḥ samabhavat sarvabhūtapramohinī
a tasmin rātrimukhe ghore pāṇḍavā vṛṣṇibhiḥ saha
c sṛñjayāś ca durādharṣā mantrāya samupāviśan
a ātmaniḥśreyasaṃ sarve prāptakālaṃ mahābalāḥ

c gajaṃ nalavanānīva vimṛdnantaṃ balaṃ mama
a na caivainaṃ mahātmānam utsahāmo nirīkṣitum
c lelihyamānaṃ sainyeṣu pravṛddham iva pāvakam

c tathā bhīṣmo raṇe kṛṣṇa tīkṣṇaśastraḥ pratāpavān
a gṛhītacāpaḥ samare vimuñcaṃś ca śitāñ śarān
c śakyo jetuṃ yamaḥ kruddho vajrapāṇiś ca devarāṭ
a varuṇaḥ pāśabhṛd vāpi sagado vā dhaneśvaraḥ
c na tu bhīṣmaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ śakyo jetuṃ mahāhave
a so 'ham evaṃ gate kṛṣṇa nimagnaḥ śokasāgare
c ātmano buddhidaurbalyād bhīṣmam āsādya saṃyuge
a vanaṃ yāsyāmi durdharṣa śreyo me tatra vai gatam
c na yuddhaṃ rocaye kṛṣṇa hanti bhīṣmo hi naḥ sadā
a yathā prajvalitaṃ vahniṃ pataṃgaḥ samabhidravan
c ekato mṛtyum abhyeti tathāhaṃ bhīṣmam īyivān
a kṣayaṃ nīto 'smi vārṣṇeya rājyahetoḥ parākramī
c bhrātaraś caiva me śūrāḥ sāyakair bhṛśapīḍitāḥ
a matkṛte bhrātṛsauhārdād rājyāt prabhraṃśanaṃ gatāḥ
c parikliṣṭā tathā kṛṣṇā matkṛte madhusūdana
a jīvitaṃ bahu manye 'haṃ jīvitaṃ hy adya durlabham
c jīvitasyādya śeṣeṇa cariṣye dharmam uttamam
a yadi te 'ham anugrāhyo bhrātṛbhiḥ saha keśava
c svadharmasyāvirodhena tad udāhara keśava
a etac chrutvā vacas tasya kāruṇyād bahuvistaram
c pratyuvāca tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sāntvayāno yudhiṣṭhiram
a dharmaputra viṣādaṃ tvaṃ mā kṛthāḥ satyasaṃgara
c yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrā durjayāḥ śatrusūdanāḥ
a arjuno bhīmasenaś ca vāyvagnisamatejasau
c mādrīputrau ca vikrāntau tridaśānām iveśvarau
a māṃ vā niyuṅkṣva sauhārdād yotsye bhīṣmeṇa pāṇḍava
c tvatprayukto hy ahaṃ rājan kiṃ na kuryāṃ mahāhave
a haniṣyāmi raṇe bhīṣmam āhūya puruṣarṣabham
c paśyatāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ yadi necchati phalgunaḥ
a yadi bhīṣme hate rājañ jayaṃ paśyasi pāṇḍava
c hantāsmy ekarathenādya kuruvṛddhaṃ pitāmaham

c vimuñcantaṃ mahāstrāṇi pātayiṣyāmi taṃ rathāt
a yaḥ śatruḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ macchatruḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ
c madarthā bhavadarthā ye ye madīyās tavaiva te
a tava bhrātā mama sakhā saṃbandhī śiṣya eva ca
c māṃsāny utkṛtya vai dadyām arjunārthe mahīpate
a eṣa cāpi naravyāghro matkṛte jīvitaṃ tyajet
c eṣa naḥ samayas tāta tārayema parasparam
e sa māṃ niyuṅkṣva rājendra yāvad dvīpo bhavāmy aham
a pratijñātam upaplavye yat tat pārthena pūrvataḥ
c ghātayiṣyāmi gāṅgeyam ity ulūkasya saṃnidhau
a parirakṣyaṃ ca mama tad vacaḥ pārthasya dhīmataḥ
c anujñātaṃ tu pārthena mayā kāryaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
a atha vā phalgunasyaiṣa bhāraḥ parimito raṇe

a evam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi mādhava
c sarve hy ete na paryāptās tava veganivāraṇe
a niyataṃ samavāpsyāmi sarvam eva yathepsitam
c yasya me puruṣavyāghra bhavān nātho mahābalaḥ
a sendrān api raṇe devāñ jayeyaṃ jayatāṃ vara
c tvayā nāthena govinda kim u bhīṣmaṃ mahāhave
a na tu tvām anṛtaṃ kartum utsahe svārthagauravāt
c ayudhyamānaḥ sāhāyyaṃ yathoktaṃ kuru mādhava
a samayas tu kṛtaḥ kaś cid bhīṣmeṇa mama mādhava
c mantrayiṣye tavārthāya na tu yotsye kathaṃ cana
e duryodhanārthe yotsyāmi satyam etad iti prabho
a sa hi rājyasya me dātā mantrasyaiva ca mādhava
c tasmād devavrataṃ bhūyo vadhopāyārtham ātmanaḥ
e bhavatā sahitāḥ sarve pṛcchāmo madhusūdana
a tad vayaṃ sahitā gatvā bhīṣmam āśu narottamam
c rucite tava vārṣṇeya mantraṃ pṛcchāma kauravam
a sa vakṣyati hitaṃ vākyaṃ tathyaṃ caiva janārdana
c yathā sa vakṣyate kṛṣṇa tathā kartāsmi saṃyuge
a sa no jayasya dātā ca mantrasya ca dhṛtavrataḥ
c bālāḥ pitrā vihīnāś ca tena saṃvardhitā vayam
a taṃ cet pitāmahaṃ vṛddhaṃ hantum icchāmi mādhava
b yasyāṅge krīḍitaṃ nityaṃ bālye ca parivardhitāḥ
b astrāṇi vidhivac caiva śikṣitāni janārdana
b taṃ hantum udyatāḥ kṛṣṇa rājyahetor vayaṃ yudhi
c pituḥ pitaram iṣṭaṃ vai dhig astu kṣatrajīvikām
d satyaṃ bṛhaspater vākyaṃ devānām agrataḥ kila
d bhāṣitaṃ guruṇā pūrvaṃ tan nibodha janārdana
d putraḥ pitaram āsādya pitā putraṃ ca mānada
d rājyārthe ghātayed evaṃ kṣatradharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato 'bravīn mahārāja vārṣṇeyaḥ kurunandanam
c rocate me mahābāho satataṃ tava bhāṣitam
a devavrataḥ kṛtī bhīṣmaḥ prekṣitenāpi nirdahet
c gamyatāṃ sa vadhopāyaṃ praṣṭuṃ sāgaragāsutaḥ

a te vayaṃ tatra gacchāmaḥ praṣṭuṃ kurupitāmaham

f caraṇopagatān gṛhya pariṣvajya ca pāṇḍavān

c svāgataṃ tava vārṣṇeya svāgataṃ te dhanaṃjaya

a kiṃ kāryaṃ vaḥ karomy adya yuṣmatprītivivardhanam

c uvāca vākyaṃ dīnātmā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d yathā pṛcchasi mām adya kathaṃ tan me ca vā vibho
a kathaṃ jayema dharmajña kathaṃ rājyaṃ labhemahi
c prajānāṃ saṃkṣayo na syāt kathaṃ tan me vadābhibho
a bhavān hi no vadhopāyaṃ bravītu svayam ātmanaḥ
c bhavantaṃ samare rājan viṣahema kathaṃ vayam

c maṇḍalenaiva dhanuṣā sadā dṛśyo 'si saṃyuge
a nādadānaṃ saṃdadhānaṃ vikarṣantaṃ dhanur na ca
c paśyāmas tvā mahābāho rathe sūryam iva sthitam
a narāśvarathanāgānāṃ hantāraṃ paravīrahan

a varṣatā śaravarṣāṇi mahānti puruṣottama

c bhavet sainyasya vā śāntis tan me brūhi pitāmaha
a tato 'bravīc chāṃtanavaḥ pāṇḍavān pāṇḍupūrvaja
c na kathaṃ cana kaunteya mayi jīvati saṃyuge

c kṣipraṃ mayi praharata yadīcchatha raṇe jayam

a evaṃ hi sukṛtaṃ manye bhavatāṃ vidito hy aham
c hate mayi hataṃ sarvaṃ tasmād evaṃ vidhīyatām
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a brūhi tasmād upāyaṃ no yathā yuddhe jayemahi

a śakyo vajradharo jetuṃ varuṇo 'tha yamas tathā
c na bhavān samare śakyaḥ sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a satyam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi pāṇḍava

a āttaśastro raṇe yatto gṛhītavarakārmukaḥ
