a nikṣiptaśastre patite vimuktakavacadhvaje
c dravamāṇe ca bhīte ca tavāsmīti ca vādini
d strījite strīpradhāne ca strīpradhāyini dharmaja
a striyāṃ strīnāmadheye ca vikale caikaputrake
c aprasūte ca duṣprekṣye na yuddhaṃ rocate mama
a imaṃ ca śṛṇu me pārtha saṃkalpaṃ pūrvacintitam
c amaṅgalyadhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā na yudhyeyaṃ kathaṃ cana
a ya eṣa draupado rājaṃs tava sainye mahārathaḥ
b apumāṃs tasya putras tu pūrvam āsīd viśāṃ pate
c śikhaṇḍī samarākāṅkṣī śūraś ca samitiṃjayaḥ
a yathābhavac ca strī pūrvaṃ paścāt puṃstvam upāgataḥ
c jānanti ca bhavanto 'pi sarvam etad yathātatham
a arjunaḥ samare śūraḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
c mām eva viśikhais tūrṇam abhidravatu daṃśitaḥ
a amaṅgalyadhvaje tasmin strīpūrve ca viśeṣataḥ
c na prahartum abhīpsāmi gṛhīteṣuṃ kathaṃ cana
a tad antaraṃ samāsādya pāṇḍavo māṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c śarair ghātayatu kṣipraṃ samantād bharatarṣabha
a na taṃ paśyāmi lokeṣu yo māṃ hanyāt samudyatam
c ṛte kṛṣṇān mahābhāgāt pāṇḍavād vā dhanaṃjayāt
a eṣa tasmāt purodhāya kaṃ cid anyaṃ mamāgrataḥ
c māṃ pātayatu bībhatsur evaṃ te vijayo bhavet
a etat kuruṣva kaunteya yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ mama
c tato jeṣyasi saṃgrāme dhārtarāṣṭrān samāgatān
 saṃjaya uvāca
a te 'nujñātās tataḥ pārthā jagmuḥ svaśibiraṃ prati
c abhivādya mahātmānaṃ bhīṣmaṃ kurupitāmaham
a tathoktavati gāṅgeye paralokāya dīkṣite
c arjuno duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ savrīḍam idam abravīt
a guruṇā kulavṛddhena kṛtaprajñena dhīmatā
c pitāmahena saṃgrāme kathaṃ yotsyāmi mādhava
a krīḍatā hi mayā bālye vāsudeva mahāmanāḥ
c pāṃsurūṣitagātreṇa mahātmā paruṣīkṛtaḥ
a yasyāham adhiruhyāṅkaṃ bālaḥ kila gadāgraja
c tātety avocaṃ pitaraṃ pituḥ pāṇḍor mahātmanaḥ
a nāhaṃ tātas tava pitus tāto 'smi tava bhārata
c iti mām abravīd bālye yaḥ sa vadhyaḥ kathaṃ mayā
a kāmaṃ vadhyatu me sainyaṃ nāhaṃ yotsye mahātmanā
c jayo vāstu vadho vā me kathaṃ vā kṛṣṇa manyase
d katham asmadvidhaḥ kṛṣṇa jānan dharmaṃ sanātanam
d nyastaśastre ca vṛddhe ca prahared dhi pitāmahe
 śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca
a pratijñāya vadhaṃ jiṣṇo purā bhīṣmasya saṃyuge
c kṣatradharme sthitaḥ pārtha kathaṃ nainaṃ haniṣyasi
a pātayainaṃ rathāt pārtha vajrāhatam iva drumam
c nāhatvā yudhi gāṅgeyaṃ vijayas te bhaviṣyati
a diṣṭam etat purā devair bhaviṣyaty avaśasya te
c hantā bhīṣmasya pūrvendra iti tan na tad anyathā
a na hi bhīṣmaṃ durādharṣaṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam
c tvad anyaḥ śaknuyād dhantum api vajradharaḥ svayam
a jahi bhīṣmaṃ mahābāho śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama
c yathovāca purā śakraṃ mahābuddhir bṛhaspatiḥ
a jyāyāṃsam api cec chakra guṇair api samanvitam
c ātatāyinam āmantrya hanyād ghātakam āgatam
a śāśvato 'yaṃ sthito dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dhanaṃjaya
c yoddhavyaṃ rakṣitavyaṃ ca yaṣṭavyaṃ cānasūyubhiḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a śikhaṇḍī nidhanaṃ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmasya bhavitā dhruvam
c dṛṣṭvaiva hi sadā bhīṣmaḥ pāñcālyaṃ vinivartate
a te vayaṃ pramukhe tasya sthāpayitvā śikhaṇḍinam
c gāṅgeyaṃ pātayiṣyāma upāyeneti me matiḥ
a aham anyān maheṣvāsān vārayiṣyāmi sāyakaiḥ
c śikhaṇḍy api yudhāṃ śreṣṭho bhīṣmam evābhiyāsyatu
a śrutaṃ te kurumukhyasya nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinam
c kanyā hy eṣā purā jātā puruṣaḥ samapadyata
d saṃjaya uvāca
d arjunasya vacaḥ śrutvā bhīṣmasya vadhasaṃyutam
d jahṛṣur hṛṣṭaromāṇaḥ sakṛṣṇāḥ pāṇḍavās tadā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity evaṃ niścayaṃ kṛtvā pāṇḍavāḥ sahamādhavāḥ
b anumānya mahātmānaṃ prayayur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
c śayanāni yathāsvāni bhejire puruṣarṣabhāḥ
d svān svān gṛhān abhigatās tāṃ rātrim avasan sukham
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam abhyavartata saṃyuge
c pāṇḍavāś ca tathā bhīṣmaṃ tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ prabhāte vimale sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
c vādyamānāsu bherīṣu mṛdaṅgeṣv ānakeṣu ca
a dhmāyatsu dadhivarṇeṣu jalajeṣu samantataḥ
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya niryātāḥ pāṇḍavā yudhi
a kṛtvā vyūhaṃ mahārāja sarvaśatrunibarhaṇam
c śikhaṇḍī sarvasainyānām agra āsīd viśāṃ pate
a cakrarakṣau tatas tasya bhīmasenadhanaṃjayau
c pṛṣṭhato draupadeyāś ca saubhadraś caiva vīryavān
a sātyakiś cekitānaś ca teṣāṃ goptā mahārathaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnas tataḥ paścāt pāñcālair abhirakṣitaḥ
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā yamābhyāṃ sahitaḥ prabhuḥ
c prayayau siṃhanādena nādayan bharatarṣabha
a virāṭas tu tataḥ paścāt svena sainyena saṃvṛtaḥ
c drupadaś ca mahārāja tataḥ paścād upādravat
a kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavān
c jaghanaṃ pālayām āsa pāṇḍusainyasya bhārata
a evaṃ vyūhya mahat sainyaṃ pāṇḍavās tava vāhinīm
c abhyadravanta saṃgrāme tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
a tathaiva kuravo rājan bhīṣmaṃ kṛtvā mahābalam
c agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ prayayuḥ pāṇḍavān prati
a putrais tava durādharṣai rakṣitaḥ sumahābalaiḥ
c tato droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ putraś cāsya mahārathaḥ
a bhagadattas tataḥ paścād gajānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
c kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca bhagadattam anuvratau
a kāmbojarājo balavāṃs tataḥ paścāt sudakṣiṇaḥ
c māgadhaś ca jayatsenaḥ saubalaś ca bṛhadbalaḥ
a tathetare maheṣvāsāḥ suśarmapramukhā nṛpāḥ
c jaghanaṃ pālayām āsus tava sainyasya bhārata
a divase divase prāpte bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhi
c āsurān akarod vyūhān paiśācān atha rākṣasān
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
c anyonyaṃ nighnatāṃ rājan yamarāṣṭravivardhanam
a arjunapramukhāḥ pārthāḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
c bhīṣmaṃ yuddhe 'bhyavartanta kiranto vividhāñ śarān
a tatra bhārata bhīmena pīḍitās tāvakāḥ śaraiḥ
c rudhiraughapariklinnāḥ paralokaṃ yayus tadā
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c tava sainyaṃ samāsādya pīḍayām āsur ojasā
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare tāvakā bharatarṣabha
c nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
a tatas tu tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vadhyamānaṃ samantataḥ
c saṃprādravad diśo rājan kālyamānaṃ mahārathaiḥ
a trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta tāvakā bharatarṣabha
c vadhyamānāḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a pīḍyamānaṃ balaṃ pārthair dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaḥ parākramī
c yad akārṣīd raṇe kruddhas tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a kathaṃ vā pāṇḍavān yuddhe pratyudyātaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
c vinighnan somakān vīrāṃs tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ācakṣe te mahārāja yad akārṣīt pitāmahaḥ
c pīḍite tava putrasya sainye pāṇḍavasṛñjayaiḥ
a prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvaja
c abhyavartanta nighnantas tava putrasya vāhinīm
a taṃ vināśaṃ manuṣyendra naravāraṇavājinām
c nāmṛṣyata tadā bhīṣmaḥ sainyaghātaṃ raṇe paraiḥ
a sa pāṇḍavān maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālāṃś ca sasṛñjayān
c abhyadravata durdharṣas tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
a sa pāṇḍavānāṃ pravarān pañca rājan mahārathān
c āttaśastrān raṇe yattān vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
d bhīṣmaḥ paramasaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
e nārācair vatsadantaiś ca śitair añjalikais tathā
f nānāśastrāstravarṣais tān vīryāmarṣapraveritaiḥ
a nijaghne samare kruddho hastyaśvam amitaṃ bahu
c rathino 'pātayad rājan rathebhyaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ padātīṃś ca samāgatān
c gajārohān gajebhyaś ca pareṣāṃ vidadhad bhayam
a tam ekaṃ samare bhīṣmaṃ tvaramāṇaṃ mahāratham
c pāṇḍavāḥ samavartanta vajrapāṇim ivāsurāḥ
a śakrāśanisamasparśān vimuñcan niśitāñ śarān
c dikṣv adṛśyata sarvāsu ghoraṃ saṃdhārayan vapuḥ
a maṇḍalīkṛtam evāsya nityaṃ dhanur adṛśyata
c saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya śakracāpanibhaṃ mahat
a tad dṛṣṭvā samare karma tava putrā viśāṃ pate
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ prāptāḥ pitāmaham apūjayan
a pārthā vimanaso bhūtvā praikṣanta pitaraṃ tava
c yudhyamānaṃ raṇe śūraṃ vipracittim ivāmarāḥ
e na cainaṃ vārayām āsur vyāttānanam ivāntakam
a daśame 'hani saṃprāpte rathānīkaṃ śikhaṇḍinaḥ
c adahan niśitair bāṇaiḥ kṛṣṇavartmeva kānanam
a taṃ śikhaṇḍī tribhir bāṇair abhyavidhyat stanāntare
c āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ kālasṛṣṭam ivāntakam
a sa tenātibhṛśaṃ viddhaḥ prekṣya bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinam
c anicchann api saṃkruddhaḥ prahasann idam abravīt
a kāmam abhyasa vā mā vā na tvāṃ yotsye kathaṃ cana
c yaiva hi tvaṃ kṛtā dhātrā saiva hi tvaṃ śikhaṇḍinī
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā śikhaṇḍī krodhamūrchitaḥ
c uvāca bhīṣmaṃ samare sṛkkiṇī parilelihan
d sarvam eva mahāyuddhaṃ śrutavantaṃ mahāraṇe
a jānāmi tvāṃ mahābāho kṣatriyāṇāṃ kṣayaṃkaram
c mayā śrutaṃ ca te yuddhaṃ jāmadagnyena vai saha
a divyaś ca te prabhāvo 'yaṃ sa mayā bahuśaḥ śrutaḥ
c jānann api prabhāvaṃ te yotsye 'dyāhaṃ tvayā saha
a pāṇḍavānāṃ priyaṃ kurvann ātmanaś ca narottama
c adya tvā yodhayiṣyāmi raṇe puruṣasattama
a dhruvaṃ ca tvā haniṣyāmi śape satyena te 'grataḥ
c etac chrutvā vaco mahyaṃ yat kṣamaṃ tat samācara
a kāmam abhyasa vā mā vā na me jīvan vimokṣyase
c sudṛṣṭaḥ kriyatāṃ bhīṣma loko 'yaṃ samitiṃjaya
a evam uktvā tato bhīṣmaṃ pañcabhir nataparvabhiḥ
c avidhyata raṇe rājan praṇunnaṃ vākyasāyakaiḥ
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c kālo 'yam iti saṃcintya śikhaṇḍinam acodayat
a ahaṃ tvām anuyāsyāmi parān vidrāvayañ śaraiḥ
c abhidrava susaṃrabdho bhīṣmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
a na hi te saṃyuge pīḍāṃ śaktaḥ kartuṃ mahābalaḥ
c tasmād adya mahābāho vīra bhīṣmam abhidrava
a ahatvā samare bhīṣmaṃ yadi yāsyasi māriṣa
c avahāsyo 'sya lokasya bhaviṣyasi mayā saha
a nāvahāsyā yathā vīra bhavema paramāhave
c tathā kuru raṇe yatnaṃ sādhayasva pitāmaham
a ahaṃ te rakṣaṇaṃ yuddhe kariṣyāmi paraṃtapa
c vārayan rathinaḥ sarvān sādhayasva pitāmaham
a droṇaṃ ca droṇaputraṃ ca kṛpaṃ cātha suyodhanam
c citrasenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca saindhavaṃ ca jayadratham
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaṃ ca sudakṣiṇam
c bhagadattaṃ tathā śūraṃ māgadhaṃ ca mahāratham
a saumadattiṃ raṇe śūram ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ ca rākṣasam
c trigartarājaṃ ca raṇe saha sarvair mahārathaiḥ
e aham āvārayiṣyāmi veleva makarālayam
a kurūṃś ca sahitān sarvān ye caiṣāṃ sainikāḥ sthitāḥ
c nivārayiṣyāmi raṇe sādhayasva pitāmaham
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam abhyadhāvat pitāmaham
c pāñcālyaḥ samare kruddho dharmātmānaṃ yatavratam
a ke 'rakṣan pāṇḍavānīke śikhaṇḍinam udāyudham
c tvaramāṇās tvarākāle jigīṣanto mahārathāḥ
a kathaṃ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ sa tasmin daśame 'hani
c ayudhyata mahāvīryaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥ
a na mṛṣyāmi raṇe bhīṣmaṃ pratyudyātaṃ śikhaṇḍinam
c kaccin na rathabhaṅgo 'sya dhanur vāśīryatāsyataḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a nāśīryata dhanus tasya rathabhaṅgo na cāpy abhūt
c yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme bhīṣmasya bharatarṣabha
e nighnataḥ samare śatrūñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a anekaśatasāhasrās tāvakānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c rathadantigaṇā rājan hayāś caiva susajjitāḥ
e abhyavartanta yuddhāya puraskṛtya pitāmaham
a yathāpratijñaṃ kauravya sa cāpi samitiṃjayaḥ
c pārthānām akarod bhīṣmaḥ satataṃ samitikṣayam
a yudhyamānaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ vinighnantaṃ parāñ śaraiḥ
c pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarva evābhyavārayan
a daśame 'hani saṃprāpte tatāpa ripuvāhinīm
c kīryamāṇāṃ śitair bāṇaiḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a na hi bhīṣmaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvaja
c aśaknuvan raṇe jetuṃ pāśahastam ivāntakam
a athopāyān mahārāja savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c trāsayan rathinaḥ sarvān bībhatsur aparājitaḥ
a siṃhavad vinadann uccair dhanurjyāṃ vikṣipan muhuḥ
c śaraughān visṛjan pārtho vyacarat kālavad raṇe
a tasya śabdena vitrastās tāvakā bharatarṣabha
c siṃhasyeva mṛgā rājan vyadravanta mahābhayāt
a jayantaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvatsainyaṃ cābhipīḍitam
c duryodhanas tato bhīṣmam abravīd bhṛśapīḍitaḥ
a eṣa pāṇḍusutas tāta śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c dahate māmakān sarvān kṛṣṇavartmeva kānanam
a paśya sainyāni gāṅgeya dravamāṇāni sarvaśaḥ
c pāṇḍavena yudhāṃ śreṣṭha kālyamānāni saṃyuge
a yathā paśugaṇān pālaḥ saṃkālayati kānane
c tathedaṃ māmakaṃ sainyaṃ kālyate śatrutāpana
a dhanaṃjayaśarair bhagnaṃ dravamāṇam itas tataḥ
c bhīmo hy eṣa durādharṣo vidrāvayati me balam
a sātyakiś cekitānaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c abhimanyuś ca vikrānto vāhinīṃ dahate mama
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā śūro rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
c vyadrāvayetāṃ sahasā sainyaṃ mama mahābalau
a vadhyamānasya sainyasya sarvair etair mahābalaiḥ
c nānyāṃ gatiṃ prapaśyāmi sthāne yuddhe ca bhārata
a ṛte tvāṃ puruṣavyāghra devatulyaparākrama
c paryāptaś ca bhavān kṣipraṃ pīḍitānāṃ gatir bhava
a evam ukto mahārāja pitā devavratas tava
c cintayitvā muhūrtaṃ tu kṛtvā niścayam ātmanaḥ
d pātayiṣye ripūn anyān pāṇḍavān pratipālayan
d pratijñāto jayo hy adya pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
e tava saṃdhārayan putram abravīc chaṃtanoḥ sutaḥ
a duryodhana vijānīhi sthiro bhava viśāṃ pate
c pūrvakālaṃ tava mayā pratijñātaṃ mahābala
a hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahātmanām
c saṃgrāmād vyapayātavyam etat karma mamāhnikam
e iti tat kṛtavāṃś cāhaṃ yathoktaṃ bharatarṣabha
a adya cāpi mahat karma prakariṣye mahāhave
c ahaṃ vā nihataḥ śeṣye haniṣye vādya pāṇḍavān
d aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ
d kiṃ punar martyadharmeṇa kṣatriyeṇa mahābala
a adya te puruṣavyāghra pratimokṣye ṛṇaṃ mahat
c bhartṛpiṇḍakṛtaṃ rājan nihataḥ pṛtanāmukhe
a ity uktvā bharataśreṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyān pratapañ śaraiḥ
c āsasāda durādharṣaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a anīkamadhye tiṣṭhantaṃ gāṅgeyaṃ bharatarṣabha
c āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ paryavārayan
a daśame 'hani tasmiṃs tu darśayañ śaktim ātmanaḥ
c rājañ śatasahasrāṇi so 'vadhīt kurunandana
a pañcālānāṃ ca ye śreṣṭhā rājaputrā mahābalāḥ
c teṣām ādatta tejāṃsi jalaṃ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ
a hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
c sārohāṇāṃ mahārāja hayānāṃ cāyutaṃ punaḥ
a pūrṇe śatasahasre dve padātīnāṃ narottamaḥ
c prajajvāla raṇe bhīṣmo vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
a na cainaṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ ke cic chekur nirīkṣitum
c uttaraṃ mārgam āsthāya tapantam iva bhāskaram
a te pāṇḍaveyāḥ saṃrabdhā maheṣvāsena pīḍitāḥ
c vadhāyābhyadravan bhīṣmaṃ sṛñjayāś ca mahārathāḥ
a sa yudhyamāno bahubhir bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadā
c avakīrṇo mahābāhuḥ śailo meghair ivāsitaiḥ
a putrās tu tava gāṅgeyaṃ samantāt paryavārayan
c mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ tato yuddham avartata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a arjunas tu raṇe rājan dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramam
c śikhaṇḍinam athovāca samabhyehi pitāmaham
a na cāpi bhīs tvayā kāryā bhīṣmād adya kathaṃ cana
c aham enaṃ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ pātayiṣye rathottamāt
a evam uktas tu pārthena śikhaṇḍī bharatarṣabha
c abhyadravata gāṅgeyaṃ śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā rājan saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥ
c hṛṣṭāv ādravatāṃ bhīṣmaṃ śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam
a virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau kuntibhojaś ca daṃśitaḥ
c abhyadravata gāṅgeyaṃ putrasya tava paśyataḥ
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dharmarājaś ca vīryavān
c tathetarāṇi sainyāni sarvāṇy eva viśāṃ pate
e samādravanta gāṅgeyaṃ śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitam
a pratyudyayus tāvakāś ca sametās tān mahārathān
c yathāśakti yathotsāhaṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
a citraseno mahārāja cekitānaṃ samabhyayāt
c bhīṣmaprepsuṃ raṇe yāntaṃ vṛṣaṃ vyāghraśiśur yathā
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahārāja bhīṣmāntikam upāgatam
c tvaramāṇo raṇe yattaṃ kṛtavarmā nyavārayat
d tvaramāṇaṃ raṇe yattaṃ saumadattir avārayat
a bhīmasenaṃ susaṃkruddhaṃ gāṅgeyasya vadhaiṣiṇam
c tvaramāṇo mahārāja saumadattir nyavārayat
a tathaiva nakulaṃ vīraṃ kirantaṃ sāyakān bahūn
c vikarṇo vārayām āsa icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitam
a sahadevaṃ tathā yāntaṃ yattaṃ bhīṣmarathaṃ prati
c vārayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvato yudhi
a rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ bhaimaseniṃ mahābalam
c bhīṣmasya nidhanaṃ prepsuṃ durmukho 'bhyadravad balī
a sātyakiṃ samare kruddham ārśyaśṛṅgir avārayat
b bhīṣmasya vadham icchantaṃ pāṇḍavaprītikāmyayā
c abhimanyuṃ mahārāja yāntaṃ bhīṣmarathaṃ prati
e sudakṣiṇo mahārāja kāmbojaḥ pratyavārayat
a virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau sametāv arimardanau
c aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddho vārayām āsa bhārata
a tathā pāṇḍusutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣiṇam
c bhāradvājo raṇe yatto dharmaputram avārayat
a arjunaṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
c bhīṣmaprepsuṃ mahārāja tāpayantaṃ diśo daśa
e duḥśāsano maheṣvāso vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a anye ca tāvakā yodhāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathān
c bhīṣmāyābhimukhaṃ yātān vārayām āsur āhave
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu sainyāni prākrośata punaḥ punaḥ
c abhidravata saṃrabdhā bhīṣmam ekaṃ mahābalam
a eṣo 'rjuno raṇe bhīṣmaṃ prayāti kurunandanaḥ
c abhidravata mā bhaiṣṭa bhīṣmo na prāpsyate hi vaḥ
a arjunaṃ samare yoddhuṃ notsahetāpi vāsavaḥ
c kim u bhīṣmo raṇe vīrā gatasattvo 'lpajīvitaḥ
a iti senāpateḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃhṛṣṭā gāṅgeyasya rathaṃ prati
a āgacchatas tān samare vāryoghān prabalān iva
c nyavārayanta saṃhṛṣṭās tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
a duḥśāsano mahārāja bhayaṃ tyaktvā mahārathaḥ
c bhīṣmasya jīvitākāṅkṣī dhanaṃjayam upādravat
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrā gāṅgeyasya rathaṃ prati
c abhyadravanta saṃgrāme tava putrān mahārathān
d ayodhayac ca samare tava putro mahārathaḥ
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma citrarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
c duḥśāsanarathaṃ prāpto yat pārtho nātyavartata
a yathā vārayate velā kṣubhitaṃ vai mahārṇavam
c tathaiva pāṇḍavaṃ kruddhaṃ tava putro nyavārayat
a ubhau hi rathināṃ śreṣṭhāv ubhau bhārata durjayau
c ubhau candrārkasadṛśau kāntyā dīptyā ca bhārata
a tau tathā jātasaṃrambhāv anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇau
c samīyatur mahāsaṃkhye mayaśakrau yathā purā
a duḥśāsano mahārāja pāṇḍavaṃ viśikhais tribhiḥ
c vāsudevaṃ ca viṃśatyā tāḍayām āsa saṃyuge
a tato 'rjuno jātamanyur vārṣṇeyaṃ vīkṣya pīḍitam
c duḥśāsanaṃ śatenājau nārācānāṃ samārpayat
e te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave
f yathaiva pannagā rājaṃs taṭākaṃ tṛṣitā yathā
a duḥśāsanas tataḥ kruddhaḥ pārthaṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
c lalāṭe bharataśreṣṭha śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a lalāṭasthais tu tair bāṇaiḥ śuśubhe pāṇḍavottamaḥ
c yathā merur mahārāja śṛṅgair atyartham ucchritaiḥ
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ putreṇa tava dhanvinā
c vyarājata raṇe pārthaḥ kiṃśukaḥ puṣpavān iva
a duḥśāsanaṃ tataḥ kruddhaḥ pīḍayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
c parvaṇīva susaṃkruddho rāhur ugro niśākaram
a pīḍyamāno balavatā putras tava viśāṃ pate
c vivyādha samare pārthaṃ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
a tasya pārtho dhanuś chittvā tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
c ājaghāna tataḥ paścāt putraṃ te navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya bhīṣmasya pramukhe sthitaḥ
c arjunaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a tasya kruddho mahārāja pāṇḍavaḥ śatrukarśanaḥ
c apraiṣīd viśikhān ghorān yamadaṇḍopamān bahūn
a aprāptān eva tān bāṇāṃś ciccheda tanayas tava
c yatamānasya pārthasya tad adbhutam ivābhavat
e pārthaṃ ca niśitair bāṇair avidhyat tanayas tava
a tataḥ kruddho raṇe pārthaḥ śarān saṃdhāya kārmuke
c preṣayām āsa samare svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
a nyamajjaṃs te mahārāja tasya kāye mahātmanaḥ
c yathā haṃsā mahārāja taḍāgaṃ prāpya bhārata
a pīḍitaś caiva putras te pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
c hitvā pārthaṃ raṇe tūrṇaṃ bhīṣmasya ratham āśrayat
e agādhe majjatas tasya dvīpo bhīṣmo 'bhavat tadā
a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ putras tava viśāṃ pate
c avārayat tataḥ śūro bhūya eva parākramī
a śaraiḥ suniśitaiḥ pārthaṃ yathā vṛtraḥ puraṃdaram
c nirbibheda mahāvīryo vivyathe naiva cārjunāt
 saṃjaya uvāca
a sātyakiṃ daṃśitaṃ yuddhe bhīṣmāyābhyudyataṃ tadā
c ārśyaśṛṅgir maheṣvāso vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a mādhavas tu susaṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghāna raṇe rājan prahasann iva bhārata
a tathaiva rākṣaso rājan mādhavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ardayām āsa rājendra saṃkruddhaḥ śinipuṃgavam
a śaineyaḥ śarasaṃghaṃ tu preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
c rākṣasāya susaṃkruddho mādhavaḥ paravīrahā
a tato rakṣo mahābāhuṃ sātyakiṃ satyavikramam
c vivyādha viśikhais tīkṣṇaiḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca
a mādhavas tu bhṛśaṃ viddho rākṣasena raṇe tadā
c dhairyam ālambya tejasvī jahāsa ca nanāda ca
a bhagadattas tataḥ kruddho mādhavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c tāḍayām āsa samare tottrair iva mahāgajam
a vihāya rākṣasaṃ yuddhe śaineyo rathināṃ varaḥ
c prāgjyotiṣāya cikṣepa śarān saṃnataparvaṇaḥ
a tasya prāgjyotiṣo rājā mādhavasya mahad dhanuḥ
c ciccheda śitadhāreṇa bhallena kṛtahastavat
a athānyad dhanur ādāya vegavat paravīrahā
c bhagadattaṃ raṇe kruddho vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ sṛkkiṇī saṃlihan muhuḥ
c śaktiṃ kanakavaiḍūryabhūṣitām āyasīṃ dṛḍhām
e yamadaṇḍopamāṃ ghorāṃ prāhiṇot sātyakāya vai
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā tasya bāhor baleritām
c sātyakiḥ samare rājaṃs tridhā ciccheda sāyakaiḥ
d sā hemavikṛtā śaktir mādhavasya bhujacyutaiḥ
e sā papāta tadā bhūmau maholkeva hataprabhā
a śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā putras tava viśāṃ pate
c mahatā rathavaṃśena vārayām āsa mādhavam
a tathā parivṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā vārṣṇeyānāṃ mahāratham
c duryodhano bhṛśaṃ hṛṣṭo bhrātṝn sarvān uvāca ha
a tathā kuruta kauravyā yathā vaḥ sātyako yudhi
c na jīvan pratiniryāti mahato 'smād rathavrajāt
e asmin hate hataṃ manye pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
a tat tatheti vacas tasya parigṛhya mahārathāḥ
c śaineyaṃ yodhayām āsur bhīṣmasya pramukhe tadā
a abhimanyuṃ tadāyāntaṃ bhīṣmāyābhyudyataṃ mṛdhe
c kāmbojarājo balavān vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a ārjunir nṛpatiṃ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c punar eva catuḥṣaṣṭyā rājan vivyādha taṃ nṛpam
a sudakṣiṇas tu samare kārṣṇiṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
c sārathiṃ cāsya navabhir icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitam
a tad yuddham āsīt sumahat tayos tatra parākrame
c yad abhyadhāvad gāṅgeyaṃ śikhaṇḍī śatrutāpanaḥ
a virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau vārayantau mahācamūm
c bhīṣmaṃ ca yudhi saṃrabdhāv ādravantau mahārathau
a aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddhaḥ samāyād rathasattamaḥ
c tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata
a virāṭo daśabhir bhallair ājaghāna paraṃtapa
b tato droṇasutaṃ yodhān dravamāṇaṃ mahāraṇe
c yatamānaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ drauṇim āhavaśobhinam
c visṛjantaṃ śarān dṛṣṭvā
a drupadaś ca tribhir bāṇair vivyādha niśitais tathā
c guruputraṃ samāsādya bhīṣmasya purataḥ sthitam
a aśvatthāmā tatas tau tu vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau bhīṣmaṃ prati samudyatau
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma vṛddhayoś caritaṃ mahat
c yad drauṇeḥ sāyakān ghorān pratyavārayatāṃ yudhi
a sahadevaṃ tathā yāntaṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvato 'bhyayāt
c yathā nāgo vane nāgaṃ matto mattam upādravat
a kṛpaś ca samare rājan mādrīputraṃ mahāratham
c ājaghāna śarais tūrṇaṃ saptatyā rukmabhūṣaṇaiḥ
a tasya mādrīsutaś cāpaṃ dvidhā ciccheda sāyakaiḥ
c athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya samare bhārasādhanam
c mādrīputraṃ susaṃhṛṣṭo daśabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e ājaghānorasi kruddha icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitam
a tathaiva pāṇḍavo rājañ śāradvatam amarṣaṇam
c ājaghānorasi kruddho bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣayā
e tayor yuddhaṃ samabhavad ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvaham
a nakulaṃ tu raṇe kruddhaṃ vikarṇaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c vivyādha sāyakaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā rakṣan bhīṣmasya jīvitam
a nakulo 'pi bhṛśaṃ viddhas tava putreṇa dhanvinā
b tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
c vikarṇaṃ saptasaptatyā nirbibheda śilīmukhaiḥ
a tatra tau naraśārdūlau bhīṣmahetoḥ paraṃtapau
c anyonyaṃ jaghnatur vīrau goṣṭhe govṛṣabhāv iva
a ghaṭotkacaṃ raṇe yattaṃ nighnantaṃ tava vāhinīm
c durmukhaḥ samare prāyād bhīṣmahetoḥ parākramī
a haiḍimbas tu tato rājan durmukhaṃ śatrutāpanam
c ājaghānorasi kruddho navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a bhīmasenasutaṃ cāpi durmukhaḥ sumukhaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ṣaṣṭyā vīro nadan hṛṣṭo vivyādha raṇamūrdhani
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe yāntaṃ bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣiṇam
c hārdikyo vārayām āsa rakṣan bhīṣmasya jīvitam
a vārṣṇeyaḥ pārṣataṃ śūraṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
c punaḥ pañcāśatā tūrṇam ājaghāna stanāntare
d   tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
d ājaghāna mahābāhuḥ pārṣataṃ taṃ mahāratham
a tathaiva pārṣato rājan hārdikyaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyādha niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatraparicchadaiḥ
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ bhīṣmahetor mahāraṇe
c anyonyātiśayair yuktaṃ yathā vṛtramahendrayoḥ
a bhīmasenam athāyāntaṃ bhīṣmaṃ prati mahābalam
c bhūriśravābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a saumadattir atho bhīmam ājaghāna stanāntare
c nārācena sutīkṣṇena rukmapuṅkhena saṃyuge
a uraḥsthena babhau tena bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
c skandaśaktyā yathā krauñcaḥ purā nṛpatisattama
a tau śarān sūryasaṃkāśān karmāraparimārjitān
c anyonyasya raṇe kruddhau cikṣipāte muhur muhuḥ
a bhīmo bhīṣmavadhākānṣkī saumadattiṃ mahāratham
c tathā bhīṣmajaye gṛdhnuḥ saumadattiś ca pāṇḍavam
d ayodhayetāṃ samare tulyavegau narottamau
e kṛtapratikṛte yattau yodhayām āsatū raṇe
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahārāja mahatyā senayā vṛtam
c bhīṣmāyābhimukhaṃ yāntaṃ bhāradvājo nyavārayat
d tatra yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
a droṇasya rathanirghoṣaṃ parjanyaninadopamam
c śrutvā prabhadrakā rājan samakampanta māriṣa
a sā senā mahatī rājan pāṇḍuputrasya saṃyuge
c droṇena vāritā yattā na cacāla padāt padam
a cekitānaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ bhīṣmaṃ prati janeśvara
c citrasenas tava sutaḥ kruddharūpam avārayat
a bhīṣmahetoḥ parākrāntaś citraseno mahārathaḥ
c cekitānaṃ paraṃ śaktyā yodhayām āsa bhārata
a tathaiva cekitāno 'pi citrasenam ayodhayat
c tad yuddham āsīt sumahat tayos tatra parākrame
a arjuno vāryamāṇas tu bahuśas tanayena te
c vimukhīkṛtya putraṃ te tava senāṃ mamarda ha
a duḥśāsano 'pi parayā śaktyā pārtham avārayat
c kathaṃ bhīṣmaṃ paro hanyād iti niścitya bhārata
a sā vadhyamānā samare putrasya tava vāhinī
c loḍyate rathibhiḥ śreṣṭhais tatra tatraiva bhārata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a atha vīro maheṣvāso mattavāraṇavikramaḥ
c samādāya mahac cāpaṃ mattavāraṇavāraṇam
a vidhunvāno dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ drāvayāṇo mahārathān
c pṛtanāṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ pātayāno mahārathaḥ
d yuktaḥ prītyā pāṇḍavānāṃ gāhamāno mahācamūm
a nimittāni nimittajñaḥ sarvato vīkṣya vīryavān
c pratapantam anīkāni droṇaḥ putram abhāṣata
a ayaṃ sa divasas tāta yatra pārtho mahārathaḥ
c jighāṃsuḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ paraṃ yatnaṃ kariṣyati
a utpatanti hi me bāṇā dhanuḥ prasphuratīva me
c yogam astrāṇi gacchanti krūre me vartate matiḥ
a dikṣu śāntāsu ghorāṇi vyāharanti mṛgadvijāḥ
c nīcair gṛdhrā nilīyante bhāratānāṃ camūṃ prati
a naṣṭaprabha ivādityaḥ sarvato lohitā diśaḥ
c rasate vyathate bhūmir anuṣṭanati vāhanam
a kaṅkā gṛdhrā balākāś ca vyāharanti muhur muhuḥ
c śivāś cāśivanirghoṣā vedayantyo mahad bhayam
a papāta mahatī colkā madhyenādityamaṇḍalāt
c sakabandhaś ca parigho bhānum āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
a pariveṣas tathā ghoraś candrabhāskarayor abhūt
c vedayāno bhayaṃ ghoraṃ rājñāṃ dehāvakartanam
a devatāyatanasthāś ca kauravendrasya devatāḥ
c kampante ca hasante ca nṛtyanti ca rudanti ca
a apasavyaṃ grahāś cakrur alakṣmāṇaṃ niśākaram
c avākśirāś ca bhagavān udatiṣṭhata candramāḥ
a vapūṃṣi ca narendrāṇāṃ vigatānīva lakṣaye
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu na ca bhrājanti daṃśitāḥ
a senayor ubhayoś caiva samantāc chrūyate mahān
c pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣo gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanaḥ
d tathā kilakilāśabdaḥ śrūyate vānarasya ca
d yasya lāṅgūlaśabdena sphuṭatīva nabhastalaṃ
a dhruvam āsthāya bībhatsur uttamāstrāṇi saṃyuge
c apāsyānyān raṇe yodhān abhyasyati pitāmaham
a hṛṣyanti romakūpāni sīdatīva ca me manaḥ
c cintayitvā mahābāho bhīṣmārjunasamāgamam
a taṃ caiva nikṛtiprajñaṃ pāñcālyaṃ pāpacetasam
c puraskṛtya raṇe pārtho bhīṣmasyāyodhanaṃ gataḥ
a abravīc ca purā bhīṣmo nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinam
c strī hy eṣā vihitā dhātrā daivāc ca sa punaḥ pumān
a amaṅgalyadhvajaś caiva yājñasenir mahārathaḥ
c na cāmaṅgalaketoḥ sa prahared āpagāsutaḥ
a etad vicintayānasya prajñā sīdati me bhṛśam
b abhyudyataṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā bhairavāstraṃ ca pāṇḍavam
c adyaiva tu raṇe pārthaḥ kuruvṛddham upādravat
a yudhiṣṭhirasya ca krodho bhīṣmārjunasamāgamaḥ
c mama cāstrābhisaṃrambhaḥ prajānām aśubhaṃ dhruvam
a manasvī balavāñ śūraḥ kṛtāstro dṛḍhavikramaḥ
c dūrapātī dṛḍheṣuś ca nimittajñaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
a ajeyaḥ samare caiva devair api savāsavaiḥ
c balavān buddhimāṃś caiva jitakleśo yudhāṃ varaḥ
a vijayī ca raṇe nityaṃ bhairavāstraś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c tasya mārgaṃ pariharan drutaṃ gaccha yatavratam
a paśya caitan mahābāho vaiśasaṃ samupasthitam
c hemacitrāṇi śūrāṇāṃ mahānti ca śubhāni ca
a kavacāny avadīryante śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c chidyante ca dhvajāgrāṇi tomarāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca
a prāsāś ca vimalās tīkṣṇāḥ śaktyaś ca kanakojjvalāḥ
c vaijayantyaś ca nāgānāṃ saṃkruddhena kirīṭinā
a nāyaṃ saṃrakṣituṃ kālaḥ prāṇān putropajīvibhiḥ
c yāhi svargaṃ puraskṛtya yaśase vijayāya ca
a hayanāgarathāvartāṃ mahāghorāṃ sudustarām
c rathena saṃgrāmanadīṃ taraty eṣa kapidhvajaḥ
d pūrvaṃ caiva mayāśrāvi tapasā ghorarūpiṇā
d brahmacaryeṇa mahatā phālgunaś carate tapaḥ
d tat tapaḥ saphalaṃ ceha kairāte savyasācinā
a brahmaṇyatā damo dānaṃ tapaś ca caritaṃ mahat
c ihaiva dṛśyate rājño bhrātā yasya dhanaṃjayaḥ
a bhīmasenaś ca balavān mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
c vāsudevaś ca vārṣṇeyo yasya nātho vyavasthitaḥ
a tasyaiṣa manyuprabhavo dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ
c tapodagdhaśarīrasya kopo dahati bhāratān
a eṣa saṃdṛśyate pārtho vāsudevavyapāśrayaḥ
c dārayan sarvasainyāni dhārtarāṣṭrāṇi sarvaśaḥ
a etad ālokyate sainyaṃ kṣobhyamāṇaṃ kirīṭinā
c mahorminaddhaṃ sumahat timineva nadīmukham
a hāhākilakilāśabdāḥ śrūyante ca camūmukhe
c yāhi pāñcāladāyādam ahaṃ yāsye yudhiṣṭhiram
a durlabhaṃ hy antaraṃ rājño vyūhasyāmitatejasaḥ
c samudrakukṣipratimaṃ sarvato 'tirathaiḥ sthitaiḥ
a sātyakiś cābhimanyuś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarau
c parirakṣanti rājānaṃ yamau ca manujeśvaram
a upendrasadṛśaḥ śyāmo mahāśāla ivodgataḥ
c eṣa gacchaty anīkāni dvitīya iva phalgunaḥ
a uttamāstrāṇi cādatsva gṛhītvānyan mahad dhanuḥ
c pārśvato yāhi rājānaṃ yudhyasva ca vṛkodaram
a ko hi necchet priyaṃ putraṃ jīvantaṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
c kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya tatas tvā viniyujmahe
a eṣa cāpi raṇe bhīṣmo dahate vai mahācamūm
c yuddhe susadṛśas tāta yamasya varuṇasya ca
d saṃjayaḥ
d putraṃ samanuśāsyaiva bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
d mahāraṇe mahārājaṃ dharmarājam ayodhayat
 etac chrutvā vacas tasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bhagadattaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥ
a citraseno vikarṇaś ca tathā durmarṣaṇo yuvā
c daśaite tāvakā yodhā bhīmasenam ayodhayan
a mahatyā senayā yuktā nānādeśasamutthayā
c bhīṣmasya samare rājan prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥ
a śalyas tu navabhir bāṇair bhīmasenam atāḍayat
c kṛtavarmā tribhir bāṇaiḥ kṛpaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a citraseno vikarṇaś ca bhagadattaś ca māriṣa
c daśabhir daśabhir bhallair bhīmasenam atāḍayan
a saindhavaś ca tribhir bāṇair jatrudeśe 'bhyatāḍayat
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
e durmarṣaṇaś ca viṃśatyā pāṇḍavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a sa tān sarvān mahārāja bhrājamānān pṛthak pṛthak
c pravīrān sarvalokasya dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathān
e vivyādha bahubhir bāṇair bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
a śalyaṃ pañcāśatā viddhvā kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥ
c kṛpasya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ madhye ciccheda bhārata
e athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
a vindānuvindau ca tathā tribhis tribhir atāḍayat
c durmarṣaṇaṃ ca viṃśatyā citrasenaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
a vikarṇaṃ daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pañcabhiś ca jayadratham
c viddhvā bhīmo 'nadad dhṛṣṭaḥ saindhavaṃ ca punas tribhiḥ
d droṇasya ca dhanur bhīmas tribhir bāṇair acicchide
a athānyad dhanur ādāya gautamo rathināṃ varaḥ
c bhīmaṃ vivyādha saṃrabdho daśabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a sa viddho bahubhir bāṇais tottrair iva mahādvipaḥ
c tataḥ kruddho mahābāhur bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
e gautamaṃ tāḍayām āsa śarair bahubhir āhave
a saindhavasya tathāśvāṃś ca sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya kālāntakasamadyutiḥ
a hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥ
c śarāṃś cikṣepa niśitān bhīmasenasya saṃyuge
a tasya bhīmo dhanurmadhye dvābhyāṃ ciccheda bhārata
c bhallābhyāṃ bharataśreṣṭha saindhavasya mahātmanaḥ
a sa cchinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
c citrasenarathaṃ rājann āruroha tvarānvitaḥ
a atyadbhutaṃ raṇe karma kṛtavāṃs tatra pāṇḍavaḥ
c mahārathāñ śarair viddhvā vārayitvā mahārathaḥ
e virathaṃ saindhavaṃ cakre sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
a nātīva mamṛṣe śalyo bhīmasenasya vikramam
c sa saṃdhāya śarāṃs tīkṣṇān karmāraparimārjitān
e bhīmaṃ vivyādha saptatyā tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca bhagadattaś ca māriṣa
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau citrasenaś ca saṃyuge
a durmarṣaṇo vikarṇaś ca sindhurājaś ca vīryavān
c bhīmaṃ te vivyadhus tūrṇaṃ śalyahetor ariṃdamāḥ
a sa tu tān prativivyādha pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c śalyaṃ vivyādha saptatyā punaś ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a taṃ śalyo navabhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
c sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena gāḍhaṃ vivyādha marmaṇi
a viśokaṃ vīkṣya nirbhinnaṃ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
c madrarājaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a tathetarān maheṣvāsāṃs tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥ
c tāḍayām āsa samare siṃhavac ca nanāda ca
a te hi yattā maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhadurmadam
c tribhis tribhir akuṇṭhāgrair bhṛśaṃ marmasv atāḍayan
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāso bhīmaseno na vivyathe
c parvato vāridhārābhir varṣamāṇair ivāmbudaiḥ
d sa tu krodhasamāviṣṭo bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
d madreśvaraṃ tribhir bāṇair bhṛśaṃ viddhvā mahāyaśāḥ
a śalyaṃ ca navabhir bāṇair bhṛśaṃ viddhvā mahāyaśāḥ
c prāgjyotiṣaṃ śatenājau rājan vivyādha vai dṛḍham
a tatas tu saśaraṃ cāpaṃ sātvatasya mahātmanaḥ
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena ciccheda kṛtahastavat
a athānyad dhanur ādāya kṛtavarmā vṛkodaram
c ājaghāna bhruvor madhye nārācena paraṃtapa
d virarāja mahābāhur lalāṭasthena patriṇā
d ekaśṛṅgo mahārāja yathā parvatasattamaḥ
d atha bhīmo mahābāhuḥ kruddhaḥ sarvān mahārathān
d vimukhīkṛtya bāṇaughais tasthau girir ivācalaḥ
a bhīmas tu samare viddhvā śalyaṃ navabhir āyasaiḥ
c bhagadattaṃ tribhiś caiva kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥ
a dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ ca vivyādha gautamaprabhṛtīn rathān
c te tu taṃ samare rājan vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a sa tathā pīḍyamāno 'pi sarvatas tair mahārathaiḥ
c matvā tṛṇena tāṃs tulyān vicacāra gatavyathaḥ
a te cāpi rathināṃ śreṣṭhā bhīmāya niśitāñ śarān
c preṣayām āsur avyagrāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a tasya śaktiṃ mahāvegāṃ bhagadatto mahārathaḥ
c cikṣepa samare vīraḥ svarṇadaṇḍāṃ mahādhanām
a tomaraṃ saindhavo rājā paṭṭiśaṃ ca mahābhujaḥ
c śataghnīṃ ca kṛpo rājañ śaraṃ śalyaś ca saṃyuge
a athetare maheṣvāsāḥ pañca pañca śilīmukhān
c bhīmasenaṃ samuddiśya preṣayām āsur ojasā
d tataḥ kruddho mahābāhur bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
d vivyādha samare vīras tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥ
d gautamapreritaṃ cāpi tomaraṃ tv anilātmajaḥ
d kṣurapreṇa dvidhā cakre prahasann iva bhārata
d hārdikyaprahitaṃ cāpi paṭṭasaṃ tilakāṇḍavat
d ciccheda samare vīro hy asaṃbhrāntarathaḥ śaraiḥ
d sa ciccheda śataghnīṃ ca saindhaveneritāṃ bhṛśam
d bhīmaseno raṇaślāghī navabhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
a tomaraṃ sa dvidhā cakre kṣurapreṇānilātmajaḥ
c paṭṭiśaṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiś ciccheda tilakāṇḍavat
a sa bibheda śataghnīṃ ca navabhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
c madrarājaprayuktaṃ ca śaraṃ chittvā mahābalaḥ
a śaktiṃ ciccheda sahasā bhagadatteritāṃ raṇe
c tathetarāñ śarān ghorāñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a bhīmaseno raṇaślāghī tridhaikaikaṃ samācchinat
c tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsāṃs tribhis tribhir atāḍayat
a tato dhanaṃjayas tatra vartamāne mahāraṇe
c jagāma sa rathenājau bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāratham
e nighnantaṃ samare śatrūn yodhayānaṃ ca sāyakaiḥ
a tau tu tatra mahātmānau sametau vīkṣya pāṇḍavau
c nāśaśaṃsur jayaṃ tatra tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabha
a athārjuno raṇe bhīṣmaṃ yodhayan vai mahāratham
c bhīṣmasya nidhanākāṅkṣī puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
a āsasāda raṇe yodhāṃs tāvakān daśa bhārata
c ye sma bhīmaṃ raṇe rājan yodhayanto vyavasthitāḥ
e bībhatsus tān athāvidhyad bhīmasya priyakāmyayā
a tato duryodhano rājā suśarmāṇam acodayat
c arjunasya vadhārthāya bhīmasenasya cobhayoḥ
a suśarman gaccha śīghraṃ tvaṃ balaughaiḥ parivāritaḥ
c jahi pāṇḍusutāv etau dhanaṃjayavṛkodarau
a tac chrutvā śāsanaṃ tasya trigartaḥ prasthalādhipaḥ
c abhidrutya raṇe bhīmam arjunaṃ caiva dhanvinau
a rathair anekasāhasraiḥ parivavre samantataḥ
c tataḥ pravavṛte yuddham arjunasya paraiḥ saha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a arjunas tu raṇe śalyaṃ yatamānaṃ mahāratham
c chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a suśarmāṇaṃ kṛpaṃ caiva tribhis tribhir avidhyata
c prāgjyotiṣaṃ ca samare saindhavaṃ ca jayadratham
a citrasenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca
c durmarṣaṇaṃ ca rājendra āvantyau ca mahārathau
a ekaikaṃ tribhir ānarchat kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ
c śarair atiratho yuddhe pīḍayan vāhinīṃ tava
a jayadratho raṇe pārthaṃ bhittvā bhārata sāyakaiḥ
c bhīmaṃ vivyādha tarasā citrasenarathe sthitaḥ
a śalyaś ca samare jiṣṇuṃ kṛpaś ca rathināṃ varaḥ
c vivyadhāte mahābāhuṃ bahudhā marmabhedibhiḥ
a citrasenādayaś caiva putrās tava viśāṃ pate
c pañcabhiḥ pañcabhis tūrṇaṃ saṃyuge niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e ājaghnur arjunaṃ saṃkhye bhīmasenaṃ ca māriṣa
a tau tatra rathināṃ śreṣṭhau kaunteyau bharatarṣabhau
c apīḍayetāṃ samare trigartānāṃ mahad balam
a suśarmāpi raṇe pārthaṃ viddhvā bahubhir āyasaiḥ
c nanāda balavan nādaṃ nādayan vai nabhastalam
a anye ca rathinaḥ śūrā bhīmasenadhanaṃjayau
c vivyadhur niśitair bāṇai rukmapuṅkhair ajihmagaiḥ
a teṣāṃ tu rathināṃ madhye kaunteyau rathināṃ varau
c krīḍamānau rathodārau citrarūpau vyarocatām
e āmiṣepsū gavāṃ madhye siṃhāv iva balotkaṭau
a chittvā dhanūṃṣi vīrāṇāṃ śarāṃś ca bahudhā raṇe
c pātayām āsatur vīrau śirāṃsi śataśo nṛṇām
a rathāś ca bahavo bhagnā hayāś ca śataśo hatāḥ
c gajāś ca sagajārohāḥ petur urvyāṃ mahāmṛdhe
a rathinaḥ sādinaś caiva tatra tatra nisūditāḥ
c dṛśyante bahudhā rājan veṣṭamānāḥ samantataḥ
a hatair gajapadātyoghair vājibhiś ca nisūditaiḥ
c rathaiś ca bahudhā bhagnaiḥ samāstīryata medinī
a chatraiś ca bahudhā chinnair dhvajaiś ca vinipātitaiḥ
b cāmarair hemadaṇḍaiś ca samāstīryata medinī
c aṅkuśair apaviddhaiś ca paristomaiś ca bhārata
d ghaṇṭābhiś ca kaśābhiś ca samāstīryata medinī
a keyūrair aṅgadair hārai rāṅkavair mṛditais tathā
b kuṇḍalair maṇicitraiś ca samāstīryata medinī
c uṣṇīṣair apaviddhaiś ca cāmaravyajanair api
a tatra tatrāpaviddhaiś ca bāhubhiś candanokṣitaiḥ
c ūrubhiś ca narendrāṇāṃ samāstīryata medinī
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma raṇe pārthasya vikramam
c śaraiḥ saṃvārya tān vīrān nijaghāna balaṃ tava
a putras tu tava taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmārjunasamāgamam
c gāṅgeyasya rathābhyāśam upajagme mahābhaye
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥ
c vindānuvindāv āvantyāv ājagmuḥ saṃyugaṃ tadā
a tato bhīmo maheṣvāsaḥ phalgunaś ca mahārathaḥ
c kauravāṇāṃ camūṃ ghorāṃ bhṛśaṃ dudruvatū raṇe
a tato barhiṇavājānām ayutāny arbudāni ca
c dhanaṃjayarathe tūrṇaṃ pātayanti sma saṃyuge
a tatas tāñ śarajālena saṃnivārya mahārathān
c pārthaḥ samantāt samare preṣayām āsa mṛtyave
a śalyas tu samare jiṣṇuṃ krīḍann iva mahārathaḥ
c ājaghānorasi kruddho bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tasya pārtho dhanuś chittvā hastāvāpaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
c athainaṃ sāyakais tīkṣṇair bhṛśaṃ vivyādha marmaṇi
a athānyad dhanur ādāya samare bhārasādhanam
c madreśvaro raṇe jiṣṇuṃ tāḍayām āsa roṣitaḥ
a tribhiḥ śarair mahārāja vāsudevaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ ca navabhir bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a tato droṇo mahārāja māgadhaś ca mahārathaḥ
c duryodhanasamādiṣṭau taṃ deśam upajagmatuḥ
a yatra pārtho mahārāja bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c kauravyasya mahāsenāṃ jaghnatus tau mahārathau
a jayatsenas tu samare bhīmaṃ bhīmāyudhaṃ yuvā
c vivyādha niśitair bāṇair aṣṭabhir bharatarṣabha
a taṃ bhīmo daśabhir viddhvā punar vivyādha saptabhiḥ
c sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharat
a udbhrāntais turagaiḥ so 'tha dravamāṇaiḥ samantataḥ
c māgadho 'pahṛto rājā sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a droṇas tu vivaraṃ labdhvā bhīmasenaṃ śilīmukhaiḥ
c vivyādha bāṇaiḥ suśitaiḥ pañcaṣaṣṭyā tam āyasaiḥ
a taṃ bhīmaḥ samaraślāghī guruṃ pitṛsamaṃ raṇe
c vivyādha navabhir bhallais tathā ṣaṣṭyā ca bhārata
a arjunas tu suśarmāṇaṃ viddhvā bahubhir āyasaiḥ
c vyadhamat tasya tat sainyaṃ mahābhrāṇi yathānilaḥ
a tato bhīṣmaś ca rājā ca saubalaś ca bṛhadbalaḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃkruddhā bhīmasenadhanaṃjayau
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrā dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c abhyadravan raṇe bhīṣmaṃ vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
a śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bhāratānāṃ pitāmaham
c abhyadravata saṃhṛṣṭo bhayaṃ tyaktvā yatavratam
a yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pārthāḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
c ayodhayan raṇe bhīṣmaṃ saṃhatāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ
a tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve puraskṛtya yatavratam
c śikhaṇḍipramukhān pārthān yodhayanti sma saṃyuge
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kauravāṇāṃ bhayāvaham
c tatra pāṇḍusutaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhīṣmasya vijayaṃ prati
a tāvakānāṃ raṇe bhīṣmo glaha āsīd viśāṃ pate
c tatra hi dyūtam āyātaṃ vijayāyetarāya vā
a dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja sarvasainyāny acodayat
c abhidravata gāṅgeyaṃ mā bhaiṣṭa narasattamāḥ
a senāpativacaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavānāṃ varūthinī
c bhīṣmam evābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā mahāhave
a bhīṣmo 'pi rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pratijagrāha tāṃ camūm
c āpatantīṃ mahārāja velām iva mahodadhiḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo daśame 'hani saṃjaya
c ayudhyata mahāvīryaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥ
a kuravaś ca kathaṃ yuddhe pāṇḍavān pratyavārayan
c ācakṣva me mahāyuddhaṃ bhīṣmasyāhavaśobhinaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ yathāyudhyanta bhārata
c yathā ca tad abhūd yuddhaṃ tat te vakṣyāmi śṛṇvataḥ
a preṣitāḥ paralokāya paramāstraiḥ kirīṭinā
c ahany ahani saṃprāptās tāvakānāṃ rathavrajāḥ
a yathāpratijñaṃ kauravyaḥ sa cāpi samitiṃjayaḥ
c pārthānām akarod bhīṣmaḥ satataṃ samitikṣayam
a kurubhiḥ sahitaṃ bhīṣmaṃ yudhyamānaṃ mahāratham
c arjunaṃ ca sapāñcālyaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃśayitā janāḥ
a daśame 'hani tasmiṃs tu bhīṣmārjunasamāgame
c avartata mahāraudraḥ satataṃ samitikṣayaḥ
a tasminn ayutaśo rājan bhūyaś ca sa paraṃtapaḥ
c bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yodhāñ jaghāna paramāstravit
a yeṣām ajñātakalpāni nāmagotrāṇi pārthiva
c te hatās tatra bhīṣmeṇa śūrāḥ sarve 'nivartinaḥ
a daśāhāni tatas taptvā bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍavavāhinīm
c niravidyata dharmātmā jīvitena paraṃtapaḥ
a sa kṣipraṃ vadham anvicchann ātmano 'bhimukhaṃ raṇe
c na hanyāṃ mānavaśreṣṭhān saṃgrāme 'bhimukhān iti
a cintayitvā mahābāhuḥ pitā devavratas tava
c abhyāśasthaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavaṃ vākyam abravīt
a yudhiṣṭhira mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśārada
c śṛṇu me vacanaṃ tāta dharmyaṃ svargyaṃ ca jalpataḥ
a nirviṇṇo 'smi bhṛśaṃ tāta dehenānena bhārata
c ghnataś ca me gataḥ kālaḥ subahūn prāṇino raṇe
a tasmāt pārthaṃ purodhāya pāñcālān sṛñjayāṃs tathā
c madvadhe kriyatāṃ yatno mama ced icchasi priyam
a tasya tan matam ājñāya pāṇḍavaḥ satyadarśanaḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ pratiyayau yattaḥ saṃgrāme saha sṛñjayaiḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato rājan pāṇḍavaś ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c śrutvā bhīṣmasya tāṃ vācaṃ codayām āsatur balam
a abhidravata yudhyadhvaṃ bhīṣmaṃ jayata saṃyuge
c rakṣitāḥ satyasaṃdhena jiṣṇunā ripujiṣṇunā
a ayaṃ cāpi maheṣvāsaḥ pārṣato vāhinīpatiḥ
c bhīmasenaś ca samare pālayiṣyati vo dhruvam
a na vai bhīṣmād bhayaṃ kiṃ cit kartavyaṃ yudhi sṛñjayāḥ
c dhruvaṃ bhīṣmaṃ vijeṣyāmaḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
d te tatheti pratijñāya puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
a tathā tu samayaṃ kṛtvā daśame 'hani pāṇḍavāḥ
c brahmalokaparā bhūtvā saṃjagmuḥ krodhamūrchitāḥ
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
c bhīṣmasya pātane yatnaṃ paramaṃ te samāsthitāḥ
a tatas tava sutādiṣṭā nānājanapadeśvarāḥ
c droṇena sahaputreṇa sahasenā mahābalāḥ
a duḥśāsanaś ca balavān saha sarvaiḥ sahodaraiḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ samaramadhyasthaṃ pālayāṃ cakrire tadā
a tatas tu tāvakāḥ śūrāḥ puraskṛtya yatavratam
c śikhaṇḍipramukhān pārthān yodhayanti sma saṃyuge
a cedibhiś ca sapāñcālaiḥ sahito vānaradhvajaḥ
c yayau śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam
a droṇaputraṃ śiner naptā dhṛṣṭaketus tu pauravam
c yudhāmanyuḥ sahāmātyaṃ duryodhanam ayodhayat
a virāṭas tu sahānīkaḥ sahasenaṃ jayadratham
c vṛddhakṣatrasya dāyādam āsasāda paraṃtapaḥ
d citrasenas tava sutaṃ vicitraśarakārmukam
a madrarājaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ sahasainyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmasenābhiguptaś ca nāgānīkam upādravat
a apradhṛṣyam anāvāryaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c droṇaṃ prati yayau yattaḥ pāñcālyaḥ saha somakaiḥ
a karṇikāradhvajaṃ cāpi siṃhaketur ariṃdamaḥ
c pratyujjagāma saubhadraṃ rājaputro bṛhadbalaḥ
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca putrās te pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
c rājabhiḥ samare sārdham abhipetur jighāṃsavaḥ
a tasminn atimahābhīme senayor vai parākrame
c saṃpradhāvatsv anīkeṣu medinī samakampata
a tāny anīkāny anīkeṣu samasajjanta bhārata
c tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā śāṃtanavaṃ raṇe
a tatas teṣāṃ prayatatām anyonyam abhidhāvatām
c prādurāsīn mahāñ śabdo dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata
a śaṅkhadundubhighoṣaiś ca vāraṇānāṃ ca bṛṃhitaiḥ
c siṃhanādaiś ca sainyānāṃ dāruṇaḥ samapadyata
a sā ca sarvanarendrāṇāṃ candrārkasadṛśī prabhā
c vīrāṅgadakirīṭeṣu niṣprabhā samapadyata
a rajomeghāś ca saṃjajñuḥ śastravidyudbhir āvṛtāḥ
c dhanuṣāṃ caiva nirghoṣo dāruṇaḥ samapadyata
a bāṇaśaṅkhapraṇādāś ca bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanāḥ
c rathagoṣaś ca saṃjagmuḥ senayor ubhayor api
a prāsaśaktyṛṣṭisaṃghaiś ca bāṇaughaiś ca samākulam
c niṣprakāśam ivākāśaṃ senayoḥ samapadyata
a anyonyaṃ rathinaḥ petur vājinaś ca mahāhave
c kuñjarāḥ kuñjarāñ jaghnuḥ padātīṃś ca padātayaḥ
a tad āsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c bhīṣmahetor naravyāghra śyenayor āmiṣe yathā
a tayoḥ samāgamo ghoro babhūva yudhi bhārata
c anyonyasya vadhārthāya jigīṣūṇāṃ raṇājire
 saṃjaya uvāca
a abhimanyur mahārāja tava putram ayodhayat
c mahatyā senayā yukto bhīṣmahetoḥ parākramī
a duryodhano raṇe kārṣṇiṃ navabhir nataparvabhiḥ
c ājaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ punaś cainaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tasya śaktiṃ raṇe kārṣṇir mṛtyor ghorām iva svasām
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho duryodhanarathaṃ prati
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā ghorarūpāṃ viśāṃ pate
c dvidhā ciccheda te putraḥ kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥ
a tāṃ śaktiṃ patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā kārṣṇiḥ paramakopanaḥ
c duryodhanaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a punaś cainaṃ śarair ghorair ājaghāna stanāntare
c daśabhir bharataśreṣṭha duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
a tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ citrarūpaṃ ca bhārata
c īkṣitṛprītijananaṃ sarvapārthivapūjitam
a bhīṣmasya nidhanārthāya pārthasya vijayāya ca
c yuyudhāte raṇe vīrau saubhadrakurupuṃgavau
a sātyakiṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe drauṇir brāhmaṇapuṃgavaḥ
c ājaghānorasi kruddho nārācena paraṃtapaḥ
a śaineyo 'pi guroḥ putraṃ sarvamarmasu bhārata
c atāḍayad ameyātmā navabhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
a aśvatthāmā tu samare sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c triṃśatā ca punas tūrṇaṃ bāhvor urasi cārpayat
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāso droṇaputreṇa sātvataḥ
c droṇaputraṃ tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna mahāyaśāḥ
a pauravo dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca śarair āsādya saṃyuge
c bahudhā dārayāṃ cakre maheṣvāsaṃ mahāratham
a tathaiva pauravaṃ yuddhe dhṛṣṭaketur mahārathaḥ
c triṃśatā niśitair bāṇair vivyādha sumahābalaḥ
a pauravas tu dhanuś chittvā dhṛṣṭaketor mahārathaḥ
c nanāda balavan nādaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya pauravaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghāna mahārāja trisaptatyā śilīmukhaiḥ
a tau tu tatra maheṣvāsau mahāmātrau mahārathau
c mahatā śaravarṣeṇa parasparam avarṣatām
a anyonyasya dhanuś chittvā hayān hatvā ca bhārata
c virathāv asiyuddhāya saṃgatau tau mahārathau
a ārṣabhe carmaṇī citre śatacandrapariṣkṛte
c tārakāśatacitrau ca nistriṃśau sumahāprabhau
a pragṛhya vimalau rājaṃs tāv anyonyam abhidrutau
c vāśitāsaṃgame yattau siṃhāv iva mahāvane
a maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi gatapratyāgatāni ca
c ceratur darśayantau ca prārthayantau parasparam
a pauravo dhṛṣṭaketuṃ tu śaṅkhadeśe mahāsinā
c tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a cedirājo 'pi samare pauravaṃ puruṣarṣabham
c ājaghāna śitāgreṇa jatrudeśe mahāsinā
a tāv anyonyaṃ mahārāja samāsādya mahāhave
c anyonyavegābhihatau nipetatur ariṃdamau
a tataḥ svaratham āropya pauravaṃ tanayas tava
c jayatseno rathe rājann apovāha raṇājirāt
a dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca samare mādrīputraḥ paraṃtapaḥ
c apovāha raṇe rājan sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
a citrasenaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ viddhvā navabhir āśugaiḥ
c punar vivyādha taṃ ṣaṣṭyā punaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a suśarmā tu raṇe kruddhas tava putraṃ viśāṃ pate
c daśabhir daśabhiś caiva vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a citrasenaś ca taṃ rājaṃs triṃśatā nataparvaṇām
c ājaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ sa ca taṃ pratyavidhyata
e bhīṣmasya samare rājan yaśo mānaṃ ca vardhayan
a saubhadro rājaputraṃ tu bṛhadbalam ayodhayat
b pārthahetoḥ parākrānto bhīṣmasyāyodhanaṃ prati
c ārjuniṃ kosalendras tu viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
e punar vivyādha viṃśatyā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a bṛhadbalaṃ ca saubhadro viddhvā navabhir āyasaiḥ
c nākampayata saṃgrāme vivyādha ca punaḥ punaḥ
a kausalyasya punaś cāpi dhanuś ciccheda phālguṇiḥ
c ājaghāna śaraiś caiva triṃśatā kaṅkapatribhiḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya rājaputro bṛhadbalaḥ
c phālguniṃ samare kruddho vivyādha bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tayor yuddhaṃ samabhavad bhīṣmahetoḥ paraṃtapa
c saṃrabdhayor mahārāja samare citrayodhinoḥ
e yathā devāsure yuddhe mayavāsavayor abhūt
a bhīmaseno gajānīkaṃ yodhayan bahv aśobhata
c yathā śakro vajrapāṇir dārayan parvatottamān
a te vadhyamānā bhīmena mātaṅgā girisaṃnibhāḥ
c nipetur urvyāṃ sahitā nādayanto vasuṃdharām
a girimātrā hi te nāgā bhinnāñjanacayopamāḥ
c virejur vasudhāṃ prāpya vikīrṇā iva parvatāḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiro maheṣvāso madrarājānam āhave
c mahatyā senayā guptaṃ pīḍayām āsa saṃgataḥ
a madreśvaraś ca samare dharmaputraṃ mahāratham
c pīḍayām āsa saṃrabdho bhīṣmahetoḥ parākramī
a virāṭaṃ saindhavo rājā viddhvā saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c navabhiḥ sāyakais tīkṣṇais triṃśatā punar ardayat
a virāṭaś ca mahārāja saindhavaṃ vāhinīmukhe
c triṃśatā niśitair bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntare
a citrakārmukanistriṃśau citravarmāyudhadhvajau
c rejatuś citrarūpau tau saṃgrāme matsyasaindhavau
a droṇaḥ pāñcālaputreṇa samāgamya mahāraṇe
c mahāsamudayaṃ cakre śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tato droṇo mahārāja pārṣatasya mahad dhanuḥ
c chittvā pañcāśateṣūṇāṃ pārṣataṃ samavidhyata
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya pārṣataḥ paravīrahā
c droṇasya miṣato yuddhe preṣayām āsa sāyakān
a tāñ śarāñ śarasaṃghais tu saṃnivārya mahārathaḥ
c droṇo drupadaputrāya prāhiṇot pañca sāyakān
a tasya kruddho mahārāja pārṣataḥ paravīrahā
c droṇāya cikṣepa gadāṃ yamadaṇḍopamāṃ raṇe
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitām
c śaraiḥ pañcāśatā droṇo vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a sā chinnā bahudhā rājan droṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
c cūrṇīkṛtā viśīryantī papāta vasudhātale
a gadāṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā pārṣataḥ śatrusūdanaḥ
c droṇāya śaktiṃ cikṣepa sarvapāraśavīṃ śubhām
a tāṃ droṇo navabhir bāṇaiś ciccheda yudhi bhārata
c pārṣataṃ ca maheṣvāsaṃ pīḍayām āsa saṃyuge
a evam etan mahad yuddhaṃ droṇapārṣatayor abhūt
c bhīṣmaṃ prati mahārāja ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
a arjunaḥ prāpya gāṅgeyaṃ pīḍayan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c abhyadravata saṃyattaṃ vane mattam iva dvipam
a pratyudyayau ca taṃ pārthaṃ bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
c tridhā bhinnena nāgena madāndhena mahābalaḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā mahendragajasaṃnibham
c paraṃ yatnaṃ samāsthāya bībhatsuḥ pratyapadyata
a tato gajagato rājā bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
c arjunaṃ śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a arjunas tu raṇe nāgam āyāntaṃ rajatopamam
c vimalair āyasais tīkṣṇair avidhyata mahāraṇe
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca kaunteyo yāhi yāhīty acodayat
c bhīṣmaṃ prati mahārāja jahy enam iti cābravīt
a prāgjyotiṣas tato hitvā pāṇḍavaṃ pāṇḍupūrvaja
c prayayau tvarito rājan drupadasya rathaṃ prati
a tato 'rjuno mahārāja bhīṣmam abhyadravad drutam
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya tato yuddham avartata
a tatas te tāvakāḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavaṃ rabhasaṃ raṇe
c sarve 'bhyadhāvan krośantas tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a nānāvidhāny anīkāni putrāṇāṃ te janādhipa
c arjuno vyadhamat kāle divīvābhrāṇi mārutaḥ
a śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bharatānāṃ pitāmaham
c iṣubhis tūrṇam avyagro bahubhiḥ sa samācinot
a somakāṃś ca raṇe bhīṣmo jaghne pārthapadānugān
c nyavārayata sainyaṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥ
a rathāgnyagāraś cāpārcir asiśaktigadendhanaḥ
c śarasaṃghamahājvālaḥ kṣatriyān samare 'dahat
a yathā hi sumahān agniḥ kakṣe carati sānilaḥ
c tathā jajvāla bhīṣmo 'pi divyāny astrāṇy udīrayan
a suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhiḥ śitaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c nādayan sa diśo bhīṣmaḥ pradiśaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
a pātayan rathino rājan gajāṃś ca saha sādibhiḥ
c muṇḍatālavanānīva cakāra sa rathavrajān
a nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan gajān aśvāṃś ca saṃyuge
c cakāra sa tadā bhīṣmaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
c niśamya sarvato rājan samakampanta sainikāḥ
a amoghā hy apatan bāṇāḥ pitus te manujeśvara
c nāsajjanta śarīreṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥ
a nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan suyuktāñ javanair hayaiḥ
c vātāyamānān paśyāma hriyamāṇān viśāṃ pate
a cedikāśikarūṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
c mahārathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥ
a aparāvartinaḥ śūrāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥ
c saṃgrāme bhīṣmam āsādya savājirathakuñjarāḥ
e jagmus te paralokāya vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
a na tatrāsīn mahārāja somakānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c yaḥ saṃprāpya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ jīvite sma mano dadhe
a tāṃś ca sarvān raṇe yodhān pretarājapuraṃ prati
c nītān amanyanta janā dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramam
a na kaś cid enaṃ samare pratyudyāti mahārathaḥ
c ṛte pāṇḍusutaṃ vīraṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
e śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca samare pāñcālyam amitaujasam
a śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe bhīṣmam āsādya bharatarṣabha
c daśabhir daśabhir bāṇair ājaghāna mahāhave
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ tu gāṅgeyaḥ krodhadīptena cakṣuṣā
c avaikṣata kaṭākṣeṇa nirdahann iva bhārata
a strītvaṃ tat saṃsmaran rājan sarvalokasya paśyataḥ
c na jaghāna raṇe bhīṣmaḥ sa ca taṃ nāvabuddhavān
a arjunas tu mahārāja śikhaṇḍinam abhāṣata
c abhitvarasva tvarito jahi cainaṃ pitāmaham
a kiṃ te vivakṣayā vīra jahi bhīṣmaṃ mahāratham
c na hy anyam anupaśyāmi kaṃ cid yaudhiṣṭhire bale
a yaḥ śaktaḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ yodhayeta pitāmaham
c ṛte tvāṃ puruṣavyāghra satyam etad bravīmi te
a evam uktas tu pārthena śikhaṇḍī bharatarṣabha
c śarair nānāvidhais tūrṇaṃ pitāmaham upādravat
a acintayitvā tān bāṇān pitā devavratas tava
c arjunaṃ samare kruddhaṃ vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a tathaiva ca camūṃ sarvāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c apraiṣīt samare tīkṣṇaiḥ paralokāya māriṣa
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan sainyena mahatā vṛtāḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ pracchādayām āsur meghā iva divākaram
a sa samantāt parivṛto bhārato bharatarṣabha
c nirdadāha raṇe śūrān vanaṃ vahnir iva jvalan
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣam
c ayodhayata yat pārthaṃ jugopa ca yatavratam
a karmaṇā tena samare tava putrasya dhanvinaḥ
c duḥśāsanasya tutuṣuḥ sarve lokā mahātmanaḥ
a yad ekaḥ samare pārthān sānugān samayodhayat
c na cainaṃ pāṇḍavā yuddhe vāyarām āsur ulbaṇam
a duḥśāsanena samare rathino virathīkṛtāḥ
c sādinaś ca mahārāja dantinaś ca mahābalāḥ
a vinirbhinnāḥ śarais tīkṣṇair nipetur dharaṇītale
c śarāturās tathaivānye dantino vidrutā diśaḥ
a yathāgnir indhanaṃ prāpya jvaled dīptārcir ulbaṇaḥ
c tathā jajvāla putras te pāṇḍavān vai vinirdahan
a taṃ bhāratamahāmātraṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c jetuṃ notsahate kaś cin nāpy udyātuṃ kathaṃ cana
e ṛte mahendratanayaṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
a sa hi taṃ samare rājan vijitya vijayo 'rjunaḥ
c bhīṣmam evābhidudrāva sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
a vijitas tava putro 'pi bhīṣmabāhuvyapāśrayaḥ
c punaḥ punaḥ samāśvasya prāyudhyata raṇotkaṭaḥ
e arjunaṃ ca raṇe rājan yodhayan sa vyarājata
a śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe rājan vivyādhaiva pitāmaham
c śarair aśanisaṃsparśais tathā sarpaviṣopamaiḥ
a na ca te 'sya rujaṃ cakruḥ pitus tava janeśvara
b jaghāna bāṇān gāṅgeyas tathā muktāñ śikhaṇḍinaḥ
c smayamānaś ca gāṅgeyas tān bāṇāñ jagṛhe tadā
a uṣṇārto hi naro yadvaj jaladhārāḥ pratīcchati
c tathā jagrāha gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhārāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ
a taṃ kṣatriyā mahārāja dadṛśur ghoram āhave
c bhīṣmaṃ dahantaṃ sainyāni pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
a tato 'bravīt tava sutaḥ sarvasainyāni māriṣa
c abhidravata saṃgrāme phalgunaṃ sarvato rathaiḥ
a bhīṣmo vaḥ samare sarvān palayiṣyati dharmavit
c te bhayaṃ sumahat tvaktvā pāṇḍavān pratiyudhyata
a eṣa tālena dīptena bhīṣmas tiṣṭhati pālayan
c sarveṣāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ raṇe śarma ca varma ca
a tridaśāpi samudyuktā nālaṃ bhīṣmaṃ samāsitum

a na cainaṃ pārthivā rājañ śekuḥ ke cin nirīkṣitum

a yamau ca cekitānaś ca kekayāḥ pañca caiva ha
